# Skyrim:Pilgrim's Trench

## Overview

Pilgrim's Trench

**Pilgrim's Trench** is a deep underwater ravine northwest of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") consisting of four submerged [shipwrecks](/wiki/Skyrim:Shipwrecks "Skyrim:Shipwrecks").

The trench is only marked as discovered if you dive down to the ships.

## Related Quests

- **[The Arms of Chaos](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arms_of_Chaos "Skyrim:The Arms of Chaos")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Arms_of_Chaos "Skyrim:Arms of Chaos"): Complete a mage's quest to reassemble two powerful staves.

## Walkthrough

The lone angler fish[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing")

The main ship (the one that isn't broken in two) has two chests containing minor loot. The first chest is just inside on the top deck beside the rest of the furniture. The second chest is on the lower deck along with five food barrels and a dresser and wardrobe both containing clothes.

There are no underwater predators at this location. [Salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(creature) "Skyrim:Salmon (creature)") swim in the waters. With the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, [arctic chars](/wiki/Skyrim:Arctic_Char "Skyrim:Arctic Char") also swim in the area, while a single [angler](/wiki/Skyrim:Angler "Skyrim:Angler") can be found beneath a rocky outcrop on the ocean floor. At least eleven [Nordic barnacles](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Barnacle "Skyrim:Nordic Barnacle") are nearby. Most are on the main ship, both inside and outside, with some on the ceilings inside.

Due to the depth, all races except [Argonians](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian "Skyrim:Argonian") will need a [waterbreathing](/wiki/Skyrim:Waterbreathing_(effect) "Skyrim:Waterbreathing (effect)") effect to explore this location. Explorers should allow 60 seconds of waterbreathing for a quick dive and three minutes for a leisurely perusal of the site.

You may learn what happened to the ships if you [summon](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Names "Skyrim:Forgotten Names") [Velehk Sain](/wiki/Skyrim:Velehk_Sain "Skyrim:Velehk Sain") in [the Midden](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Midden "Skyrim:The Midden"). He offers to give you some items he obtained during his time as a pirate in [Mundus](/wiki/Lore:Mundus "Lore:Mundus") when he and his companions sank some Imperial ships. The treasure is magically hidden on an island southeast of the trench (see [notes](#Notes)).

## Notes

- South of Pilgrim's Trench is a small unmarked camp consisting of a sheltered bedroll, a campfire, and some containers. Sitting on a barrel is a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:For_Shelly "Skyrim:For Shelly") written by [Trius](/wiki/Skyrim:Trius "Skyrim:Trius"), the camp's absent founder. If you fast travel to Pilgrim's Trench, you will arrive at this camp. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=84016&y=109776&zoom=17&legacy=true)
- There are two [shrines of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines#Shrine_of_Talos "Skyrim:Shrines") nearby, one to the southeast on an island, and the other to the south past the unmarked camp and east of [Hob's Fall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Hob%27s_Fall_Cave "Skyrim:Hob's Fall Cave") on the mainland.
  - Behind the statue of Talos on the island are some skeletal remains with a random [battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Battleaxe "Skyrim:Battleaxe"), an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"), and a copy of the [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Importance of Where](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Importance_of_Where "Skyrim:The Importance of Where")*. If you released Velehk Sain after summoning him in the Midden, his hidden treasure may be found south of the shrine at the base of the rocks. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=89647&y=109961&zoom=17&legacy=true)
  - At the feet of the statue of Talos on the mainland are a random [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword"), a random [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield"), a pair of random [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Boots "Skyrim:Armor"), a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), a [potion of the defender](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_the_Defender "Skyrim:Potion of the Defender"), and a copy of the [Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") skill book *[Words and Philosophy](/wiki/Skyrim:Words_and_Philosophy "Skyrim:Words and Philosophy")*.

# Skyrim:Pilgrimage

## Overview

Alessandra praying at the Shrine of Arkay

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Alessandra](/wiki/Skyrim:Alessandra "Skyrim:Alessandra").
2. Deliver [Alessandra's dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Alessandra%27s_Dagger "Skyrim:Alessandra's Dagger") to [Andurs](/wiki/Skyrim:Andurs "Skyrim:Andurs") in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").
3. Return to Alessandra.

### A Daughter's Path

Alessandra is the priestess of [Arkay](/wiki/Lore:Arkay "Lore:Arkay") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). She tends the [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Riften) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Riften)"), located beneath the [Temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara"), by herself. When you speak with her, you will note a certain bitterness about her position: *"I didn't ask for this job, I got stuck with it thanks to my father."* Her father was a Priest of Arkay and it was his desire that she follow his footsteps. As a result, her entire life has been spent around the dead, learning the proper burial rituals and prayers. While she seems to have accepted her lot in life, albeit reluctantly, she feels the need to make peace with her father. Unfortunately, her father did not live to see his daughter become a priest. Alessandra holds her father's ceremonial dagger as well as the one she received when she did complete the training. She asks you to journey to the [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Whiterun) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Whiterun)") in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") (see [Bugs](#Bugs)) to place her ceremonial dagger with her father's remains, fulfilling her honor-bound obligation to him and making peace with his memory. The dagger needs to be delivered to [Andurs](/wiki/Skyrim:Andurs "Skyrim:Andurs"), the caretaker at the Whiterun Hall of the Dead, who will inter it with her father's remains. If you agree to help her deliver the dagger, she'll appreciate your help and entrust you with it.

### The Pilgrimage

Travel to Whiterun and talk to Andurs in the Hall of the Dead. Hand [Alessandra's dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Alessandra%27s_Dagger "Skyrim:Alessandra's Dagger") to him and he will be delighted to see she finally decided to return it to her father: *"I will make sure this finds its way to his tomb as soon as possible. Thank you for bringing it, my child."*

Return to Alessandra and tell her that you have fulfilled her request. She will tell you she felt a caress on her cheek some time ago and she thinks it was a message from her father: *"We've made peace with one another without even uttering a single word and I'm content for the first time in my life."* She will then thank you for your selfless act, and tell you that you are welcome to come back and speak to her anytime.

The reward for this quest is one of the following five adept [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") spell tomes: [Close Wounds](/wiki/Skyrim:Close_Wounds "Skyrim:Close Wounds"), [Greater Ward](/wiki/Skyrim:Greater_Ward "Skyrim:Greater Ward"), [Heal Other](/wiki/Skyrim:Heal_Other "Skyrim:Heal Other"), [Repel Lesser Undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Repel_Lesser_Undead "Skyrim:Repel Lesser Undead"), and [Turn Undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Turn_Undead_(spell) "Skyrim:Turn Undead (spell)"), though there are some [bugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Pilgrimage#Bugs "Skyrim:Pilgrimage") with the quest reward.

## Bugs

- Alessandra says Andurs is in Windhelm, but he is actually in Whiterun.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.6, fixes this bug.
- When completing the quest, Alessandra may not give any reward, though her dialogue suggests otherwise: *"Here, please accept this as a token of your selfless action."* There is a minimum [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") skill level requirement of 40 before she gives you anything.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
- When given, the reward is every Restoration spell tome in the list, instead of a single random spell tome.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
- You can put Alessandra's dagger in a display case and complete the mission as though you still had the dagger.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 10, 200, 250.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformRiften13 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformRiften13`.

## Overview

Pinefrost Tower

**Pinefrost Tower** is a small ruined [tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Towers "Skyrim:Imperial Towers") northwest of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") containing leveled [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals").

## Walkthrough

The fallen tower is atop [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar")'s western mountains a short distance south of [Northwatch Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwatch_Keep "Skyrim:Northwatch Keep"). Two leveled snow animals or creatures (which may include [frost trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll"), [ice wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wolf "Skyrim:Ice Wolf"), [ice wraiths](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith "Skyrim:Ice Wraith"), or [snow bears](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Bear "Skyrim:Snow Bear")) guard the tower. There is a lit campfire with a pot hanging over it; inside the pot is a bowl of [venison stew](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison_Stew "Skyrim:Venison Stew"). Behind the fire are three pieces of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood"). Across the ramp near the lit campfire is a short flight of stairs. At the end of the stairs is an apprentice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing [leveled loot](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"). In front of the chest is a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and a random one-handed [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword").

# Skyrim:Pinemoon Cave

## Overview

| # of [Wood Chopping Blocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Chop_Wood "Skyrim:Chop Wood") | 1 |

Pinemoon Cave

**Pinemoon Cave** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") northwest of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") containing [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") and [wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf "Skyrim:Wolf"). It contains only one zone, *[Pinemoon Cave](#Pinemoon_Cave)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Culling the Beast](/wiki/Skyrim:Culling_the_Beast "Skyrim:Culling the Beast")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Kill the thin-blooded [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Kill the Vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Vampire "Skyrim:Kill the Vampire")**: Do menial work for [Sybille Stentor](/wiki/Skyrim:Sybille_Stentor "Skyrim:Sybille Stentor") by assaulting a vampire lair.
- **[Onmund's Request](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund%27s_Request "Skyrim:Onmund's Request")**: Help [Onmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund "Skyrim:Onmund") negotiate the return of a family amulet from [Enthir](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthir "Skyrim:Enthir"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

In front of the entrance is a small campsite with an extinguished campfire surrounded by several sawn logs arranged as seating. Nearby is also a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Chop_Wood "Skyrim:Chop Wood"), while three [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") mushrooms are growing around the entrance to the cave.

### Pinemoon Cave

The first area

The cave is contrasted between brightly lit areas and deep shadows, allowing for easy sneaking. It contains the highest concentration of [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") in the game, with a total of 66 fly amanita mushrooms.

You enter into a short tunnel lit by a lantern atop a barrel. The tunnel opens into the first of two cavern rooms, where you will encounter two leveled wolves. There are many rock pillars in this first room, which is brightly lit by three braziers on stands. Around this chamber are several deer skulls mounted on posts.

There is a small tunnel opposite you upon entering the chamber. It takes a couple turns before opening into the main area containing two vampires and one master vampire. There is a vampire standing near where you enter on a raised section above the main part of the room, with an earthen ramp leading down in front of where you enter. The vampire will have their back to you unless they have been alerted to your presence. The master vampire is visible at the back of the room wandering near a podium on another raised area. The third vampire is wandering near some wooden benches arranged in front of the podium.

The podium

Below the raised section via which you enter is a table with several barrels on either side containing [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") and [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"), as well as two sets of shelves farther to the right. These hold seven bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), four bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), and a random [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Stamina"). Against the southern wall of the room is another table with a dagger and a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_(dead) "Skyrim:Nord (dead)") corpse on top that may be [reanimated](/wiki/Skyrim:Reanimate "Skyrim:Reanimate") during the fight. There are more barrels on either side of the table.

On the raised area with the podium are two lit braziers on stands, one on either side of the podium, and a novice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). Two ramps, one wooden and one earthen, lead up to this area. There is a short tunnel leading from the western wall of the room to a bedroom, hosting an unowned double bed, an empty cage, and an unlocked large chest. You can find a copy of the [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Incident at Necrom](/wiki/Skyrim:Incident_at_Necrom "Skyrim:Incident at Necrom")* on a small table next to the cage.

## Notes

- The cave was once intended to house a unique faction of vampires, the Quarra Clan (presumably a part or splinter faction of the [Quarra Clan](/wiki/Lore:Quarra_Clan "Lore:Quarra Clan") of vampires previously seen in *[Morrowind](/wiki/Morrowind:Morrowind "Morrowind:Morrowind")*), under the leadership of Jelkar. They would have played a role in a set of [unused vampire-related quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Unfinished_Quests "Skyrim:Unfinished Quests").

# Skyrim:Pinepeak Cavern

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Cave.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Cave.png) | Cave: Pinepeak Cavern ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Pinepeak+Cavern)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Pinepeak_Cavern "Lore:Pinepeak Cavern")) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 2 |
| Occupants | |
| [Bears](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear "Skyrim:Bear") | |
| Important Treasure | |
| *[Heavy Armor Forging](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor_Forging "Skyrim:Heavy Armor Forging")* | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| PinepeakCavernExterior, PinepeakCavern01 | |
| Region | |
| [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") | |
| Location | |
| North of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") | |
| [Ore Veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") | |
| # of [Corundum](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore "Skyrim:Corundum Ore") | 1 |

Pinepeak Cavern

**Pinepeak Cavern** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") north of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") containing [bears](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear "Skyrim:Bear"). It contains only one zone, *[Pinepeak Cavern](#Pinepeak_Cavern)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Animal Extermination](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Extermination_(B) "Skyrim:Animal Extermination (B)")**: Fulfill a contract given to the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") to clear out a beast den. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Arniel's Endeavor](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor")**: Uncover an ancient Dwemer secret. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[A New Order](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Order "Skyrim:A New Order")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Recruit [Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran")'s old allies for the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

A warm welcome

Following the road north out of Ivarstead, cross the [Treva River](/wiki/Skyrim:Treva_River "Skyrim:Treva River") as if you were going to climb the "[7,000 steps](/wiki/Skyrim:Climb_the_Steps "Skyrim:Climb the Steps")" to High Hrothgar, and turn north at the start of the steps. The cave is on the shore opposite town. A bear guards the entrance. Two dead [hunters](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunter "Skyrim:Hunter") lie at the mouth of the cavern, and in front of the cave by a large rock is a [canis root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root").

### Pinepeak Cavern

Cavern interior

A short tunnel soon opens into the main cave, with blood splattered on the floor. A rock formation is in the middle of the chamber, and a ledge starts on your right and curves around the cave. A bear will be sleeping or roaming at the end of the ledge. There is nothing else of interest on the ledge. By the ledge below the bear is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), a leveled potion of healing, a smashed cart, a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), and a kettle containing a [diamond](/wiki/Skyrim:Diamond "Skyrim:Diamond"). To the right are the remains of an unfortunate person; among the bones is an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"). Finally, to the right of the remains is a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") and a copy of the [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Heavy Armor Forging](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor_Forging "Skyrim:Heavy Armor Forging")*.

## Notes

- Pinepeak Cavern also [appears](/wiki/Online:Pinepeak_Cavern "Online:Pinepeak Cavern") in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

## Bugs

- You may not be able to pick up the diamond. Nudge the kettle to tilt it slightly without dislodging the diamond, allowing you to reach the gem. You can also use the [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") or [Telekinesis](/wiki/Skyrim:Telekinesis_Effect "Skyrim:Telekinesis Effect") on the kettle, then take the diamond.

Pinewatch

**Pinewatch** is a [shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Shacks "Skyrim:Shacks") northeast of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). It contains two zones: *[Pinewatch](#Pinewatch)* and *[Pinewatch Bandit's Sanctuary](#Pinewatch_Bandit.27s_Sanctuary)*.

The cottage rests above a secret underground cave, which can be entered and cleared and the items for both related quests collected prior to starting the quests. With *[Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire")* installed, [Lakeview Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Lakeview_Manor "Skyrim:Lakeview Manor") is a short distance to the north, beyond the pool.

## Related Quests

- **[No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned")**: Find the [24 gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") to restore the Crown of Barenziah.
- **[Silver Lining](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Lining "Skyrim:Silver Lining")**: Recover a stolen [silver mold](/wiki/Skyrim:Curious_Silver_Mold "Skyrim:Curious Silver Mold") for a [silversmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Endon "Skyrim:Endon").

### Exterior

Along the path to the house from the road are two [thistles](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle "Skyrim:Thistle"), six [purple mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower"), three [red mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower"), and two [blue mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"). The cart in front of the cottage contains four [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek") and eight [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"). There is a small pool just to the northeast, with two [mudcrabs](/wiki/Skyrim:Mudcrab "Skyrim:Mudcrab") and a [Nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot") plant. There is a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack") on the south side of the house, and a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block") and a fenced garden at the rear. The garden contains six leek plants, five potato plants, and two [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bushes. To the right of the door, behind a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrel and sack, a  "Danger") Danger shadowmark is painted on the wall.

To the north are two [iron ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein"), and to the northwest is a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein"). Another corundum ore vein can be found due south, and another iron ore vein can be found to the east-southeast. With *Hearthfire* installed, there are two [stone quarries](/wiki/Skyrim:Quarried_Stone "Skyrim:Quarried Stone") nearby: one by the north side of the cottage, and the second farther north beyond the two iron ore veins near the location of Lakeview Manor.

Down the road to the southwest is a [bandit-controlled bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places_Falkreath#Bandit_Bridge:_Pinewatch "Skyrim:Unmarked Places Falkreath"), a lookout post where bandits and a [falling boulder trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Falling_Boulders "Skyrim:Falling Boulders") await unwary passersby. Going east toward [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen"), you will find another [bandit camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places_Falkreath#Bandit_Camp:_Helgen_Cliffs "Skyrim:Unmarked Places Falkreath") in a shallow cave crevice.

| Crops | Plants |
| --- | --- |
| 6 [Leek](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek")  5 [Potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") | 2 [Blue Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower")  6 [Purple Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower")  3 [Red Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower")  2 [Snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries")  2 [Thistle](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle "Skyrim:Thistle") |

### Pinewatch

The entrance is kept adept-locked at all times. The cottage is occupied by [Rhorlak](/wiki/Skyrim:Rhorlak "Skyrim:Rhorlak"), who will turn hostile when you enter unless you are on the quest [Silver Lining](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Lining "Skyrim:Silver Lining") (see the quest page for details). Everything inside the cottage (except the items held by Rhorlak) is marked as owned, and taking anything is considered stealing. However, entering the cottage is not considered trespassing.

Upon entering, you are in a single room the full size of the cottage. On your immediate left is a rack hanging from the ceiling which holds two [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant") and a whole [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)"). In the southern corner is a stack of crates over a flight of stairs that lead down to the basement along the southwest wall. The occupant is usually found downstairs. Opposite the doors, against the northwest wall is a dresser containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"), with two common [books](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books") on top. To the right is a wooden bench, and farther to the right is a small round wooden table with a small mead barrel on top. At the far end of the wall are some barrels and a cupboard holding an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"), a [Potion of True Shot](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_True_Shot "Skyrim:Potion of True Shot"), and three [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow"). On the floor in front of the cupboard are two [sabre cat pelts](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabre_Cat_Pelt "Skyrim:Sabre Cat Pelt"). Against the northeast wall is a long wooden table holding two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a [banded iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Banded_Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Banded Iron Shield"), a random [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword"), an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet"), a random [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe"), a [hunting bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow"), a random [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"), and two iron arrows. Above the table are two [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, a bunch of dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), and a bunch of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear").

In the eastern corner are more barrels with a crate on top, and beside these is another long wooden table against the southeast wall. On this table are three bottles of Nord mead, two potatoes, a [raw rabbit leg](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg"), a [pheasant breast](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant_Breast "Skyrim:Pheasant Breast"), a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish") steak, a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), and some [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and cheese. Hanging over this table are two more racks holding a total of four [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), a pheasant, and a whole salmon. To the right is a set of shelves holding six common books, two [hats](/wiki/Skyrim:Hat "Skyrim:Hat"), a pair of [leather bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Bracers "Skyrim:Leather Bracers"), a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic"), and two pairs of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots"). Beside the shelves is a round table, and near the door, pinned to the wall by an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), is a *[warning note](/wiki/Skyrim:Warning "Skyrim:Warning")*.

Pinewatch downstairs

Descend the stairs to another room of the same size. On your left is a cupboard holding two [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), two potatoes, two raw rabbit legs, and four [salt piles](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"). To the right is a fireplace, with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") on a hearthstone and a bulb of garlic beside it. On the mantelpiece are three iron daggers, a bowl of [troll fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat"), and a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"). To the right of the fireplace is a pile of firewood with a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") leaning against it, and behind the firewood is another cupboard which holds only clutter. Hanging over the cupboard are three bunches of dried elves ear and two bunches of dried frost mirriam. Coming out of the middle of the northeast wall is a single owned bed, with an end table to the left holding two bottles of Nord mead. To the right is a dresser containing clothes, with a [steel mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Mace "Skyrim:Steel Mace") on top. Under the bed is a pair of random [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Boots "Skyrim:Armor").

Against the southeast wall is a round wooden table and chairs with a loaf of bread and two more bottles of Nord mead. To the right is an empty set of shelves, with a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") beside it on the floor and two loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") on the floor in front. To the right of the shelves is a long wooden table holding a *[Note to Rhorlak](/wiki/Skyrim:Note_to_Rhorlak "Skyrim:Note to Rhorlak")*, a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), five loose coins, a random war axe, a quiver of iron arrows, and a [bear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap"). On the wall immediately to the left of the table is a button that swings open the shelves, revealing a tunnel behind. There is a bucket containing three bottles of wine immediately behind the shelves, which are a bonus as mentioned in the note to Rhorlak. Most of the bandits below are leveled, and most are within earshot of several others, which can lead to some challenging battles.

Beneath the cottage

At the bottom, the tunnel opens into a large chamber with architecture similar to Nordic barrows, with wooden platforms on scaffolding linked by wooden bridges. On your immediate right, leaning against the wall is a woodcutter's axe, while on your immediate left is a set of shelves holding a quiver of random [arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Arrows "Skyrim:Arrows"), a bear trap, and a copy of the [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Red Kitchen Reader](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Red_Kitchen_Reader "Skyrim:The Red Kitchen Reader")*. Farther to the left is the corpse of a [High Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf_(NPC) "Skyrim:High Elf (NPC)") with an iron dagger in their back, in front of another set of shelves holding a random [healing potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Healing"), a random [stamina potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Stamina"), a [hide shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Shield "Skyrim:Hide Shield"), an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet"), and a woodcutter's axe. To the right is a cart containing several cheese wheels and potatoes, with a flight of wooden stairs descending to the ground level below. To the right of the tunnel past a wall of wooden planking is a narrow bridge linking to the first platform.

On the far side of the first bridge is a bandit standing guard, with a second farther to the left. Beneath the platforms and bridge is a rubble-choked chamber. On the far side of the first bridge is a crossroads, with a second bridge behind continuing to the north, a door on the right that is barred from the other side (which will be a shortcut back out later), and a bridge crossing to a level-locked door to the west. Behind this door is a small alcove with a set of shelves holding four bottles of alto wine, three bottles of wine, a random potion of health, a random potion of stamina, a random [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), a random [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"), and a bottle of [frostbite venom](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Venom "Skyrim:Frostbite Venom"). Another bridge leads past the alcove to the north and meets up with a second western bridge connecting to the other northern bridge across the gap; continuing to the north leads into another chamber. Another bandit patrols the bridge heading west; any noise at this point can alert the bandit and cause them to investigate. The chamber to the north contains nothing of interest, and only provides an alternative route down to the ground level in the first chamber. In this chamber, there is a wooden ramp on the left and an earthen ramp on the right, both descending to the ground. A short tunnel heading southwest leads back beneath the platforms and bridges in the first chamber.

Spike pit

At ground level, near the southern corner of the chamber is an apprentice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") by a rock pillar with a torch above it, close to the front of the chamber and the first wooden bridge crossed previously. There are several carts nearby, with several cabbages strewn across the ground. To the north of the stairs is a [trap door](/wiki/Skyrim:Trap_Door "Skyrim:Trap Door"), with a lever to the right and another at the rear that both operate the door. The corpses of two [Khajiit](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit_(dead) "Skyrim:Khajiit (dead)") lie on top of the trap door. Under the flight of stairs is a tunnel, with a bear trap partway along it. After two turns, the tunnel descends into a small [spike pit](/wiki/Skyrim:Spike_Pit "Skyrim:Spike Pit") beneath the trap door. Among the stakes are several human bones, the bodies of two more dead Khajiit, a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), and a lit [torch](/wiki/Skyrim:Torch "Skyrim:Torch"). Returning to ground level, a short distance east of the trap door is a woodcutter's axe stuck in a block of wood, and beyond that is another bear trap on the ground.

Pinewatch chamber

Following the platforms and crossing the bridges to the west leads to a narrow corridor and a small empty room, with another chamber beyond containing a total of three bandits. One of the bandits is usually found working a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), a second patrols the chamber, and the third just stands around. The chamber is filled with stacks of crates, barrels, sacks, and furniture. There is an unlocked chest near the bottom of a ramp to the north of the grindstone. The ramp leads up to a stone walkway running across the chamber. At the top of the ramp is an [oil lantern](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Lanterns "Skyrim:Oil Lanterns") hanging above a broken urn, while an intact [urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn") is on the walkway to the east. At the rear of the chamber, to the north, part of the walkway is separated from the rest. A wooden ramp leads up to a novice-locked chest on this separate section of walkway. Beneath this section, a path descends to the southeast to a wooden door that leads into *[Pinewatch Bandit's Sanctuary](#Pinewatch_Bandit.27s_Sanctuary)*. Just in front and to the left of the door is a final bandit standing against the wall, and four loose coins are on the ground in front of the door.

### Pinewatch Bandit's Sanctuary

Pinewatch sanctuary

The architecture in this zone is still that of typical [Nordic barrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins"). Ahead is a chamber with [bone chimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Chimes "Skyrim:Bone Chimes") hanging from the ceiling in front, which may be avoided by passing to the left. The chamber beyond is filled with stacks of crates and barrels in rows on either side of a long wooden table in the center. There are three bandits sitting at the table, one of which is a magic-user who has a preference for shock magic. All three of the bandits carry a copy of *[Roras's Letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Roras%27s_Letter "Skyrim:Roras's Letter")*, which details a plot to break into the treasure room by Roras, whom the previous warning note has revealed to be dead. On the table are five bottles of Nord mead, four of them in a basket. A path runs behind the stack on the left, with a bear trap on the ground at either end. There are four common books on top of a barrel near the front of the chamber. Partway along the stack on the left is a novice-locked chest, just before a rock pillar. Nearby on the same side, just after the pillar, is an expert-locked chest. There is a barrel next to the second chest with a basket on top containing another five bottles of Nord mead. Along the southwest wall is an earthen ramp, which starts at the rear of the room and rises toward the front. At the top of the ramp is a short narrow tunnel heading west into another chamber. You can hear a bandit singing or talking to themselves as they patrol the chamber ahead.

There are several rock pillars supporting the ceiling and blocking a clear view of the next chamber. There is only the one bandit patrolling this chamber. Between the pillars is a bear trap, and against the northern wall are two level-locked square cages. The left-hand cage can be opened with the [Pinewatch Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinewatch_Key "Skyrim:Pinewatch Key"), which is carried by [Rigel Strong-Arm](/wiki/Skyrim:Rigel_Strong-Arm "Skyrim:Rigel Strong-Arm"). However, neither cage contains anything of interest. To the southwest is a large arch with wooden beams supporting it. To the right under the arch is a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), and just beyond is the body of a dead bandit near part of a walkway that has fallen from above. At the end of the chamber is a narrow flight of stone stairs leading up to a wooden door.

Dead draugr

Beyond the door is a chamber guarded by a single bandit with five upright sarcophagi against the walls, in front of each of which is a [dead draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Draugr "Skyrim:Containers"). To the west is a level-locked wooden door, and to the east an irregular tunnel. The door opens to reveal a small room containing a novice-locked chest with an adept-locked [tension cable](/wiki/Skyrim:Tension_Cable "Skyrim:Tension Cable") that triggers a [spear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_Trap "Skyrim:Spear Trap") from directly behind the chest. There are two small coin purses on the floor to the right of the chest. Against the walls are two sets of shelves holding a quiver of random [arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Arrows "Skyrim:Arrows"), an empty random [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), an [unusual gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem"), a random poison, eight common [books](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books"), a random [light armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") [cuirass](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor"), a pair of random boots, a random potion of healing, s small coin purse, and four loose coins.

Bandit dormitory

The tunnel to the east turns south, with another copy of the *Warning* and another iron dagger on the ground at the turning. Ahead, the tunnel opens into a cave that is being used as a dormitory. Opposite, a bandit is sleeping in a single bed, with four other unowned single beds in the chamber. Any fighting will alert four more leveled bandits, who are behind the wooden wall to the left on which is a mounted elk's head. To the southwest is a long wooden table and a chair, with another copy of *Roras's letter* on the table. There are two dressers between some of the beds opposite, one of which has a random [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow") and a random [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword"). On the left, against a wooden wall, are two sets of shelves holding three sets of random armor, two random [helmets](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet"), and three pairs of random boots. To the left of these shelves is yet another copy of the *Warning* stuck to the wall with another iron dagger.

Bandit bar

Behind the wooden wall to the east is a chamber with a bar set up at the far end and two long wooden tables and chairs at the near end. Both tables have a bottle of Nord mead on top. Against the other side of the wooden wall are two more sets of shelves, which are empty. In front of the bar is a campfire with two pots hanging over it, one containing two baked potatoes, and the other holding four portions of grilled leeks. Beside the fire is a woodcutter's axe. The counter is in a L-shape, and has a bottle of Nord mead on top, and an [iron warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Warhammer "Skyrim:Iron Warhammer"), three bottles of wine, two random poisons, and a sack of food underneath. Behind the counter is a set of shelves holding eight more bottles of Nord mead. Beside the shelves is a stack of barrels. In the middle of the north wall is a short tunnel, with yet another *Warning* pinned to the wall by an iron dagger to the left.

Bone chime trapped room

The tunnel leads to another chamber, with many bone chimes hanging from ropes strung across the room, and two long wooden tables and chairs laid end-to-end. Behind the tables is another wooden wall, with the skull of a mammoth on top. Care must be taken to avoid the chimes; start on the right, pass the tables on the right, and then hug the wooden wall to avoid any noise. Against the east wall is a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"). On the tables and floor are more copies of the *Warning*, a *[Father's Missive](/wiki/Skyrim:Father%27s_Missive "Skyrim:Father's Missive")* that expresses a father's concern over his daughter's banditry, and *[Rigel's letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Rigel%27s_Letter "Skyrim:Rigel's Letter")*, which is an explanation to her father of why she has turned to banditry. Against the wooden wall is another set of shelves holding seven common books, six bottles of alto wine, a bottle of wine, a random potion of healing, and a [troll skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Skull "Skyrim:Troll Skull"). In the southwestern corner is a set of shelves holding ten more common books.

Rigel's sleeping quarters

Behind the wooden wall to the north is Rigel Strong-Arm's sleeping quarters. She is the bandit chief, is well armed, and is at the highest possible level. She carries the Pinewatch Key and the [Pinewatch Treasure Room Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinewatch_Treasure_Room_Key "Skyrim:Pinewatch Treasure Room Key"). Her quarters contain an unowned double bed, with an end table to the right holding a filled random soul gem. To the left is an apprentice-locked chest with a random, possibly enchanted [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe") leaning against it. Beside the bed on the floor is a common book, and against the back of the wooden wall is a dresser with a potion of minor healing on top.

There is a narrow tunnel in the west wall, just in front of the entrance to Rigel's sleeping quarters. Along this tunnel are a few loose coins and a small coin purse. At the end is a wider corridor, with a dead draugr lying in front of an upright sarcophagus to the left, and a master-locked wooden door with bone chimes hanging in front to the right; the door is opened with the Pinewatch Treasure Room Key. Beyond the door is a short corridor leading to an iron door, which opens onto the walkway that had partially collapsed with the dead bandit below. The gap ahead is spanned by wooden logs. At this end is a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate"), which shoots a barrage of [poison darts](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap") across from either side. At the far end is another wooden door and another corridor, which turns to the south. Just past the turning is another pressure plate, this one triggering a row of [swinging blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Blades "Skyrim:Swinging Blades") ahead. At the other end is yet another pressure plate, which triggers a [battering ram](/wiki/Skyrim:Battering_Ram "Skyrim:Battering Ram") in the next corridor heading west. A metal pressure plate near the end of this corridor doesn't appear to trigger anything. Around the corner to the north is another wooden door, which has a [swinging mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Mace "Skyrim:Swinging Mace") trap behind it.

Treasure room

The door opens into the treasure room, which is an old catacomb. On a raised section in the middle is a broken sarcophagus, with a final pressure plate in front that triggers a spear trap with many spears thrusting from different directions. The sarcophagus is filled with treasure, including pieces of [ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Ore "Skyrim:Ebony Ore"), [quicksilver](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore"), [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore "Skyrim:Gold Ore"), [corundum](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore "Skyrim:Corundum Ore"), and [silver ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore "Skyrim:Silver Ore"), two [silver](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ingot "Skyrim:Silver Ingot") and two [gold ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ingot "Skyrim:Gold Ingot"), a [garnet](/wiki/Skyrim:Garnet "Skyrim:Garnet"), an [emerald](/wiki/Skyrim:Emerald "Skyrim:Emerald"), an [amethyst](/wiki/Skyrim:Amethyst "Skyrim:Amethyst"), two small coin purses, many loose coins, a random potion of healing, a random enchanted helmet, two [silver candlesticks](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Candlestick "Skyrim:Silver Candlestick"), and a [curious silver mold](/wiki/Skyrim:Curious_Silver_Mold "Skyrim:Curious Silver Mold"). There is a dead draugr to the left of the sarcophagus that can also be looted. Behind the sarcophagus is a chest, and beside the chest is an iron door that leads back to *Pinewatch*, bringing you to the barred door found near the beginning of the cave system.

## Notes

- A [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer")'s large stone table can be found due north of the cottage, past the area for Lakeview Manor near the shores of [Lake Ilinalta](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Ilinalta "Skyrim:Lake Ilinalta"). Upon the table is a leveled [weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons") and a copy of the [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[2920, Hearth Fire, v9](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Hearth_Fire,_v9 "Skyrim:2920, Hearth Fire, v9")*. Southwest of the table is a dead [wood cutter](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Cutter "Skyrim:Wood Cutter") and the unique iron battleaxe [The Woodsman's Friend](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Woodsman%27s_Friend "Skyrim:The Woodsman's Friend").

## Bugs

- Rigel respawns with the rest of Pinewatch.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.1, fixes this bug.
- The [Light Foot](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Foot "Skyrim:Light Foot") perk does not work on the first pressure plate that activates the darts.
- When loading a quicksave made in Pinewatch, you are sent back to the entrance of the main house, although progress is still saved. **?**
