# Skyrim:Places

## Overview

There is a large variety of **places** in *[Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim")*; for reference, see the key of the [icons used to mark places on maps](/wiki/Skyrim:Maps#Icons "Skyrim:Maps"). This page only lists some of the most interesting locations in the game. Other places are listed on the following dedicated pages:

- **[All-Maker Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:All-Maker_Stones "Skyrim:All-Maker Stones")** — Standing stones found in the wilderness of [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")
- **[Barracks](/wiki/Skyrim:Barracks "Skyrim:Barracks")** — Guard barracks throughout Skyrim
- **[Bodies of Water](/wiki/Skyrim:Bodies_of_Water "Skyrim:Bodies of Water")** — Lakes, rivers, and seas
- **[Castles](/wiki/Skyrim:Castles "Skyrim:Castles")** — Castles and Jarl longhouses
- **[Cemeteries](/wiki/Skyrim:Cemeteries "Skyrim:Cemeteries")** — Where the dead of Skyrim are buried
- **[Dragon Mounds](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Mounds "Skyrim:Dragon Mounds")** — Sites where Dragons were buried
- **[Guild Halls](/wiki/Skyrim:Guild_Halls "Skyrim:Guild Halls")** — The various headquarters for the guilds of Skyrim
- **[Holds](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds")** — The holds (political regions) that make up Skyrim
- **[Houses](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses")** — Properties you can purchase as a home across Skyrim
- **[Inns](/wiki/Skyrim:Inns "Skyrim:Inns")** — Inns, taverns, and places where you can rent a room
- **[Jails](/wiki/Skyrim:Jails "Skyrim:Jails")** — The jails found throughout Skyrim
- **[Shrines](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines "Skyrim:Shrines")** — Shrines to the Nine Divines
- **[Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Stables "Skyrim:Stables")** — Stables, where you can buy [horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses "Skyrim:Horses")
- **[Standing Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Standing_Stones "Skyrim:Standing Stones")** — Magical stones which grant special abilities or powers
- **[Stores](/wiki/Skyrim:Stores "Skyrim:Stores")** — Merchant stores
- **[Temples](/wiki/Skyrim:Temples "Skyrim:Temples")** — The various temples of the [Nine Divines](/wiki/Lore:Nine_Divines "Lore:Nine Divines")
- **[Word Walls](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall")** — Locations where word walls can be found
- **[Worldspaces](/wiki/Skyrim:Worldspaces "Skyrim:Worldspaces")** — Exterior areas that are technically separate from the main world of Skyrim
- **[Other Places](/wiki/Skyrim:Other_Places "Skyrim:Other Places")** — Other places that do not fit into another category
- **[Unmarked Places](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places "Skyrim:Unmarked Places")** — Places that do not appear on the map

Places added by [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"), [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"), [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire"), and [Creation Club](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") are annotated with "DG", "DB", "HF", and "CC" superscripts, respectively.

**Note:** The [Skyrim-Places category](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places "Category:Skyrim-Places") provides an index of all places in the game.

## Cities

Each city (with the exception of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") on [Solstheim](/wiki/Lore:Solstheim "Lore:Solstheim")) is located in a different [hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds") and is home to that hold's ruler, or [jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl"). The five largest cities (the major cities) are walled, allowing their maps (or *cells* as they are called in the [Creation Kit](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Creation_Kit "Skyrim Mod:Creation Kit")) to be treated separately from the main map. [Carriages](/wiki/Skyrim:Carriage "Skyrim:Carriage") are available for hire outside each major city to transport the player to any other major city.

Fast traveling to a major city places you just inside its main gate, but each major city also has a keep or palace where the jarl resides, which is a separate fast-travel destination and is listed below. Additionally, Riften has a third fast-travel destination once you have joined the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"), namely the entrance to the guild's [headquarters](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(place) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (place)").

### Major Cities

:    **[Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth")** — A major city in the southwest of Skyrim near the border of High Rock, and the capital of the Reach. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Markarth)

    :    **[Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep")** — An ancient Dwarven keep built into the mountainside, used as a palace by the Jarl of Markarth. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Understone+Keep)
:    **[Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften")** — A major city in the southeast of Skyrim near the borders of Morrowind and Cyrodiil, and the capital of the Rift. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Riften)

    :    **[Mistveil Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistveil_Keep "Skyrim:Mistveil Keep")** — A castle located at the southern end of Riften. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mistveil+Keep)
    :    **[Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(place) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (place)")** — The headquarters of the Thieves Guild located with the sewers beneath Riften, known as The Ratway. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Thieves+Guild)
:    **[Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude")** — A major city on the northwest coast of Skyrim, and the capital of both Haafingar and the entire province. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Solitude)

    :    **[Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace")** — The current seat of power for Solitude, Haafingar, and Skyrim; and home to the High King of Skyrim. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Blue+Palace)
:    **[Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun")** — A major city in the center of Skyrim, and the capital of Whiterun Hold. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Whiterun)

    :    **[Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach")** — The residence of the Jarl of Whiterun Hold, the hold's seat of political power, and the location of the hold's jail. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dragonsreach)
:    **[Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm")** — A major city in the northeast of Skyrim near the Dunmeth Pass to Morrowind, and the capital of Eastmarch. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Windhelm)

    :    **[Palace of the Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:Palace_of_the_Kings "Skyrim:Palace of the Kings")** — A large castle at the far end of the Valunstrad district in Windhelm. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Palace+of+the+Kings)

### Other Cities

:    **[Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar")** — A city on the northern coast of Skyrim, and the capital of the Pale. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dawnstar)
:    **[Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath")** — A city in the south of Skyrim, and the capital of Falkreath Hold. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Falkreath)
:    **[Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal")** — A city in the north of Skyrim, and the capital of Hjaalmarch. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Morthal)
:    **[Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A city on the southwest coast of Solstheim. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Raven+Rock)
:    **[Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold")** — A city on the northeast coast of Skyrim, and the capital of Winterhold hold. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Winterhold)

    :    **[College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)")** — A school of the arcane arts. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=College+of+Winterhold)

### Towns

Major towns and similar important settlements, smaller than a [city](/wiki/Skyrim:Cities "Skyrim:Cities") but larger than a minor settlement, farm, mill, or shack. Towns typically act as small quest hubs.

:    **[Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge")** — A milling town in southern Haafingar. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dragon+Bridge)
:    **[Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen")** — A town in eastern Falkreath Hold. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Helgen)
:    **[Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead")** — A milling town in the western Rift. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ivarstead)
:    **[Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten")** — A mining town in the northern Reach. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Karthwasten)
:    **[Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood")** — A lumber milling town in southern Whiterun Hold. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Riverwood)
:    **[Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead")** — A farming town in western Whiterun Hold. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Rorikstead)
:    **[Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone")** — A mining town in the northern Rift. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Shor%27s+Stone)
:    **[Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A village on Solstheim. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Skaal+Village)

### Private Estates

Purchasable estates that appear on the map with the same icon as towns. Three are added by the *[Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire")* official add-on, while one is added by the [Tundra Homestead](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Homestead "Skyrim:Tundra Homestead") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club").

:    **[Heljarchen Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Heljarchen_Hall "Skyrim:Heljarchen Hall")**[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") — A piece of property in the Pale, north of Loreius Farm and south of Fort Dunstad. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Heljarchen+Hall+%28HF%29)
:    **[Lakeview Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Lakeview_Manor "Skyrim:Lakeview Manor")**[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") — A piece of property in Falkreath Hold, north of Pinewatch. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lakeview+Manor+%28HF%29)
:    **[Tundra Homestead](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Homestead_(place) "Skyrim:Tundra Homestead (place)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Homestead "Skyrim:Tundra Homestead") — A cottage that can be purchased in Whiterun Hold, located just northeast of Battle-Born Farm. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Tundra+Homestead+%28CC%29)
:    **[Windstad Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Windstad_Manor "Skyrim:Windstad Manor")**[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") — A piece of property in Hjaalmarch, north of Ustengrav and east of the Abandoned Shack. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Windstad+Manor+%28HF%29)

### Minor Settlements

Settlements smaller than towns. Minor settlements consist of only one to a few buildings.

:    **[Black-Briar Lodge](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Lodge "Skyrim:Black-Briar Lodge")** — A large remote building east of Riften. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Black-Briar+Lodge)
:    **[Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary")** — An active Dark Brotherhood sanctuary west of Falkreath. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dark+Brotherhood+Sanctuary)
:    **[Darkwater Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Crossing "Skyrim:Darkwater Crossing")** — A small mining settlement south of Windhelm. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Darkwater+Crossing)
:    **[Dawnstar Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dawnstar Sanctuary")** — A disused Dark Brotherhood sanctuary on the shore of the Sea of Ghosts near Dawnstar. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dawnstar+Sanctuary)
:    **[Goldenglow Estate](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenglow_Estate "Skyrim:Goldenglow Estate")** — A honey farm west of Riften containing mercenaries, skeevers, and the farm's owner Aringoth. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Goldenglow+Estate)
:    **[High Hrothgar](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Hrothgar "Skyrim:High Hrothgar")** — A small settlement southeast of Whiterun roughly halfway up the Throat of the World. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=High+Hrothgar)
:    **[Honningbrew Meadery](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Meadery "Skyrim:Honningbrew Meadery")** — A small meadery southeast of Whiterun owned by Sabjorn. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Honningbrew+Meadery)
:    **[Japhet's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Japhet%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Japhet's Folly")** — A self-contained worldspace far northeast of Skyrim containing Blood Horkers and their leader Haldyn. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Japhet%27s+Folly)
:    **[Kolskeggr Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolskeggr_Mine "Skyrim:Kolskeggr Mine")** — A small gold mine and settlement east-northeast of Markarth initially containing Forsworn. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Kolskeggr+Mine)
:    **[Kynesgrove](/wiki/Skyrim:Kynesgrove "Skyrim:Kynesgrove")** — A small settlement south of Windhelm. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Kynesgrove)
:    **[Left Hand Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Left_Hand_Mine "Skyrim:Left Hand Mine")** — A small iron mine and settlement southeast of Markarth. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Left+Hand+Mine)
:    **[Nightgate Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightgate_Inn "Skyrim:Nightgate Inn")** — An inn west of Windhelm. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Nightgate+Inn)
:    **[Old Hroldan Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Hroldan_Inn "Skyrim:Old Hroldan Inn")** — A remote inn in the Reach where Tiber Septim once stayed. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Old+Hroldan+Inn)
:    **[Soljund's Sinkhole](/wiki/Skyrim:Soljund%27s_Sinkhole "Skyrim:Soljund's Sinkhole")** — A small moonstone mine and settlement east of Markarth initially containing draugr. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Soljund%27s+Sinkhole)
:    **[Stonehills](/wiki/Skyrim:Stonehills "Skyrim:Stonehills")** — A small mining settlement east of Morthal. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Stonehills)
:    **[Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(settlement) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (settlement)")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A Telvanni tower settlement east of Fort Frostmoth on Solstheim. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Tel+Mithryn)
:    **[Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy")** — The Aldmeri Dominion's diplomatic mission to Skyrim northwest of Solitude. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Thalmor+Embassy)
:    **[Thirsk Mead Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Thirsk_Mead_Hall "Skyrim:Thirsk Mead Hall")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A mead hall south-southwest of Skaal Village on Solstheim. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Thirsk+Mead+Hall)
:    **[Whistling Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Whistling_Mine "Skyrim:Whistling Mine")** — A small iron mine and settlement southeast of Winterhold. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Whistling+Mine)

### Orc Strongholds

Small settlements controlled by Orc tribes. Entry is only granted to Orcs or those who complete certain quests.

:    **[Dushnikh Yal](/wiki/Skyrim:Dushnikh_Yal "Skyrim:Dushnikh Yal")** — A prosperous Orc stronghold in the southwest of Skyrim, southeast of Markarth. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dushnikh+Yal)
:    **[Largashbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur "Skyrim:Largashbur")** — An accursed Orc stronghold beset by giants in the southeast of Skyrim, west-southwest of Riften. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Largashbur)
:    **[Mor Khazgur](/wiki/Skyrim:Mor_Khazgur "Skyrim:Mor Khazgur")** — An Orc stronghold in the far northwest of Skyrim, west of Solitude and north of Markarth. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mor+Khazgur)
:    **[Narzulbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Narzulbur "Skyrim:Narzulbur")** — An Orc stronghold in the east of Skyrim, southeast of Windhelm. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Narzulbur)

### Farms

Farms that grow various crops.

:    **[Brandy-Mug Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Brandy-Mug_Farm "Skyrim:Brandy-Mug Farm")** — A wheat farm, a short distance east of Windhelm Stables. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Brandy-Mug+Farm)
:   **[Corpselight Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Corpselight_Farm "Skyrim:Corpselight Farm")** — A small farmstead located in Falkreath. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Corpselight+Farm)
:   **[Cowflop Farmhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Cowflop_Farmhouse "Skyrim:Cowflop Farmhouse")** — A small farmhouse located in Rorikstead. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Cowflop+Farmhouse)
:   **[Fellstar Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellstar_Farm "Skyrim:Fellstar Farm")** — A farm in Ivarstead, located across the road from the lumber mill and south of the bridge to High Hrothgar. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fellstar+Farm)
:    **[Goldenhills Plantation](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenhills_Plantation "Skyrim:Goldenhills Plantation")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Farming "Skyrim:Farming") — An abandoned farm east of Rorikstead. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Goldenhills+Plantation+%28CC%29)
:    **[Hlaalu Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Hlaalu_Farm "Skyrim:Hlaalu Farm")** — A small farm east of Windhelm. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hlaalu+Farm)
:    **[Hollyfrost Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Hollyfrost_Farm "Skyrim:Hollyfrost Farm")** — A large farm with a single-roomed farmhouse east of Windhelm. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hollyfrost+Farm)
:    **[Katla's Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Katla%27s_Farm "Skyrim:Katla's Farm")** — A small farm and stable along the Karth River, outside of Solitude. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Katla%27s+Farm)
:   **[Lemkil's Farmhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Lemkil%27s_Farmhouse "Skyrim:Lemkil's Farmhouse")** — A small farm in Rorikstead. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lemkil%27s+Farmhouse)
:   **[Lylvieve Family's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Lylvieve_Family%27s_House "Skyrim:Lylvieve Family's House")** — A small farmhouse on the northwestern side of Dragon Bridge, located next to Horgeir's House. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lylvieve+Family%27s+House)
:    **[Merryfair Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Merryfair_Farm "Skyrim:Merryfair Farm")** — A poor, small farm northwest of Riften, owned and run by Dravin Llanith and his wife Synda Llanith. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Merryfair+Farm)
:    **[Old Attius Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Attius_Farm "Skyrim:Old Attius Farm")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — An abandoned Imperial farm south-southeast of Raven Rock. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Old+Attius+Farm)

### Wheat Mills

Farms that grow wheat and have wheat mills.

:    **[Battle-Born Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle-Born_Farm "Skyrim:Battle-Born Farm")** — A farm just outside Whiterun, owned by the Battle-Born clan who are influential in the city. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Battle-Born+Farm)
:    **[Chillfurrow Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Chillfurrow_Farm "Skyrim:Chillfurrow Farm")** — A small farm just outside of Whiterun, owned by Nazeem. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Chillfurrow+Farm)
:    **[Loreius Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Loreius_Farm "Skyrim:Loreius Farm")** — A small farm in the Pale, north of Whitewatch Tower. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Loreius+Farm)
:    **[Pelagia Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagia_Farm "Skyrim:Pelagia Farm")** — A large farm south of Whiterun owned by Severio Pelagia. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Pelagia+Farm)
:    **[Salvius Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Salvius_Farm "Skyrim:Salvius Farm")** — A small farm east of Markarth. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Salvius+Farm)
:    **[Sarethi Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Sarethi_Farm "Skyrim:Sarethi Farm")** — A farm east of Ivarstead that cultivates Nirnroot. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sarethi+Farm)
:    **[Snow-Shod Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow-Shod_Farm "Skyrim:Snow-Shod Farm")** — A small farm south of Riften that is owned by Vulwulf Snow-Shod. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Snow-Shod+Farm)

### Wood Mills

Wood mills are found by water and can be used as a source of lumber.

:    **[Anga's Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Anga%27s_Mill "Skyrim:Anga's Mill")** — A small wood mill built along the north bank of the River Yorgrim, west of Windhelm. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Anga%27s+Mill)
:   **[Dragon Bridge Lumber Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge_Lumber_Camp "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge Lumber Camp")** — A sawmill and lumber camp in the southwestern part of Dragon Bridge. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dragon+Bridge+Lumber+Camp)
:    **[Half-Moon Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Half-Moon_Mill "Skyrim:Half-Moon Mill")** — A lumber mill that supplies Helgen and Falkreath. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Half-Moon+Mill)
:    **[Heartwood Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Heartwood_Mill "Skyrim:Heartwood Mill")** — A struggling lumber mill on the shores of Lake Honrich, west of Goldenglow Estate. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Heartwood+Mill)
:    **[Mixwater Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Mixwater_Mill "Skyrim:Mixwater Mill")** — A lumber mill on the White River, southwest of Windhelm and southeast of Gallows Rock. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mixwater+Mill)
:    **[Solitude Sawmill](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Sawmill "Skyrim:Solitude Sawmill")** — A wood mill southwest of Solitude. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Solitude+Sawmill)

### Shacks

Remote dwellings in the wilderness. They may or may not be inhabited, and the occupants may not be friendly.

:    **[Abandoned Lodge](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_Lodge "Skyrim:Abandoned Lodge")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small shack north-northeast of Raven Rock. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Abandoned+Lodge)
:    **[Abandoned Shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_Shack "Skyrim:Abandoned Shack")** — An isolated house in Hjaalmarch, east of Solitude. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Abandoned+Shack)
:    **[Alchemist's Shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemist%27s_Shack "Skyrim:Alchemist's Shack")** — A small shack south of Ivarstead. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Alchemist%27s+Shack)
:    **[Angi's Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Angi%27s_Camp "Skyrim:Angi's Camp")** — A cabin and camp southeast of Falkreath. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Angi%27s+Camp)
:    **[Anise's Cabin](/wiki/Skyrim:Anise%27s_Cabin "Skyrim:Anise's Cabin")** — A small shack west-southwest of Riverwood. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Anise%27s+Cabin)
:    **[Cliffside Retreat](/wiki/Skyrim:Cliffside_Retreat "Skyrim:Cliffside Retreat")** — A small shack south of Dragon Bridge. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Cliffside+Retreat)
:    **[Crabber's Shanty](/wiki/Skyrim:Crabber%27s_Shanty "Skyrim:Crabber's Shanty")** — A small run-down shack on the River Hjaal. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Crabber%27s+Shanty)
:    **[Drelas' Cottage](/wiki/Skyrim:Drelas%27_Cottage "Skyrim:Drelas' Cottage")** — An isolated cottage at the foot of a mountain in northern Whiterun Hold, and south of Morthal. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Drelas%27+Cottage)
:    **[Froki's Shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Froki%27s_Shack "Skyrim:Froki's Shack")** — A small shack southeast of Ivarstead. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Froki%27s+Shack)
:    **[Hall of the Vigilant](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Vigilant "Skyrim:Hall of the Vigilant")** — A secluded lodge south-southwest of Dawnstar, home to the Vigilants of Stendarr. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hall+of+the+Vigilant)
:    **[Hrodulf's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrodulf%27s_House "Skyrim:Hrodulf's House")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — An abandoned shack southwest of Fort Frostmoth and southeast of Kolbjorn Barrow. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Hrodulf%27s+House)
:    **[Hunter's Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunter%27s_Rest "Skyrim:Hunter's Rest")** — A small shack northwest of Falkreath. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hunter%27s+Rest)
:    **[Ironback Hideout](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironback_Hideout "Skyrim:Ironback Hideout")** — A dilapidated house to the northwest of Solitude, a short distance east of The Steed Stone. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ironback+Hideout)
:    **[Lund's Hut](/wiki/Skyrim:Lund%27s_Hut "Skyrim:Lund's Hut")** — A small shack northwest of Rorikstead containing skeevers. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lund%27s+Hut)
:    **[Meeko's Shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Meeko%27s_Shack "Skyrim:Meeko's Shack")** — A run-down shack owned by the canine follower Meeko, who has inherited the home from his unfortunate owner. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Meeko%27s+Shack)
:    **[Pinewatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinewatch "Skyrim:Pinewatch")** — A shack northeast of Falkreath containing bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Pinewatch)
:    **[Ramshackle Trading Post](/wiki/Skyrim:Ramshackle_Trading_Post "Skyrim:Ramshackle Trading Post")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — An old shack south of Kagrumez and west-northwest of Ashfallow Citadel. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Ramshackle+Trading+Post)
:    **[Redwater Den](/wiki/Skyrim:Redwater_Den "Skyrim:Redwater Den")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A shack northwest of Riften containing bandits and vampires. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Redwater+Den+%28DG%29)
:    **[Riverside Shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverside_Shack "Skyrim:Riverside Shack")** — A small shack east of Gallows Rock and west-southwest of Kynesgrove, along the eastern bank of the White River. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Riverside+Shack)
:    **[Traitor's Post](/wiki/Skyrim:Traitor%27s_Post "Skyrim:Traitor's Post")** — A crumbling shack and bandit outpost east of Windhelm, and just north of the Sacellum of Boethiah. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Traitor%27s+Post)

## Notes

- Version 2.0.7 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") replaces Brandy-Mug Farm's settlement map icon with the one used for small farms.

## Docks

:    **[East Empire Company Warehouse](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Warehouse "Skyrim:East Empire Company Warehouse")** — A warehouse on the Solitude docks immediately southeast of the city. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=East+Empire+Company+Warehouse)
:    **[Icewater Jetty](/wiki/Skyrim:Icewater_Jetty "Skyrim:Icewater Jetty")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A small isolated dock far west of Solitude and northwest of Northwatch Keep. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Icewater+Jetty+%28DG%29)
:    **[Northshore Landing](/wiki/Skyrim:Northshore_Landing "Skyrim:Northshore Landing")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small abandoned dock on the northwest coast of Solstheim inhabited by mudcrabs. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Northshore+Landing)
:    **[Riften Docks](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Docks "Skyrim:Riften Docks")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowfoot_Sanctum "Skyrim:Shadowfoot Sanctum") — An extensive dock located on the western side of Riften. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?centeron=Riften+Docks+%28CC%29)

## Lighthouses

:    **[Frostflow Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostflow_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Frostflow Lighthouse")** — A lighthouse west-southwest of Winterhold containing Falmer, chaurus, and frostbite spiders. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Frostflow+Lighthouse)
:    **[Solitude Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Solitude Lighthouse")** — A stone building on the northern coast of Skyrim that helps to guide ships into Solitude harbor. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Solitude+Lighthouse)

## Camps

:    **[Bujold's Retreat](/wiki/Skyrim:Bujold%27s_Retreat "Skyrim:Bujold's Retreat")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A camp east of Thirsk Mead Hall containing Nords exiled from the hall by rieklings. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Bujold%27s+Retreat)
:    **[Dragon Bridge Overlook](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge_Overlook "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge Overlook")** — A small Forsworn camp south of Dragon Bridge. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dragon+Bridge+Overlook)
:    **[Druadach Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Druadach_Redoubt "Skyrim:Druadach Redoubt")** — A small Forsworn camp and cave south of Mor Khazgur. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Druadach+Redoubt)
:    **[Haknir's Shoal](/wiki/Skyrim:Haknir%27s_Shoal "Skyrim:Haknir's Shoal")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small pirate camp north-northwest of Skaal Village. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Haknir%27s+Shoal)
:    **[Halted Stream Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Halted_Stream_Camp "Skyrim:Halted Stream Camp")** — A small bandit camp and iron mine north of Whiterun. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Halted+Stream+Camp)
:    **[Karthspire](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthspire "Skyrim:Karthspire")** — A large Forsworn camp and cave east of Markarth. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Karthspire)
:    **[Knifepoint Ridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Knifepoint_Ridge "Skyrim:Knifepoint Ridge")** — A small bandit camp and iron and corundum mine northwest of Falkreath. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Knifepoint+Ridge)
:    **[Last Vigil](/wiki/Skyrim:Last_Vigil "Skyrim:Last Vigil")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small camp northeast of Riften. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Last+Vigil+%28DB%29)
:    **[Robber's Gorge](/wiki/Skyrim:Robber%27s_Gorge "Skyrim:Robber's Gorge")** — A small bandit camp and cave west-southwest of Morthal. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Robber%27s+Gorge)
:    **[Serpent's Bluff Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Serpent%27s_Bluff_Redoubt "Skyrim:Serpent's Bluff Redoubt")** — A small Forsworn camp and ruin southwest of Rorikstead. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Serpent%27s+Bluff+Redoubt)

- You can set up your own **[campsite](/wiki/Skyrim:Campsite "Skyrim:Campsite")** with the [Camping](/wiki/Skyrim:Camping "Skyrim:Camping") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed. The campsite adds a fast travel marker to your map, although you can only have one campsite set up at a time.

## Caves

:    **[Ashfall's Tear](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashfall%27s_Tear "Skyrim:Ashfall's Tear")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal") — A small cave north of Raven Rock containing a hidden Tribunal Temple shrine to the goddess Almalexia. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Ashfall%27s+Tear+%28CC%29)
:    **[Benkongerike](/wiki/Skyrim:Benkongerike "Skyrim:Benkongerike")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A medium-sized cave southeast of Saering's Watch containing bristlebacks and rieklings. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Benkongerike)
:   **[Blackbone Isle Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackbone_Isle_Grotto "Skyrim:Blackbone Isle Grotto")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Dread "Skyrim:Dead Man's Dread") — A small cave connected to the sea, situated on Blackbone Isle. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Blackbone+Isle+Grotto)
:    **[Bleakcoast Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleakcoast_Cave "Skyrim:Bleakcoast Cave")** — A small cave east-southeast of Winterhold containing frost trolls. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bleakcoast+Cave)
:    **[Blind Cliff Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Blind_Cliff_Cave "Skyrim:Blind Cliff Cave")** — A medium-sized cave southwest of Karthwasten along the banks of the Karth River containing Forsworn. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Blind+Cliff+Cave)
:    **[Bloated Man's Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloated_Man%27s_Grotto "Skyrim:Bloated Man's Grotto")** — A small cave north of Falkreath containing animals and spriggans. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bloated+Man%27s+Grotto)
:    **[Bloodchill Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodchill_Cavern "Skyrim:Bloodchill Cavern")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodchill_Manor "Skyrim:Bloodchill Manor") — A small cave southwest of Winterhold containing a subterranean vampiric player home. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bloodchill+Cavern+%28CC%29)
:    **[Bonechill Passage](/wiki/Skyrim:Bonechill_Passage "Skyrim:Bonechill Passage")** — A small cave east of Falkreath containing leveled animals. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bonechill+Passage)
:    **[Boulderfall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Boulderfall_Cave "Skyrim:Boulderfall Cave")** — A small cave northwest of Riften containing necromancers. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Boulderfall+Cave)
:    **[Brinewater Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Brinewater_Grotto "Skyrim:Brinewater Grotto")** — A small cave north of Solitude containing horkers or bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Brinewater+Grotto)
:    **[Bristleback Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Bristleback_Cave "Skyrim:Bristleback Cave")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small cave in the northwest of Solstheim island containing bristlebacks and rieklings. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Bristleback+Cave)
:    **[Brittleshin Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Brittleshin_Pass "Skyrim:Brittleshin Pass")** — A small passage through the mountains between Whiterun Hold and Falkreath Hold containing a necromancer and skeletons. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Brittleshin+Pass)
:    **[Broken Fang Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Fang_Cave "Skyrim:Broken Fang Cave")** — A small cave southeast of Rorikstead containing skeletons and vampires. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Broken+Fang+Cave)
:    **[Broken Helm Hollow](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Helm_Hollow "Skyrim:Broken Helm Hollow")** — A small cave in the southeast corner of The Rift containing bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Broken+Helm+Hollow)
:    **[Broken Oar Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Oar_Grotto "Skyrim:Broken Oar Grotto")** — A small cave north of Solitude containing Blackblood Marauders and their leader Captain Hargar. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Broken+Oar+Grotto)
:    **[Bronze Water Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Bronze_Water_Cave "Skyrim:Bronze Water Cave")** — A small cave west of Windhelm containing leveled animals. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bronze+Water+Cave)
:    **[Brood Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Brood_Cavern "Skyrim:Brood Cavern")** — A small cave southwest of Morthal containing leveled animals. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Brood+Cavern)
:    **[Bruca's Leap Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Bruca%27s_Leap_Redoubt "Skyrim:Bruca's Leap Redoubt")** — A small cave southwest of Dragon Bridge containing Forsworn. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bruca%27s+Leap+Redoubt)

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Castle+Karstaag+Caverns)
:    **[Castle Karstaag Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Karstaag_Ruins "Skyrim:Castle Karstaag Ruins")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — An icy clearing outside Castle Karstaag Caverns. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Castle+Karstaag+Ruins)

:    **[Clearspring Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Clearspring_Cave "Skyrim:Clearspring Cave")** — A small cave west of Shor's Stone containing a troll. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Clearspring+Cave)
:    **[Cold Rock Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Cold_Rock_Pass "Skyrim:Cold Rock Pass")** — A small passage through a mountain south-southwest of Morthal containing a frost troll. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Cold+Rock+Pass)
:    **[Coldcinder Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Coldcinder_Cave "Skyrim:Coldcinder Cave")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small cave southeast of Raven Rock containing ash spawn and netches. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Coldcinder+Cave)

:    **[Cragwallow Slope](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragwallow_Slope "Skyrim:Cragwallow Slope")** — A medium-sized cave southeast of Windhelm home to conjurers and atronachs. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Cragwallow+Slope)
:    **[Cronvangr Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Cronvangr_Cave "Skyrim:Cronvangr Cave")** — A medium-sized cave southwest of Kynesgrove containing vampires and frostbite spiders. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Cronvangr+Cave)
:    **[Crystaldrift Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Crystaldrift_Cave "Skyrim:Crystaldrift Cave")** — A small cave southwest of Riften containing leveled animals. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Crystaldrift+Cave)
:    **[Darkfall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkfall_Cave "Skyrim:Darkfall Cave")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A small cave south of Mor Khazgur containing frostbite spiders and trolls. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Darkfall+Cave+%28DG%29)
:   **[Darkfall Passage](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkfall_Passage "Skyrim:Darkfall Passage")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A small cave only accessible through Darkfall Cave serving as the only access to the Forgotten Vale.

:    **[Red Scar Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Scar_Cavern "Skyrim:Red Scar Cavern")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause "Skyrim:The Cause") — A cave located east of Shor's Stone, occupied by the Mythic Dawn cult. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Red+Scar+Cavern)

:   **[Rielle](/wiki/Skyrim:Rielle "Skyrim:Rielle")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause "Skyrim:The Cause") — A medium-sized Ayleid ruin located beneath the Jerall Mountains, just east of the Pale Pass. It straddles the border between the Rift in Skyrim and County Bruma in Cyrodiil. In Skyrim, it is accessed from the north by way of Varlais Cavern, a cave entrance located to the south of Arcwind Point. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Rielle+%28CC%29)
:    **[Rimerock Burrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Rimerock_Burrow "Skyrim:Rimerock Burrow")** — A small cave northwest of Dragon Bridge containing an atronach and the powerful conjurer Sebastian Lort. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Rimerock+Burrow)
:    **[Runoff Caverns](/wiki/Skyrim:Runoff_Caverns "Skyrim:Runoff Caverns")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Seasons "Skyrim:Forgotten Seasons") — A large cave west of Lost Valley Redoubt containing mercenaries, Dwarven automatons, atronachs, ice wraiths, spriggans, and animals. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Runoff+Caverns+%28CC%29)

:    **[Soljund's Sinkhole](/wiki/Skyrim:Soljund%27s_Sinkhole "Skyrim:Soljund's Sinkhole")** — A small moonstone mine and settlement east of Markarth initially containing draugr. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Soljund%27s+Sinkhole)

:    **[Swindler's Den](/wiki/Skyrim:Swindler%27s_Den "Skyrim:Swindler's Den")** — A small cave east of Rorikstead containing bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Swindler%27s+Den)
:    **[Tolvald's Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolvald%27s_Cave "Skyrim:Tolvald's Cave")** — A large cave northeast of Shor's Stone containing Falmer, chaurus, frostbite spiders, and skeevers. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Tolvald%27s+Cave)
:    **[Uttering Hills Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Uttering_Hills_Cave "Skyrim:Uttering Hills Cave")** — A small cave southwest of Windhelm containing bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Uttering+Hills+Cave)

:    **[Wolfskull Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolfskull_Cave "Skyrim:Wolfskull Cave")** — A medium-sized cave west of Solitude containing bandits or necromancers and draugr. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Wolfskull+Cave)
:    **[Yngvild](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngvild "Skyrim:Yngvild")** — A medium-sized cave east-northeast of Dawnstar containing draugr and Yngvild ghosts. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Yngvild)

## Notes

- Version 2.0.9 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") replaces Yngvild's cave map icon with the one used for [Nordic ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins").
- Version 3.0.6 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch") replaces the cave map icon for Soljund's Sinkhole with the one used for [mines](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines").

## Daedric Shrines

:    **[Shrine of Azura](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Azura "Skyrim:Shrine of Azura")** — The shrine to the Daedric Prince Azura. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Shrine+of+Azura)
:    **[Sacellum of Boethiah](/wiki/Skyrim:Sacellum_of_Boethiah "Skyrim:Sacellum of Boethiah")** — The shrine to the Daedric Prince Boethiah. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sacellum+of+Boethiah)
:    **[Haemar's Shame](/wiki/Skyrim:Haemar%27s_Shame "Skyrim:Haemar's Shame")** — A medium-sized cave east of Helgen containing vampires. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Haemar%27s+Shame)
:    **[Giant's Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Grove "Skyrim:Giant's Grove")** — A grove accessed through Fallowstone Cave containing a giant whose tribe has defiled a shrine of Malacath. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Giant%27s+Grove)
:    **[Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Mehrunes_Dagon "Skyrim:Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon")** — The shrine to the Daedric Prince Mehrunes Dagon. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Shrine+of+Mehrunes+Dagon)
:    **[Statue to Meridia](/wiki/Skyrim:Statue_to_Meridia "Skyrim:Statue to Meridia")** — The shrine to the Daedric Prince Meridia. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Statue+to+Meridia)
:   **[Abandoned House](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_House "Skyrim:Abandoned House")** — A building in Markarth next to Arnleif and Sons Trading Company with a shrine to the Daedric Prince Molag Bal. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Abandoned+House)
:    **[Reachcliff Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Reachcliff_Cave "Skyrim:Reachcliff Cave")** — A small cave east-southeast of Markarth containing draugr. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Reachcliff+Cave)
:   **[Shrine of Nocturnal](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Nocturnal "Skyrim:Shrine of Nocturnal")** — The Thieves Guild's headquarters in Riften. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Ragged+Flagon+-+Cistern)
:    **[Shrine to Peryite](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_to_Peryite "Skyrim:Shrine to Peryite")** — The shrine to the Daedric Prince Peryite. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Shrine+to+Peryite)

## Dragon Lairs

:    **[Ancient's Ascent](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient%27s_Ascent "Skyrim:Ancient's Ascent")** — A mountaintop dragon lair southwest of Helgen. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ancient%27s+Ascent)
:    **[Autumnwatch Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Autumnwatch_Tower "Skyrim:Autumnwatch Tower")** — A dragon lair south of Ivarstead. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Autumnwatch+Tower)
:    **[Bonestrewn Crest](/wiki/Skyrim:Bonestrewn_Crest "Skyrim:Bonestrewn Crest")** — A mountaintop dragon lair south of Windhelm. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bonestrewn+Crest)
:    **[Dragontooth Crater](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragontooth_Crater "Skyrim:Dragontooth Crater")** — A dragon lair north-northwest of Karthwasten. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dragontooth+Crater)
:    **[Eldersblood Peak](/wiki/Skyrim:Eldersblood_Peak "Skyrim:Eldersblood Peak")** — A mountaintop dragon lair south of Morthal. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Eldersblood+Peak)
:    **[Lost Tongue Overlook](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Tongue_Overlook "Skyrim:Lost Tongue Overlook")** — A dragon lair south of Riften. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lost+Tongue+Overlook)
:    **[Mount Anthor](/wiki/Skyrim:Mount_Anthor "Skyrim:Mount Anthor")** — A mountaintop dragon lair south-southwest of Winterhold. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mount+Anthor)
:    **[Northwind Summit](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwind_Summit "Skyrim:Northwind Summit")** — A mountaintop dragon lair northwest of Shor's Stone. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Northwind+Summit)
:    **[Saering's Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:Saering%27s_Watch "Skyrim:Saering's Watch")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A dragon lair in the shadow of Frykte Peak on Solstheim. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Saering%27s+Watch)
:    **[Shearpoint](/wiki/Skyrim:Shearpoint "Skyrim:Shearpoint")** — A mountaintop dragon lair northeast of Whiterun. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Shearpoint)
:    **[Skyborn Altar](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyborn_Altar "Skyrim:Skyborn Altar")** — A mountaintop dragon lair east-southeast of Morthal. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Skyborn+Altar)

## Dwarven Ruins

:    **[Alftand](/wiki/Skyrim:Alftand "Skyrim:Alftand")** — A large Dwarven ruin southwest of Winterhold containing Dwarven automatons, Falmer, frostbite spiders, and skeevers. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Alftand)
:    **[Arkngthamz](/wiki/Skyrim:Arkngthamz "Skyrim:Arkngthamz")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A small Dwarven ruin southeast of Dushnikh Yal containing Dwarven automatons, Falmer, and chaurus. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Arkngthamz+%28DG%29)
:    **[Avanchnzel](/wiki/Skyrim:Avanchnzel "Skyrim:Avanchnzel")** — A medium-sized Dwarven ruin west of Riften containing Dwarven automatons. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Avanchnzel)
:   **[Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach")** — An immense, naturally lit cavern inhabited by hordes of Falmer and containing the ruins of a Dwemer city. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Blackreach)

    :   **[Debate Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Debate_Hall "Skyrim:Debate Hall")** — A small Dwarven ruin in Blackreach occupied by Falmer and their servants.
    :   **[Derelict Pumphouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Derelict_Pumphouse "Skyrim:Derelict Pumphouse")** — A small Dwarven ruin in Blackreach occupied by a Dwarven spider.
    :   **[Farm Overseer's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Farm_Overseer%27s_House "Skyrim:Farm Overseer's House")** — A small Dwarven building in Blackreach.
    :   **[Hall of Rumination](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Rumination "Skyrim:Hall of Rumination")** — A small Dwarven ruin in Blackreach occupied by Falmer and their servants.
    :   **[Pumping Station](/wiki/Skyrim:Pumping_Station "Skyrim:Pumping Station")** — A small Dwarven ruin in Blackreach occupied by Falmer servants.
    :   **[Reeking Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Reeking_Tower "Skyrim:Reeking Tower")** — A small Dwarven ruin in Blackreach occupied by frostbite spiders.
    :   **[Silent City Catacombs](/wiki/Skyrim:Silent_City_Catacombs "Skyrim:Silent City Catacombs")** — A small Dwarven ruin in Blackreach occupied by Falmer.
    :   **[Silent Ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Silent_Ruin "Skyrim:Silent Ruin")** — A small Dwarven ruin in Blackreach.
    :   **[Sinderion's Field Laboratory](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinderion%27s_Field_Laboratory "Skyrim:Sinderion's Field Laboratory")** — A small Dwarven building in Blackreach serving as Sinderion's alchemical foothold in the cavern.
    :   **[War Quarters](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Quarters "Skyrim:War Quarters")** — A small Dwarven building in Blackreach.
:    **[Bthardamz](/wiki/Skyrim:Bthardamz "Skyrim:Bthardamz")** — A large Dwarven ruin west-northwest of Karthwasten containing Afflicted and Dwarven automatons. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bthardamz)
:    **[Deep Folk Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Deep_Folk_Crossing "Skyrim:Deep Folk Crossing")** — An ancient Dwarven bridge over a weir with structures at either end in the northern part of the Reach. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Deep+Folk+Crossing)
:    **[Fahlbtharz](/wiki/Skyrim:Fahlbtharz "Skyrim:Fahlbtharz")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A large Dwarven ruin east of the Water Stone containing rieklings, albino spiders, oil spiders, and Dwarven automatons. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Fahlbtharz)
:    **[Great Lift at Alftand](/wiki/Skyrim:Great_Lift_at_Alftand "Skyrim:Great Lift at Alftand")** — A Dwarven lift to Blackreach located northeast of Nightgate Inn and southeast of Wayward Pass. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Great+Lift+at+Alftand)
:    **[Great Lift at Mzinchaleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Great_Lift_at_Mzinchaleft "Skyrim:Great Lift at Mzinchaleft")** — A Dwarven lift to Blackreach located south of Mzinchaleft. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Great+Lift+at+Mzinchaleft)
:    **[Great Lift at Raldbthar](/wiki/Skyrim:Great_Lift_at_Raldbthar "Skyrim:Great Lift at Raldbthar")** — A Dwarven lift to Blackreach located west-southwest of Anga's Mill and east of Irkngthand. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Great+Lift+at+Raldbthar)
:    **[Irkngthand](/wiki/Skyrim:Irkngthand "Skyrim:Irkngthand")** — A large Dwarven ruin west of Windhelm containing bandits, Dwarven automatons, Falmer, frostbite spiders, and skeevers. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Irkngthand)
:    **[Kagrenzel](/wiki/Skyrim:Kagrenzel "Skyrim:Kagrenzel")** — A small Dwarven ruin southeast of Windhelm containing Falmer. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Kagrenzel)
:    **[Kagrumez](/wiki/Skyrim:Kagrumez "Skyrim:Kagrumez")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small Dwarven ruin south of the Temple of Miraak. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Kagrumez)
:    **[Mzinchaleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzinchaleft "Skyrim:Mzinchaleft")** — A medium-sized Dwarven ruin southwest of Dawnstar containing bandits, Dwarven automatons, Falmer, and chaurus. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mzinchaleft)
:    **[Mzulft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzulft "Skyrim:Mzulft")** — A large Dwarven ruin south-southeast of Windhelm containing Dwarven automatons, Falmer, and chaurus. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mzulft)
:    **[Nchardak](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchardak "Skyrim:Nchardak")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A large Dwarven ruin north-northeast of Tel Mithryn. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Nchardak)
:   **[Nchuand-Zel](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel "Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel")** — A large Dwarven ruin accessed from inside Understone Keep. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Nchuand-Zel)
:    **[Raldbthar](/wiki/Skyrim:Raldbthar "Skyrim:Raldbthar")** — A medium-sized Dwarven ruin west-southwest of Windhelm. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Raldbthar)
:    **[Reachwind Eyrie](/wiki/Skyrim:Reachwind_Eyrie "Skyrim:Reachwind Eyrie")** — A small Dwarven tower east-southeast of Markarth. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Reachwind+Eyrie)
:    **[Ruins of Bthalft](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruins_of_Bthalft "Skyrim:Ruins of Bthalft")** — A small Dwarven ruin south of Ivarstead containing bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ruins+of+Bthalft)
:    **[Ruins of Rkund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruins_of_Rkund "Skyrim:Ruins of Rkund")** — A small Dwarven ruin in the mountains southwest of Riften containing a wispmother and wisps. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ruins+of+Rkund)
:    **[Tower of Mzark](/wiki/Skyrim:Tower_of_Mzark "Skyrim:Tower of Mzark")** — A small Dwarven tower in Blackreach. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Tower+of+Mzark)
