### General Landmarks

:    **[Altar of Thrond](/wiki/Skyrim:Altar_of_Thrond "Skyrim:Altar of Thrond")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A landmark west of the Temple of Miraak next to a small cave containing hagravens. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Altar+of+Thrond)
:    **[Bard's Leap Summit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bard%27s_Leap_Summit "Skyrim:Bard's Leap Summit")** — A wooden plank at the very top of Lost Valley Redoubt. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bard%27s+Leap+Summit)
:    **[Blackbone Isle](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackbone_Isle "Skyrim:Blackbone Isle")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Dread "Skyrim:Dead Man's Dread") — A haunted island in the Sea of Ghosts. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Blackbone+Isle+%28CC%29)
:    **[Brodir Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Brodir_Grove "Skyrim:Brodir Grove")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small circle of stones northeast of Raven Rock containing reavers. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Brodir+Grove)
:    **[Deep Folk Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Deep_Folk_Crossing "Skyrim:Deep Folk Crossing")** — An ancient Dwarven bridge over a weir with structures at either end in the northern part of the Reach. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Deep+Folk+Crossing)
:   **[Druadach Mountains](/wiki/Skyrim:Druadach_Mountains "Skyrim:Druadach Mountains")** — A mountain range in western Skyrim serving as a natural barrier to separate Skyrim from High Rock and Hammerfell. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Druadach+Mountains)
:    **[Frykte Peak](/wiki/Skyrim:Frykte_Peak "Skyrim:Frykte Peak")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — One of the highest points on Solstheim, near Saering's Watch. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Frykte+Peak)
:    **[Giant's Tooth](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Tooth "Skyrim:Giant's Tooth")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Bittercup "Skyrim:Bittercup") — A small island in the Sea of Ghosts. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Giant%27s+Tooth+%28CC%29)
:    **[Gjukar's Monument](/wiki/Skyrim:Gjukar%27s_Monument "Skyrim:Gjukar's Monument")** — A stone monument commemorating an ancient battle southeast of Rorikstead. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Gjukar%27s+Monument)
:    **[Horker Island](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Island "Skyrim:Horker Island")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A large island east of Skaal Village occupied by horkers. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Horker+Island)
:    **[Hvitkald Peak‎](/wiki/Skyrim:Hvitkald_Peak "Skyrim:Hvitkald Peak")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — One of the highest points on Solstheim, west of the Abandoned Lodge. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Hvitkald+Peak)
:   **[Jerall Mountains](/wiki/Skyrim:Jerall_Mountains "Skyrim:Jerall Mountains")** — A mountain range that stretches along the southern border of Skyrim. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Jerall+Mountains)
:    **[Mortrag Peak](/wiki/Skyrim:Mortrag_Peak "Skyrim:Mortrag Peak")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — One of the highest points on Solstheim, south of Castle Karstaag Ruins. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Mortrag+Peak)
:    **[Mount Moesring](/wiki/Skyrim:Mount_Moesring "Skyrim:Mount Moesring")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — One of the highest points on Solstheim, south of Moesring Pass. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Mount+Moesring)
:    **[Orphan Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Orphan_Rock "Skyrim:Orphan Rock")** — A wooded valley with a central rock plateau northeast of Helgen containing witches or hags led by a hagraven. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Orphan+Rock)
:    **[Reachwind Eyrie](/wiki/Skyrim:Reachwind_Eyrie "Skyrim:Reachwind Eyrie")** — A small Dwarven tower east-southeast of Markarth. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Reachwind+Eyrie)
:    **[Ruins of Bthalft](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruins_of_Bthalft "Skyrim:Ruins of Bthalft")** — A small Dwarven ruin south of Ivarstead containing bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ruins+of+Bthalft)
:    **[Ruins of Rkund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruins_of_Rkund "Skyrim:Ruins of Rkund")** — A small Dwarven ruin in the mountains southwest of Riften containing a wispmother and wisps. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ruins+of+Rkund)
:    **[Sky Haven Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Sky_Haven_Temple "Skyrim:Sky Haven Temple")** — A large mountaintop fort that served as the major Blades temple and outpost in Skyrim, now long abandoned and in Forsworn territory. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sky+Haven+Temple)
:    **[Stalhrim Source](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim_Source "Skyrim:Stalhrim Source")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small outdoor Nordic ruin east of Broken Tusk Mine and southwest of Mortrag Peak. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Stalhrim+Source)
:    **[Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:Throat of the World")** — The highest mountain in Tamriel, located southeast of Whiterun. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Throat+of+the+World)
:   **[Velothi Mountains](/wiki/Skyrim:Velothi_Mountains "Skyrim:Velothi Mountains")** — A mountain range that stretches along the eastern border of Skyrim. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Velothi+Mountains)
:    **[Weynon Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Weynon_Stones "Skyrim:Weynon Stones")** — A landmark consisting of a circle of stones. It is located between Korvanjund and Fort Dunstad, just south of the path. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Weynon+Stones)

### Clearings

:    **[Autumnshade Clearing](/wiki/Skyrim:Autumnshade_Clearing "Skyrim:Autumnshade Clearing")** — A circular glade inhabited by a spriggan and its attending animals. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Autumnshade+Clearing)
:    **[Clearpine Pond](/wiki/Skyrim:Clearpine_Pond "Skyrim:Clearpine Pond")** — A pond with a small island, located west-southwest of Solitude, just to the northeast of Pinemoon Cave. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Clearpine+Pond)
:    **[Clearspring Tarn](/wiki/Skyrim:Clearspring_Tarn "Skyrim:Clearspring Tarn")** — A small mountain pool on the cliff overlooking Eastmarch, due east of Snapleg Cave and west of Shor's Stone. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Clearspring+Tarn)
:    **[Headwaters of Harstrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Headwaters_of_Harstrad "Skyrim:Headwaters of Harstrad")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — The source of the Harstrad River. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Headwaters+of+Harstrad)
:    **[Mara's Eye Pond](/wiki/Skyrim:Mara%27s_Eye_Pond "Skyrim:Mara's Eye Pond")** — A small lake due east of Gallows Rock. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mara%27s+Eye+Pond)

### Groves

:    **[Ancestor Glade](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancestor_Glade "Skyrim:Ancestor Glade")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A small glade in a cavern east-southeast of Falkreath. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ancestor+Glade+%28DG%29)
:    **[Evergreen Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Evergreen_Grove "Skyrim:Evergreen Grove")** — A grove of trees concealing a small pond fed by a rocky stream, just southwest of Half-Moon Mill. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Evergreen+Grove)
:    **[Giant's Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Grove "Skyrim:Giant's Grove")** — A grove accessed through Fallowstone Cave containing a giant whose tribe has defiled a shrine of Malacath. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Giant%27s+Grove)
:    **[Greenspring Hollow](/wiki/Skyrim:Greenspring_Hollow "Skyrim:Greenspring Hollow")** — A shallow outdoor cave west-northwest of Whiterun containing a leveled animal. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Greenspring+Hollow)
:    **[Shrouded Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Grove "Skyrim:Shrouded Grove")** — A grove with a small cave located in the Pale. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Shrouded+Grove)
:    **[Witchmist Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Witchmist_Grove "Skyrim:Witchmist Grove")** — A small shack north of Bonestrewn Crest and south of Kynesgrove. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Witchmist+Grove)

### Passes

:    **[Brittleshin Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Brittleshin_Pass "Skyrim:Brittleshin Pass")** — A small passage through the mountains between Whiterun Hold and Falkreath Hold containing a necromancer and skeletons. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Brittleshin+Pass)
:    **[Cold Rock Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Cold_Rock_Pass "Skyrim:Cold Rock Pass")** — A small passage through a mountain south-southwest of Morthal containing a frost troll. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Cold+Rock+Pass)
:   **[Dunmeth Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Dunmeth_Pass "Skyrim:Dunmeth Pass")** — A mountain pass and one of the few traversable roads through the Velothi Mountains between northwest Morrowind and northeast Skyrim. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dunmeth+Pass)
:    **[Moesring Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Moesring_Pass "Skyrim:Moesring Pass")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A mountain pass due northwest of the Temple of Miraak, inhabited by rieklings guarding the nearby Strange Vessel. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Moesring+Pass)
:   **[Skybound Watch Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Skybound_Watch_Pass "Skyrim:Skybound Watch Pass")** — A small Nordic tower and ruin northeast of Helgen containing bandits and a giant frostbite spider. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Skybound+Watch+Pass)
:    **[Wayward Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Wayward_Pass "Skyrim:Wayward Pass")** — A pass through the mountains in the southwest of Winterhold. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Wayward+Pass)

### Imperial Camps

:    **[Eastmarch Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Eastmarch Imperial Camp")** — An Imperial camp in Eastmarch, located southeast of Mzulft and north of Stony Creek Cave. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Eastmarch+Imperial+Camp)
:    **[Falkreath Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Falkreath Imperial Camp")** — An Imperial camp in Falkreath Hold, located east-northeast of Glenmoril Coven and north of Knifepoint Ridge. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Falkreath+Imperial+Camp)
:    **[Hjaalmarch Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch Imperial Camp")** — An Imperial camp in Hjaalmarch, located south of Ustengrav and northwest of Stonehills. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hjaalmarch+Imperial+Camp)
:    **[Pale Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Pale_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Pale Imperial Camp")** — An Imperial camp in the Pale, located west of Dawnstar and northwest of Mzinchaleft. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Pale+Imperial+Camp)
:    **[Reach Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Reach_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Reach Imperial Camp")** — An Imperial camp in the Reach, located south of Bthardamz and west of Karthwasten. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Reach+Imperial+Camp)
:    **[Rift Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Rift_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Rift Imperial Camp")** — An Imperial camp in the Rift, located south of Ivarstead and west of the Ruins of Bthalft. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Rift+Imperial+Camp)
:    **[Whiterun Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Whiterun Imperial Camp")** — An Imperial camp in Whiterun Hold, located east of Rorikstead and far west of Whiterun. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Whiterun+Imperial+Camp)
:    **[Windhelm Military Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm_Military_Camp "Skyrim:Windhelm Military Camp")** — An Imperial camp set up east of Brandy-Mug Farm for the attack on Windhelm. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Windhelm+Military+Camp)
:    **[Winterhold Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Winterhold Imperial Camp")** — An Imperial camp in Winterhold Hold, located southeast of Dawnstar and northwest of Frostflow Lighthouse. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Winterhold+Imperial+Camp)

### Stormcloak Camps

:    **[Falkreath Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Falkreath Stormcloak Camp")** — A Stormcloak camp in Falkreath Hold, located east of Helgen. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Falkreath+Stormcloak+Camp)
:    **[Haafingar Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Haafingar Stormcloak Camp")** — A Stormcloak camp in Haafingar, located northeast of Dragon Bridge and south of the Statue to Meridia. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Haafingar+Stormcloak+Camp)
:    **[Hjaalmarch Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch Stormcloak Camp")** — A Stormcloak camp in Hjaalmarch, located east of Ustengrav and west of Mzinchaleft. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hjaalmarch+Stormcloak+Camp)
:    **[Pale Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Pale_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Pale Stormcloak Camp")** — A Stormcloak camp in the Pale, located southeast of Bronze Water Cave on the south shore of Lake Yorgrim. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Pale+Stormcloak+Camp)
:    **[Reach Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Reach_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Reach Stormcloak Camp")** — A Stormcloak camp in the Reach, located west of Liar's Retreat and northeast of Karthwasten. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Reach+Stormcloak+Camp)
:    **[Rift Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Rift_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Rift Stormcloak Camp")** — A Stormcloak camp in the Rift, located northeast of Sarethi Farm and west of Rift Watchtower. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Rift+Stormcloak+Camp)
:    **[Solitude Military Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Military_Camp "Skyrim:Solitude Military Camp")** — A Stormcloak camp set up west of Katla's Farm for the attack on Solitude. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Solitude+Military+Camp)
:    **[Whiterun Military Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Military_Camp "Skyrim:Whiterun Military Camp")** — A Stormcloak camp set up east of Pelagia Farm for the attack on Whiterun. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Whiterun+Military+Camp)
:    **[Whiterun Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Whiterun Stormcloak Camp")** — A Stormcloak camp in Whiterun Hold, located south of the Ritual Stone and east of White River Watch. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Whiterun+Stormcloak+Camp)
:    **[Winterhold Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Winterhold Stormcloak Camp")** — A Stormcloak camp in Winterhold Hold, located northeast of Windhelm and south of Snow Veil Sanctum. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Winterhold+Stormcloak+Camp)

### Civil War Forts

:    **[Fort Amol](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Amol "Skyrim:Fort Amol")** — A medium-sized fort southwest of Windhelm initially occupied by warlocks. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Amol)
:    **[Fort Dunstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dunstad "Skyrim:Fort Dunstad")** — A large fort south of Dawnstar initially occupied by bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Dunstad)
:    **[Fort Greenwall](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greenwall "Skyrim:Fort Greenwall")** — A large fort north-northwest of Riften initially occupied by bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Greenwall)
:    **[Fort Greymoor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greymoor "Skyrim:Fort Greymoor")** — A medium-sized fort west of Whiterun initially occupied by bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Greymoor)
:    **[Fort Hraggstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim:Fort Hraggstad")** — A medium-sized fort west of Solitude initially occupied by bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Hraggstad)
:    **[Fort Kastav](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Kastav "Skyrim:Fort Kastav")** — A medium-sized fort south of Winterhold initially occupied by warlocks and skeletons. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Kastav)
:    **[Fort Neugrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Neugrad "Skyrim:Fort Neugrad")** — A medium-sized fort east of Falkreath initially occupied by bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Neugrad)
:    **[Fort Snowhawk](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Snowhawk "Skyrim:Fort Snowhawk")** — A medium-sized fort west of Morthal initially occupied by necromancers and skeletons. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Snowhawk)
:    **[Fort Sungard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Sungard "Skyrim:Fort Sungard")** — A large fort east-southeast of Markarth initially occupied by Forsworn. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Sungard)

### Fort Settlements

:    **[Castle Volkihar](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Volkihar "Skyrim:Castle Volkihar")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A large castle on an island far northwest of Solitude connected to Volkihar Keep. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Castle+Volkihar+%28DG%29)

    :   **[Volkihar Courtyard](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Courtyard "Skyrim:Volkihar Courtyard")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — The courtyard attached to Castle Volkihar and Volkihar Keep.
    :    **[Volkihar Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Keep "Skyrim:Volkihar Keep")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A large fortress on an island far northwest of Solitude connected to Castle Volkihar which serves as the Volkihar vampire clan's home. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Castle+Volkihar+%28DG%29)
:    **[Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A large fort southeast of Riften which serves as the Dawnguard's base of operations. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Dawnguard+%28DG%29)
:    **[High Hrothgar](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Hrothgar "Skyrim:High Hrothgar")** — A small settlement southeast of Whiterun roughly halfway up the Throat of the World. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=High+Hrothgar)

### Fort Dungeons

:    **[Ashfallow Citadel](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashfallow_Citadel "Skyrim:Ashfallow Citadel")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small Imperial fort east of Highpoint Tower and northwest of the Sun Stone being used as a base of operations by the Morag Tong. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Ashfallow+Citadel)
:    **[Bloodlet Throne](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodlet_Throne "Skyrim:Bloodlet Throne")** — A small fort southwest of Helgen containing vampires, wolves, gargoyles, and death hounds. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bloodlet+Throne)
:    **[Broken Tower Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Tower_Redoubt "Skyrim:Broken Tower Redoubt")** — A medium-sized fort east of Karthwasten containing Forsworn. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Broken+Tower+Redoubt)
:    **[Cracked Tusk Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Cracked_Tusk_Keep "Skyrim:Cracked Tusk Keep")** — A medium-sized fort west of Falkreath containing Orc bandits and hunters led by Ghunzul. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Cracked+Tusk+Keep)
:    **[Darklight Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Darklight_Tower "Skyrim:Darklight Tower")** — A medium-sized fort southwest of Riften containing hagravens, hags, and witches. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Darklight+Tower)
:    **[Driftshade Refuge](/wiki/Skyrim:Driftshade_Refuge "Skyrim:Driftshade Refuge")** — A medium-sized fort southeast of Dawnstar containing Silver Hands. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Driftshade+Refuge)
:    **[Faldar's Tooth](/wiki/Skyrim:Faldar%27s_Tooth "Skyrim:Faldar's Tooth")** — A medium-sized fort west of Riften containing bandits, wolves, and skeevers. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Faldar%27s+Tooth)
:    **[Fellglow Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellglow_Keep "Skyrim:Fellglow Keep")** — A medium-sized fort east-northeast of Whiterun containing warlocks, atronachs, and vampires, and the mages' leader, the Caller. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fellglow+Keep)
:    **[Fort Fellhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Fellhammer "Skyrim:Fort Fellhammer")** — A medium-sized fort and iron mine south of Dawnstar containing bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Fellhammer)
:    **[Fort Frostmoth](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Frostmoth "Skyrim:Fort Frostmoth")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small fort south of Highpoint Tower and northeast of Hrodulf's House occupied by ash spawn and General Falx Carius. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Fort+Frostmoth)
:    **[Gallows Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallows_Rock "Skyrim:Gallows Rock")** — A small fort southwest of Windhelm containing Silver Hands and their leader Krev the Skinner. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Gallows+Rock)
:    **[Harmugstahl](/wiki/Skyrim:Harmugstahl "Skyrim:Harmugstahl")** — A small fort north of Karthwasten containing the warlock Kornalus and his enchanted frostbite spiders. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Harmugstahl)
:    **[Highpoint Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Highpoint_Tower "Skyrim:Highpoint Tower")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small fort east of Raven Rock containing albino spiders, ash spawn, and Neloth's former apprentice Ildari Sarothril. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Highpoint+Tower)
:    **[Ilinalta's Deep](/wiki/Skyrim:Ilinalta%27s_Deep "Skyrim:Ilinalta's Deep")** — A medium-sized fort north of the Lady Stone containing necromancers and skeletons. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ilinalta%27s+Deep)
:    **[Mistwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch "Skyrim:Mistwatch")** — A medium-sized fort east of Darkwater Crossing containing the Mistwatch Bandits and their leader. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mistwatch)
:    **[Morvunskar](/wiki/Skyrim:Morvunskar "Skyrim:Morvunskar")** — A small fort southwest of Windhelm containing warlocks and their leader Naris the Wicked. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Morvunskar)
:    **[Nightcaller Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightcaller_Temple "Skyrim:Nightcaller Temple")** — A small fort on the clifftop overlooking Dawnstar. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Nightcaller+Temple)
:    **[Northwatch Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwatch_Keep "Skyrim:Northwatch Keep")** — A small fort northwest of Dragon Bridge containing Thalmor. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Northwatch+Keep)
:    **[Treva's Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:Treva%27s_Watch "Skyrim:Treva's Watch")** — A medium-sized fort southeast of Ivarstead containing bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Treva%27s+Watch)
:    **[Western Watchtower](/wiki/Skyrim:Western_Watchtower "Skyrim:Western Watchtower")** — A small fort west of Whiterun. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Western+Watchtower)

## Notes

- Version 4.1.1 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch") replaces Western Watchtower's fort map icon with the one used for [Imperial towers](/wiki/Skyrim:Towers "Skyrim:Towers").

## Mines

:    **[Bilegulch Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Bilegulch_Mine "Skyrim:Bilegulch Mine")** — A small orichalcum mine northwest of Falkreath containing Orc bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bilegulch+Mine)
:    **[Broken Tusk Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Tusk_Mine "Skyrim:Broken Tusk Mine")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small heart stone mine north of Raven Rock containing rieklings. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Broken+Tusk+Mine)
:   **[Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:Cidhna Mine")** — A medium-sized silver mine and forced-labor prison camp in southern Markarth. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Cidhna+Mine)
:    **[Damphall Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Damphall_Mine "Skyrim:Damphall Mine")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small iron and silver mine north of Raven Rock containing reavers. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Damphall+Mine)
:   **[Dushnikh Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Dushnikh_Mine "Skyrim:Dushnikh Mine")** — A small orichalcum mine supporting the Orc stronghold of Dushnikh Yal. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dushnikh+Mine)
:    **[Embershard Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Embershard_Mine "Skyrim:Embershard Mine")** — A small iron mine southwest of Riverwood containing bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Embershard+Mine)
:   **[Fenn's Gulch Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Fenn%27s_Gulch_Mine "Skyrim:Fenn's Gulch Mine")** — A small silver mine in northwestern Karthwasten. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fenn%27s+Gulch+Mine)
:    **[Fort Fellhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Fellhammer "Skyrim:Fort Fellhammer")** — A medium-sized fort and iron mine south of Dawnstar containing bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Fellhammer)
:    **[Gloombound Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Gloombound_Mine "Skyrim:Gloombound Mine")** — A small ebony and iron mine supporting the Orc stronghold of Narzulbur. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Gloombound+Mine)
:   **[Goldenrock Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenrock_Mine "Skyrim:Goldenrock Mine")** — A small corundum mine in southeastern Darkwater Crossing. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Goldenrock+Mine)
:    **[Halted Stream Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Halted_Stream_Camp "Skyrim:Halted Stream Camp")** — A small bandit camp and iron mine north of Whiterun. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Halted+Stream+Camp)
:   **[Iron-Breaker Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron-Breaker_Mine "Skyrim:Iron-Breaker Mine")** — A small iron mine in eastern Dawnstar. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Iron-Breaker+Mine)
:    **[Knifepoint Ridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Knifepoint_Ridge "Skyrim:Knifepoint Ridge")** — A small bandit camp and iron and corundum mine northwest of Falkreath. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Knifepoint+Ridge)
:    **[Kolskeggr Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolskeggr_Mine "Skyrim:Kolskeggr Mine")** — A small gold mine and settlement east-northeast of Markarth initially containing Forsworn. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Kolskeggr+Mine)
:    **[Left Hand Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Left_Hand_Mine "Skyrim:Left Hand Mine")** — A small iron mine and settlement southeast of Markarth. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Left+Hand+Mine)
:    **[Lost Prospect Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Prospect_Mine "Skyrim:Lost Prospect Mine")** — A small gold mine east-northeast of Riften. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lost+Prospect+Mine)
:   **[Mor Khazgur Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mor_Khazgur_Mine "Skyrim:Mor Khazgur Mine")** — A small orichalcum mine supporting the Orc stronghold of Mor Khazgur. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mor+Khazgur+Mine)
:    **[Northwind Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwind_Mine "Skyrim:Northwind Mine")** — A small iron mine northwest of Shor's Stone containing skeletons. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Northwind+Mine)
:   **[Quicksilver Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Mine "Skyrim:Quicksilver Mine")** — A small quicksilver mine in western Dawnstar. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Quicksilver+Mine)
:    **[Raven Rock Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock_Mine "Skyrim:Raven Rock Mine")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small ebony mine in northern Raven Rock initially containing draugr, frostbite spiders, skeevers, and the dragon priest Zahkriisos. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Raven+Rock+Mine)
:   **[Redbelly Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Redbelly_Mine "Skyrim:Redbelly Mine")** — A small ebony mine in western Shor's Stone initially containing frostbite spiders. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Redbelly+Mine)
:   **[Rockwallow Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Rockwallow_Mine "Skyrim:Rockwallow Mine")** — A small iron mine in eastern Stonehills. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Rockwallow+Mine)
:   **[Sanuarach Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanuarach_Mine "Skyrim:Sanuarach Mine")** — A small silver mine in northern Karthwasten initially containing Silver-Blood mercenaries. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sanuarach+Mine)
:    **[Soljund's Sinkhole](/wiki/Skyrim:Soljund%27s_Sinkhole "Skyrim:Soljund's Sinkhole")** — A small moonstone mine and settlement east of Markarth initially containing draugr. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Soljund%27s+Sinkhole)
:   **[Steamscorch Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Steamscorch_Mine "Skyrim:Steamscorch Mine")** — A small malachite mine in northeastern Kynesgrove. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Steamscorch+Mine)
:    **[Whistling Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Whistling_Mine "Skyrim:Whistling Mine")** — A small iron mine and settlement southeast of Winterhold. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Whistling+Mine)

## Notes

- Version 3.0.6 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch") replaces the [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") map icon for Soljund's Sinkhole with the one used for mines.

## Nordic Dwellings

:    **[Four Skull Lookout](/wiki/Skyrim:Four_Skull_Lookout "Skyrim:Four Skull Lookout")** — A small outdoor Nordic ruin south of Karthwasten containing bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Four+Skull+Lookout)
:    **[Hamvir's Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Hamvir%27s_Rest "Skyrim:Hamvir's Rest")** — A small outdoor graveyard and Nordic ruin northwest of Whiterun containing skeletons and a draugr. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hamvir%27s+Rest)
:    **[Journeyman's Nook](/wiki/Skyrim:Journeyman%27s_Nook "Skyrim:Journeyman's Nook")** — A small outdoor Nordic ruin southeast of Winterhold containing a bandit. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Journeyman%27s+Nook)
:    **[Kjenstag Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Kjenstag_Ruins "Skyrim:Kjenstag Ruins")** — A small outdoor Nordic ruin east-northeast of Morthal. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Kjenstag+Ruins)
:    **[Lost Valkygg](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Valkygg "Skyrim:Lost Valkygg")** — A small Nordic ruin northeast of Labyrinthian containing draugr. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lost+Valkygg)
:    **[Moldering Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Moldering_Ruins "Skyrim:Moldering Ruins")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A small camp and concealed cave west of Rorikstead containing vampires and dead draugr. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Moldering+Ruins+%28DG%29)
:    **[North Skybound Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:North_Skybound_Watch "Skyrim:North Skybound Watch")** — A small Nordic tower and ruin northeast of Helgen containing bandits and a giant frostbite spider. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Skybound+Watch+Pass)
:    **[Roadside Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Roadside_Ruins "Skyrim:Roadside Ruins")** — A small outdoor Nordic ruin northwest of Falkreath containing a spriggan. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Roadside+Ruins)
:    **[Skytemple Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Skytemple_Ruins "Skyrim:Skytemple Ruins")** — A small outdoor Nordic ruin north of the College of Winterhold containing a draugr and skeletons. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Skytemple+Ruins)
:    **[Snowclad Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowclad_Ruins "Skyrim:Snowclad Ruins")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small outdoor Nordic ruin northwest of the Temple of Miraak containing werebears. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Snowclad+Ruins)
:    **[Windward Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Windward_Ruins "Skyrim:Windward Ruins")** — A small outdoor Nordic ruin southwest of Dawnstar containing skeevers. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Windward+Ruins)
:    **[Yorgrim Overlook](/wiki/Skyrim:Yorgrim_Overlook "Skyrim:Yorgrim Overlook")** — A small outdoor Nordic ruin on the southern slope of the mountain range directly south of Winterhold. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Yorgrim+Overlook)

## Nordic Ruins

:    **[Angarvunde](/wiki/Skyrim:Angarvunde "Skyrim:Angarvunde")** — A medium-sized Nordic ruin west of Riften containing draugr. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Angarvunde)
:    **[Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund "Skyrim:Ansilvund")** — A medium-sized Nordic ruin north of Riften containing draugr and necromancers led by Lu'ah Al-Skaven. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ansilvund)
:    **[Arcwind Point](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcwind_Point "Skyrim:Arcwind Point")** — A small outdoor Nordic ruin south of Ivarstead containing draugr, skeletons and, after Dragon Rising, a dragon. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Arcwind+Point)
:    **[Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(place) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (place)")** — A medium-sized Nordic ruin west of Riverwood containing bandits, draugr, and skeevers. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bleak+Falls+Barrow)
:    **[Blind Cliff Bastion](/wiki/Skyrim:Blind_Cliff_Bastion "Skyrim:Blind Cliff Bastion")** — A medium-sized cave southwest of Karthwasten along the banks of the Karth River containing Forsworn. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Blind+Cliff+Cave)
:    **[Bloodskal Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodskal_Barrow "Skyrim:Bloodskal Barrow")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small Nordic ruin north of Raven Rock containing reavers. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Bloodskal+Barrow)
:    **[Bromjunaar Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Bromjunaar_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Bromjunaar Sanctuary")** — A hidden location reached by equipping the wooden mask while inside a building in Labyrinthian.
:    **[Champion's Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Champion%27s_Rest "Skyrim:Champion's Rest")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Umbra "Skyrim:Umbra") — A medium-sized Nordic ruin located in the Rift, east of Shor's Stone. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Champion%27s+Rest+%28CC%29)
:    **[Dead Men's Respite](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Men%27s_Respite "Skyrim:Dead Men's Respite")** — A small Nordic ruin southwest of Morthal containing draugr and frostbite spiders. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dead+Men%27s+Respite)
:    **[Deepwood Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Deepwood_Redoubt "Skyrim:Deepwood Redoubt")** — A large Nordic ruin west of Dragon Bridge containing Forsworn. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Deepwood+Redoubt)
:    **[Dustman's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dustman%27s_Cairn "Skyrim:Dustman's Cairn")** — A medium-sized Nordic ruin northwest of Whiterun containing Silver Hands, draugr, frostbite spiders, and skeevers. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dustman%27s+Cairn)
:    **[Folgunthur](/wiki/Skyrim:Folgunthur "Skyrim:Folgunthur")** — A medium-sized Nordic ruin southeast of Solitude containing draugr, frostbite spiders, and the draugr Mikrul Gauldurson. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Folgunthur)
:    **[Forelhost](/wiki/Skyrim:Forelhost "Skyrim:Forelhost")** — A medium-sized Nordic ruin southeast of Riften containing Dragon Cultists, draugr, skeevers, and the dragon priest Rahgot. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Forelhost)
:    **[Frostmere Crypt](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostmere_Crypt "Skyrim:Frostmere Crypt")** — A medium-sized Nordic ruin south-southwest of Dawnstar containing bandits and the unique wispmother the Pale Lady. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Frostmere+Crypt)
:    **[Geirmund's Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Geirmund%27s_Hall "Skyrim:Geirmund's Hall")** — A small Nordic ruin east of Ivarstead containing draugr, frostbite spiders, skeevers, and the draugr Sigdis Gauldurson. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Geirmund%27s+Hall)
:    **[Gyldenhul Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Gyldenhul_Barrow "Skyrim:Gyldenhul Barrow")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small Nordic ruin east of Skaal Village containing the spirit and treasure of Haknir Death-Brand. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Gyldenhul+Barrow)
:    **[Hag Rock Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag_Rock_Redoubt "Skyrim:Hag Rock Redoubt")** — A small Nordic ruin south of Markarth containing Forsworn. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hag+Rock+Redoubt)
:    **[Hag's End](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag%27s_End "Skyrim:Hag's End")** — A small Nordic ruin west of Dragon Bridge containing a hagraven, hags, and witches. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hag%27s+End)
:    **[High Gate Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Gate_Ruins "Skyrim:High Gate Ruins")** — A medium-sized Nordic ruin west of Dawnstar containing draugr and the dragon priest Vokun. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=High+Gate+Ruins)
:    **[Hillgrund's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Hillgrund%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Hillgrund's Tomb")** — A small Nordic ruin southwest of Windhelm containing draugr. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hillgrund%27s+Tomb)
:    **[Ironbind Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironbind_Barrow "Skyrim:Ironbind Barrow")** — A small Nordic ruin southwest of Winterhold containing draugr and the tomb of Warlord Gathrik. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ironbind+Barrow)
:    **[Kilkreath Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Kilkreath_Ruins "Skyrim:Kilkreath Ruins")** — A large ruined temple west of Solitude containing corrupted shades created by the necromancer Malkoran. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Kilkreath+Ruins)
:    **[Kolbjorn Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolbjorn_Barrow "Skyrim:Kolbjorn Barrow")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small Nordic ruin southeast of Raven Rock containing draugr, spiders, and the dragon priest Ahzidal. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Kolbjorn+Barrow)
:    **[Korvanjund](/wiki/Skyrim:Korvanjund "Skyrim:Korvanjund")** — A medium-sized Nordic ruin northeast of Whiterun containing draugr. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Korvanjund)
:    **[Labyrinthian](/wiki/Skyrim:Labyrinthian "Skyrim:Labyrinthian")** — A large Nordic ruin southeast of Morthal containing draugr, skeletons, trolls, wisps, and the dragon priest Morokei. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Labyrinthian)
:    **[Lost Valley Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Valley_Redoubt "Skyrim:Lost Valley Redoubt")** — A massive Nordic ruin inhabited by Forsworn and hagravens. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lost+Valley+Redoubt)
:    **[Ragnvald](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragnvald "Skyrim:Ragnvald")** — A medium-sized Nordic ruin north of Markarth containing draugr and the dragon priest Otar the Mad. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ragnvald)
:    **[Rannveig's Fast](/wiki/Skyrim:Rannveig%27s_Fast "Skyrim:Rannveig's Fast")** — A small Nordic ruin east-northeast of Rorikstead containing subjugated ghosts and Sild the Warlock. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Rannveig%27s+Fast)
:    **[Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Saarthal "Skyrim:Saarthal")** — A medium-sized Nordic ruin southwest of Winterhold. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Saarthal)
:   **[Shalidor's Maze](/wiki/Skyrim:Shalidor%27s_Maze "Skyrim:Shalidor's Maze")** — A small Nordic ruin east of Labyrinthian containing atronachs and a dremora. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Shalidor%27s+Maze)
:    **[Shriekwind Bastion](/wiki/Skyrim:Shriekwind_Bastion "Skyrim:Shriekwind Bastion")** — A small Nordic ruin north of Falkreath containing vampires and skeletons. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Shriekwind+Bastion)
:    **[Shroud Hearth Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Shroud_Hearth_Barrow "Skyrim:Shroud Hearth Barrow")** — A medium-sized Nordic ruin east of Ivarstead containing draugr and skeletons. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Shroud+Hearth+Barrow)
:    **[Silent Moons Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Silent_Moons_Camp "Skyrim:Silent Moons Camp")** — A small Nordic ruin northwest of Whiterun containing bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Silent+Moons+Camp)
:    **[Silverdrift Lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Silverdrift_Lair "Skyrim:Silverdrift Lair")** — A small Nordic ruin south-southeast of Dawnstar containing draugr. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Silverdrift+Lair)
:    **[Sivdur's Respite](/wiki/Skyrim:Sivdur%27s_Respite "Skyrim:Sivdur's Respite")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldbrand "Skyrim:Goldbrand") — A Nordic ruin located north of Windhelm. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sivdur%27s+Respite+%28CC%29)
:   **[Skuldafn](/wiki/Skyrim:Skuldafn "Skyrim:Skuldafn")** — A large Nordic ruin with a portal to Sovngarde containing draugr, dragons, and a dragon priest. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Skuldafn)
:    **[Snow Veil Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Veil_Sanctum "Skyrim:Snow Veil Sanctum")** — A medium-sized Nordic ruin north-northeast of Windhelm containing draugr. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Snow+Veil+Sanctum)
:    **[Twilight Sepulcher](/wiki/Skyrim:Twilight_Sepulcher "Skyrim:Twilight Sepulcher")** — The location of the Pilgrim's Path and main entrance to Nocturnal's Ebonmere portal, resting place for the Skeleton Key. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Twilight+Sepulcher)
:    **[Ustengrav](/wiki/Skyrim:Ustengrav "Skyrim:Ustengrav")** — A medium-sized Nordic ruin northeast of Morthal containing bandits, warlocks, draugr, skeletons, and frostbite spiders. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ustengrav)
:    **[Vahlok's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Vahlok%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Vahlok's Tomb")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small Nordic ruin south-southeast of Thirsk Mead Hall containing corrupted shades, draugr, and the dragon priest Vahlok the Jailor. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Vahlok%27s+Tomb)
:    **[Valthume](/wiki/Skyrim:Valthume "Skyrim:Valthume")** — A medium-sized Nordic ruin southeast of Markarth containing draugr, frostbite spiders, skeevers, and the dragon priest Hevnoraak. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Valthume)
:    **[Volskygge](/wiki/Skyrim:Volskygge "Skyrim:Volskygge")** — A medium-sized Nordic ruin west of Solitude containing bandits, draugr, frostbite spiders, and the dragon priest Volsung. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Volskygge)
:    **[Volunruud](/wiki/Skyrim:Volunruud "Skyrim:Volunruud")** — A medium-sized Nordic ruin southeast of Morthal containing draugr and the ghost of Kvenel the Tongue. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Volunruud)
:    **[White Ridge Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Ridge_Barrow "Skyrim:White Ridge Barrow")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A medium-sized Nordic ruin in the northern part of Solstheim inhabited by bandits and spiders. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=White+Ridge+Barrow)
:    **[Yngol Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngol_Barrow "Skyrim:Yngol Barrow")** — A small Nordic ruin northeast of Windhelm containing the shade of an ancient Nord warrior. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Yngol+Barrow)
:    **[Ysgramor's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysgramor%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Ysgramor's Tomb")** — A small Nordic ruin northwest of Winterhold containing Companion ghosts, frostbite spiders, and skeevers. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ysgramor%27s+Tomb)

## Notes

- Version 2.0.9 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") replaces [Yngvild](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngvild "Skyrim:Yngvild")'s [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") map icon with the one used for Nordic ruins.

## Ships and Shipwrecks

:    **[Dainty Sload](/wiki/Skyrim:Dainty_Sload "Skyrim:Dainty Sload")** — A ship docked north of Solitude. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dainty+Sload)
:   **[Dead Man's Dread](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Dread_(place) "Skyrim:Dead Man's Dread (place)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Dread "Skyrim:Dead Man's Dread") — An ancient ship located within the Grotto on Blackbone Isle. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dead+Man%27s+Dread)
:    **[Hela's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Hela%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Hela's Folly")** — A shipwreck northeast of Dawnstar. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hela%27s+Folly)
:    **[The Katariah](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Katariah "Skyrim:The Katariah")** — The personal transport vessel of the Emperor, Titus Mede II. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Katariah)
:   **[The North Wind](/wiki/Skyrim:The_North_Wind "Skyrim:The North Wind")** — A ship docked at the Windhelm docks. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+North+Wind)
:   **[Northern Maiden](/wiki/Skyrim:Northern_Maiden "Skyrim:Northern Maiden")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A ship initially docked at the Windhelm docks. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=141040&y=34208&zoom=15)
:    **[Orphan's Tear](/wiki/Skyrim:Orphan%27s_Tear "Skyrim:Orphan's Tear")** — A shipwreck west of Ravenscar Hollow on the northern coast. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Orphan%27s+Tear)
:    **[Pilgrim's Trench](/wiki/Skyrim:Pilgrim%27s_Trench "Skyrim:Pilgrim's Trench")** — A deep underwater ravine northwest of Winterhold consisting of four submerged shipwrecks. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Pilgrim%27s+Trench)
:   **[Red Wave](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Wave "Skyrim:Red Wave")** — A pirate ship docked at Solitude. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Red+Wave)
:   **[The Sea Squall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Sea_Squall "Skyrim:The Sea Squall")** — A ship docked in Dawnstar's Northstar Port. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Sea+Squall)
:    **[Wreck Of The Brinehammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Wreck_Of_The_Brinehammer "Skyrim:Wreck Of The Brinehammer")** — A shipwreck northwest of Dawnstar along the shore of the Sea of Ghosts. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Wreck+Of+The+Brinehammer)
:    **[Wreck of the Icerunner](/wiki/Skyrim:Wreck_of_the_Icerunner "Skyrim:Wreck of the Icerunner")** — An Imperial ship which will run aground east of Solitude containing Blackblood Marauders and the assassin Deeja. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Wreck+of+the+Icerunner)
:    **[Wreck of The Pride of Tel Vos](/wiki/Skyrim:Wreck_of_The_Pride_of_Tel_Vos "Skyrim:Wreck of The Pride of Tel Vos")** — A shipwreck on a small island east of Winterhold. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Wreck+of+The+Pride+of+Tel+Vos)
:    **[Wreck of the Strident Squall](/wiki/Skyrim:Wreck_of_the_Strident_Squall "Skyrim:Wreck of the Strident Squall")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A shipwreck south-southeast of Raven Rock containing reavers. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Wreck+of+the+Strident+Squall)
:    **[Wreck of the Winter War](/wiki/Skyrim:Wreck_of_the_Winter_War "Skyrim:Wreck of the Winter War")** — A shipwreck east-southeast of Snow Veil Sanctum and far northeast of Windhelm. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Wreck+of+the+Winter+War)

### Imperial Towers

:    **[Abandoned Prison](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_Prison "Skyrim:Abandoned Prison")** — A small Imperial prison southwest of Windhelm containing the ghosts of its drowned prisoners. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Abandoned+Prison)
:    **[Falkreath Watchtower](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Watchtower "Skyrim:Falkreath Watchtower")** — A small ruined tower north of Falkreath containing a necromancer. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Falkreath+Watchtower)
:    **[Pinefrost Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinefrost_Tower "Skyrim:Pinefrost Tower")** — A small ruined tower northwest of Dragon Bridge containing leveled animals. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Pinefrost+Tower)
:    **[Refugees' Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Refugees%27_Rest "Skyrim:Refugees' Rest")** — A small ruined tower east of Windhelm containing leveled animals. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Refugees%27+Rest)
:    **[Rift Watchtower](/wiki/Skyrim:Rift_Watchtower "Skyrim:Rift Watchtower")** — A small tower east of Ivarstead containing Orc bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Rift+Watchtower)
:    **[Shor's Watchtower](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Watchtower "Skyrim:Shor's Watchtower")** — A small tower north-northeast of Shor's Stone. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Shor%27s+Watchtower)
:    **[Snowpoint Beacon](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowpoint_Beacon "Skyrim:Snowpoint Beacon")** — A small tower southwest of Winterhold containing bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Snowpoint+Beacon)
:    **[Stendarr's Beacon](/wiki/Skyrim:Stendarr%27s_Beacon "Skyrim:Stendarr's Beacon")** — A small tower southeast of Riften. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Stendarr%27s+Beacon)
:    **[Whitewatch Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Whitewatch_Tower "Skyrim:Whitewatch Tower")** — A small tower north-northeast of Whiterun. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Whitewatch+Tower)
:    **[Widow's Watch Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Widow%27s_Watch_Ruins "Skyrim:Widow's Watch Ruins")** — A small ruined tower west-northwest of Solitude containing a hag. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Widow%27s+Watch+Ruins)

### Nordic Towers

:    **[Bannermist Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Bannermist_Tower "Skyrim:Bannermist Tower")** — A small ruined Nordic tower northwest of Falkreath containing bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bannermist+Tower)
:    **[Bleakwind Bluff](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleakwind_Bluff "Skyrim:Bleakwind Bluff")** — A small ruined Nordic tower inhabited by hagravens and Forsworn, located northwest of Rorikstead on an outcrop of rock. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bleakwind+Bluff)
:    **[Cradle Stone Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Cradle_Stone_Tower "Skyrim:Cradle Stone Tower")** — A small ruined Nordic tower west of Bard's Leap Summit containing a hagraven. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Cradle+Stone+Tower)
:    **[Dead Crone Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Crone_Rock "Skyrim:Dead Crone Rock")** — A small ruined Nordic tower inhabited by Forsworn, located south-southwest of Markarth, just above Hag Rock Redoubt. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dead+Crone+Rock)
:    **[Myrwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Myrwatch_(place) "Skyrim:Myrwatch (place)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Myrwatch "Skyrim:Myrwatch") — A mage tower player home east of Morthal. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Myrwatch+%28CC%29)
:    **[Nilheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Nilheim "Skyrim:Nilheim")** — A small ruined Nordic tower east-northeast of Ivarstead containing bandits disguised as guards. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Nilheim)
:    **[Peak's Shade Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Peak%27s_Shade_Tower "Skyrim:Peak's Shade Tower")** — A small ruined Nordic tower east of Falkreath containing a spriggan. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Peak%27s+Shade+Tower)
:    **[South Skybound Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:South_Skybound_Watch "Skyrim:South Skybound Watch")** — A small Nordic tower and ruin northeast of Helgen containing bandits and a giant frostbite spider. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Skybound+Watch+Pass)
:    **[Sundered Towers](/wiki/Skyrim:Sundered_Towers "Skyrim:Sundered Towers")** — A small pair of linked ruined Nordic towers southeast of Karthwasten containing Forsworn and hagravens. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sundered+Towers)
:    **[Valtheim Towers](/wiki/Skyrim:Valtheim_Towers "Skyrim:Valtheim Towers")** — A small pair of linked ruined Nordic towers east of Whiterun containing bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Valtheim+Towers)

## Notes

- Version 2.0.7 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") replaces the Imperial tower map icon for Widow's Watch Ruins with the one for Nordic towers.
- Version 4.1.1 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch") replaces Western Watchtower's [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") map icon with the one used for Imperial towers.

# Skyrim:Potema's Catacombs

## Overview

Potema's Catacombs

**Potema's Catacombs** is a series of catacombs designed to house the [Wolf Queen](/wiki/Skyrim:Queen_Potema "Skyrim:Queen Potema") of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). The catacombs have three interior zones: *[Potema's Catacombs](#Potema.27s_Catacombs)*, *[Potema's Refuge](#Potema.27s_Refuge)*, and *[Potema's Sanctum](#Potema.27s_Sanctum)*.

Aside from the spirit of Queen Potema, the caves contain a few powerful [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") and Potema's [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") minions.

## Related Quests

- **[Culling the Beast](/wiki/Skyrim:Culling_the_Beast "Skyrim:Culling the Beast")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Kill the thin-blooded [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The Wolf Queen Awakened](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen_Awakened "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen Awakened")**: Potema must be stopped.

### Temple of the Divines

Enter the Temple of the Divines and proceed to the rear of the temple. At the end of the pews, on the left, is a stairway heading down. The key obtained from [Styrr](/wiki/Skyrim:Styrr "Skyrim:Styrr") will open the barred gate. Continue through the corridor, finding a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") on the right, and enter the opening in the wall.

### Potema's Catacombs

Begin on a small landing. Ahead is a dead tree with harvestable [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") behind it. Before descending the stairs, to the right in an arched opening on the wall is another harvestable hanging moss and a random potion or poison. There are numerous bottles of alto wine, wine, empty wine bottles, and food barrels found throughout the catacombs. Follow the corridor as it continues back under the dead tree, heading south, and ends in a passage blocked by spears.

[Queen Potema](/wiki/Skyrim:Queen_Potema "Skyrim:Queen Potema") will now speak, offering thanks for halting her binding (see [Wolfskull Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolfskull_Cave "Skyrim:Wolfskull Cave")). She then promises some unpleasant post-death opportunities, and the spears lower. In the next room, a [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") is waiting on the right behind a stack of crates. There is an [oil slick](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Slick "Skyrim:Oil Slick") in a planter, with an [oil lantern](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Lanterns "Skyrim:Oil Lanterns") hanging above. The corridor continues through light cobwebs and ends at a stairwell, with the stairs up blocked by a cave-in. The only option is to go down two flights. At the bottom are two unlocked chests, an iron warhammer, and a random battleaxe.

Ambush!

In the next room, two draugr wait on a lower level, while a leveled [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") waits to your right on the upper level. There is a convenient oil slick on the floor below, with oil lanterns above. In a cage hanging from the ceiling is a dead draugr, along with a [philter of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Philter_of_Strength "Skyrim:Philter of Strength") (although this may be knocked to the floor if you employ the oil slick or area effect magic). The [lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Surfeit of Thieves](/wiki/Skyrim:Surfeit_of_Thieves "Skyrim:Surfeit of Thieves")* can be found on one of the tables. There is another dead draugr partially buried beneath dirt before the next gate.

Dead draugr against the wall

In the next room, a draugr is patrolling. Watch out for the [flame spout trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Spout_Trap "Skyrim:Flame Spout Trap") directly in front of the dead draugr standing against the wall, holding a lootable random sword point down and a lootable ancient Nord helmet on its head. There is a set of shelves around to the left against the northwest wall holding two bottles of Nord mead and a pair of iron boots. There is another dead draugr lying on the floor by the opposite wall. Beyond this is a closed gate, with its lever on the right. Through the gate, you will find yourself at the top of a short flight of stairs, with another flight directly across leading up to a waiting draugr. The room continues along a wall to the right, where another slumbering draugr lies on a table, and a second patrols. On a ledge along the wall to the left is a [philter of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Philter_of_Health "Skyrim:Philter of Health") and a [conjurer's draught](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjurer%27s_Draught "Skyrim:Conjurer's Draught").

Floating draugr

Continue down the stairs to a waiting leveled vampire. After dispatching the vampire, follow the corridor as it turns to the northeast into a flooded room. There are two draugr that rise from the flooded part of the room. A [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") that activates a [spike wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Spike_Wall "Skyrim:Spike Wall") trap is at the end of the walkway leading out. Before bypassing the pressure plate, step left off of the walkway to find a large [urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn") under the water.

Indoor plumbing

The next room opens into a naturally lit cavern with a large hole in the roof. Head down the stairs to meet two draugr, both slumbering against the southwest wall. Also in the cavern is a cage hanging from a large pillar containing a dead draugr with a random potion of magicka underneath. Opposite the cage is a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") and a novice-[trapped](/wiki/Skyrim:Tension_Cable "Skyrim:Tension Cable") chest, with a pair of random gauntlets on top. The trap triggers a [poison dart trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap") from behind the chest unless disarmed. At the far end of the room are stairs down to a single lever at an apparent dead end. Activate the lever to rotate a stone blocking a doorway and align the gateway within, or simply dart through when the opening is clear.

Daylight

The next room contains an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs"), a random potion of healing, a random potion of health, a bottle of [frostbite venom](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Venom "Skyrim:Frostbite Venom"), a salt pile, a thistle branch, a bulb of garlic, a sprig of snowberries, and a loose sample of hanging moss all on the floor, in addition to several hanging moss growing down the walls. The large unlocked double doors at the southeast end of the room lead to **Potema's Refuge**.

### Potema's Refuge

Treasure room

Through the doors is a typical Nordic crypt passage with hanging moss growing from the ceiling. The passage descends through open double doors before entering a partially darkened room, with a leveled draugr below a trapdoor in the room above. The passage continues to the north before climbing a flight of stairs to three more rotating doors with three corresponding levers. To the left of the levers is a potion of minor healing and a salt pile. A gated room to the right contains a leveled vampire. Once the vampire is dealt with, look behind an empty black sarcophagus in the same room for a lever. This opens a hidden door leading to a chamber containing a large urn, an unlocked chest, and four [burial urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn"). Back in the tunnel, each of the levers operates a single door, in sequential order. Throwing each lever when the corresponding visible gate is open will allow passage through the three gates. However, the gates may continue to slowly rotate, effectively blocking access back once passed. Once through the doors, the room opens to the left where two [spellcaster traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Spellcaster_Trap "Skyrim:Spellcaster Trap"), both of which shoot Firebolts, are placed. To disarm the traps, an arrow or a ranged spell will knock the two [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") out of place. Alternatively, making use of the pillars in the center of the room will allow you to sidle up to the traps and remove the soul gems manually. The passage continues, passing through a natural cave before climbing more stairs to a door.

Deathlord and vampire attack

Through the door is a room containing a leveled draugr reclining on one of two thrones, with a vampire in attendance. The vampire will address you as he approaches before attacking. Make sure to retrieve the key to [Potema's Sanctum key](/wiki/Skyrim:Potema%27s_Sanctum_Key "Skyrim:Potema's Sanctum Key") from either the armrest of the draugr's throne or the vampire's corpse. The master-locked iron door on the south wall is unlocked with the key, and leads down to a door to Potema's Sanctum.

### Potema's Sanctum

Beyond the door is a short passage to an iron door. Through the door is a semi-circular room guarded by a leveled vampire. The room contains three burial urns, a large urn, and a stone table with a dead draugr laid out on top along with two bowls of bone meal, a thistle branch, an iron helmet, and a dagger (see [bugs](#Bugs)). On the floor are the remains of a skeleton that can be looted. The next door leads to a passage with two thrones, one on either side of the doorway. A leveled draugr will be sitting in the left-hand throne, which has two resist element potions on top. However, the potions may become dislodged during the fight, to be found afterward on the floor. There is a skeleton and a magic-using draugr at the bottom of the stairs. Above the thrones are shield racks holding banded iron shields with crossed ancient Nord greatswords and war axes, respectively. At the bottom of the stairs is a broken sarcophagus with a shield and an ancient Nord battleaxe beside it, and an iron door to the left.

The morgue

The next door opens to a room filled with dead draugr and a dead vampire. Upon entering, Potema will speak, urging you onward. She then raises two of the draugr and the vampire, and unlocks the gate at the far end of the room. The fight with the draugr and vampire is straightforward; however, damage can be reduced or avoided by reanimating the dead before Potema does, or simply by looting the enemies' bodies before fully entering the room so they are unarmed during the battle. After the fight, continue forward through a small crypt. Before exiting the crypt, there are two random [potions of resist shock](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Shock "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Shock") to the right of the door. These will be useful in the boss battle that awaits through the next door.

The main event

There is nothing of interest in the next room except what the draugr are carrying, so focus on the ensuing battle. Upon entering, Potema issues a challenge, then begins shooting revolving [lightning bolts](/wiki/Skyrim:Lightning_Bolt "Skyrim:Lightning Bolt") at regular intervals. Resist shock potions and/or equipment will be advantageous here. In this form, Potema is resistant to arrows, but not magic. Potema will also raise and reanimate draugr in waves to fight for her. There may also be level-appropriate beasts summoned to join the fight. Some schools of thought on ensuring survival in this battle include: reanimating corpses to fight for you before Potema is able, summoning [storm atronachs](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm_Atronach "Skyrim:Storm Atronach") to assist you as they are immune to electricity, or sniping at draugr with arrows from the hallway leading into the battle room. The defeat of each wave of draugr drives Potema farther across the battle zone and into the locked room at the far end. When the battle in the main room is over, the locked door will open. Potema's ghost will then rise from her throne, making the skull comprising Potema's Remains available. Depending upon your level, Potema may respawn and need to be put down multiple times. She may also resurrect the fallen from the battle behind you to assist her. Once defeated, retrieve Potema's skull from the throne. The chest to the left of the throne contains the [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") skill book *[Legend of Krately House](/wiki/Skyrim:Legend_of_Krately_House "Skyrim:Legend of Krately House")*.

The Queen

Continue through the iron door behind the throne to a snowy, naturally lit open-roofed stairway leading to a barred door. Through the door, in the middle of the room is a plinth supporting a low-level piece of armor. On either side of the plinth is a small alcove, each containing a seated draugr. Removing the loot will awaken the draugr, one higher level than the other. Rather, take out the draugr individually, and then, if desired, remove the loot. Exit through the iron door at the end of the room. You will emerge high on a mountainside looking down on the *[Dainty Sload](/wiki/Skyrim:Dainty_Sload "Skyrim:Dainty Sload")*, docked outside Solitude. Turn to face the door behind you, and find a chest, a helmet, a poison, and a random resist element potion on the right, and a random battleaxe on the left. This exit will not be marked on your map.

## Notes

- When you use reanimation spells near where Potema speaks to you, you may hear her say *"What is the meaning of this?"*, just like other NPCs commonly comment.
- All of the spinning gated doors have a small amount of "creep" to them after you have used the lever to stop them, which will eventually block the return passage. Consider these one-way doors.

## Bugs

- A draugr corpse in the Catacombs is partially imbedded into a wall, making it impossible to loot the helmet on its head.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.8, fixes this bug.
- The dagger is awkwardly placed in front of the altar. It floats above the floor, and may fall through it, unable to be picked up.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.1, fixes this bug.
  - Placing a Rune Spell and setting it off may dislodge it, making it available to collect.

## Maps

- 

  Potema's Catacombs or Seclude Chamber
- 

  Potema's Refuge
- 

  Potema's Sanctum

# Skyrim:Preemptive Strike

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Dawnguard Dawnguard.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Dawnguard_Dawnguard.png) | **Destroy the [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") before it turns its allies.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Gunmar](/wiki/Skyrim:Gunmar "Skyrim:Gunmar") |
| Location(s): | Random [Bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") Camp or [Warlock](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock "Skyrim:Warlock") Lair |
| Reward: | Leveled enchanted item |
| ID: | DLC1RH03 |

Preemptive Strike

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak with [Gunmar](/wiki/Skyrim:Gunmar "Skyrim:Gunmar").
2. Travel to radiant location: a [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") camp or [warlock](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock "Skyrim:Warlock") lair.
3. Destroy the [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") before it turns its allies into vampires.
4. Report back to Gunmar.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Gunmar will inform you that he has located another vampire, hiding among outlaws, and will task you with eliminating it before it turns its companions into vampires. He will then mark a random location on your map: either a [bandit camp](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Bandit_Camps "Category:Skyrim-Places-Bandit Camps") or a [warlock lair](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock_Lairs "Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock Lairs") (including locations added by [official add-ons](/wiki/Skyrim:Add-ons "Skyrim:Add-ons")).

Travel to the location and dispose of the vampire hiding there. You won't need to kill all other enemies to complete the quest, although in practice you often won't have much choice. Once the vampire is slain, return to Gunmar for your reward: a leveled enchanted item.

## Notes

- Despite Gunmar stating that the vampire is hiding among "*necromancers*", as you will be sent to a generic warlock lair, you will end up fighting any number of [spellcasters](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock "Skyrim:Warlock").
- If [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") is installed, some radiant locations may be on [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim"). If you are in Skyrim, you will not receive a quest marker pointing you to the quest location, but must travel to Solstheim first (at which point any quest markers you have to quests in Skyrim will disappear).

## Bugs

- The vampire you are sent to destroy, and its "allies" you are supposed to save, do not appear in the radiant destination location. This has been widely reported, and in a number of locations. It likely affects all locations. The objective "Kill the (Vampire) at (dungeon)" will remain active.
  - Waiting 24 hours can fix this.
- If Silver Hands occupy the target dungeon, they will kill the vampire before you can reach it and the quest will instantly complete upon entering the dungeon.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 2.0.3, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| Preemptive Strike (DLC1RH03) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | Gunmar has sent me to <Alias=Dungeon> where I am to destroy the <Alias=Vampire> before it turns its allies into vampires. *Objective 10:* Kill the <Alias=Vampire> at <Alias=Dungeon> |
| 100 |  | *Objective 100:* Return to Gunmar |
| 255 | ☑ | Gunmar sent me to <Alias=Dungeon> where I destroyed the <Alias=Vampire> before it could turn its allies into vampires. |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC1RH03 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC1RH03`.

# Skyrim:Private Lessons

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Teach [Lynea](/wiki/Skyrim:Lynea "Skyrim:Lynea") how to fish.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Viriya](/wiki/Skyrim:Viriya "Skyrim:Viriya") |
| Location(s): | [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") |
| Reward: | [Lynea's Amulet of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Lynea%27s_Amulet_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Lynea's Amulet of Dibella") |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =4 ([Lynea](/wiki/Skyrim:Lynea "Skyrim:Lynea")) |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE001\_Misc\_Markarth |
| Added by: | [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Tusked Terror](/wiki/Skyrim:Tusked_Terror "Skyrim:Tusked Terror") | **Next →** [Spirits Away](/wiki/Skyrim:Spirits_Away "Skyrim:Spirits Away") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Tusked Terror](/wiki/Skyrim:Tusked_Terror "Skyrim:Tusked Terror") | | → Next | [Spirits Away](/wiki/Skyrim:Spirits_Away "Skyrim:Spirits Away") | | |

Private Lessons

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Read *[Wanted: Fishing Tutor](/wiki/Skyrim:Wanted:_Fishing_Tutor "Skyrim:Wanted: Fishing Tutor")*.
2. Speak to [Lynea](/wiki/Skyrim:Lynea "Skyrim:Lynea") about private fishing lessons.
3. Meet Lynea on the docks near the Warrens.
4. Catch fish with Lynea.
5. Speak to Lynea.

## Detailed Walkthrough

The fishing spot

This quest can be started after [Tusked Terror](/wiki/Skyrim:Tusked_Terror "Skyrim:Tusked Terror") has been completed by talking to Viriya:

:   **Know of anyone in need of fishing work around Skyrim?**
:   *"You're headed to Markarth. It's all in this note."*

She will then hand you a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Wanted:_Fishing_Tutor "Skyrim:Wanted: Fishing Tutor") from a woman named [Lynea](/wiki/Skyrim:Lynea "Skyrim:Lynea") who wants fishing lessons. Head to the [Silver-Blood Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver-Blood_Inn "Skyrim:Silver-Blood Inn") in Markarth and speak with Lynea:

:   **You're the one in search of a fishing instructor?**
:   *"Indeed."*
:   **I know just the spot. We can fish off the docks near the Warrens.**
:   *"If that's what you want. I'll see you there, soon."*

Go to the docks near the Warrens and speak to her:

:   *"Is there anything else you need?"*
:   **No, let's begin.**
:   *"Of course."*

Once you have caught three fish in front of Lynea, she will say:

:   *"Well now. I guess I owe you my thanks."*

    :   **Did you enjoy the lesson?**
    :   *"I couldn't be more pleased. Take this small token of my appreciation."*
    :   **As much as I enjoy fishing, I have other things to do. Pay up.**
    :   *"You could have just asked."*

She will then give you her [amulet of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Lynea%27s_Amulet_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Lynea's Amulet of Dibella") as a reward.

## Bugs

- Lynea may not appear at the docks after agreeing to meet her there, and will instead stay in the Silver-Blood Inn indefinitely.
- The wanted notice remains marked as a quest item after the quest ends. **?**
  -  Use the console command `player.removeitem xx000B2C 1` to remove the item from your inventory.

| 10 |  | I spoke to Lynea about fishing lessons, and she agreed to meet me on the docks near the Warrens in Markarth when she is ready to begin. *Objective 10:* Meet Lynea on the docks near the Warrens |
| 25 |  | I met Lynea on the docks near the Warrens. I should catch several fish in order to demonstrate proper fishing technique. *Objective 20:* Catch fish with Lynea (0/3) |
| 40 |  | I caught several fish while Lynea watched on. I should speak with her now that the lesson is complete. *Objective 40:* Speak to Lynea |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE001_Misc_Markarth stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE001_Misc_Markarth`.
