# Skyrim:Promises to Keep

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Help [Louis Letrush](/wiki/Skyrim:Louis_Letrush "Skyrim:Louis Letrush") get [Frost](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost "Skyrim:Frost") from [Sibbi Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Sibbi_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Sibbi Black-Briar").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Louis Letrush](/wiki/Skyrim:Louis_Letrush "Skyrim:Louis Letrush") |
| Location(s): | [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), [Black-Briar Lodge](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Lodge "Skyrim:Black-Briar Lodge") |
| Reward: | Leveled Gold, [Frost](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost "Skyrim:Frost") if you persuade Louis Letrush to let you keep him |
| ID: | MS03 |
| Difficulty: | Easy |

Louis Letrush and Frost

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Louis Letrush](/wiki/Skyrim:Louis_Letrush "Skyrim:Louis Letrush") about Frost.
2. Talk to [Sibbi Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Sibbi_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Sibbi Black-Briar") about it.
3. *(Optional)* Tell [Maven Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Maven_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Maven Black-Briar") about the plan.
4. *(Optional)* Use [key to a stash of gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Keys#Sibbi.27s_Stash_Key "Skyrim:Keys") on lodge strongbox.
5. Steal [Frost](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost "Skyrim:Frost")'s [lineage papers](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost%27s_Identity_Papers "Skyrim:Frost's Identity Papers").
6. Steal [Frost](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost "Skyrim:Frost").
7. Return to [Louis Letrush](/wiki/Skyrim:Louis_Letrush "Skyrim:Louis Letrush").

### See a Man About a Horse

When visiting the [Bee and Barb](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bee_and_Barb "Skyrim:The Bee and Barb") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") [bard](/wiki/Skyrim:Bard_(class) "Skyrim:Bard (class)") named [Louis Letrush](/wiki/Skyrim:Louis_Letrush "Skyrim:Louis Letrush") will recruit you into doing a favor for him. Apparently, Louis has purchased a valuable horse named [Frost](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost "Skyrim:Frost") from [Sibbi Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Sibbi_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Sibbi Black-Briar"). Unfortunately, Sibbi was locked up in the [Riften Jail](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Jail "Skyrim:Riften Jail") before the deal could be finalized. Louis asks you to discuss the situation with Sibbi in the jail, then deliver the horse and its [lineage papers](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost%27s_Identity_Papers "Skyrim:Frost's Identity Papers") to him.

### Possession is Nine-Tenths of the Law

At the jail, bribe or persuade the guard to be allowed in. Visit Sibbi in his cell where he explains the whole story of how he ended up in jail. He also mentions that the horse he owes to Louis is not "actually" his; in fact, it's owned by the Black-Briar estate, namely [Maven Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Maven_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Maven Black-Briar"). However, Sibbi does not want to back out on the deal with Louis, so he offers you the second half of the payment owed if you steal Frost from [Black-Briar Lodge](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Lodge "Skyrim:Black-Briar Lodge"). He also directs you to where the lineage papers are at the lodge. If you're feeling put upon, you can persuade Sibbi to give you [the key](/wiki/Skyrim:Sibbi%27s_Stash_Key "Skyrim:Sibbi's Stash Key") to the lodge strongbox containing two-hundred fifty gold.

### Horse Rustling at the Black-Briar Lodge

Frost located at the stables

Make your way east of Riften to the Black-Briar Lodge. The lodge is heavily guarded, and the mercenary guards will attack on sight. The lodge doors are leveled, but can be opened using the [Black-Briar Lodge Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Lodge_Key "Skyrim:Black-Briar Lodge Key") that each guard carries.

The easiest way to complete the in-lodge requirements is to kill or evade the outside mercenaries, then enter by the back door. This puts you on a level below, and mostly out of sight of, the dining room containing four mercenaries above. The reason for bothering with the upper level at all is to get the [unusual gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") in the master bedroom on the upper level. If your sneaking skills are high, you can just slink into the bedroom and grab the Stone. If not, or if you just want to kill all the mercenaries, your position as you come in by the back door is perfect, forcing the guards to funnel toward you down a long narrow hall, enabling you to snipe them one by one.

To the right of the ladder in the basement is the lodge strongbox. The strongbox is master level but can be opened using Sibbi's stash key if you got it from him back at the jail. Around the corner, you will find Frost's lineage papers on a table. Take the papers and leave the lodge.

Steal the horse named Frost and follow the road away from the lodge until you get close to Louis' quest marker, then cut north to meet him. There are bandits and spiders between the road and Louis, so be prepared to fight them and protect both Louis and Frost; if either dies, the quest will fail. A few well-timed save games will serve you well in case one of them dies.
For your completion conversation with Louis, there are multiple options:

- Let him go with the horse and receive the leveled gold payment. He will then ride the horse to [Whiterun Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Stables "Skyrim:Whiterun Stables"). It is possible though to receive the payment and then immediately steal the horse; the quest will count as finished without double-crossing Louis. Note that stealing the horse will make Louis attack you.
- [Persuade](/wiki/Skyrim:Persuade "Skyrim:Persuade") him to give you the horse and the payment, threatening to tell Maven about everything. If this persuade check succeeds, he will give you the money and run away.
- Tell him that if he was dead, you could keep both the money and the horse. He may attack you or run away.

The latter two will grant you Frost as a [horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse"), although it won't appear in the statistics as a "horse owned"; still, it behaves like an owned horse (helping in fights, waiting where you leave it, and so on), and more importantly, you can mount him in front of witnesses without it being considered stealing.

(Possibly only if you have already told Maven): If you give Louis the horse, or if you blackmail him out of the money, as of the most recent patch Louis remains "essential" at this point, so you cannot cut Louis down as he flees with or without Frost (presumably this is to allow for the later encounter with him and thugs, whether they are his own thugs or Maven's). If you threaten to kill him, he may fight or he may run away, but either way he will be non-essential. (Striking him is considered an assault, but with Louis himself as the only witness, so your bounty will vanish when he dies, unless he runs far enough for someone else to witness his death.)

### Consequences

- If you persuade Louis into letting you keep Frost, a [random event](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Thug_sent_by_Louis_Letrush "Skyrim:World Interactions") may occur in which a [thug](/wiki/Skyrim:Thug "Skyrim:Thug") appears in front of you claiming to have a "message" from Louis, and then proceeds to attack you. This event may happen more than once.
- If you kill the Black-Briar Mercenaries and take Frost but do not bring the horse to Louis, you will eventually be tracked down by Black-Briar thugs who have a bounty on you. Kill them and you will find a note instructing them to "deal with you" (and kill if necessary).
- If you tell Maven and then deliver the horse to Louis, you may [encounter](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Louis_Letrush_vs_Thug "Skyrim:World Interactions") a thug and Louis. The thug will kill Louis unless you intervene, and the survivor will attack you.
- If you deliver the horse to Louis without telling Maven, you may encounter a thug and Louis. Again, the thug will kill Louis unless you intervene, but he will then ignore you and walk away if you don't initiate combat.

### Reward

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 500 |
| 10–19 | 750 |
| 20–29 | 1,000 |
| 30–39 | 1,250 |
| 40+ | 1,500 |

## Notes

- The three door locks are leveled differently. The top floor is the easiest, and the bottom floor is the hardest.
- Originally, Letrush was intended to hide in [the Ratway](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway "Skyrim:The Ratway") near [Gian the Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Gian_the_Fist "Skyrim:Gian the Fist"), but stages 110 and 150 and related scenes no longer exist.
- Frost will likely die if given to Louis, as his route to Whiterun Stables passes through the bandit-occupied [Fort Greenwall](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greenwall "Skyrim:Fort Greenwall"). This can be prevented by clearing the fort beforehand, as the bandits there will be replaced by soldiers of the faction that currently controls Riften.
- Take care when traveling near Black-Briar Lodge while this quest is active. For example, fast-traveling to nearby [Lost Prospect Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Prospect_Mine "Skyrim:Lost Prospect Mine") could trigger a dragon to spawn near the lodge, potentially killing Frost before you can intervene.

## Bugs

- Louis gets duplicated outside of Whiterun near the stables, sometimes stuck in the ground.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.8, fixes this bug.
- If you inform Maven before you have gone to the lodge and stolen the lineage papers, your quest may inexplicably update to show completion of "Steal Frost's Lineage Papers". This bug deprives you of the quest marker on the papers when you get inside Black-Briar Lodge, but you can still complete the quest as normal. Picking up the lineage papers advances the quest. If you simply cannot do without the quest marker and want to inform Maven, steal the Lineage Papers first, then tell Maven, then go back to the lodge and steal the horse (see strategy paragraph in main section, above).
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
- After you first speak to Louis, Maven has an incongruous dialogue option to inform her about the theft, even though you have not yet spoken to Sibbi and don't yet know about the plot to steal the horse.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.4, fixes this bug.
- Upon meeting Louis with the horse and making the exchange, he may run off instead of mounting Frost, leaving you to take the horse. This happens when you exit his speech early after asking about your pay.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.4, fixes this bug.
- The basement door is missing its key setting, forcing guards to use the upper two entrances.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.8, fixes this bug.
- Sometimes Louis is hostile when you are going to give him the horse and will attack you on sight. This might occur after stealing items in the house. To work around this bug, just wait for a day in the city and try again.
- Intimidating Louis into giving you Frost you will not yield [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") experience, while persuading him does.
- If the game is saved while riding Frost and then re-loaded, it's possible Louis will appear standing in the same place where you are sitting. If you trot or gallop, Louis will likewise appear to walk or run, though remaining stuck in the same place on Frost's back. **?**

## Quest Stages

| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* (Optional) Steal the Lodge Stash |

| 30 |  | *Objective 30:* Steal Frost |

| 275 | ☑ |  |
| 300 | ☒ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 15, 250.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MS03 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MS03`.

# Skyrim:Prophet (Dawnguard)

## Overview

This article is about the Dawnguard version of this mission. For the vampire version, see [Prophet (Vampire)](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Vampire) "Skyrim:Prophet (Vampire)").

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Dawnguard Dawnguard.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Dawnguard_Dawnguard.png) | **Find and rescue [a Moth Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dexion_Evicus "Skyrim:Dexion Evicus") from the [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Vampire_Clan "Skyrim:Volkihar Vampire Clan").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |

_05.jpg)

[Dexion Evicus](/wiki/Skyrim:Dexion_Evicus "Skyrim:Dexion Evicus") reads the Elder Scroll for the Dawnguard

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran"), then to [Serana](/wiki/Skyrim:Serana "Skyrim:Serana").
2. Ask around for a [Moth Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Moth_Priest "Skyrim:Moth Priest").
3. Search along the road south of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge").
4. Investigate the scene of the attack.
5. Rescue the Moth Priest from [Forebears' Holdout](/wiki/Skyrim:Forebears%27_Holdout "Skyrim:Forebears' Holdout").
6. Report back to Isran.

### The Interrogation

*"You're a resource. You're an asset."*

Once you have recruited [Sorine Jurard](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorine_Jurard "Skyrim:Sorine Jurard") and [Gunmar](/wiki/Skyrim:Gunmar "Skyrim:Gunmar") into the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)"), and [Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran") has welcomed them to [Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard"), you are told to follow Isran for a little interrogation session with the newly arrived vampire, named [Serana](/wiki/Skyrim:Serana "Skyrim:Serana"). When asked what she is doing in the enemy fort, she will explain: *"I'd rather not be here either, but I needed to talk to you. It's important, so please just listen before your friend, here, loses his patience. It's... well, it's about me. And the Elder Scroll that was buried with me. I'm guessing you figured this part out already, but my father's not exactly a good person. Even by vampire standards."* She then proceeds to explain that her father once was a better person but stumbled upon a prophecy that foretold vampires could control the sun, thus not be afraid of daylight. She finishes with: *"That's what he's after. He wants to control the sun, have vampires control the world."* Serana and her mother tried to stop him from taking over the world, so Serana was sealed away with the scroll, to keep it from her father. She realizes she is in a fort filled with vampire hunters, but agrees to try and persuade Isran to let her help.

Once again, you will have to do the talking, although Isran will be his usual paranoid self: *"All right, you've heard what it has to say. Now tell me, is there any reason I shouldn't kill this bloodsucking fiend right now?"* Regardless of your choice, Isran will agree to let Serana help out, but will turn to Serana and let her know: *"Don't feel like a guest, because you're not. You're a resource. You're an asset. In the meantime, don't make me regret my sudden outburst of tolerance and generosity, because if you do, your friend here is going to pay for it."* While Serana can't help but make fun of Isran's anger, she will turn to you and remind you that she carries the Elder Scroll on her back and that it is necessary to read it to understand the prophecy. The only people who can read the scrolls are the blind [Moth Priests](/wiki/Lore:Cult_of_the_Ancestor_Moth "Lore:Cult of the Ancestor Moth") who live in the [Imperial City](/wiki/Lore:Imperial_City "Lore:Imperial City") in [Cyrodiil](/wiki/Lore:Cyrodiil "Lore:Cyrodiil"), a long way from Skyrim. Luckily, Isran noticed an Imperial scholar passing by on the road just a few days ago. He is unwilling to waste men looking for him, but suggests that you ask innkeepers or carriage drivers all over Skyrim. Serana, however, suggests the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") as a place where a scholar would go. Either way, Serana feels adventurous and will be your follower on the search for the scholar.

### Searching for the Priest

You will face three different options, either asking the numerous [carriage drivers](/wiki/Skyrim:Carriage "Skyrim:Carriage") parked all over Skyrim, asking the innkeepers in the various cities, or taking a trip to the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)"). It is also possible to just wander around Skyrim; if you come to the area south of Dragon Bridge where the Moth Priest was kidnapped from, then you can continue on with the quest even if you haven't done this part. See the table below for a list of options, conditions, and dialogue:

| Option | Conditions | Dialogue |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Carriage Drivers | All of them will provide information, although you will have to persuade them (with a [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") skill of 50), or successfully bribe them to get the information. | **Have you seen a Moth Priest?**  *"That's one of them Imperial scholars, right? Old man with a gray robe?*  **That's right. You've seen him?**  *"Might be that I have, but I can't say for sure. I got enough troubles on my mind just tryin' to scrape by out here."* **Please, it's very important that I find him. (Persuade)** **Passed:** *"Now that I think on it, I did see your priest. He tried to hire me for a trip to Dragon Bridge, but I told him that ain't one of my stops."*  **Failed:** *"Can't help you, friend. I might remember better if my pockets weren't so light."*  **Maybe this will put your mind at ease. (Bribe)** **Passed:** *"Ah yes, I remember your Moth Priest now. He wanted me to take him out to Dragon Bridge, but I told him it ain't one of my stops."*  **Failed:** *"An' maybe it won't."*  **Never mind, I'll look somewhere else.**  *"Suits me just fine."* |
| Innkeepers | The only innkeepers that provide information are the current innkeeper ([Corpulus Vinius](/wiki/Skyrim:Corpulus_Vinius "Skyrim:Corpulus Vinius") or [Sorex Vinius](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorex_Vinius "Skyrim:Sorex Vinius")) at the [Winking Skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Winking_Skeever "Skyrim:The Winking Skeever") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") and [Hulda](/wiki/Skyrim:Hulda "Skyrim:Hulda") at [The Bannered Mare](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bannered_Mare "Skyrim:The Bannered Mare") in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). You will have to persuade them (with a Speech skill of 50) or successfully bribe them to get the information. | **Heard anything about a Moth Priest passing through?**  *"Have I heard anything? It was the talk of the city for three days straight. Ain't too often we get a visitor like that.*  **Where is he now?**  *"Oh, he just left a short while ago. He said he'd finished up his work and it was time to move on. That's all I can tell you. He asked me not to let anyone know where he was going. I suppose he didn't want the attention."* **It's important that I find him right away. (Persuade)** **Passed:** *"Ah, well, in that case I'll tell you what I know. He took the road southwest out of town, and said he was going to be crossing over the Dragon Bridge. That's all that he told me. I hope it helps."*  **Failed:** *"It's like I said, I'm not going to talk about it."*  **Finding that Moth Priest is worth a lot to me. (Bribe)** **Passed:** *"I can see that. He said he was heading for Dragon Bridge next. I hope that helps you."*  **Failed:** *"Sorry, but that Moth Priest's comings and goings are none of my business, and none of yours either."*  **I'll try my luck elsewhere.**  *"Never much cared for folks who can't mind their own business."* |
| College of Winterhold | The librarian in the [Arcanaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arcanaeum "Skyrim:The Arcanaeum"), [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub"), will provide the information without any demands. Your rank at the College does not affect this, although certain College quests can temporarily block dialogue. | **I need to find a Moth Priest.**  *"A Moth Priest? What in Oblivion do you need a Moth Priest for?"*  **My business is my own. Just tell me what I need to know.**  "*Fine, fine. No need to get your breeches in a twist. The obvious answer is to go to the Imperial City. The Moth Priests make their home in the White Gold Tower. Sometimes they go out looking for Elder Scrolls. Lucky for you, there's a Moth Priest in Skyrim right now, doing just that. He stopped in to do some research in the library, then left for Dragon Bridge. If you hurry, you might catch him there.*" |

### The Ambush at Dragon Bridge

_02.jpg)

The ambush

With all clues pointing to the small settlement of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge"), travel there and ask the locals if they have seen a Moth Priest. Some will not even have the topic, while others will claim they know nothing about a traveling priest. [Azzada](/wiki/Skyrim:Azzada_Lylvieve "Skyrim:Azzada Lylvieve") and [Michel Lylvieve](/wiki/Skyrim:Michel_Lylvieve "Skyrim:Michel Lylvieve") will both suggest talking to a guard: *"A Moth Priest? I'm sorry, but I don't know anything about that. Try asking one of the guards."* Following their advice and asking a local guard will have him say: *"Ah, so that was a Moth Priest, then? He rode through town not long ago with an escort of soldiers. They didn't stop, just headed south across the Dragon Bridge."* The only other person people who ever noticed a caravan traveling through town is young [Clinton Lylvieve](/wiki/Skyrim:Clinton_Lylvieve "Skyrim:Clinton Lylvieve"), who will tell you: *"I don't know what a Moth Priest is, but I did see an old man in a robe not long ago. He was riding in a wagon with some Imperial guards. They didn't stop to visit, though. They rode through town heading south, and went across the big bridge. It was only just a little bit ago. I bet you can catch them if you hurry up."*

Head southeast out of town and cross the old bridge. Stay on the path and before long you will see signs of a roadside attack, an overturned cart, a dead [horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse"), a bloodstained [corpse](/wiki/Skyrim:Corpse "Skyrim:Corpse"), a copy of the book *[Effects of the Elder Scrolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Effects_of_the_Elder_Scrolls "Skyrim:Effects of the Elder Scrolls")*, and a dead [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"). Examine the vampire and read the [vampire's note](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire%27s_Note "Skyrim:Vampire's Note"). The note points you towards a place named [Forebears' Holdout](/wiki/Skyrim:Forebears%27_Holdout "Skyrim:Forebears' Holdout"), apparently where the attackers dragged the Moth Priest. Follow the bloodstains over the bridge to the east until you reach yet another attacked cart, with two corpses: a [Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard_(dead) "Skyrim:Redguard (dead)") and a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_(dead) "Skyrim:Nord (dead)"). Follow the blood spatters to the northeast until you reach five standing stones, and the entrance to Forebears' Holdout.

### Forebears' Holdout

_03.jpg)

*"The more you fight me, the more you will suffer, mortal."*

_04.jpg)

*"I serve my master's will."*

Head down the slope and around the corner. Before long you will land on a balcony in a huge chamber with a river, and what resembles an old interior fort with a patrolling vampire, and a bluish orb glowing on the other side. Sneak down the stairs to the south and watch out for two patrolling [death hounds](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Hound "Skyrim:Death Hound") on the ground level. Cross the narrow bridge leading west and follow the wall until an opening reveals a huge bonfire. You will likely be detected by two vampires and two of their thralls, so dispose of them and make use of Serana as she is quite strong with her ranged attacks. Head up the stairs where [Malkus](/wiki/Skyrim:Malkus "Skyrim:Malkus"), the author of the note, will be busy trying to enthrall the imprisoned priest.

**Malkus**: *"The more you fight me, the more you will suffer, mortal."*
**Priest**: *"I will resist you, monster. I must!"*
**Malkus**: *"How much longer can you keep this up, Moth Priest? Your mind was strong, but you're exhausted from the struggle."*
**Priest**: *"Must... resist..."*
**Malkus**: *"Yes, I can feel your defenses crumbling. You want it to end. You want to give in to me. Now, acknowledge me as your master!"*
**Priest**: *"Yes. master*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]*."*

Dispose of Malkus and claim the [Weystone Focus](/wiki/Skyrim:Weystone_Focus "Skyrim:Weystone Focus") from his corpse. Follow the marker up the stairs and activate the Weystone Source with the Focus you took from Malkus. The magical barrier will disappear and reveal the Moth Priest, although not in the state you expected. Instead, he will chant: *"I serve my master's will. But my master is dead, and his enemies will pay!"* The enthralled priest will then attack with everything he has got, so fight him until he yields. He will then stutter: *"That... that wasn't me you were fighting. I could see through my eyes, but I could not control my actions. Thank you for breaking that foul vampire's hold over me."* You can now ask him several questions, but first he will introduce himself: *"I'm quite alright, thanks to you. [Dexion Evicus](/wiki/Skyrim:Dexion_Evicus "Skyrim:Dexion Evicus") is my name. I'm a Moth Priest of the White Gold Tower. These vampires claimed they had some purpose in store for me, but they wouldn't say what. Probably hoping to ransom me, the fools. Now tell me, whom do you represent, and what do you want with me?"* When you introduce yourself as a member of the Dawnguard, and that you need him to read an Elder Scroll, he will prove quite knowledgeable: *"You have an Elder Scroll? Remarkable! If my knowledge of history serves me, I recall that the Dawnguard was an ancient order of vampire hunters. I will be happy to assist you with your Elder Scroll. Just tell me where I need to go."* When you tell him to go to Fort Dawnguard, he will immediately be on his way and you are to report back to Isran. Before leaving, loot the chest nearby then exit the same way you came.

### The Elder Scroll

When you return to [Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard"), you will find Dexion Evicus in the main chamber, facing Isran. Isran will confirm that Dexion has the Elder Scroll and is ready to start reading it. When you speak to the priest he will prove to be overwhelmed with joy: *"Ah, my rescuer! It's good to see you again. It's not exactly the hospitality I'm used to, but your man Isran has seen to my needs well enough. And might I add, this is a remarkable fortress. I have colleagues back home that would love to study this place in detail."* When you tell him to read the Elder Scroll he will begin:

.jpg)

*"Among the night's children, a dread lord will rise."*

***Now, if everyone will please be quiet, I must concentrate.***

***I see a vision before me, an image of a great bow. I know this weapon! It is Auriel's Bow!***

***Now a voice whispers, saying "Among the night's children, a dread lord will rise."***

***In an age of strife, when dragons return to the realm of men, darkness will mingle with light and the night and day will be as one.***

***The voice fades and the words begin to shimmer and distort. But wait, there is more here.***

***The secret of the bow's power is written elsewhere. I think there is more to the prophecy, recorded in other scrolls.***

***Yes, I see them now... One contains the ancient secrets of the dragons, and the other speaks of the potency of ancient blood.***

***My vision darkens, and I see no more.***

***To know the complete prophecy, we must have the other two scrolls.***

This ends the quest and starts the next three quests, [Chasing Echoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Chasing_Echoes "Skyrim:Chasing Echoes"), [Scroll Scouting](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_Scouting "Skyrim:Scroll Scouting") and [Seeking Disclosure](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeking_Disclosure "Skyrim:Seeking Disclosure").

## Notes

- After rescuing the Moth Priest and returning to Fort Dawnguard all the ordinary Dawnguard members will start greeting you as a friend, and become available as followers. Also, at the same time, if you are not already [Blood-Kin](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood-Kin "Skyrim:Blood-Kin") to the Orcs, [Durak](/wiki/Skyrim:Durak "Skyrim:Durak") will grant you that status, which will immediately grant you access to all [Orc Strongholds](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds").
  - The Dawnguard members who patrol [Dayspring Canyon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dayspring_Canyon "Skyrim:Dayspring Canyon") ([Mogrul](/wiki/Skyrim:Mogrul_(Dawnguard) "Skyrim:Mogrul (Dawnguard)"), [Ollrod](/wiki/Skyrim:Ollrod "Skyrim:Ollrod"), [Tilde](/wiki/Skyrim:Tilde "Skyrim:Tilde"), and [Vori](/wiki/Skyrim:Vori "Skyrim:Vori")) won't be affected.
  - The Blood-Kin reward won't apply if you're an Orc, as they always have access to Orc Strongholds by default. The ability to recruit Durak as a follower, however, will.
- If you pickpocket the Weystone Focus and activate the Weystone Source without being detected, the Moth Priest will be freed and immediately attack the surrounding vampires. After defeating them, he will still be aggressive towards you, but he should then have significantly less health and be an easier fight.
- If Serana raises a Thrall that survives the battle, it may begin to sleep in one of the coffins after your conversation with Dexion is finished.
- Once Dexion is set free, the [elk](/wiki/Skyrim:Elk "Skyrim:Elk") outside the cave entrance will immediately respawn once you and Serana exit.
- When Dexion reads Serana's [Scroll](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Scroll_(Sun) "Skyrim:Elder Scroll (Sun)"), it can also still be seen on her back.
- After Serana has told you to locate a Moth Priest, you can speak with Gunmar and he'll give you some [Dawnguard Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Armor "Skyrim:Dawnguard Armor") pieces.
- Serana will not automatically become your follower if you don't speak to her about where to find a Moth Priest, or if you have another follower with you.
- Once your initial coversations with Isran and Serana are finished, it is possible to talk to [Sorine Jurard](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorine_Jurard "Skyrim:Sorine Jurard") and start the [Bolstering the Ranks](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolstering_the_Ranks "Skyrim:Bolstering the Ranks") quest to rescue [Florentius Baenius](/wiki/Skyrim:Florentius_Baenius "Skyrim:Florentius Baenius") and return him to [Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard") before finishing this one, so he can also be present when Dexion reads the Scroll.

## Bugs

- If Dexion is outside of the magic barrier when you first see him, or if you manage to speak with him and tell him to meet you at Fort Dawnguard before he becomes hostile towards you, he ends up becoming permanently hostile after that point.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
  - Reloading and making sure he is in the magic barrier, then playing the quest sequence in the proper order (rescue, defeat, then speak to him) will resolve this.
  - It is also possible to use [Bend Will](/wiki/Skyrim:Bend_Will "Skyrim:Bend Will")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") on Dexion if you've got two or more words of the shout to let him stop attacking everyone.
  - If reloading does not get Dexion to spawn inside the magic barrier, it is also possible to complete the quest by simply *not* interacting with the magic barrier. You can defeat the vampires and send Dexion to Fort Dawnguard without him ever turning hostile. Deactivating the magic barrier is not mandatory for completing the quest and if you looted the Weystone Focus from Malkus' body, it will cease to be a quest item (and thus can be dropped) after reporting back to Isran.
  - Doing this may turn the Dawnguard hostile towards you.
  -  Before quest stage 41, use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") command `prid xx007B88`, followed by `moveto xx00313A`.
  -  It is also possible to fix this by adding him to your own faction via the console. Select him by clicking on him or typing `prid xx007B88`, and then typing `addfac 0005A1A4 1`.
  -  If the previous solution doesn't work for you, select Dexion, and use the console command `disable` followed by `enable`.
  -  If the previous solution doesn't work for you, open the console and select Dexion, either by clicking on him or entering `prid xx007b88` (the first two digits vary depending on loaded mods), then use the command `setav aggression 0`. This makes Dexion passive again and the quest can proceed normally.
- Malkus may spawn inside the magic barrier, not allowing you to loot the [Weystone Focus](/wiki/Skyrim:Weystone_Focus "Skyrim:Weystone Focus") key needed to deactivate the barrier.
- After the cutscene between Isran, Gunmar, and Sorine when you first enter the fort, the three NPCs can become stuck as "busy" when given the quest update to follow Isran.
  - Walking through the main gate to outside then waiting 24 hours, or curing yourself from vampirism if you became a normal vampire when you have chosen the Dawnguard side, can possibly fix this. This is caused by two divergent scripts running at the same time.
- After Dexion finishes reading the Elder Scroll, the quest dialogue might not progress.
  -  Use the console command `setstage DLC1VQ03Hunter 200` to complete the quest.
- The quest may fail to start after completing the previous quest. If this happens, enter the following command into the console: `setstage dlc1vq03hunter 5` then wait a few in-game hours for Serana to appear in the fort, then follow Isran. **?**
- Serana normally leaves your service as a follower for a while upon completion of [Bloodline](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodline "Skyrim:Bloodline"), throughout the following quest [A New Order](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Order "Skyrim:A New Order"), until after the start of Prophet, but sometimes can remain a follower during all that time. When this happens, it causes an oddity in Prophet's starting scene: Serana is supposed to have arrived at Dawnguard on her own and to have been interrogated and possibly tortured. Despite having been with you all along, she will still give dialogue indicating she got here alone and is a prisoner. The glitch is otherwise harmless, as Serana is to be released to rejoin you as a follower at the end of that scene anyway. **?**
- Dexion can sometimes execute the animation of reading the Elder Scroll without actually holding the scroll up in his hands. The scene still progresses normally; it is only a visual glitch. **?**
- When Dexion reads the Elder Scroll, Serana still carries it on her back, so, for a brief moment the same Elder Scroll exists twice (from the Player's perspective, but internally, most likely, Dexion just plays an animation, without actually having an instance of Elder Scroll "item".) **?**
- The entire room of Fort Dawnguard will be black and will not light up even using [Candlelight](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlelight "Skyrim:Candlelight") or [Magelight](/wiki/Skyrim:Magelight "Skyrim:Magelight"). The next three quests will also not start even after the player has initiated dialogue with the respective NPCs. **?**
  - Wait 30 days and try again.
- If the Stormcloaks win the war, female Stormcloak soldiers in Dragon Bridge won't say anything about the Moth Priest if you ask them about it.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.7, addresses this issue. The female Stormcloak soldiers there had no audio recorded. You'll need to ask someone else.

| 55 |  | I'm one step behind the Moth Priest. After leaving Dragon Bridge, I searched along the road for any sign of his passing. I found an overturned wagon and some dead vampires and Imperial guards. Was this the Moth Priest's wagon? *Objective 35:* Investigate the scene of the attack *(if not already done)* |
| 57 |  | I'm one step behind the Moth Priest. After leaving Dragon Bridge, I searched along the road for any sign of his passing. I found an overturned wagon and some dead Imperial guards and vampires. Was this the Moth Priest's wagon? *Objective 37:* Read the Vampire's Note *(if not already done)* |
| 60 |  | Harkon's vampire agents have captured the Moth Priest and taken him to a place called Forebears' Holdout. I must rescue him before the vampires can break his will. *Objective 40:* Rescue the Moth Priest |
| 65 |  | Harkon's agents have captured the Moth Priest! I have tracked them to Forebears' Holdout, but the vampires have enthralled the moth priest and I will have to confront him in order to break their hold. |
| 66 |  | Harkon's agents have captured the Moth Priest! I have tracked them to Forebears' Holdout, but the vampires have enthralled the Moth Priest and I will have to confront him in order to break their hold. *Objective 42:* Defeat the enthralled Moth Priest *(if not already done)* |
| 70 |  | Harkon's agents captured the Moth Priest and enthralled him, but I was able to break their hold on his mind. *Objective 45:* Speak to the Moth Priest |
| 80 |  | I rescued the Moth Priest from his vampire captors and asked him to meet me at Fort Dawnguard. I must return to Isran and tell him of our success. *Objective 50:* Report your success to Isran |
| 90 |  | With the Moth Priest safely back at Fort Dawnguard, he can now read Serana's Elder Scroll and learn more about the prophecy that Harkon is hoping to use to gain power over the sun. |
| 100 |  | With the Moth Priest safely back at Fort Dawnguard, he can now read Serana's Elder Scroll and learn more about the prophecy that Harkon is hoping to use to gain power over the sun. *Objective 60:* Speak to the Moth Priest |
| 200 | ☑ | After the Moth Priest's reading, we have more questions than answers. The old priest saw a vision of a weapon called Auriel's Bow, but we need to find two more Elder Scrolls in order to unravel the rest of the prophecy. |
| *Unknown* |  | *Objective 41:* Deactivate the magic barrier |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 61, 67.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC1VQ03Hunter stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC1VQ03Hunter`.

# Skyrim:Prophet (Vampire)

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Likelolwhat](/wiki/User:Likelolwhat "User:Likelolwhat"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Likelolwhat](/wiki/User:Likelolwhat "User:Likelolwhat") (None), checked by [RobinHood70](/wiki/User:RobinHood70 "User:RobinHood70") |

This article is about the vampire version of this quest. For the Dawnguard version, see [Prophet (Dawnguard)](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Dawnguard) "Skyrim:Prophet (Dawnguard)").

.jpg)

[Dexion Evicus](/wiki/Skyrim:Dexion_Evicus "Skyrim:Dexion Evicus") reading the Elder Scroll for the vampires

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Lord Harkon](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord_Harkon "Skyrim:Lord Harkon").
2. Listen to Harkon's speech.
3. Locate a [Moth Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dexion_Evicus "Skyrim:Dexion Evicus").
4. Seduce the Moth Priest.
5. Report back to Lord Harkon.

### The Speech

Seek out [Lord Harkon](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord_Harkon "Skyrim:Lord Harkon") as directed by [Garan Marethi](/wiki/Skyrim:Garan_Marethi "Skyrim:Garan Marethi") at the end of the [previous quest](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bloodstone_Chalice "Skyrim:The Bloodstone Chalice"). The leader of the [Volkihar](/wiki/Lore:Volkihar "Lore:Volkihar") is in his chambers, located east of the entrance to the Cathedral. Question him about wanting to speak with you, and he will let you in on his plan to end the sun's tyranny: *"Yes, I did. When I told you that I was grateful for my daughter's safe return, I told the truth. But I did not tell you everything."* There are two options, both of which end up at the same place. If you tell him you suspected as much, and he will respond: *"Good. Strong instincts and a cunning mind will serve you as well as blade, spell or claw."* If you instead ask when he plans to start trusting you, you'll be told: *"Do not presume to tell me who I can and cannot trust. I possess the wisdom of a dozen lifetimes, and I will make my own judgements. Now be silent, and hear what I have to say."*

[Lord Harkon](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord_Harkon "Skyrim:Lord Harkon") giving his proclamation

Now, he will speak of his plans, and your part in them. After the monologue, follow him to the balcony overlooking the main hall of [Volkihar Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Keep "Skyrim:Volkihar Keep"), where he will give a speech to the other resident vampires. He will command them, and you, to find a [Moth Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Moth_Priest "Skyrim:Moth Priest"), as Moth Priests are the only people able to read [Elder Scrolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Scroll "Skyrim:Elder Scroll"):

:   *"Scions of the night! Hear my words! The prophesied time is at last upon us. Soon we will claim dominion over the sun itself, and forge a new realm of eternal darkness. Now that I have reclaimed one of my Elder Scrolls, we must find a Moth Priest to read it. I have spread false rumors about the discovery of an Elder Scroll in Skyrim to lure a Moth Priest here. Now it is time to see if those efforts have borne fruit. Go forth, and search the land for rumors of a Moth Priest within our borders. Look to the cities. Speak to innkeepers, carriage drivers, anyone who would meet a traveler. Go now, and carry out this task. This is my command!"*

As Harkon said, there are two potential sources to check out: innkeepers and carriage drivers. [Serana](/wiki/Skyrim:Serana "Skyrim:Serana") will approach you after the speech and give you another lead: the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)"). According to her, wizards always know about things people shouldn't know about. She will also request to accompany you on the trip, as she is feeling restless after being trapped underground for so long.

### In Pursuit of a Priest

When you do as Harkon and Serana suggested and talk to the people of Skyrim, you have a few options. Carriage drivers are the easiest: all of them know immediately what you are talking about, and they are positioned outside all the major cities. You'll have to pass a [Speech check](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech#Skill_Usage "Skyrim:Speech") to get the information for free; otherwise it will cost you.

**Have you seen a Moth Priest?**

:   *"That's one of them Imperial scholars, right? Old man with a gray robe?"*

**That's right. You've seen him?**

:   *"Might be that I have, but I can't say for sure. I got enough troubles on my mind just tryin' to scrape by out here."*

At this point you have several options:

| Option | Dialogue | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Please, it's very important that I find him. **(Persuade)** | **Passed:** *"Now that I think on it, I did see your priest. He tried to hire me for a trip to Dragon Bridge, but I told him that ain't one of my stops."*  **Failed:** *"Can't help you, friend. I might remember better if my pockets weren't so light."* | **Passed:** Obtain information **Failed:** Nothing |
| Maybe this will put your mind at ease. **(Bribe)** | **Passed:** *"Ah yes, I remember your Moth Priest now. He wanted me to take him out to Dragon Bridge, but I told him it ain't one of my stops."*  **Failed:** *"An' maybe it won't."* |
| Never mind, I'll look somewhere else. | *"Suits me just fine."* | Nothing |

Innkeepers are another choice; however, only [Corpulus Vinius](/wiki/Skyrim:Corpulus_Vinius "Skyrim:Corpulus Vinius") or [Sorex Vinius](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorex_Vinius "Skyrim:Sorex Vinius") at the [Winking Skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Winking_Skeever "Skyrim:The Winking Skeever") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") and [Hulda](/wiki/Skyrim:Hulda "Skyrim:Hulda") at [The Bannered Mare](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bannered_Mare "Skyrim:The Bannered Mare") in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") have a clue, and they require a Speech check (50) or a bribe as well.

**Heard anything about a Moth Priest passing through?**

:   *"Have I heard anything? It was the talk of the city for three days straight. Ain't too often we get a visitor like that."*

**Where is he now?**

:   *"Oh, he just left a short while ago. He said he'd finished up his work and it was time to move on. That's all I can tell you. He asked me not to let anyone know where he was going. I suppose he didn't want the attention."*

At this point you have several options:

| Option | Dialogue | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- |
| It's important that I find him right away. **(Persuade)** | **Passed:** *"Ah, well, in that case I'll tell you what I know. He took the road southwest out of town, and said he was going to be crossing over the Dragon Bridge. That's all that he told me. I hope it helps."*  **Failed:** *"It's like I said, I'm not going to talk about it."* | **Passed:** Obtain information **Failed:** Nothing |
| Finding that Moth Priest is worth a lot to me. **(Bribe)** | **Passed:** *"I can see that. He said he was heading for Dragon Bridge next. I hope that helps you."*  **Failed:** *"Sorry, but that Moth Priest's comings and goings are none of my business, and none of yours either."* |
| I'll try my luck elsewhere. | *"Never much cared for folks who can't mind their own business."* | Nothing |

It takes a bit of travel, but [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub"), the librarian at the College of Winterhold will tell you there is a Moth Priest in Skyrim for free: *"The obvious answer is to go to the Imperial City. The Moth Priests make their home in the White Gold Tower. Sometimes they go out looking for Elder Scrolls. Lucky for you, there's a Moth Priest in Skyrim right now, doing just that. He stopped in to do some research in the library, then left for [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge"). If you hurry, you might catch him there."* He will always tell you this regardless of your standing at the College, though College quests like [Containment](/wiki/Skyrim:Containment "Skyrim:Containment") and [The Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Staff of Magnus") can block this dialogue.

Once you have arrived in Dragon Bridge, ask people **"Know anything about a Moth Priest visiting Dragon Bridge?"**, seven people have the asking dialogue option, two of them can lead you the direction, all are listed in the below table.

| House | Person Name | Reponse |
| --- | --- | --- |
| [Lylvieve Family's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Lylvieve_Family%27s_House "Skyrim:Lylvieve Family's House") | [Azzada Lylvieve](/wiki/Skyrim:Azzada_Lylvieve "Skyrim:Azzada Lylvieve") | *A Moth Priest? I'm sorry, but I don't know anything about that. Try asking one of the guards.* |
| [Lylvieve Family's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Lylvieve_Family%27s_House "Skyrim:Lylvieve Family's House") | [Clinton Lylvieve](/wiki/Skyrim:Clinton_Lylvieve "Skyrim:Clinton Lylvieve") | *I don't know what a Moth Priest is, but I did see an old man in a robe not long ago. He was riding in a wagon with some Imperial guards. They didn't stop to visit, though. They rode through town heading south, and went across the big bridge. It was only just a little bit ago. I bet you can catch them if you hurry up.* |
| [Lylvieve Family's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Lylvieve_Family%27s_House "Skyrim:Lylvieve Family's House") | [Michel Lylvieve](/wiki/Skyrim:Michel_Lylvieve "Skyrim:Michel Lylvieve") | *A Moth Priest? I'm sorry, but I don't know anything about that. Try asking one of the guards.* |
| [Horgeir's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Horgeir%27s_House "Skyrim:Horgeir's House") | [Horgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Horgeir "Skyrim:Horgeir") | *Nah. I don't think so.* |
| [Horgeir's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Horgeir%27s_House "Skyrim:Horgeir's House") | [Lodvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Lodvar "Skyrim:Lodvar") | *A Moth Priest? I'm sorry, but I don't know anything about that. Try asking one of the guards.* |
| [Horgeir's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Horgeir%27s_House "Skyrim:Horgeir's House") | [Olda](/wiki/Skyrim:Olda "Skyrim:Olda") | *Nah. I don't think so.* |
| [Four Shields Tavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Four_Shields_Tavern "Skyrim:Four Shields Tavern") | [Aldepius](/wiki/Skyrim:Aldepius "Skyrim:Aldepius") [CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Steel_Soldier "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Steel Soldier") | *Ah, so that was a Moth Priest, then? He rode through town not long ago with an escort of soldiers. They didn't stop, just headed south across the Dragon Bridge.* |

Head across the Dragon Bridge and make your way south along the road until you come across a wrecked carriage. Among the wreckage are a dead [horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse"), a bloodstained [corpse](/wiki/Skyrim:Corpse "Skyrim:Corpse"), a copy of the book *[Effects of the Elder Scrolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Effects_of_the_Elder_Scrolls "Skyrim:Effects of the Elder Scrolls")*, and a dead [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"). Search the vampire to find a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire%27s_Note "Skyrim:Vampire's Note") directing you to [Forebears' Holdout](/wiki/Skyrim:Forebears%27_Holdout "Skyrim:Forebears' Holdout"), a ruin up the hill to the northeast. Follow the blood spatters, and when you reach the four standing stones, the entrance is to the north.

### Forebears' Holdout

_02.jpg)

The barrier with the Moth Priest inside

Inside, you will see what appears to be a ruined underground fort inside a large natural cavern divided by a river. Past the fort, you may notice the large blue-green orb on the platform; this is your target.

Head left down the stairs and across the bridge. There is a [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)") warrior patrolling the walls of the fort, and more enemies inside, including an [armored troll](/wiki/Skyrim:Armored_Troll "Skyrim:Armored Troll"). However you wish to deal with them, make your way to the interior of the fort, climb the stairs and head across the platform to the orb from before. It is actually a magical barrier, and it contains the Moth Priest, [Dexion Evicus](/wiki/Skyrim:Dexion_Evicus "Skyrim:Dexion Evicus"), trapped inside. If you are stealthy enough as you go up the stairs, you can overhear a conversation between a Dawnguard lieutenant and his [commander](/wiki/Skyrim:Vanik "Skyrim:Vanik"):

:   **Dawnguard Lieutenant**: *"Those vampires put up a hell of a fight."*
:   **Vanik**: *"I just hope we weren't too late. I'm not sure what they did to this Moth Priest, but he doesn't look right."*
:   **Dawnguard Lieutenant**: *"You think they turned him?"*
:   **Vanik**: *"I don't know, maybe. Won't know until we get him out of there."*
:   **Dawnguard Lieutenant**: *"How do we do that?"*
:   **Vanik**: *"I'm working on it, now give me some silence so I can think."*

Kill them, and search the corpse of [Malkus](/wiki/Skyrim:Malkus "Skyrim:Malkus"), located between the barrier and the west wall, for the [weystone focus](/wiki/Skyrim:Weystone_Focus "Skyrim:Weystone Focus"). With this in hand, go up the western stairs and find the weystone source on another platform overlooking the barrier. Activating the source with the focus in your possession will drop the barrier, and Dexion will emerge, chanting, *"I serve my master's will."* His demeanor will then change: *"But my master is dead, and his enemies will pay!"* He attacks you with all his might, so fight back until he yields. While he is kneeling, use your Vampire's Seduction power on him. Activate him after this to feed on him and make him your thrall. He will be awestruck: *"By the divines! It's as if my eyes have been opened! I am blinded by the light of your majesty. I... I must obey you. What would you have of me, master?"* Order him to travel to Castle Volkihar, where you must return as well.

### Prophet

When you arrive, your new thrall will be waiting in the main hall, along with your fellow vampires. Talk to Harkon at the far end of the hall. When you tell him what you have done, he will say, *"Yes, I see that. I trust his capture was not too difficult a task?"* You then have three options; whichever one you choose, he will then give you your next instruction: *"Well, your thrall awaits and we have given him the Elder Scroll. Command him to read it, and let us hear the words of prophecy together."*

Order Dexion to read the Elder Scroll, and he will be excited: *"Ah, yes, the Elder Scroll! I admit, I'm looking forward to this."* Then he will produce the Scroll and read from it, leaving you with more questions than answers:

|  |
| --- |
| ***"I see a vision before me, an image of a great bow. I know this weapon! It is Auriel's Bow!***  ***Now a voice whispers, saying "Among the night's children, a dread lord will rise."***  ***In an age of strife, when dragons return to the realm of men, darkness will mingle with light and the night and day will be as one.***  ***The voice fades and the words begin to shimmer and distort. But wait, there is more here.***  ***The secret of the bow's power is written elsewhere. I think there is more to the prophecy, recorded in other scrolls.***  ***Yes, I see them now... One contains the ancient secrets of the dragons, and the other speaks of the potency of ancient blood.***  ***My vision darkens, and I see no more.***  ***To know the complete prophecy, we must have the other two scrolls."*** |

Thus ends Prophet, and begins the next two quests, [Chasing Echoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Chasing_Echoes "Skyrim:Chasing Echoes") and [Seeking Disclosure](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeking_Disclosure "Skyrim:Seeking Disclosure").

## Notes

- If you do not possess the power [Vampire's Seduction](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire%27s_Seduction "Skyrim:Vampire's Seduction") when you are required to enthrall [Dexion Evicus](/wiki/Skyrim:Dexion_Evicus "Skyrim:Dexion Evicus"), you will transform to vampiric level 2 immediately and gain it. If you have been cured of vampirism, you will need to ask Serana to make you a vampire again, then wait for 24 hours to regain the power.
- Be careful with your aim when using Vampire's Seduction, as it can only be used once each day. If you miss, you'll have to wait a full 24 hours to try again. Dexion will remain patiently cowering on the ground where you defeated him, however.
- Clinton Lylvieve sometimes wanders outside the borders of the town, in which case, the dialogue option for the Moth Priest will not be available. Wait for him to get closer to town and it will become available again.
- After you are told to go to Dragon Bridge, you can instead head straight to Forebears' Holdout, where at a point inside, the quest will update and proceed normally.

## Bugs

- Talking to the guards in Dragon Bridge may not bring up a dialogue option to ask them about the Moth Priest, even when you have been directed towards them by other citizens.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.5, fixes this bug.
- If you exit the castle before Harkon finishes his speech, Serana might not come up and talk to you, preventing quest progression. **?**
- It is possible for Dexion to escape the barrier prematurely and become permanently hostile to you.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
- Once you defeat the enthralled Moth Priest and use your seduction power on him, the option to feed may not appear. Instead, he simply stands there and says *"I am not afraid of you"* and *"Your kind are a blight on Tamriel, monster."*
  -  Use the console command `setstage DLC1VQ03Vampire 70` to progress.
- When the Moth Priest reads the scroll, the quest may not progress.
  - Use the console command `setstage DLC1VQ03Vampire 120` to advance to the next stage.
  - Hitting the Moth Priest with anything should also fix this.
- Upon returning to Castle Volkihar with Dexion Evicus, he may become hostile towards the castle's inhabitants and attack them, preventing the quest from progressing. **?**
  - Open the console, select Dexion, and enter the code `setav aggression 0` to remove his hostility. You may have to reload a previous save before entering the code if Dexion has already engaged in combat with the vampires.
- After using Vampire's Seduction to feed on the Moth Priest, he may remain hostile. This will prevent you from commanding him to go to Volkihar Castle.
  - Leaving the cave and reentering should remove his hostility.
- This quest may not activate after completion of the previous quest.
  - Use the console command `setstage DLC1VQ03Vampire 5` to start the quest.
- If the Stormcloaks win the war, female Stormcloak soldiers in Dragon Bridge won't say anything about the Moth Priest if you ask them about it.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.7, addresses this issue. The female Stormcloak soldiers there had no audio recorded. You'll need to ask someone else.

## Quest Stages

| Prophet (DLC1VQ03Vampire) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 5 |  | When I returned to Castle Volkihar, I was informed that Lord Harkon was waiting to speak to me. *Objective 10:* Speak to Harkon |
| 10 |  | When I returned to Castle Volkihar, Lord Harkon told me of a prophecy hidden in the Elder Scrolls that, if fulfilled, would end the tyranny of the sun over vampires. Now he has asked me to join him as he makes a proclamation to the court. *Objective 20:* Listen to Harkon's speech |
| 20 |  | Eager to unlock the secrets of an ancient prophecy thought to be hidden within Serana's Elder Scroll, Harkon has ordered his court to find a Moth Priest. *Objective 23:* Locate a Moth Priest  *Objective 24:* (Optional) Ask carriage drivers about the Moth Priest  *Objective 26:* (Optional) Ask innkeepers in cities about the Moth Priest |
| 30 |  | Eager to unlock the secrets of an ancient prophecy thought to be hidden within Serana's Elder Scroll, Harkon has ordered his court to find a Moth Priest. *Objective 25:* (Optional) Visit the College of Winterhold to ask about the Moth Priest |
| 40 |  | Eager to unlock the secrets of an ancient prophecy thought to be hidden within Serana's Elder Scroll, Harkon has ordered his court to find a Moth Priest. I now have reason to suspect that there's a Moth Priest in Solitude. *Objective 26:* (Optional) Ask innkeepers in cities about the Moth Priest  *Objective 28:* Ask people in Dragon Bridge if they saw the Moth Priest *(if not already done)* |
| 45 |  | I learned that a Moth Priest recently visited Solitude. He was thought to have stayed at the Winking Skeever. *Objective 27:* Speak to the innkeeper in Solitude |
| 47 |  | Harkon has ordered his court to find a Moth Priest who can read Serana's Elder Scroll. I now have reason to believe that a Moth Priest has recently visited Dragon Bridge. *Objective 28:* Ask people in Dragon Bridge if they saw the Moth Priest *(if not already done)* |
| 50 |  | Harkon has ordered his court to find a Moth Priest who can read Serana's Elder Scroll. I followed the trail to Dragon Bridge and learned that a Moth Priest had just passed through town. He was last seen heading south along the road. *Objective 30:* Search along the road that leads south from Dragon Bridge *(if not already done)* |
| 55 |  | I'm one step behind the Moth Priest. After leaving Dragon Bridge, I searched along the road for any sign of his passing. I found an overturned wagon and some dead vampires and Imperial guards. Was this the Moth Priest's wagon? *Objective 35:* Investigate the scene of the attack *(if not already done)* |
| 57 |  | I'm one step behind the Moth Priest. After leaving Dragon Bridge, I searched along the road for any sign of his passing. I found an overturned wagon and some dead Imperial guards and vampires. Was this the Moth Priest's wagon? *Objective 37:* Read the Vampire's Note *(if not already done)* |
| 60 |  | Following Harkon's command to locate a Moth Priest, I followed the trail to Dragon Bridge. There, I learned that a rival band of vampires abducted the Moth Priest I've been tracking and took him to a place called Forebears' Holdout. *Objective 38:* Capture the Moth Priest |
| 65 |  | After a rival vampire faction captured the Moth Priest, I tracked them to Forebears' Holdout. Their leader has enthralled the priest and I will have to confront him in order to assert my own hold over him. |
| 66 |  | After a rival vampire faction captured the Moth Priest, I tracked them to Forebears' Holdout. Their leader has enthralled the priest and I will have to confront him in order to assert my own hold over him. *Objective 39:* Defeat the enthralled Moth Priest *(if not already done)* |
| 67 |  | After a rival vampire faction captured and enthralled the Moth Priest, I fought him and forced him to submit. Now it is my turn to enthrall the Moth Priest by using my newfound powers. *Objective 40:* Use your Vampire's Seduction power on the Moth Priest |
| 70 |  | Eager to hear the contents of Serana's Elder Scroll, Harkon commanded the court to find a Moth Priest. I have now captured one and made him my thrall, commanding him to return to Castle Volkihar. I must report this success to Harkon. *Objective 47:* Command the Moth Priest to go to Volkihar Castle |
| 80 |  | *Objective 50:* Report your success to Harkon |
| 100 |  | With the Moth Priest safely back at Castle Volkihar, the time has come to hear the prophecies contained within the Elder Scroll. *Objective 60:* Command the Moth Priest to read the Elder Scroll |
| 120 |  | *Objective 80:* Speak to Harkon |
| 130 |  | After the Moth Priest's reading, we have more questions than answers. The old priest saw a vision of a weapon called Auriel's Bow, but we need to read two more Elder Scrolls in order to unravel the rest of the prophecy. |
| 200 | ☑ | After the Moth Priest's reading, we have more questions than answers. The old priest saw a vision of a weapon called Auriel's Bow, but we need to find two more Elder Scrolls in order to unravel the rest of the prophecy. |
| *Unknown* |  | *Objective 41:* Deactivate the magic barrier  *Objective 45:* Feed on the Moth Priest to make him your thrall  *Objective 70:* Command the Moth Priest to read the scroll |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 61, 68, 90, 110.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC1VQ03Vampire stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC1VQ03Vampire`.

# Skyrim:Protected NPCs

## Overview

Certain NPCs in Skyrim are **protected** at some point during gameplay. This means that when their health depletes (usually down to 10% of its maximum, but this will occur even if the NPC's health would have been reduced to zero), they enter a state called "bleedout", where they fall to their knees and are ignored by all hostile entities until their health regenerates. Unlike the similar [essential](/wiki/Skyrim:Essential_NPCs "Skyrim:Essential NPCs") status, they can still be killed if they are attacked by the player, where they will die as easily as non-protected NPCs.

A permanent [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") accompanying the player is set as protected, regardless of whether or not they are normally. This also applies to the player's [spouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage") and anyone [recruited](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebuilding_the_Blades "Skyrim:Rebuilding the Blades") into the [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades").

To be killed, a protected NPC must have their health fall to zero from a direct hit by the player. An important keyword in this definition is "direct." This can sometimes lead to your follower or spouse surviving attacks from you when you don't expect them to. Namely:

- Fall damage from the [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") shout will not kill a protected NPC.
- A poison slipped into your spouse's or inactive follower's pocket (Note: Only inactive followers can be pickpocketed) using the [Poisoned skill perk](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisoned "Skyrim:Poisoned") will only bring the Protected NPC into bleedout, even if that same poison would kill the protected NPC if it were applied to the player's weapon.

For a list of protected NPCs, see [Category:Skyrim-Protected NPCs](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Protected_NPCs "Category:Skyrim-Protected NPCs") and for a list of protected creatures, see [Category:Skyrim-Protected Creatures](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Protected_Creatures "Category:Skyrim-Protected Creatures").

## Notes

- Hostiles (like [Draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") and [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit")) have a state similar to being "protected", but it does not offer the same benefit: when they enter the bleedout state, their attackers will ignore them and instead concentrate on any other hostiles in the area (such as other Draugr and bandits) before finally turning their attention back on them, even if they are still in bleedout. If there are no other hostiles in the area, the attackers will concentrate on them until they are destroyed.
- Active Followers can still kill protected NPCs, but conjured creatures cannot.

## Bugs

- A protected NPC may still be killed by other NPCs if they are attacked during bleedout, commonly by area of effect magic, poison or delayed power attacks.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version Beta 1.9.26.0.8, fixes this bug.
- Characters brought to the bleedout state may not stand back up, leading to them crawling along the floor.
  - Using [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force"), casting [paralyze](/wiki/Skyrim:Paralyze_(spell) "Skyrim:Paralyze (spell)") or sprinting into them may reset their animation.
- Sometimes, after entering the bleedout state and standing back up, NPCs may not have regenerated their health: rather, it remains at the percentage when they fell to their knees originally. This might happen two or more times in a row before they finally regain full health.

Protecting the Bloodline

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Fura Bloodmouth](/wiki/Skyrim:Fura_Bloodmouth "Skyrim:Fura Bloodmouth") or [Garan Marethi](/wiki/Skyrim:Garan_Marethi "Skyrim:Garan Marethi").
2. Travel to radiant location: a [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") camp or [warlock](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock "Skyrim:Warlock") lair.
3. Kill the feral-blooded [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") before it turns its allies into vampires.
4. Return to the quest giver.

## Detailed Walkthrough

You will be asked to kill a vampire before it turns its allies. [Fura Bloodmouth](/wiki/Skyrim:Fura_Bloodmouth "Skyrim:Fura Bloodmouth") will say:
*"A feral-blooded has holed up with a group of bandits/necromancers. Likely wants to create a nest of broodlings."*
"We don't need competition for blood, and we don't want the mortals getting up in arms making things difficult for us."
"Go destroy the feral beast before this becomes a problem."

When hunting the vampire, it will be at a random location, either a [bandit camp](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Bandit_Camps "Category:Skyrim-Places-Bandit Camps") or [warlock lair](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock_Lairs "Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock Lairs"). This can include locations added by [official add-ons](/wiki/Skyrim:Add-ons "Skyrim:Add-ons") such as [Hrodulf's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrodulf%27s_House "Skyrim:Hrodulf's House") in [Solstheim](/wiki/Lore:Solstheim "Lore:Solstheim").

# Skyrim:Proudspire Manor

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | Never (storage is [safe](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Safe_Locations "Skyrim:Containers")) |
