| # of [Cooking Pots/Spits](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") | 1 |

Proudspire Manor

**Proudspire Manor** is a three-story house that can be purchased in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude").

This manor is the most expensive [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses") available for purchase in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"). It has many amenities available for purchase, including an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"), an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter"), and [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") (see [bugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Proudspire_Manor#Bugs "Skyrim:Proudspire Manor")) for your crafting needs.

To purchase the home, you must first complete the two quests [The Man Who Cried Wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Man_Who_Cried_Wolf "Skyrim:The Man Who Cried Wolf") and [Elisif's Tribute](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif%27s_Tribute "Skyrim:Elisif's Tribute"). Upon completion, Elisif will permit you to purchase the house from [Falk Firebeard](/wiki/Skyrim:Falk_Firebeard "Skyrim:Falk Firebeard") for 25,000 gold. Ownership of this home and helping five citizens within the hold is required to become a thane of [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar"). [Jordis the Sword-Maiden](/wiki/Skyrim:Jordis_the_Sword-Maiden "Skyrim:Jordis the Sword-Maiden") is the housecarl of Proudspire and joins you after you become a thane.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Jordis the Sword-Maiden](/wiki/Skyrim:Jordis_the_Sword-Maiden "Skyrim:Jordis the Sword-Maiden") ‡ [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower") |

‡ This person moves here once you have purchased the property and become thane.

## Related Quests

- **[No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned")**: Find the [24 gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") to restore the Crown of Barenziah.
- **[The Man Who Cried Wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Man_Who_Cried_Wolf "Skyrim:The Man Who Cried Wolf")**: Investigate reports of strange happenings in [Wolfskull Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolfskull_Cave "Skyrim:Wolfskull Cave").
- **[Elisif's Tribute](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif%27s_Tribute "Skyrim:Elisif's Tribute")**: Take Torygg's war horn to the Shrine of Talos.
- **[Thane of Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Haafingar "Skyrim:Thane of Haafingar")**: Gain the title of [Thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane") of [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

It is located between the [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College") and [Vittoria Vici's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici%27s_House "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici's House") and is near the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace"). There are a number of harvestable plants outside, including [dragon's Tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue") plants, [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") and [blue mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"). There are three entrances to the manor; one provides direct access to the basement and crafting stations while both the other entrances lead into the second floor and the main reception area.

### Proudspire Manor

Once purchased and prior to purchasing any of the upgrades the property is far from empty. It is dirty and dusty with cobwebs throughout. However with the exception of four [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels, five food sacks, two cupboards in the basement, a food barrel in the reception area and the child's bedroom[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") all other items found prior to purchasing the upgrades will also be available after the upgrades have been purchased. The upgrades improve the quality of the furniture found in the manor and adds various items of furniture, many rugs and other items of interest. Unusually, the Child's Bedroom upgrade does not remove any crafting areas, it does remove two sets of shelves holding several [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") and [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") from the upstairs private dining room. As such it is worth purchasing this separately from the other upgrades enabling you to collect the items from the shelves before returning and purchasing the child's bedroom.

#### Top Floor

Climbing to the top floor leads past a food barrel and stack of crates halfway up the stairs that are removed when purchasing the living room upgrade. At the top of the stairs is a large vase containing a [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bush. The room has a long wooden table with a bottle of [spiced wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Spiced_Wine "Skyrim:Spiced Wine"), a bunch of [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton") and a [potion of regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration") on top and three chairs arranged around it. There are many more crates stacked around the room which are removed and replaced with the living room upgrade. A door in the west wall opens into the master bedroom containing a large double bed coming out from the west wall with an end table to the left with a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") on top, a stool to the right and an unlocked empty [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") at the foot of the bed. There is an unlocked [safe](/wiki/Skyrim:Safe "Skyrim:Safe") in the corner, two small wardrobe; one of which has an [unusual gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") on top, narrow table, small unit, and low table and chair with a potion of regeneration on top.

#### Second Floor

Here you will find a set of shelves, a low table with two chairs and a stool around it and a copy of *[The Wolf Queen, v8](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen,_v8 "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen, v8")* on top. There are also a crate, food barrel, narrow table and two more chairs stacked in the corner and by the entrance from the porch area another narrow table with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") on top. The kitchen is directly off of the reception and contains a wooden table laid with two bottles of spiced wine, a potion of regeneration, three [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish") steak, and a bunch of tundra cotton. There are three wall shelves, one of which has two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") on, a narrow table with an iron dagger on top and a food sack underneath, a sideboard with a small mead barrel on top and two open crates, one of which is on a small set of shelves. The open crates contain a total of three bunches of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), two [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek") and a [tomato](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato"). Outside in the patio area are three food barrels and several stacks of crates.

#### Basement

The stairs down to the basement have a stack of crates and rugs halfway down. At the bottom in an alcove on the right are a set of shelves filled with small mead barrels, a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and two bottles of Nord mead, a cupboard holding two food sacks and some cheap crockery, and a food barrel with eight [iron ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot") on top. The next area, which becomes the enchanting area, contains two practice dummies, the base of an archery target, and a set of shelves holding a bunch of tundra cotton, three [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") bulbs, a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), a single loose [septim](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), a set of [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots"). Past the partition where the [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") is placed is an extinguished fire pit in the middle with a [silver ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ingot "Skyrim:Silver Ingot") on the surround, a cupboard holding several loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and cheese wheels, four food barrels behind the cupboard and three food sacks beside it and two stacks of crates including an open one containing a [red apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") and three [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"). There are two stacks of two open crates by the basement entrance, the bottom crate of each contains bread and cheese and a sample of [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"), a gourd, a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"), and an [orange dartwing](/wiki/Skyrim:Orange_Dartwing "Skyrim:Orange Dartwing"). The housecarl's room in the basement contains an unowned bedroll, two food barrels, three food sacks and many crates, rugs and unused pieces of furniture. This doesn't get upgraded like normal when you become [thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Haafingar "Skyrim:Thane of Haafingar") and the [housecarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Housecarl "Skyrim:Housecarl") moves into the manor (see [bugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Proudspire_Manor#Bugs "Skyrim:Proudspire Manor")), unlike with other houses.

When upgraded, everything that is not the housecarl's room will be removed, except for the silver ingot and [clothes iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes_Iron "Skyrim:Clothes Iron") in the alchemy laboratory, the two bottles of Nord mead and single bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), the stack of eight iron ingots and the pair of [tongs](/wiki/Skyrim:Tongs "Skyrim:Tongs") above it, as well as the three baskets directly below the staircase. Therefore, it is advised to take all of the items that will be removed (anything that is not listed above) and store it in a safe place. Note that all the storage containers, except for the barrel that the iron ingots and tongs sit on, will be removed on upgrade.

## Costs and Upgrades

| Proudspire Manor | | | | | | | | | |

[†](#note_Childroom)Child's Bedroom only available if [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") is installed. Choosing this upgrade will create a new room next to the master bedroom.

#### Bedroom

The large double bed has been replaced by a luxury four poster double bed, the end table, chest, safe and two small wardrobes remain unchanged. The stool to the right of the bed has been replaced with a small round table. The small unit has been upgraded, the narrow table now holding a platter of three [sweet rolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll") and a plate of two [green](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple") and a red apple, and low table and chair have all been upgraded now holding a plate of bread and cheese and a bottle of alto wine. Added to the room are a wash basin, a wall shelf holding a bottle of wine, a bottle of spiced wine, three bottles of Nord mead, two weapon racks, and a two-shelf bookcase with a bunch of tundra cotton on top, beside the safe.

#### Living Room

This actually upgrades both the main reception area on the second floor and the private dining room on the top floor. In the reception area, the low table and two chairs, stool, set of shelves, two narrow tables and wooden bench have all been upgraded. The shelves now hold a bowl of [void salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Void_Salts "Skyrim:Void Salts"), two bottles of [frostbite venom](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Venom "Skyrim:Frostbite Venom"), a [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") flower, [potion of haggling](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Haggling "Skyrim:Potion of Haggling"), bowl of [glow dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Glow_Dust "Skyrim:Glow Dust") and two samples of [slaughterfish scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Scales "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Scales"). On the low table is a plate of bread and cheese with a bottle of wine and [tomato](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato") beside it. One of the narrow tables is now a small cupboard with a small table beside it with a platter of two sweet rolls, two [boiled creme treats](/wiki/Skyrim:Boiled_Creme_Treat "Skyrim:Boiled Creme Treat"), and two red apples. A large vase containing a [juniper tree](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries") has been added. Around by the porch entrance the narrow table has been upgraded and now has a copy of *[Thief of Virtue](/wiki/Skyrim:Thief_of_Virtue "Skyrim:Thief of Virtue")* on top with a wall shelf above holding a [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health"), and copies of *[The Talos Mistake](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Talos_Mistake "Skyrim:The Talos Mistake")* and *[Olaf and the Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Olaf_and_the_Dragon "Skyrim:Olaf and the Dragon")*. Two more large vases added, one by the porch entrance and the other by the stairs down to the basement, both contain snowberry bushes. Both flights of stairs have been cleared of all crates, barrels, etc. There is now a large vase halfway up the stairs to the top floor containing another snowberry bush.

Upstairs the table and chairs in the middle of the room have been upgraded. All the stacks of crates have been removed and two sets of shelves, a two-shelf bookcase, a small cupboard and wooden bench have been added around the room. On the sets of shelves are two baskets; one contains a bunch of tundra cotton and the other two bunches of lavender, a deathbell flower, another bunch of tundra cotton, copies of *[Lost Legends](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Legends "Skyrim:Lost Legends")*, *[Biography of Barenziah, v3](/wiki/Skyrim:Biography_of_Barenziah,_v3 "Skyrim:Biography of Barenziah, v3")*, *[The Cake and The Diamond](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cake_and_The_Diamond "Skyrim:The Cake and The Diamond")*, a [draught of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Strength "Skyrim:Draught of Strength"), potion of health, and a potion of regeneration. On the small cupboard is a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum"), [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"), and potion of health. On the table in the middle of the room is a bottle of spiced wine and a potion of regeneration.

#### Alchemy Laboratory

When this upgrade is purchased the two stacks of open crates by the entrance have been replaced with two better quality open crates containing the same items. The fire pit has been cleaned and relit. The cupboard, four food barrels, three food sacks and all the crates have been removed and three sets of shelves and a two-shelf bookcase have been added. There is an alchemy lab in the northern corner with a wall shelf above and a small table beside it. A stack of two open crates are against the wall between the bookcase and one of the sets of shelves and another open crate opposite with a rack hanging above holding a [garlic braid](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic_Braid "Skyrim:Garlic Braid"), two bunches of [dried elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Dried Elves Ear") and a bunch of [dried frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Dried Frost Mirriam"). Six more garlic braids are hanging directly from the ceiling in two groups of three. All of the furniture and two baskets hold various ingredients, potions and food items as listed below:

† Item of random strength.

#### Enchanting Laboratory

This upgrade clears out the alcove by the bottom of the stairs and the area that contained the practice dummies. In the alcove the set of shelves and cupboard are removed although the bottles of mead and wine remain. A smaller unit holds three small mead barrels. The food barrel with eight [iron ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot") on top remain and along the back wall are a row of five weapon racks with the middle one holding an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"). In the larger area two mannequins replace the practice dummies. There is an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter") installed in the corner with two shield plaques above, one on each wall, both hold an [iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield") with crossed [iron greatswords](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Greatsword "Skyrim:Iron Greatsword"). There is an open crate containing a filled [common](/wiki/Skyrim:Common_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Common Soul Gem") and a filled [petty soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem"). Behind this is a gem stand holding an empty [lesser soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Lesser Soul Gem"). To the left of these are two weapon plaques on the wall. There is a two-shelf bookcase with a wall shelf over it. On the shelf is an empty [grand](/wiki/Skyrim:Grand_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Grand Soul Gem") and an empty lesser soul gem.

#### Patio Decorations

Once this is purchased all the crates and barrels are cleared and a small square empty wooden table and two chairs, a large planter and a wooden bench are installed around the entrance. It is an upgrade that may be worth *not* purchasing.

#### Kitchen

Purchasing this upgrade improves the quality of the existing furniture, adds a bowl of bread and plate with a [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese") on top of the narrow table and a bottle of alto wine on the wall shelf above. Adds a fireplace with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") on a stand in front and a joint of [raw beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Beef "Skyrim:Raw Beef") and a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") in a cast iron pot on the floor. It adds a small cupboard with an open crate on top containing four tomatoes and above this on the wall shelf it adds a [potion of plentiful healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Healing"), a small unit holding an [empty wine bottle](/wiki/Skyrim:Empty_Wine_Bottle "Skyrim:Empty Wine Bottle"), a two-shelf bookcase, a small round table beside main table with bread and cheese on top.

#### Children's Bedroom

This upgrade adds a new room to the existing house. On the top floor just outside the master bedroom, it adds a door into a bedroom containing two children's beds coming out from the southwest wall with long unlocked chests at the foot of the beds. A small unit between the beds holds a [blue](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Dartwing "Skyrim:Blue Dartwing") and an [orange dartwing](/wiki/Skyrim:Orange_Dartwing "Skyrim:Orange Dartwing"), a [grass pod](/wiki/Skyrim:Grass_Pod "Skyrim:Grass Pod"), a bunch of lavender, a bowl containing three [purple mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") and seven [red mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower"), a [pearl](/wiki/Skyrim:Pearl "Skyrim:Pearl"), an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"), copies of *[Pirate King of the Abecean](/wiki/Skyrim:Pirate_King_of_the_Abecean "Skyrim:Pirate King of the Abecean")*, *[Walking the World, Vol XI](/wiki/Skyrim:Walking_the_World,_Vol_XI "Skyrim:Walking the World, Vol XI")*, and *[A Children's Anuad](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Children%27s_Anuad "Skyrim:A Children's Anuad")*. To the left of the beds is a small round table with a [blue butterfly wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Butterfly_Wing "Skyrim:Blue Butterfly Wing") and a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll") on a plate with a [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute") leaning against the wall beside it. To the right of the beds is another small round table with a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute") on top and beside this is a large map of [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") on a stand. There is a long wooden table and bench against the southeast wall with a platter holding a [honey nut treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Honey_Nut_Treat "Skyrim:Honey Nut Treat"), a [boiled creme treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Boiled_Creme_Treat "Skyrim:Boiled Creme Treat") and a [long taffy treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Taffy_Treat "Skyrim:Long Taffy Treat"), a red and a green apple. Against the northeast wall is a tall wardrobe, a wash basin, a child's practice dummy, an unlocked wooden chest containing minor loot with a wall shelf above holding a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum"), some [charcoal](/wiki/Skyrim:Charcoal "Skyrim:Charcoal"), copies of *[Cats of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Cats_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Cats of Skyrim")*, and *[Yellow Book of Riddles](/wiki/Skyrim:Yellow_Book_of_Riddles "Skyrim:Yellow Book of Riddles")* and a flute. This upgrade also removes two of the sets of shelves from the private dining room to accommodate the door. It will also remove the items on the shelves: two baskets; one contains a bunch of tundra cotton and the other two bunches of lavender, a deathbell flower, another bunch of tundra cotton, copies of *Lost Legends*, *Biography of Barenziah, v3*, *The Cake and The Diamond*, draught of strength, potion of health, and a potion of regeneration. It is worth collecting these items prior to purchasing this upgrade.

## Notes

- Strangely, the *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")* notes that *"This dwelling is currently empty. It was the scene of a gruesome murder, and there's rumors of it being haunted."*. This text seems to be mistakenly copied from the description of the [Abandoned House](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_House "Skyrim:Abandoned House") in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth").
- Oddly enough, there are no apparent downsides to using the manor as a home without officially buying it but instead using the stolen Fletcher's key to open the back door. Sleeping in the bed inside gives a well-rested bonus, and all containers are safe for storage.
- Once a [housecarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Housecarl "Skyrim:Housecarl") moves into the manor, the basement bedroom should be refurnished to include a small one-person bed, but often doesn't, due to a [bug](/wiki/Skyrim:Proudspire_Manor#Bugs "Skyrim:Proudspire Manor").
- There is no tanning rack in the manor, though there is one down the street at the blacksmith.
- There is no smelter in all of Solitude. If you live in Proudspire Manor and need to make ingots from ore, the nearest smelter is in [Broken Oar Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Oar_Grotto "Skyrim:Broken Oar Grotto") on the coastline, which is inhabited by Blackblood Marauders.
- The [flag](/wiki/Skyrim:Flag "Skyrim:Flag") embedded in the map in the children's bedroom has no Havok physics and will float if dropped.
- Adopted children living here will have unique dialogue comments about Solitude:
  - *Do you think I could be a Bard? I really like singing.* (girls)
  - *The Palace looks so pretty. I wish they'd let me inside...* (girls)
  - *I saw a Thalmor the other day. He was really scary!* (girls)
  - *When I grow up, I wanna join the Legion!* (boys)
- If you ask your spouse "How are the kids?" they will reply with one of the following, depending on their [voicetype](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Dialogue#Adoption_Dialogue "Skyrim:Generic Dialogue"):
  - *Oh, fine. So many guards on the street here I hardly have to worry.* (Arrogant)
  - *Very well, love. This is a beautiful house, and Solitude is so safe, so diverse. It's a wonderful place to raise a child.* (Neutral)
  - *Fine, just fine. This house is perfect for a growing family.* (Nord)
  - *Meh. Children get soft when they're coddled in a place like this.* (Orc)
- Proudspire Manor also appears as [player housing](/wiki/Online:Proudspire_Manor "Online:Proudspire Manor") in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

## Bugs

- There are a few bugs which affect all houses, see the [bugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses#Bugs "Skyrim:Houses") section of the Houses page for details and fixes.
- If you try to put too many books in a bookcase they will disappear and you will no longer be able to access that bookcase.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4, fixes this bug.
- Proudspire Manor can be entered through the patio door using the [Solitude Fletcher's key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Solitude_Fletcher "Skyrim:Key to Solitude Fletcher"), so the manor does not need to be purchased to obtain its [unusual gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem").
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.9.26.0.8, fixes this bug.
- The housecarl's bedroom in the basement will not be furnished after you are made thane.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
  -  You can use the following console commands to fix the issue: `prid e25d4` followed by `enable`.
    -  If two boxes on the right of the room do not disappear (partly overlapping a chair), you can use the following console commands `prid e273a` followed by `disable`.
- A [spouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage#NPCs_available_to_be_married "Skyrim:Marriage") living in Proudspire Manor will sometimes prefer to sleep on the housecarl's bedroll rather than the bed in your master bedroom. However, you will still receive the Lover's Comfort and Mother's/Father's Love bonuses if you go to sleep when your spouse and children do.
  -  You can use the console commands above to replace the bedroll with the new furnishings or you can enter the commands `prid e2735` and `disable` to remove the bedroll and make your spouse sleep in the master bedroom.
  - If you plan to marry Jordis the Sword-Maiden and kids are not adopted yet, you can ask her right after the marriage ceremony to live in her property. Then travel to Proudspire Manor and ask her to live in your house in Solitude. She will immediately switch her behavior to spouse script (will be sleeping in master bed, etc). But if you hire and dismiss her she'll switch to housecarl script again (will be guarding entrances, sleeping at ground floor, etc).
- Rugs below the living room and the second floor tables will not appear despite purchasing the living room furnishings.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
  -  You can use the following console commands to fix the issue: `prid e25d7` followed by `enable`.
- After installing [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire"), the cooking pot in the kitchen disappears and the barrel under the stairs may be missing.
  -  The [Unofficial Hearthfire Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Hearthfire_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Hearthfire Patch"), version 1.0.1, fixes this bug.
  -  You can use the following console command to spawn the pot, being inside the manor: `player.placeatme 001010b3 1` then click at spawned pot so its ID can be seen and fix coordinates by these commands: `setpos x 652``setpos y -970``setpos z 0``setangle x 0``setangle y 0``setangle z 88.8084`.
- After purchasing the child's bedroom, its door may not appear making it inaccessible.
  -  You can use the following console commands to fix the issue: `prid xx00418a` followed by `disable`. Alternatively, it's sometimes caused by the section of the wall that used to be there not disabling when the door is put in. Use `prid d89eb` followed by `disable` to disable this wall section.
  -  In addition, the crates in front of the door may not vanish. The following console commands will cause them to vanish: `prid xx00418b` followed by `disable`.
- The side door onto the balcony cannot be opened even if you have the house key. **?**
  - Jordis has the key to the door. Completing the Thane of Haafingar quest will unlock it.
  -  It can also be fixed using the console command `unlock` with the door selected.
- The quest objective "Visit Proudspire Manor, your new home" will not be completed if you don't enter through the correct door.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
  - Follow the quest marker and enter through the side door, up the stairs, opposite the entrance to [Vittoria Vici's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici%27s_House "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici's House"). This will cause the quest objective to update.
- If you have purchased Proudspire Manor and placed armor on the mannequins prior to the Battle For Solitude quest, the armor may have disappeared permanently if you enter the house during the battle. **?**
- You cannot mount fish on either of the two fish plaques added by the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") if you have already done so in another house. See [this section](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing#Bugs "Skyrim:Fishing") for details.
  - The [Official Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch"), version 1.6.629, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Proving Honor

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Companions.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Companions.png) | **Claim a [Fragment of Wuuthrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fragment_of_Wuuthrad "Skyrim:Fragment of Wuuthrad") from [Dustman's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dustman%27s_Cairn "Skyrim:Dustman's Cairn").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Skjor](/wiki/Skyrim:Skjor "Skyrim:Skjor") |
| Location(s): | [Dustman's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dustman%27s_Cairn "Skyrim:Dustman's Cairn"), [Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr") |
| Reward: | A [Skyforge Steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Steel Sword") weapon, Word for the [Fire Breath](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Breath "Skyrim:Fire Breath") shout |
| ID: | C01 |
| Suggested Level: | 6 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Take Up Arms](/wiki/Skyrim:Take_Up_Arms "Skyrim:Take Up Arms"), one [radiant quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions#Radiant_Quests "Skyrim:Companions") | **Next →** [The Silver Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Silver_Hand "Skyrim:The Silver Hand") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Take Up Arms](/wiki/Skyrim:Take_Up_Arms "Skyrim:Take Up Arms"), one [radiant quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions#Radiant_Quests "Skyrim:Companions") | | → Next | [The Silver Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Silver_Hand "Skyrim:The Silver Hand") | | |

A fragment of Wuuthrad in Dustman's Cairn

## Quick Walkthrough

1. After completing one Radiant Quest, talk to [Skjor](/wiki/Skyrim:Skjor "Skyrim:Skjor").
2. Team up with [Farkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Farkas "Skyrim:Farkas") and travel to [Dustman's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dustman%27s_Cairn "Skyrim:Dustman's Cairn").
3. Locate a [Fragment of Wuuthrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fragment_of_Wuuthrad "Skyrim:Fragment of Wuuthrad").
4. Participate in your own initiation.

### The Trial of the Whelp

After completing one [radiant quest](#Radiant_Quests), your job providers, [Aela the Huntress](/wiki/Skyrim:Aela_the_Huntress "Skyrim:Aela the Huntress") and [Farkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Farkas "Skyrim:Farkas"), will point you towards Skjor when asked for more work: *"Skjor was looking for you, earlier."* When asked for a reason, their response will differ. Aela will answer: *"He didn't say, but you'd better move fast. There's probably something I could find for you to do, but best to check with him."*, while Farkas will say: *"Don't know. He just said he needed to talk to you before you do anything else. I don't like making him angry, but there is some work for you if you want it."*

Skjor will reveal that a scholar has discovered another fragment of the legendary battleaxe, [Wuuthrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Wuuthrad "Skyrim:Wuuthrad"). He asks you to retrieve it and will direct you to [Farkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Farkas "Skyrim:Farkas") who will serve as your Shield-Brother for the task, both helping you survive the quest and supervising you to ensure you complete the mission "honorably". When approached, Farkas becomes a temporary follower. If you already have a follower, they will return to your home or to their base location and await you there until you've completed the quest. If asked, Farkas will elaborate on the origins of Wuuthrad. Your destination is [Dustman's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dustman%27s_Cairn "Skyrim:Dustman's Cairn"), a barrow northwest of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). You can either have him follow you all the way or ask him to meet you there.

### Dustman's Cairn

The place is crawling with [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), so be prepared for a long trek. There is a [Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") skill book *[The Battle of Sancre Tor](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_of_Sancre_Tor "Skyrim:Battle of Sancre Tor")* in the first room. The second chamber contains an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter") and two thrones, with the only available path blocked by a gate. Locate the northernmost room and pull the lever, which will drop another gate and trap you inside, after which the lever will break. From the other side, Farkas says he will find a way to release you, then is unexpectedly confronted by a group of [Silver Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Hand "Skyrim:Silver Hand") members, leaving you trapped to watch the scene unfold.

### Eyes on the Prey

Farkas transforming to fight the Silver Hand

The Silver Hand turns out to be there for a reason. While you watch, Farkas will transform into a [werewolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Werewolves "Skyrim:Werewolves") and wipe out the opposition within seconds. After opening the gate, Farkas will reveal that only certain [Companion](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") members are blessed with the ability. Proceed forward through the linear cave system until you reach the entrance to the second zone, Dustman's Crypt.

Farkas fighting a Frostbite Spider

After continuing through the next door, you will cross the bridge where you can see the lower room you are headed towards. If you stand idle in this caged walkway, at least one archer will attack you from the room below. After crossing the bridge, you will go around a corner and be in a long down-sloped hallway. If you run ahead to attack the Silver Hand, or choose to follow Farkas, a few draugr will awaken from the crypts lining the walls and attack you from behind. Make your way through the crypt and fight all Silver Hand members and draugr. In the large chamber under the bridge, open the chest for the [Dustman's Cairn Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Dustman%27s_Cairn_Key "Skyrim:Dustman's Cairn Key") and unlock the door to the north. A few [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") will attack in the next tunnel. When you reach an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"), head east and fight the residing [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), then head downstream using the small bridges and face the draugr. Follow the linear path through the catacombs and open the iron door.

### A Fragment and a Shout

A [Fire Breath](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Breath "Skyrim:Fire Breath") word wall

The chamber ahead appears quiet at first, but the many sealed alcoves and coffins should hint at what to expect. Loot the many minor containers for treasure, then follow the map marker to the altar where the [Fragment of Wuuthrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fragment_of_Wuuthrad "Skyrim:Fragment of Wuuthrad") rests. Approach the [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") behind the altar to learn one of the words for the [Fire Breath](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Breath "Skyrim:Fire Breath") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"). Finally, pick up the fragment and prepare as numerous draugr burst out of the coffins to attack you and Farkas. Additionally, the iron door will now be locked, preventing any strategic backtracking. After the battle, a path will open from the balcony above, so make your way to a tunnel initially inaccessible in the first zone, which will land you back near the entrance to Skyrim.

### The Initiation

Back in Whiterun, you will find [Vilkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilkas "Skyrim:Vilkas") waiting for you just outside [Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr"). He will then lead you around the building where the entire group of Companions will be gathered. Guild head [Kodlak Whitemane](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak_Whitemane "Skyrim:Kodlak Whitemane") will give a short speech and welcome you to the Companions, while Farkas will swear eternal loyalty to you. You are now an official member of the Companions, but will have to complete yet another radiant quest before your next [major assignment](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Silver_Hand "Skyrim:The Silver Hand"). You will also be able to buy [Skyforge](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge "Skyrim:Skyforge") [Steel weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons") and [Wolf Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf_Armor "Skyrim:Wolf Armor") from [Eorlund Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Eorlund_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Eorlund Gray-Mane") from now on, and he will give you one Skyforge Steel weapon of your choice for free. You can also find Skyforge Steel weapons and Wolf Armor in the [Merchant Chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Merchant_Chests "Skyrim:Containers") underneath the Skyforge from here on out as well.

Eorlund will comment on the Skyforge Steel weapon of your selection. You can choose between five weapon types:

| Weapon Type | Comment |
| --- | --- |
| [Sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge_Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Skyforge Steel Sword") | *"A blade! It will be as sharp as [Fralia](/wiki/Skyrim:Fralia_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Fralia Gray-Mane")'s tongue!"* |
| [Dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge_Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Skyforge Steel Dagger") | *"Ah, the sneaky type, eh? I think we can fix you right up."* |
| [Battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge_Steel_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Skyforge Steel Battleaxe") | *"Just like [Ysgramor](/wiki/Lore:Ysgramor "Lore:Ysgramor") himself."* |
| [Greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge_Steel_Greatsword "Skyrim:Skyforge Steel Greatsword") | *"Sure you can handle that? Ha! Of course you can."* |
| [War Axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge_Steel_War_Axe "Skyrim:Skyforge Steel War Axe") | *"Now that's a smart weapon. Light, strong, useful. Crack some skulls for me."* |

## Notes

- Farkas, like many other [followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers"), is incapable of sneaking properly. He tends to prefer charging into battle over staying in hiding, and getting him to stay in hiding may require you to retreat farther from the enemies than would be necessary if you were alone. However, if he does charge into battle, it is not necessary to follow him. Since he is an [essential](/wiki/Skyrim:Essential_NPCs "Skyrim:Essential NPCs") character, he cannot be killed, and the outcome of the quest is not affected by how much damage he takes, or your behavior. (i.e. as long as you survive, and the objectives are achieved, when you return to Jorrvaskr, he will report that you were "honorable"). Thus, when he charges into battle, you can chose to stay in hiding, and continue making stealth attacks at your own pace. If your stealth is successful, the enemies will act as if Farkas came alone.
- The draugr in the closed tombs lining the walls of the final room can be killed off before picking up the fragment, making the final battle much easier.
- Two of the Silver Hand that attack while you are trapped have a short exchange regarding which Companion they have found:

:   **First Silver Hand:** *"Which one is that?"*
:   **Second Silver Hand:** *"It doesn't matter. He wears that armor, he dies."*

:   This is ironic, since Farkas is the only male member of the Circle who is *not* wearing the [Wolf Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf_Armor "Skyrim:Wolf Armor") of the Companions.

    -  Version 1.2 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") changes his outfit to Wolf Armor.

- If you have already learned the first two words of Fire Breath, the Word Wall may contain a word you already know.
- At one point, it was intended that either Farkas or Aela could accompany you, but this was changed to Farkas only before the game was released (see [this section](/wiki/Skyrim:Aela_the_Huntress#Missing_Dialogue "Skyrim:Aela the Huntress") for details).

## Bugs

- Farkas can be a crippling liability because of his defective class specification. Regardless of level, he has 15 Heavy Armor and 25 Two-Handed, rendering him useless at higher levels.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.
- When Farkas transforms into a werewolf, he drops his [Skyforge Steel Greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge_Steel_Greatsword "Skyrim:Skyforge Steel Greatsword"), and has to use a noticeably weaker iron one instead.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
  - Although you can't trade items with him yet, you can still fix this by simply putting him into command mode (target him and hold Activate until the cursor changes) then targeting the sword or a [Silver Great Sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Greatsword "Skyrim:Silver Greatsword") and pressing Activate again. The Skyforge Sword will do a little more damage against human enemies, but the Silver Sword will do considerably more damage against the swarms of draugr in the word wall room.
  - This transformation also causes him to level up correctly in his class, increasing his health by several hundred points at higher levels: his skills will still be broken, but it does make him capable of surviving a few more hits.
- After pulling the lever and getting trapped behind the gate, the game may freeze or crash at the point when Farkas is supposed to transform into a werewolf and then free you.
  - Reloading an earlier save and entering the location again may work.
  -  Use the [Console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") command `disable`, exit and re-enter the console, the use `enable` to get him unstuck.
  -  Use the [Console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") command `kill`, followed by `resurrect` on Farkas to reset him can also work.
  - Hitting Farkas with Unrelenting Force before triggering the lever may put him in a position where he is able to overcome the freeze.
- While inside the locked alcove trap, Farkas may not help you.
  -  This can be caused due to a Draugr being in Farkas' detect enemy range. After trapping yourself, go into the Console and enter `tai`, next enter `tfc`, exit console mode, follow the tunnel until you encounter the first Draugr, enter Console mode and click on the Draugr, enter `kill 1a693`, either click the Draugr again or double click on any object to clear the reference, enter `tfc`, enter `tai`, leave Console mode. Farkas should now kill the Silver Hand fighter, return to human form, and go throw the release lever.
  -  He may simply return to an earlier part of the dungeon and stay there, not realizing you are trapped. This seems more likely to happen if you have brought another follower with you. Reload an earlier save, return to the switch-trap alcove, and just outside of it do `prid 1a693` then `moveto player` in the Console, then go flip the switch while he's still within visual range. He may nevertheless take some time to notice you are trapped (perhaps a minute) and trigger the werewolf scene. This tip and the above one can be combined (in reverse order), to first return him to the right area, then to trigger the werewolf scene if he just stands around or leaves again.
  - Alternatively, restart outside Dustman's Cairn, leave any other followers outside, enter with Farkas, and ensure you kill all Draugr on your way to the switch-trap alcove (many are slumbering in their wall niches) and try again. Make sure Farkas is in the room with this alcove before you throw the trap switch.
  -  Another option is to use `tcl` in the Console (click first until you are highlighting nothing in the Console at all, or the command won't work) to escape the trap, and just go do the rest of the dungeon by yourself. You'll need to fight your way through a number of Silver Hand, but the undead at the end can simply be run away from, if you get your Fire Breath shout off the wall, and the fragment of Wuuthrad. It is the taking of the latter that triggers the fight, so you can explore and plunder the area and discover the exit tunnel before taking that item (doing so is also what locks the original entranceway).
- Farkas may not stand up from a crouching position, even if you do. This only appears to happen after Farkas transforms into a werewolf.
- Or he may remain in werewolf form, emitting werewolf breathing sounds, but return to talking as a human. This will fix itself after a cell transition, e.g. to the inner crypt or back out again. **?**
- There is a chance the leveled enemies in Dustman's Cairn will not generate at your current level. At low levels you may fight regular and Restless Draugr throughout most of the dungeon, but may unexpectedly be swarmed by Draugr Scourges and Deathlords in the word wall room, easily overwhelming you and Farkas.
- Farkas may disappear if you visit some locations, like the Whiterun Hall of the Dead, while this quest is active. **?**
  -  Use the Console to bring Farkas to you. Enter `prid 1A693` and then `moveto player`. Farkas will reappear and resume normal scripting. If you were heading to Dustman's Cairn, be sure to do this while you are still outside. If you cleared Dustman's and were returning to Jorrvaskr, be sure to do it before following Vilkas to the gathered Circle. You will see Farkas actually run to his correct spot.
- When returning to Whiterun and taking part in the ceremony inducting you into the Companions, the other participants in the ceremony may stop talking, causing the quest to not complete.
  - Talk to Vilkas upon your return to Jorrvaskr and have him lead you to the induction ceremony. The stop dialogue issue seems to happen when you start the ceremony without him.(If Vilkas won't move sprint into him to push him closer to the left side of Jorrvaskr)
  - Using the [Wait](/wiki/Skyrim:Controls#General_Gameplay "Skyrim:Controls") command for one hour after the dialogue stops unfreezes the companions and completes the quest.
  - Commit a minor crime in front of a guard, such as punching an NPC, before the ceremony begins. Afterwards, a guard will confront you about your crime, allowing you to leave by being taken to jail. Once you serve your jail time or escape, return to Jorrvaskr and talk to Kodlak to complete the quest.
- When returning to Whiterun and taking part in the ceremony inducting you into the Companions, some of the other participants in the ceremony may not be in place and therefore the cutscene will not activate.
  -  Stand in the general area of the gathering (the sparring area) and use the Console to bring the missing NPCs to you (Vilkas should be summoned last because he actually starts the cutscene). First use `prid <RefID>` then `moveto player`. The RefIDs for the Companions are: Farkas (`0001A693`), Skjor (`0001A691`), Aela (`0001A697`), Kodlak (`0001A68F`), Vilkas (`0001A695`).
- The game might get stuck after you follow Vilkas to the meeting.
  - Attempting to Wait during the dialogue may allow it to complete.
- When returning to Whiterun and taking part in the ceremony inducting you into the Companions, if you have [Automove](/wiki/Skyrim:Controls "Skyrim:Controls") active when the cutscene starts, you may continue to move during the cutscene. **?**
- Vilkas may not appear in front of Jorrvaskr and the game won't give you the objective Follow Vilkas. You don't need to activate this objective to finish the quest.
  - To fix this, go into Jorrvaskr and talk to him and he will give you the objective.
- When returning to Jorrvaskr Vilkas does not appear outside, he is inside doing his usual daily routine. Instead, the quest marker points to Skjor. After turning in the shards, the quest ends and the companions questline simply stops. The quest log has the miscelaneous quest "Talk to the companions leaders for work", but they never offer work, and the "Proving Honor" quest is marked as completed and grayed out, despite that the last objective (return to Jorrvaskr) is left incomplete, and the Companions questline simply ends at that point, with no possibility of continuing on without console commands to initiate the next quest in the series. Also, there is no free weapon given by Eorlund, he will not sell Skyforge Steel, and will not train in Smithing.
  - Try entering Whiterun through the main gate instead. This may trigger the Vilkas event.
  - While outside Whiterun, enter the console command 'SetStage C02 1' to trigger the initiation event when you next enter the city and approach Jorrvaskr. (You may not be offered a Skysteel Weapon as usual, but will be able to continue the questline after you complete an additional Radiant quest.)
- If you tell Farkas to meet you at Dustman's Cairn, then proceed to enter the crypt without talking to him first, he will not follow you. If you proceed to pull the lever trap, you will get stuck.

## Quest Stages

| Proving Honor (C01) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | The Companions leaders say they don't have any more work for me, but that I should speak to Skjor about "the next steps." *Objective 10:* Speak to Skjor |
| 20 |  | The Companions have given me one final challenge before inducting me. I'm to retrieve a fragment of Wuuthrad, the Blade of Ysgramor, from <Alias=Dungeon> while Farkas judges my valor. *Objective 20:* Speak to Farkas |
| 30 |  | *Objective 30:* Retrieve the fragment |
| 40 |  | *Objective 40:* Return to Jorrvaskr |
| 200 | ☑ | I successfully retrieved a fragment of Wuuthrad, the Blade of Ysgramor, to earn my place in the Companions. |
| *Unknown* |  | *Objective 110:* Follow Vilkas |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 1.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage C01 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest C01`.

# Skyrim:Pumping Station

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Dwarven Ruin: Pumping Station | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | No |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 18 |
| Occupants | |
| [Falmer Servants](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Servant "Skyrim:Falmer Servant") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| BlackreachZcell04 | |
| Region | |
| [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach") | |
| Location | |
| Northeastern part of Blackreach's city | |

Pumping Station

**Pumping Station** is a small [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") in [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach") occupied by [Falmer servants](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Servant "Skyrim:Falmer Servant"). It is part of the Dwemer city in the western part of Blackreach. There are no usable entrances to this building directly from the grounds of the city, as the main entrance has been blocked by a cave-in both inside and out; entry must therefore be made through either the [Silent City Catacombs](/wiki/Skyrim:Silent_City_Catacombs "Skyrim:Silent City Catacombs") or the [Debate Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Debate_Hall "Skyrim:Debate Hall").

## Pumping Station

The interior, viewed from the door to the Debate Hall

Upon entering from the [Silent City Catacombs](/wiki/Skyrim:Silent_City_Catacombs "Skyrim:Silent City Catacombs"), you emerge in the western part of the zone, at the bottom of a flight of stairs heading up to the east. At the top of the stairs is a closed gate to the south. A [Falmer servant](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Servant "Skyrim:Falmer Servant") may come to investigate any noise. Through the gate, you enter a large, partially demolished room containing a second Falmer servant. To the south, a cave-in blocks the exit to the grounds of the city. A flight of stairs in the northeast corner of the room leads up to a raised walkway that runs along the east side of the room, with doors to the north and south. There is a matching raised walkway along the west side of the room, above where you enter, but no stairs lead up to the western walkway; the only easy access to that walkway is via the exterior balcony to the north.

Through the door to the north of the eastern walkway is a small exterior semicircular balcony that leads to the door opening to the western walkway. At the southern end of the western walkway is a closed metal gate opening to an alcove containing an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), with a [Dwemer cog](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Cog "Skyrim:Dwemer Cog") leaning up against it. The southern door on the eastern walkway exits to an exterior bridge leading to the [Debate Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Debate_Hall "Skyrim:Debate Hall").

## Maps

- 

  Pumping Station

# Skyrim:Purewater Run

Purewater Run

**Purewater Run** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") south-southeast of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") containing [slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Slaughterfish").

## Related Quests

- **[Interception](/wiki/Skyrim:Interception "Skyrim:Interception")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard_Elite_Armaments "Skyrim:Redguard Elite Armaments"): Aid the Hammerfell resistance.

## Walkthrough

The first area

The submerged Dwarven head and two Dwarven chests

Through the entrance, the cave is full of shallow water populated by several ingredient fish, including [abecean longfin](/wiki/Skyrim:Abecean_Longfin "Skyrim:Abecean Longfin"), [silverside perch](/wiki/Skyrim:Silverside_Perch "Skyrim:Silverside Perch"), and [histcarp](/wiki/Skyrim:Histcarp "Skyrim:Histcarp"). Straight ahead of the entrance are two large [Nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot") plants and a [quicksilver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore Vein").

With the [Redguard Elite Armaments](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard_Elite_Armaments "Skyrim:Redguard Elite Armaments") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, during the quest [Interception](/wiki/Skyrim:Interception "Skyrim:Interception"), [Fijeh](/wiki/Skyrim:Fijeh "Skyrim:Fijeh") and later [Rakeed](/wiki/Skyrim:Rakeed "Skyrim:Rakeed") and a locked chest that can only be opened with the [Remnant Supply Chest key](/wiki/Skyrim:Remnant_Supply_Chest_Key "Skyrim:Remnant Supply Chest Key") will be found here. The chest contains [Remnant Agent Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Remnant_Agent_Armor "Skyrim:Remnant Agent Armor"), [Remnant Agent Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Remnant_Agent_Boots "Skyrim:Remnant Agent Boots"), [Remnant Agent Gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Remnant_Agent_Gloves "Skyrim:Remnant Agent Gloves"), [Remnant Agent Hood](/wiki/Skyrim:Remnant_Agent_Hood "Skyrim:Remnant Agent Hood"), [Remnant Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Remnant_Shield "Skyrim:Remnant Shield"), two [Remnant Scimitars of Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Remnant_Scimitar_of_Fire "Skyrim:Remnant Scimitar of Fire"), two [Potions of Extended Invisibility](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Extended_Invisibility "Skyrim:Potion of Extended Invisibility"), and *[The Ebon Arm](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ebon_Arm "Skyrim:The Ebon Arm")*.

To the east is a deep pool partially hidden by a waterfall. It contains two unlocked Dwarven chests near a large Dwarven head, several [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(creature) "Skyrim:Salmon (creature)"), two slaughterfish, and seven patches of [slaughterfish eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Egg "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Egg") in and around the chests, over the Dwarven head, and on the walls. A second waterfall cascades down the cave wall between the deep pool and ore vein. A copy of the [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Cherim's Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Cherim%27s_Heart "Skyrim:Cherim's Heart")* can be found inside one of the underwater chests. There is a small air pocket directly above the chests.

Getting out of the pool is tricky; you must jump at just the right spot. It is advised to have any followers wait outside so that they don't get in your way.

## Notes

- Outside the cave, following the waterfalls north to the point just before the stream merges with another larger stream, you will find a lootable skeleton on a ledge under a tree with a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and a leveled [warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Warhammer "Skyrim:Warhammer") nearby. To the east, an unlocked chest is on the south bank a short distance downstream from the skeleton.

## Bugs

- Followers may get stuck at the entrance to the dungeon due to a disconnected navmesh.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.10, fixes this bug.
- Followers may get stuck in the pool with the Dwarven head.
  - The easiest way to avoid this is to ask them to wait outside, although even if they become stuck in the pool, they will normally rejoin you when you leave the cave.
- The main water plane is filled with holes, allowing you to slip through at the borders.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, fixes this bug.
- One of the patches of slaughterfish eggs on the Dwarven head can't be interacted with.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.3, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Purity of Revenge

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Companions.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Companions.png) | **Retrieve the Fragments of Wuuthrad and wipe out the [Silver Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Hand "Skyrim:Silver Hand").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Vilkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilkas "Skyrim:Vilkas") |
| Location(s): | [Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr"), [Driftshade Refuge](/wiki/Skyrim:Driftshade_Refuge "Skyrim:Driftshade Refuge") |
| Reward: | None |
| ID: | C05 |
| Suggested Level: | 6 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Blood's Honor](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood%27s_Honor "Skyrim:Blood's Honor") | **Next →** [Glory of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Glory_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:Glory of the Dead") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Blood's Honor](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood%27s_Honor "Skyrim:Blood's Honor") | | → Next | [Glory of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Glory_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:Glory of the Dead") | | |

[Farkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Farkas "Skyrim:Farkas") and [Njada](/wiki/Skyrim:Njada_Stonearm "Skyrim:Njada Stonearm") with [Kodlak](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak_Whitemane "Skyrim:Kodlak Whitemane")'s body

## Quick Walkthrough

1. With [Vilkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilkas "Skyrim:Vilkas") as a shield brother, infiltrate the [Silver Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Hand "Skyrim:Silver Hand")'s refuge.
2. Retrieve the [Fragments of Wuuthrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fragments_of_Wuuthrad "Skyrim:Fragments of Wuuthrad").
3. (Optional) Wipe out the [Silver Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Hand "Skyrim:Silver Hand").
4. Return to [Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr").

### Revenge Served Cold

After the death of [Kodlak Whitemane](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak_Whitemane "Skyrim:Kodlak Whitemane"), [Vilkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilkas "Skyrim:Vilkas") is looking for revenge. He wants to go after the [Silver Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Hand "Skyrim:Silver Hand") for the attack on Jorrvaskr and the further affront of stealing the [fragments of Wuuthrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fragments_of_Wuuthrad "Skyrim:Fragments of Wuuthrad"). With no questions asked, Vilkas will then act as your follower all the way to the Silver Hand hideout at [Driftshade Refuge](/wiki/Skyrim:Driftshade_Refuge "Skyrim:Driftshade Refuge"), a small fort southeast of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"). Upon arrival at the fort, dispose of the two Silver Hand members outside, a guard at the entrance and an archer on the roof, then head inside. Vilkas will equip the helmet of his [Wolf Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf_Armor "Skyrim:Wolf Armor") for the duration of the assault.

### Den of the Silver Hand

Not surprisingly, Driftshade Refuge is crawling with hostile Silver Hand members, so take advantage of your follower and kill the opposition one by one. In the two-leveled room with many boxes on the floor, make sure to search for *[An Explorer's Guide to Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:An_Explorer%27s_Guide_to_Skyrim "Skyrim:An Explorer's Guide to Skyrim")* which will add a few map markers for later exploration. It is located on a bookshelf beneath an elk head mounted on the wall. The tunnel north of the room contains a locked door, so unlock it and wipe out yet another Silver Hand. In the next room, a set of spears blocks the entrance but the corresponding lever is easily located right next to the spears. Proceed forward and enter Driftshade Cellar.

After the first turn, make sure to loot the hidden treasure chest, then follow the path and make use of the [Spike Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Spike_Wall "Skyrim:Spike Wall") trap to dispose of yet another enemy. Ignore the locked cell with the dead [werewolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Werewolves "Skyrim:Werewolves"), activate the trap again and run to the area behind it for another treasure chest. Hit the pullbar on the wall to get back out, and head forward to another room with two enemies and, hidden on a shelf, the [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") skill book *[The Rear Guard](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rear_Guard "Skyrim:The Rear Guard")*. The cellar now turns into a snowy cave, and the next room is in two levels, with a Silver Hand sniper on the ledge above. Kill him and examine the cages, one of them holds a living werewolf, who will attack you if you pick the lock, the other one contains a dead [horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses "Skyrim:Horses").

The Fragments of Wuuthrad

### The Fragments of Wuuthrad

After passing through a torture chamber, the next large chamber contains more enemies, an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"), a coin purse, and two potions on a bookshelf behind the fireplace. Take the only available path, leading back to an initially inaccessible part of Driftshade Refuge. The first chamber contains the three remaining members of the Silver Hand, the [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") skill book *[2920, Morning Star, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Morning_Star,_v1 "Skyrim:2920, Morning Star, v1")*, the [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block") skill book *[Warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Warrior_(book) "Skyrim:Warrior (book)")*, a treasure chest with considerable loot and finally, the stolen Fragments of [Wuuthrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Wuuthrad "Skyrim:Wuuthrad"). Use the door to the south for an easy escape route, then return to [Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr"). As soon as you arrive, [Vilkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilkas "Skyrim:Vilkas") will inform you that you should meet up at the Skyforge and pay your respects to the deceased, but now avenged, [Whitemane](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak_Whitemane "Skyrim:Kodlak Whitemane"). This will end the quest and start the next one, [Glory of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Glory_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:Glory of the Dead").

## Notes

- If you have a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Follower "Skyrim:Follower") with you, Vilkas will replace that follower during this quest. Be sure to give any important equipment to your follower before entering Jorrvaskr, as Vilkas won't help if you're overencumbered, and you won't be able to trade things with him yet.
- Kodlak's body cannot be interacted with or searched, as the quest script makes it uninteractable. You can, however, pick up a [steel warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Warhammer "Skyrim:Steel Warhammer") found next to it.
- Vilkas tells you that no one else got hurt in the Jorrvaskr assault if you ask him if anyone else was injured. However, this is clearly incorrect, as [Athis](/wiki/Skyrim:Athis "Skyrim:Athis") is wounded, and [Ria](/wiki/Skyrim:Ria "Skyrim:Ria") is tending to him.
- Don't bother transforming into a werewolf during this mission--thanks to a [bug](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilkas#Bugs "Skyrim:Vilkas"), Vilkas will become hostile towards the player upon witnessing them as a werewolf.
- When clearing out Driftshade Refuge, unlike [Farkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Farkas "Skyrim:Farkas") during "[Proving Honor](/wiki/Skyrim:Proving_Honor "Skyrim:Proving Honor")" and [Aela the Huntress](/wiki/Skyrim:Aela_the_Huntress "Skyrim:Aela the Huntress") during "[The Silver Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Silver_Hand "Skyrim:The Silver Hand")", Vilkas will make no comments whatsoever, except for his standard combat dialogue. You can, however, still ask him for training in [two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") weapons.
- Version 2.1.0 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") reserves Driftshade Refuge to block radiant quests until this one is finished. After that point it should switch over to regular bandits and then become available for use in standard radiant questing.

## Bugs

- The shortcut to zoom in on the map point will not work for this quest for some people. The map point is nevertheless visible at the location specified in this article.
- If Driftshade Refuge has already been cleared, this quest cannot be started normally without a workaround. Before you begin Blood's Honor, wait 30 in-game days after you have cleared Driftshade Refuge to allow that dungeon to reset (you will have to revert to a slightly earlier save to do this). This should allow Purity of Revenge to begin normally upon completion of Blood's Honor. An easy way to check if the dungeon has been reset is to check the doors--if they have all been shut, it is reset (e.g., if the formerly barred door is barred again).
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.0, fixes this bug.
  -  The console may aid in fixing this. Click on Vilkas and use the `disable` and then `enable` commands, then use `setstage c05 0` and talk to him.
  -  Another method that has worked is to reset the interior of Driftshade Refuge by typing `ResetInterior DriftshadeSanctuary01` into the console. Then go and visit Driftshade Refuge and confirm that it is reset. It should be populated with Silver Hand fighters. Do this before talking to Vilkas, and when you do speak to him the next quest may start.
- Kodlak's corpse in Jorrvaskr causes him to appear without his Wolf Armor equipped.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.
- The Silver Hand radiant quests are available until the last stages of Purity of Revenge, in particular if you return to Whiterun before Vilkas and speak to Aela the Huntress to get a radiant quest. Note that you can't exploit this to get a third Silver Hand radiant quest, since Aela will offer such quests only if you previously completed just one radiant quest from the Silver Hand pool.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, addresses this issue. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=12948)) Those quests are no longer available once this one begins.
- Fast traveling to [Fort Fellhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Fellhammer "Skyrim:Fort Fellhammer") during this quest may automatically complete the optional objective to wipe out the Silver Hand members at Driftshade Refuge, though they may not actually be dead when you arrive.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, addresses this issue. The bandits at Fort Fellhammer all had a script attached to them when they never needed one.
- If Blood's Honor has already been completed and this quest won't begin because the [Helm of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Jarl_-_Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Jarl - Caves)") miscellaneous quest is active, it is possible to proceed through Driftshade Refuge without killing anyone (use stealth, fear or invisibility as needed) and take the Helm of Winterhold from the chest at the end. Once the Helm is returned to the Jarl of Winterhold to complete that quest, return to [Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr") and Purity of Revenge will begin. **?**
  -  A possibility to start this quest is by completing the Helm of Winterhold quest by typing `setstage favor158 20` into the console before talking with Vilkas.
  - Should the "Retrieve the Helm of Winterhold" quest pose a repetition problem, simply go to the Jarl Korir, take the quest one more time and enter `setstage favor158 20` on the console. This quest shouldn't be a problem anymore. On the console, proceed by tapping `ResetInterior DriftshadeSanctuary01`. Then return to Vilkas and on the console, enter `setstage c05 0`.
- Even after wiping out the Silver Hand, you may not be able to wait (i.e., to end your run as a werewolf) getting the message there are still enemies nearby. **?**
- If Blood's Honor has already been completed and this quest won't begin, and you've tried all other possible solutions, the quest may be skipped entirely to avoid any bugs. Load a game right after accepting Blood's Honor from Kodlak, and while standing in any interior cell, type `setstage c04 200`, then `setstage c05 200`, and finally `setstage c06 00` to start the next quest and attend the funeral bug-free. **?**

## Quest Stages

| Purity of Revenge (C05) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | Vilkas has come with me to avenge the death of Kodlak by wiping out the Silver Hand. *Objective 10:* Retrieve the fragments of Wuuthrad  *Objective 11:* (Optional) Wipe out the Silver Hand |
| 20 |  | Vilkas and I avenged Kodlak's death by bringing ruin to the Silver Hand. *Objective 20:* Return to Jorrvaskr |
| 200 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 1.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage C05 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest C05`.
