The [wolf spirit](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf_Spirit "Skyrim:Wolf Spirit") appears when the Flame is activated

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Farkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Farkas "Skyrim:Farkas") or [Vilkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilkas "Skyrim:Vilkas") about work for the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions").
2. Agree to help them purify themselves.
3. Collect a [Glenmoril witch head](/wiki/Skyrim:Glenmoril_Witch_Head "Skyrim:Glenmoril Witch Head") and travel to [Ysgramor's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysgramor%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Ysgramor's Tomb").
4. Fight the [wolf spirit](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf_Spirit "Skyrim:Wolf Spirit") of [Farkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Farkas%27s_Wolf_Spirit "Skyrim:Farkas's Wolf Spirit") or [Vilkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilkas%27s_Wolf_Spirit "Skyrim:Vilkas's Wolf Spirit").

### A Melancholy Companion

When you speak to either Farkas or Vilkas about work, the response may be a bit out of the ordinary. Each has something weighing on them, a personal matter. Play the good therapist here and ask what the trouble is. They will reveal that they have been pondering [Kodlak's](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak_Whitemane "Skyrim:Kodlak Whitemane") choice in the [Glory of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Glory_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:Glory of the Dead") quest and want to follow suit: to be cured of [lycanthropy](/wiki/Skyrim:Werewolf "Skyrim:Werewolf").

### The Right Ingredients

If you have a Glenmoril witch head in your inventory from your previous adventures in the [Blood's Honor](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood%27s_Honor "Skyrim:Blood's Honor") quest, the brother will urge you on to Ysgramor's Tomb. If you do not have one, the Companion is eager to procure one. Travel to [Glenmoril Coven](/wiki/Skyrim:Glenmoril_Coven "Skyrim:Glenmoril Coven") to take a head. There are five [Glenmoril witches](/wiki/Skyrim:Glenmoril_Witch "Skyrim:Glenmoril Witch") laid up in the coven. Depending on how many heads you gathered in the previous visit to the coven, harvest what you need. If you did not [cure yourself of lycanthropy](/wiki/Skyrim:Lycanthropy#Curing_Lycanthropy "Skyrim:Lycanthropy") in the previous quest and wish to be rid of it now, harvest a head for yourself as well. However, you will need to finish the quest by curing the active follower, before you can cure yourself.

### The Ritual

When you have one of the heads, return to Ysgramor's tomb. As you did for Kodlak in [Glory of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Glory_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:Glory of the Dead"), activate the Flame of the Harbinger by tossing in the head. This will release the wolf spirit of the brother wanting to be cured. You must destroy the wolf spirit in order for him to be purged of his wolfish ways.

When the spirit is destroyed, Vilkas or Farkas will describe a soothing sensation and a clear mind and thank you for your help with a leveled amount of gold.

### Reward

| Levels[†](#intnote_LevelNote) | Reward[‡](#intnote_RewardBug) | USLEEP Reward |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 100 | 100 |
| 10–19 | 150 | 150 |
| 20–29 | 300 | 200 |
| 30–39 | 300 | 250 |
| 40+ | 300 | 300 |

[†](#note_LevelNote)Level is based on when the player completed the previous quest (or level one for the first quest), not the player's level when receiving the quest or its reward.

[‡](#note_RewardBug)The reward amounts for radiant Companions quests do not progress as intended.

-  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.3, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=20007))

## Bugs

- On agreeing to rid Vilkas of his lycanthropy, he will follow you out of Jorrvaskr. The quest marker will appear on Ysgramor's Tomb but disappear after a few seconds. Vilkas will stop following you but the game will act as though he still is, which results in your not being able to take another follower or complete the quest.
  - Have two witch's heads in your inventory and save the game before you hand over each Companion mission. When you ask for a new job and Vilkas asks you to cure him, reload your last save and ask Vilkas to join you. Inside Ysgramor's Tomb, part ways with Vilkas and then speak to him again to tell him you've finished the last mission. Ask him for more work and accept to cure his lycanthropy. He will then follow you to the font where you can throw in the witch's head and fight his wolf spirit. The game then asks you to talk to Vilkas, but you cannot. You can, however, purify yourself once this has happened by throwing another witch's head into the font and fighting your own wolf spirit. Be aware that the game still thinks Vilkas is a follower, so you will be unable to have a genuine follower once you have done this.
  - If you lead/take Vilkas back to Jorrvaskr and go inside you can get rid of above issue with him as a permanent follower and take on another follower as normal.
  - Speak to Vilkas first. If he does not immediately asked to be cured, take his radiant quest then speak to him with the witch's head in your inventory. He should then ask - however you should not take it. Refuse him, and instead check to see if Farkas is offering any work. If Farkas is now offering work but only a random/radiant quest, take it and then speak to him again (once completed) with the head in your inventory. He should now ask you to help him rid his lycanthropy. Help him (Farkas) first, and then go back and help Vilkas with his personal request.
    - If Farkas still will not offer any work, purity quest nor radiant quest, go and speak with Aela and do a quest for her. This will unlock Farkas' quests.
  - Alternatively, wait until Vilkas offers the cue dialogue of "Is there any work to be done?", but immediately close the dialogue box. Fast-travel to anywhere, then come back. Farkas should now offer the cue dialogue, and you can perform the quest with him. Repeat with Vilkas.
  - Do the purity quest with Farkas first. After this is done, when you return to Vilkas, do a regular quest and then pick the purity quest again. Vilkas will now follow you without a glitch.
  -  Take Vilkas to Ysgramor's Tomb as described, split ways, report the success of the last errand, and agree to help Vilkas with his wolf spirit. Instead of activating the Flame Of The Harbinger, enter quest stage 100 by using the console command `setstage CR13 100`. Vilkas is now cured. Repeat with Farkas, but this time, activate the Flame.
  - Complete a couple of random requests from Farkas and Aela, then get the [Dragon Seekers](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Seekers "Skyrim:Dragon Seekers") quest from Vilkas. Slay the dragon with Farkas and this will resolve the follower issue.
  - To fix the bug, talk to Vilkas to get a regular quest. Complete the regular "looking for work" quest, then go speak to Farkas. He should now ask for help curing his lycanthropy. You should now be able to complete the quest normally.
  - To fix the bug alternatively, If you have the Dawnguard add-on, then complete a basic task for Vilkas and then talk to Aela. Complete tasks for her until she gives you a quest to find one of three Werewolf Totems. Aela will then accompany you on the quest for them, replacing your "invisible follower". This then allows you to complete the "Purity" quest for Farkas first, then Vilkas.
- Activating the blue fire during this quest for Farkas and Vilkas may not remove a Glenmoril Witch Head from your inventory when it did for [Kodlak](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak_Whitemane "Skyrim:Kodlak Whitemane")'s spirit during [Glory of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Glory_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:Glory of the Dead").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.

| 15 |  | <Alias=Questgiver> wants to be cured of lycanthropy, and has asked me to help him. We must take a Glenmoril Witch's head to the Tomb of Ysgramor to perform the same ceremony which cured Kodlak. *Objective 15:* Cleanse <Alias=Questgiver> of beastblood |
| 17 |  | *Objective 17:* Kill <Alias=Questgiver>'s wolf spirit |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Talk to <Alias=Questgiver> |
| 100 | ☑ | I helped <Alias=Questgiver> cure himself of lycanthropy. |
| 200 | ☑ |  |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage CR13 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest CR13`.

# Skyrim:Put A Fork In It

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Pass [Sheogorath](/wiki/Skyrim:Sheogorath "Skyrim:Sheogorath")'s trial to earn his staff.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | *[Mysterious Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Mysterious_Note_(Staff_of_Sheogorath) "Skyrim:Mysterious Note (Staff of Sheogorath)")* in [The Retching Netch](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Retching_Netch "Skyrim:The Retching Netch") |
| Location(s): | [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim"), [The Retching Netch](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Retching_Netch "Skyrim:The Retching Netch"), [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(tower) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (tower)") |
| Reward: | [Staff of Sheogorath](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Sheogorath_(item) "Skyrim:Staff of Sheogorath (item)") |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE019\_StaffOfSheogorathQuest |
| Added by: | [Staff of Sheogorath](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Sheogorath "Skyrim:Staff of Sheogorath") |
| --- | |
| |  | | --- | | **Prerequisites:** Access to a [Staff Enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_Enchanter "Skyrim:Staff Enchanter") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | Prerequisites: | Access to a [Staff Enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_Enchanter "Skyrim:Staff Enchanter") | | |

Hunt netches with a kitchen utensil

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Travel to [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") and enter [The Retching Netch](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Retching_Netch "Skyrim:The Retching Netch").
2. Read the [mysterious note](/wiki/Skyrim:Mysterious_Note_(Staff_of_Sheogorath) "Skyrim:Mysterious Note (Staff of Sheogorath)") and take the [Fork of Horripilation](/wiki/Skyrim:Fork_of_Horripilation "Skyrim:Fork of Horripilation").
3. Kill the two specified [bull netches](/wiki/Skyrim:Bull_Netch "Skyrim:Bull Netch") using the fork and loot the artifacts from their bodies.
4. Craft the [Staff of Sheogorath](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Sheogorath_(item) "Skyrim:Staff of Sheogorath (item)") using a [Staff Enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_Enchanter "Skyrim:Staff Enchanter").

### Something Waiting for You

The mysterious message from Sheogorath

A [mysterious note](/wiki/Skyrim:Mysterious_Note_(Staff_of_Sheogorath) "Skyrim:Mysterious Note (Staff of Sheogorath)") can be found pinned to a keg on the ground floor of [The Retching Netch](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Retching_Netch "Skyrim:The Retching Netch") cornerclub in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock"), along with the [Fork of Horripilation](/wiki/Skyrim:Fork_of_Horripilation "Skyrim:Fork of Horripilation"). The items will be hard to miss, as they are surrounded by a green glow before you approach.

The note outlines a proposed combat challenge from [Sheogorath](/wiki/Skyrim:Sheogorath "Skyrim:Sheogorath"), the Daedric Prince of Madness. You are instructed to use the fork to kill two specific [bull netches](/wiki/Skyrim:Bull_Netch "Skyrim:Bull Netch") on Solstheim, and recover two "familiar" artifacts from their bodies. Specifically, you will need to recover the [Branch of the Tree of Shades](/wiki/Skyrim:Branch_of_the_Tree_of_Shades "Skyrim:Branch of the Tree of Shades") and [Ciirta's Eye](/wiki/Skyrim:Ciirta%27s_Eye "Skyrim:Ciirta's Eye"), two items which originally appeared in the [Symbols of Office](/wiki/Shivering:Symbols_of_Office "Shivering:Symbols of Office") quest in *[Shivering Isles](/wiki/Shivering:Shivering_Isles "Shivering:Shivering Isles")*.

### Netch Hunt

You must take the fork in order to accept Sheogorath's combat trial. Note that while the fork is literally a kitchen utensil and has very low damage, it is neither [generic cutlery](/wiki/Skyrim:Fork_(item) "Skyrim:Fork (item)"), which is not a weapon, nor the harder to find [fork *weapon*](/wiki/Skyrim:Fork_(weapon) "Skyrim:Fork (weapon)"), which is weapon type "other" - it actually has the [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") weapon type, allowing your skills and perks to interact with it normally (e.g. it will make no noise when sneak attacking), although both fork weapons do the same base damage of 1. It also weighs *12 times* as much as a normal fork, equivalent to the weight of a [Daedric Dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Dagger "Skyrim:Daedric Dagger"). It has a special enchantment that allows you to deal damage to the Bull Netches while holding the fork, which are otherwise immune to damage.

The first bull netch is located close by on the [Isle of Basalt](/wiki/Skyrim:Isle_of_Basalt "Skyrim:Isle of Basalt"), a small volcanic island directly west of the [Earth Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Earth_Stone "Skyrim:Earth Stone"). Kill the beast as instructed and claim Ciirta's Eye from its corpse. The second netch can be found due west of [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village"), next to an icy waterfall. It will drop the Branch of the Tree of Shades when killed. Once you have obtained both artifacts, you will need to use them to craft your true reward: the [Staff of Sheogorath](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Sheogorath_(item) "Skyrim:Staff of Sheogorath (item)").

### Staff Crafting

In addition to the two items obtained from the netches, crafting the Staff of Sheogorath will require two [Heart Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_Stone "Skyrim:Heart Stone") and access to a [Staff Enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_Enchanter "Skyrim:Staff Enchanter"). Heart Stones are readily available on Solstheim, and can be [mined](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") from [deposits](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_Stone_Deposit "Skyrim:Heart Stone Deposit") all over the island. In order to use the Staff Enchanter in [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(tower) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (tower)"), the player must complete the quest [Reluctant Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Reluctant_Steward "Skyrim:Reluctant Steward") for [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth"). However, any staff enchanter will do, such as the one added by the [Myrwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Myrwatch "Skyrim:Myrwatch") or [Bloodchill Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodchill_Manor "Skyrim:Bloodchill Manor") Creations.

Once you have obtained the necessary crafting ingredients and access to the Staff Enchanter, you can craft the Staff of Sheogorath to complete the quest. The staff has a powerful area of effect [paralysis](/wiki/Skyrim:Paralysis "Skyrim:Paralysis") enchantment.

## Notes

- With the [Saints & Seducers](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers") Creation installed, the Isle of Basalt where you find one of the netches is also home to several [Bliss Bugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Bliss_Bug "Skyrim:Bliss Bug") as well as a [Monarch Butterfly](/wiki/Skyrim:Monarch_Butterfly "Skyrim:Monarch Butterfly") and [Green Butterfly](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Butterfly "Skyrim:Green Butterfly"). These appear regardless of whether or not you have the Staff of Sheogorath Creation installed.
- At release, you would receive this quest upon installing the [Staff of Sheogorath](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Sheogorath "Skyrim:Staff of Sheogorath") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") and be instructed to travel to [Solstheim](/wiki/Dragonborn:Solstheim "Dragonborn:Solstheim"). Upon arriving on the island, you would then be directed to the cornerclub. This was changed by the [Anniversary Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Anniversary_Edition "Skyrim:Anniversary Edition") update.
- The recommended Staff Enchanter to use for this is the one at Myrwatch due to this also requiring two Heart Stones (that are readily available near the enchanter there.) The other staff enchanters are the one at Tel Mithryn (which first requires completion of the side quest "Reluctant Steward") and the one at Bloodchill Manor.

## Quest Stages

| Put A Fork In It () | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | There's something waiting for me on the island of Solstheim. I should travel there and investigate. *Objective :* Travel to Solstheim |
| 20 |  | There's something waiting for me in Raven Rock, I should see what it is. *Objective :* Investigate the Retching Netch  *Objective :* Take the Fork of Horripilation |
| 30 |  | I've accepted Sheogorath's combat trial. I'll need to find these special Bull Netches, kill them with the Fork of Horripilation, and obtain the artifacts. *Objective :* Obtain the Eye of Ciirta  *Objective :* Obtain the Branch of the Tree of Shades |
| 40 |  | I've killed the Bull Netches and obtained the artifacts. I need to gain access to a Staff Enchanter and combine them to create The Staff of Sheogorath. *Objective :* Craft the Staff of Sheogorath |
| 50 | ☑ | I have completed the trial, and crafted the Staff of Sheogorath. |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage quest stage`, where `quest` is the internal name of the quest, and `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest quest`, where `quest` is the internal name of the quest.

| [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") | [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), Wind District | [Lucia](/wiki/Skyrim:Lucia "Skyrim:Lucia") [HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") |

[†](#note_Dervenin)Dervenin will no longer be available for this quest once [The Mind of Madness](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mind_of_Madness "Skyrim:The Mind of Madness") is finished.

## Walkthrough

If you talk to one of the quest givers, they will ask you for some gold. Giving them one gold piece completes the quest and rewards you with the blessing [The Gift of Charity](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gift_of_Charity "Skyrim:The Gift of Charity").

## Notes

- This quest does not have any stages or objectives.
- This quest can be repeated indefinitely.
- You will not have the option to give a beggar gold for four in-game hours after you last gave a beggar gold, or if you have no gold.
- Because this is a favor quest which affects the quest giver's disposition, it will count toward the "Help the People" part of the [thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane") quest for the quest giver's hold.

# Skyrim:Quest all Drunks Have

## Overview

## Radiant Options

This is a radiant quest which you can receive from any of the following people.

| Region | QuestGiverHome | QuestGiver |
| --- | --- | --- |
| [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"), [House of Clan Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:House of Clan Shatter-Shield") | [Torbjorn Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Torbjorn_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:Torbjorn Shatter-Shield") |
| [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") | [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy") | [Razelan](/wiki/Skyrim:Razelan "Skyrim:Razelan") |
| [The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") | [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"), [Iron-Breaker Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron-Breaker_Mine "Skyrim:Iron-Breaker Mine") | [Karl](/wiki/Skyrim:Karl "Skyrim:Karl") |
| [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") | [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"), [The Warrens](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warrens "Skyrim:The Warrens") | [Cosnach](/wiki/Skyrim:Cosnach "Skyrim:Cosnach") |
| [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") | [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"), [The Warrens](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warrens "Skyrim:The Warrens") | [Degaine](/wiki/Skyrim:Degaine "Skyrim:Degaine") |
| [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") | [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood"), [Sleeping Giant Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping_Giant_Inn "Skyrim:Sleeping Giant Inn") | [Embry](/wiki/Skyrim:Embry "Skyrim:Embry") |
| [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") | [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"), [Birna's Oddments](/wiki/Skyrim:Birna%27s_Oddments "Skyrim:Birna's Oddments") | [Ranmir](/wiki/Skyrim:Ranmir "Skyrim:Ranmir") |

## Walkthrough

If you talk to one of the quest givers while having alcohol in your inventory, you will have the option to share a drink with them. This then makes them your friend, meaning that you can take low value items that belong to them and that they may occasionally give you a gift.

## Notes

- This quest does not have any stages or objectives.
- This quest can be repeated indefinitely.
- Certain expensive drinks will not give you the option to share a drink.
  - Version 1.3.3 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") partially fixes this bug.
- Because this is a favor quest which affects the quest giver's disposition, it will count towards the "Help the People" part of the [thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane") quest for the quest giver's hold.
- Because this quest is unmarked, completing it won't help with progress towards the "[Hero of the People](/wiki/Skyrim:Hero_of_the_People "Skyrim:Hero of the People")" [Achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements").
- Only drunks with the "[MaleDrunk](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleDrunk "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleDrunk")" voicetype can be quest givers for this quest.

# Skyrim:Quests

## Overview

A [Word Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") ([concept art](/wiki/Skyrim:Concept_Art "Skyrim:Concept Art"))

**Quests** are sorted below by their type or starting location.

### Main Quest

- **[Main Quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Main_Quest "Skyrim:Main Quest")** — Walkthrough for all parts of the game's main quest

### Faction Quests

- **[College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction)#Quests "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)")** — All quests for the College of Winterhold
- **[Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions#Quests "Skyrim:Companions")** — All quests for the Companions
- **[Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood#Quests "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood")** — All quests for the Dark Brotherhood
- **[Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion#Quests "Skyrim:Imperial Legion")** — All quests for the Imperial Legion
- **[Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks#Quests "Skyrim:Stormcloaks")** — All quests for the Stormcloaks
- **[Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Quests "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)")** — All quests for the Thieves Guild

### Other Quests

- **[Daedric Quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Quests "Skyrim:Daedric Quests")** — All quests related to the [Daedric Princes](/wiki/Lore:Daedric_Princes "Lore:Daedric Princes")
- **[Side Quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Side_Quests "Skyrim:Side Quests")** — All quests that are not part of a questline, including four [quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Divine_Quests "Skyrim:Divine Quests") related to the [Eight Divines](/wiki/Lore:Eight_Divines "Lore:Eight Divines"), one quest for the [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College#Quests "Skyrim:Bards College"), and nine [Dungeon Quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Quests "Skyrim:Dungeon Quests")

### Official Add-On and Creation Club Quests

- **[Dawnguard Quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Quests "Skyrim:Dawnguard Quests")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — All quests added by the *[Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard")* add-on
- **[Hearthfire Quests](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Hearthfire-Quests "Category:Skyrim-Hearthfire-Quests")**[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") — All quests added by the *[Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire")* add-on

### Miscellaneous Quests

- **[Miscellaneous Quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Quests "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Quests")** — Most miscellaneous quests, i.e., short quests that are displayed in the "Miscellaneous" section of your journal
- **[Thane Quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_Quests "Skyrim:Thane Quests")** — Summary of miscellaneous quests related to becoming a Thane of the various holds of Skyrim, including relevant prerequisites and other information
- Some additional varieties of miscellaneous quest not listed on the "Miscellaneous Quests" page above include:
  - **[Bounty Quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty_Quests "Skyrim:Bounty Quests")** — Miscellaneous quests involving hunting enemies for the Jarls for pay
  - **[Dungeon Miscellaneous Quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Miscellaneous_Quests "Skyrim:Dungeon Miscellaneous Quests")** — Miscellaneous quests related to specific dungeons
  - **[Tutorials](/wiki/Skyrim:Tutorials "Skyrim:Tutorials")** — Miscellaneous quests comprising lessons on the crafting skills

## Achievements

[Achievements](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") related to completing quests are:

- 8 achievements are obtained by completing the [main quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Main_Quest "Skyrim:Main Quest")
- 15 achievements are obtained by completing faction quests:
  - 3 for the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)")
  - 3 for the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions")
  - 3 for the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood")
  - 3 for the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)")
  - 3 can be obtained from either the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") or the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks")
-  **[Sideways](/wiki/Skyrim:Sideways "Skyrim:Sideways")** (20 points/Bronze) — Complete 10 [side quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Side_Quests "Skyrim:Side Quests")
-  **[Hero of the People](/wiki/Skyrim:Hero_of_the_People "Skyrim:Hero of the People")** (30 points/Bronze) — Complete 50 Misc [Objectives](/wiki/Skyrim:Objectives "Skyrim:Objectives")

## Knotwork

Some categories of quests can be distinguished by the decorative knotwork displayed alongside the quests' titles in your journal. Quests involving a choice between divergent factions (e.g., [Bloodline](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodline "Skyrim:Bloodline")) will display both knotworks, with one on the left (e.g., Volkihar Vampire) and the other on the right (e.g., Dawnguard).

## Bugs

- Quests may disappear from the bottom of the list in your journal as other quests and objectives are added or completed. This affects both active and completed quests. Missing active quests are still active and may reappear if objectives are completed, but *only* the newly completed objectives will appear; old objectives, whether completed or not, won't be displayed. This typically occurs when your total quests (both active and complete) are well over 200.

  **Mod Notes**: Most likely, the limit is exactly 255 when you include completed miscellaneous quests. This is the maximum value that can be stored in a single byte.

  - It may be possible to mitigate this issue by completing the oldest active quests first. That way, only completed quests will disappear.
  - This bug can also be used to remove infinitely repeating quests such as [The Dark Brotherhood Forever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dark_Brotherhood_Forever "Skyrim:The Dark Brotherhood Forever") or "Talk to the Companions leaders for work" from your quest list. If you complete these quests early, they'll eventually disappear as you complete other quests.

# Skyrim:Quicksilver Mine

## Overview

|  |  |  |

Quicksilver Mine

**Quicksilver Mine** is a small [quicksilver](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver "Skyrim:Quicksilver") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") in western [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"). It contains only one zone, *[Quicksilver Mine](#Quicksilver_Mine)*.

It is owned by [Leigelf](/wiki/Skyrim:Leigelf "Skyrim:Leigelf"), who will [buy quicksilver ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_Ore "Skyrim:Mine Ore") from you.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Borgny](/wiki/Skyrim:Borgny "Skyrim:Borgny")  [Edith](/wiki/Skyrim:Edith "Skyrim:Edith")  [Harald](/wiki/Skyrim:Harald "Skyrim:Harald")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigil_Enforcer_Armor_Set "Skyrim:Vigil Enforcer Armor Set")  [Lond](/wiki/Skyrim:Lond "Skyrim:Lond") |

## Related Quests

- **[Mine Ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_Ore "Skyrim:Mine Ore")**: Get paid to [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") ore. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Unholy Vigil](/wiki/Skyrim:Unholy_Vigil "Skyrim:Unholy Vigil")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigil_Enforcer_Armor_Set "Skyrim:Vigil Enforcer Armor Set"): Investigate the mysterious disappearances of [Vigilants of Stendarr](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigilants_of_Stendarr "Skyrim:Vigilants of Stendarr") in [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale").[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club")

### Exterior

A [smelter](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter") is near the mine entrance, which is west of the jetty where *[The Sea Squall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Sea_Squall "Skyrim:The Sea Squall")* is docked.

### Quicksilver Mine

.jpg)

Secret chamber with a shrine to Molag Bal[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club")

The entrance leads into a tunnel descending to the southwest. At the bottom, it turns southeast and enters the main mining area, with a maze of ledges above you on both sides. There are three quicksilver ore veins on the ground level: one on your right by a wooden ramp, and two more at the rear on a wall beside each other. To the left of the ramp is a cart containing a piece of [quicksilver ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore") and some [pickaxes](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"). More pickaxes are scattered throughout the mine. There is a campfire behind the central pillar on this level, and to the left of the fire is an open crate containing two rolled rugs and a copy of the [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Cherim's Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Cherim%27s_Heart "Skyrim:Cherim's Heart")*.

Ascending the ramp by the first ore vein and then following the path to the southeast will lead you to the rear of the mine. You will find a wooden table with a [mammoth steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Steak "Skyrim:Mammoth Steak"), a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"), a piece of [cooked beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooked_Beef "Skyrim:Cooked Beef"), a [carrot](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot"), and three pieces of [clam meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Clam_Meat "Skyrim:Clam Meat") here. To the left of the table, on the ground, is a fourth ore vein. Following the ledge to the left, you will find a table with a woodcutter's axe, a [leather helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Helmet "Skyrim:Leather Helmet"), and a couple pieces of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") on top. Staying against the wall and continuing around the mine, you will find a fifth ore vein. A ramp leads to some planking that forms a bridge across to the far side of the mine, where a set of shelves holds a [potion of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Magicka"), a [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Stamina"), a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a woodcutter's axe, a loaf of bread, three bottles of wine, and a piece of quicksilver ore.

## Notes

- The *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")* describes the mine as follows:

:   *"This mine is located on the outskirts of town to the west. Fruki, Land*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]*, Borgny, and Edith work here. This is the only Quicksilver mine inside Skyrim's borders, but despite this, the mine is suffering— from marauders and falling production. In fact, it is practically shut down as Leigelf spends his time obsessing over his wife and the competing mine. More proud than sensible, Leigelf's negligence is causing all of his workers to consider quitting in frustration or fear of attack."*

- You can take freely everything from inside the mine without being flagged for theft, even if you have yet to sell quicksilver ore to Leigelf.

## Maps

- 

  Quicksilver Mine

| # of [Cooking Pots/Spits](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") | 1 |
| [Shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") | [Loot](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Loot") Loot |

Radiant Raiment

**Radiant Raiment** is a [clothing](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing "Skyrim:Clothing") store run by [Taarie](/wiki/Skyrim:Taarie "Skyrim:Taarie") and her sister [Endarie](/wiki/Skyrim:Endarie "Skyrim:Endarie"), situated on the right as you enter [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") through the main gate. It sells various clothing of all types and expenses.

It is situated next door to [Bits and Pieces](/wiki/Skyrim:Bits_and_Pieces "Skyrim:Bits and Pieces"), opposite [The Winking Skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Winking_Skeever "Skyrim:The Winking Skeever").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Endarie](/wiki/Skyrim:Endarie "Skyrim:Endarie") [Apparel](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Apparel")  [Taarie](/wiki/Skyrim:Taarie "Skyrim:Taarie") [Apparel](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Apparel") |

## Related Quests

- **[Fit for a Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Fit_for_a_Jarl "Skyrim:Fit for a Jarl")**: Model some clothes for [Elisif the Fair](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif_the_Fair "Skyrim:Elisif the Fair").

## Radiant Raiment

The main shop area

The entrance is adept-locked out of hours, both [Endarie](/wiki/Skyrim:Endarie "Skyrim:Endarie") and [Taarie](/wiki/Skyrim:Taarie "Skyrim:Taarie") carry copies of the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Radiant_Raiments "Skyrim:Key to Radiant Raiments"). When entering there is a wooden bench against the east wall and opposite against the west wall is a small wardrobe containing [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") and having a [snow fox pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Fox_Pelt "Skyrim:Snow Fox Pelt") on top. The ceiling is vaulted and has a central pillar supporting it. As the room opens up there is a narrow table with a basket containing two bunches of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") on it, against the east wall, with another wooden bench to the right of the table. The counter is in front of the south wall and extends two thirds of the way across the shop. Against the west wall, around the corner from the entrance are double doors leading to the residence, with a small round table to the left of it, this has a plate of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and cheese on top and another wooden bench to the left of that with a [hide helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Helmet "Skyrim:Hide Helmet") on a ledge above it. In front of the counter is an open crate containing two bunches of [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton"). On the counter, the cupboard against the south wall behind it and two small sets of shelves in the southwest corner are several pieces of [clothing](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"), [fine clothing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes"), [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots") and a [circlet](/wiki/Skyrim:Circlet "Skyrim:Circlet") that are [displayed merchandise](#Displayed_Merchandise) and a [silver and sapphire circlet](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_and_Sapphire_Circlet "Skyrim:Silver and Sapphire Circlet") that isn't. On a ledge above the counter is an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet"). Behind the counter to the east is an alcove with two sets of shelves and two pieces of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood") in a basket, the smaller set of shelves holds a [sabre cat pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabre_Cat_Pelt "Skyrim:Sabre Cat Pelt"), a [goat hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Hide "Skyrim:Goat Hide") and a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"), while the large set has a master-locked [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox"), various pieces of displayed merchandise, two [jade and sapphire circlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Jade_and_Sapphire_Circlet "Skyrim:Jade and Sapphire Circlet") and a goat hide. Under the counter is an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and woodcutter's axe.

Through the double doors is a large dining and cooking area, with a wooden bench along the south wall with a small table at the end of it. Opposite the doors is a low table and chair with a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"), a common book and a [plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Plate "Skyrim:Plate") filled with loaves of bread, an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge") and a [tomato](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato") on the table. Against the north wall is a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") on a stand with a small cupboard holding a [platter](/wiki/Skyrim:Platter "Skyrim:Platter") filled with a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), two [baked potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a [raw rabbit leg](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg"), a [pheasant breast](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant_Breast "Skyrim:Pheasant Breast") and a couple of pieces of cheese to the left and to the right is a long wooden table and bench laid for two, with two portions of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), two [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish"), a loaf of bread, a couple of wheels of cheese, a [potion of regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration") and a bunch of tundra cotton. There are wall shelves above the table holding crockery. Against the west wall is a narrow table with a bowl of bread and a plate holding a [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese"), with an iron dagger. Above this is a wall shelf holding a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"). To the south is a stairwell with a flight leading up to the top floor and one down to the cellar.

At the top of the stairs is a T-shaped landing with three doors, one to the west, one to the north and one to the east. On the landing, either side of the door to the north is on one side, a narrow table with a basket containing a bunch of lavender and on the other, a small cupboard with a [goblet](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet") and [jug](/wiki/Skyrim:Jug "Skyrim:Jug") on top. The north wall to the left of the east door has two bookcases against it, these hold fourteen common books, a [solution of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Solution_of_Strength "Skyrim:Solution of Strength") and a [potion of extreme stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Extreme_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Extreme Stamina"), while opposite against the south wall is a wooden bench with a small table holding another common book beside it.

The door to the west opens into a bedroom that contains a single bed in the northwest corner with a small table beside it, a wardrobe against the east wall containing fine clothes and small wardrobe against the south wall with shelves above it. There is a bottle of alto wine, a [bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl") of bread, a plate holding a sliced eidar cheese and an iron dagger. The door to the north opens into another bedroom, this one has a partition wall coming out from the north wall. The bed is on the west side of this wall with a small table beside the bed and an open crate at the foot of it containing a bunch of lavender. There is also a tall wardrobe against the west wall with a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum") beside it. The other half of the room has a tall wardrobe against the partition wall, and unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") against the north wall, a cupboard against the east wall with a jug and goblet on top, with a large round wooden table to the right of it, on this table is the [business ledger](/wiki/Skyrim:Business_Ledger "Skyrim:Business Ledger"), a [thistle branch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch") and a plate of [red](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") and [green apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"). There is also a small table against the south wall with a bowl containing a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") on it.

The door to the east opens into the largest bedroom with a large double bed coming out from the northeast corner with a small table on the right holding a bottle of alto wine. There are several wall shelves above the bed holding fine clothes and a small coin purse. In the northwest corner is a tall wardrobe, with a small set of shelves to the left, against the west wall, these hold two bottles of [frostbite venom](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Venom "Skyrim:Frostbite Venom"), two samples of [slaughterfish scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Scales "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Scales"), a bowl of [glow dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Glow_Dust "Skyrim:Glow Dust"), a [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") flower and a [potion of haggling](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Haggling "Skyrim:Potion of Haggling"). There is a washbasin to the left of the shelves. In the southeast corner is a small wardrobe with a large coin purse and a copy of *[Fall of the Snow Prince](/wiki/Skyrim:Fall_of_the_Snow_Prince "Skyrim:Fall of the Snow Prince")* on top and a basket beside it containing two bunches of lavender. In front of this is a low table and chair, with a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a plate of bread and cheese and a goblet on the table. Against the south wall is a narrow table with a bowl of bread and a plate holding a sliced eidar cheese on top.

Descending the stair to the cellar, it is heavily vaulted with a cupboard against the west wall holding loaves of bread, [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") and several pieces of cheese, to the right of this is a rack with a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braid, two bunches of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and a bunch of dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") hanging from it. Against the north wall is a square wooden table with a couple of empty wine bottles and a common book on it, while in an alcove to the east is a long wooden table with a [thistle branch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch"), a [leek](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), a bunch of elves ear and a deathbell flower on top, a stack of [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels beside it and an unlocked chest underneath.

## Displayed Merchandise

The following items are sitting out in the store, for example on the store counters. They can be purchased from the merchant, or else can be stolen. Other items may also be present in the store, but those other items are not available for purchase. They [respawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") after ten days.

- Clothing: 7 [Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots"), 1 [Chef's Hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Chef%27s_Hat "Skyrim:Chef's Hat"), 1 [Chef's Tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Chef%27s_Tunic "Skyrim:Chef's Tunic"), 1 [Clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"), 1 [College Robes](/wiki/Skyrim:College_Robes "Skyrim:College Robes"), 2 [Fine Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Boots "Skyrim:Fine Boots"), 3 [Fine Clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes"), 3 [Fine Hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Hat "Skyrim:Fine Hat"), 1 [Hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Hat "Skyrim:Hat"), 2 [Miner's Clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner%27s_Clothes "Skyrim:Miner's Clothes"), 1 [Mourner's Hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Mourner%27s_Hat "Skyrim:Mourner's Hat")
- Jewelry: 1 [Gold and Emerald Circlet](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_and_Emerald_Circlet "Skyrim:Gold and Emerald Circlet"), 1 [Silver and Sapphire Circlet](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_and_Sapphire_Circlet "Skyrim:Silver and Sapphire Circlet")

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in Radiant Raiment's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be [pickpocketed](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") or stolen. They are [restocked](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") every two days.

## Notes

- This store has the largest inventory of enchanted jewelry in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"), making it a useful stop if you are searching for a particular enchantment to add to your repertoire.
- There is a  "Loot") Loot [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Shadowmarks "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") to the bottom left of the entrance door.
- In [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online"), a store bearing the same name was housed where the [blacksmith shop](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Blacksmith "Skyrim:Solitude Blacksmith") currently is. The current building housed a [home furnishings store](/wiki/Online:Furnishers "Online:Furnishers") called [Dragon's Hearth](/wiki/Online:Dragon%27s_Hearth "Online:Dragon's Hearth").
- [Gisli](/wiki/Skyrim:Gisli "Skyrim:Gisli") can sometimes be found behind the counter of the shop, though she doesn't sell anything.
- Either of the two sisters might run up to you in the store after entering, acting like you are in the private quarters, even though you aren't. All dialogue options are still available even though they might follow you around.

## Bugs

- Sometimes [Endarie](/wiki/Skyrim:Endarie "Skyrim:Endarie") will accuse you of trespassing in the Radiant Raiment between 8am and 8pm even though the door to the shop is open. This seems related to disposition towards [ServicesSolitudeRadiantRaiments](/wiki/Skyrim:ServicesSolitudeRadiantRaiments "Skyrim:ServicesSolitudeRadiantRaiments") or [SolitudeRadiantRaimentsFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:SolitudeRadiantRaimentsFaction "Skyrim:SolitudeRadiantRaimentsFaction").
  - Doing a [favor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fit_for_a_Jarl "Skyrim:Fit for a Jarl") for [Taarie](/wiki/Skyrim:Taarie "Skyrim:Taarie") or wearing [Radiant Raiment fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant_Raiment_Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Radiant Raiment Fine Clothes") (or other fine clothes) and exiting and re-entering may help.
- You can't interact with either of the goat hides in the shop.
- Endarie's merchant chest appears to sometimes hit an item cap, causing some items not to be sold, such as [Amulets of the Divines](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear#Amulets_of_the_Divines "Skyrim:Specialty Gear"). This can become particularly noticeable when additions such as [Lord's Mail](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord%27s_Mail "Skyrim:Lord's Mail")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") or [Nordic Jewelry](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Jewelry "Skyrim:Nordic Jewelry")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") add items to the beginning of her inventory (internally), thus forcing additional items off the end of it.

Ragnvald, nestled in the valley north of Markarth

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Find the sarcophagus.
2. Retrieve [Saerek's Skull Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Saerek%27s_Skull_Key "Skyrim:Saerek's Skull Key").
3. Retrieve [Torsten's Skull Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Torsten%27s_Skull_Key "Skyrim:Torsten's Skull Key").
4. Open the sarcophagus.
5. Kill [Otar the Mad](/wiki/Skyrim:Otar_the_Mad "Skyrim:Otar the Mad").

### Two Heroes, Two Keys

According to [legend](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Secrets_of_Ragnvald "Skyrim:The Secrets of Ragnvald"), the ancient ruin of [Ragnvald](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragnvald "Skyrim:Ragnvald") was once populated by [Nords](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") and ruled by a fearsome chieftain named Otar. At some point, Otar went mad due to evil voices within his head and turned into a servant of the ancient [dragons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon"), causing havoc and leading to dark times in Ragnvald. Eventually, the Nords decided to stop Otar and sent in two champions, Torsten and Saerek. Although they couldn't destroy him, they managed to seal him off inside the ruin, using separate keys to ensure he never escaped from his containment. Ragnvald has long since been abandoned, but the [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") [guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Guards "Skyrim:Guards") are aware of the dangers lurking within, and will rightfully warn you about the place: *"There's an evil to the north, friend, and its name is Ragnvald. A tomb like so many in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"), where the dead have found no peace."*

### Ragnvald

Straight north of [Salvius Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Salvius_Farm "Skyrim:Salvius Farm"), an unmarked path will start in the middle of nowhere, leading directly to the huge exterior area of Ragnvald. The ruin is only guarded by two [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") enemies, but the area is otherwise devoid of life and sound. Following the building on the southwest side of the entrance all the way to the back will lead to a dead bandit and a coin purse. Enter Ragnvald Temple through the main gate and proceed through the nearly destroyed first chamber with a dead draugr on a table. Take the only available path downwards and keep an eye out for helpful potions and minor loot along the way. The path will eventually lead to a large, complex chamber guarded by three leveled draugr. Fight them and proceed in a western direction until you face an odd-looking sarcophagus in front of a set of stairs leading to a sealed area. Touch one of the empty slots and read the inscription. The quest will trigger at this point and add map markers to the two items needed, located in different zones within Ragnvald.

### The Two Guardians

As told in the [legend](#Two_Heroes.2C_Two_Keys), the next step is to claim [Saerek's Skull Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Saerek%27s_Skull_Key "Skyrim:Saerek's Skull Key") and [Torsten's Skull Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Torsten%27s_Skull_Key "Skyrim:Torsten's Skull Key") from the heroes that managed to seal off Otar the Mad back in ancient times. The two guardians still protect the keys with their lives, and you will have to fight both of them to complete this quest. Check the map markers for doors leading in two different directions and choose which zone to enter first, [Ragnvald Canal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragnvald_Canal "Skyrim:Ragnvald Canal") or [Ragnvald Crypts](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragnvald_Crypts "Skyrim:Ragnvald Crypts").

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Guardian Torsten  **Ragnvald Canal** The door opens to a huge water-filled room guarded by three leveled draugr enemies. Follow the stream as it bends, making sure to surface in the alcove halfway through for a boss-leveled chest behind a door, but beware of the hidden [flamethrower trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Flamethrower_Statues "Skyrim:Flamethrower Statues") activated when you touch the door; it can be deactivated by pulling the nearby handle. Proceed west and head up the bridge where a small crack in the woodworks will allow you to proceed forward. Follow the path until you reach a large open area, with [Torsten's Skull Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Torsten%27s_Skull_Key "Skyrim:Torsten's Skull Key") on a pedestal. Claim the skull, which will cause [Guardian Torsten](/wiki/Skyrim:Guardian_Torsten "Skyrim:Guardian Torsten") to burst out of his sarcophagus, along with two leveled draugr. Finish the fight, examine the room for loot, then return to the pedestal and cross the bridge leading east. This is a shortcut back to Ragnvald Temple, although you will have to traverse a hallway full of [swinging blade traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Blades "Skyrim:Swinging Blades"). | Guardian Saerek  **Ragnvald Crypts** Head down the wooden bridge and fight the lonely draugr guarding the first room. Two paths leads south, both of them ending in the same chamber, although the one on the left is filled with traps triggered by [pressure plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate"). In the crypts, a total of five draugr will awaken from their slumber and attack. In the next chamber is an [oil slick](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Slicks "Skyrim:Oil Slicks") which can be used to damage the enemies that inhabit it. Examine the alcove for the [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") skill book *[Mystery of Talara, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:Mystery_of_Talara,_v_2 "Skyrim:Mystery of Talara, v 2")* in front of the booby-trapped minor loot chest, then head up the stairs to the north. You will emerge on the level above, with free access to [Saerek's Skull Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Saerek%27s_Skull_Key "Skyrim:Saerek's Skull Key") on an alcove to the east. As soon as you take it, [Guardian Saerek](/wiki/Skyrim:Guardian_Saerek "Skyrim:Guardian Saerek") will burst forth, accompanied by two draugr from the alcoves above. Defeat the guardians and backtrack west over the bridge, a quick shortcut back to Ragnvald Temple. |

### Otar the Mad

_04.jpg)

Otar the Mad

With both Skull Keys in your possession, return to the sealed sarcophagus in the western part of Ragnvald Temple and insert them into the empty slots. The locks will then disappear, and before long, [Dragon Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") [Otar the Mad](/wiki/Skyrim:Otar_the_Mad "Skyrim:Otar the Mad") will emerge. Otar uses [shock](/wiki/Skyrim:Shock_Damage "Skyrim:Shock Damage") as his primary weapon. He tends to summon a [storm atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm_Atronach "Skyrim:Storm Atronach") in the beginning of the fight, and he also uses the unique [Staff of the Storm Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_the_Storm_Wall "Skyrim:Staff of the Storm Wall") with very high Shock damage. Otar will rarely follow you if you stay away from him, but he will bombard you with his staff that casts [Wall of Storms](/wiki/Skyrim:Wall_of_Storms "Skyrim:Wall of Storms"). The [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") shout is ineffective against him. He can prove to be a challenging enemy to face, especially at low levels.

After the battle, it is time for your reward. From Otar's corpse, claim his valuable staff, the [Dragon Priest Mask](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest_Mask "Skyrim:Dragon Priest Mask") [Otar](/wiki/Skyrim:Otar "Skyrim:Otar") with [resist shock](/wiki/Skyrim:Resist_Shock "Skyrim:Resist Shock"), [fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Resist_Fire "Skyrim:Resist Fire") and [frost](/wiki/Skyrim:Resist_Frost "Skyrim:Resist Frost") enchantments, along with a huge amount of gold. In the chamber behind the sarcophagus, the boss-leveled chest holds even more gold, while the [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") in the back of the chamber provides a word for the [Kyne's Peace](/wiki/Skyrim:Kyne%27s_Peace "Skyrim:Kyne's Peace") shout. When all is said and done, reclaim the two Skull Keys from the sarcophagus, as they can be sold for a high price, and exit Ragnvald the way you came.

## Bugs

- The book *[The Secrets of Ragnvald](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Secrets_of_Ragnvald "Skyrim:The Secrets of Ragnvald")* is present in the game files, but can not be found anywhere in the game.
- Using a hostile spell on Otar's casket while you have both skull keys in your inventory (or one in your inventory and one used on the casket), will cause the casket to open prematurely, and Otar to emerge and attack.
- Sometimes the gate to the word wall area will close straight after opening. **?**

## Quest Stages

| Ragnvald (dunRagnvaldQST) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Unlock the Sarcophagus in Ragnvald |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 1, 2, 20, 30, 40.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage dunRagnvaldQST stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest dunRagnvaldQST`.

# Skyrim:Ragnvald

## Overview

Ragnvald

**Ragnvald** is a medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") north of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") and the [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") [Otar the Mad](/wiki/Skyrim:Otar_the_Mad "Skyrim:Otar the Mad"). It contains three zones: *[Ragnvald Temple](#Ragnvald_Temple)*, *[Ragnvald Crypts](#Ragnvald_Crypts)*, and *[Ragnvald Canal](#Ragnvald_Canal)*.

Its [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") teaches part of the [Kyne's Peace](/wiki/Skyrim:Kyne%27s_Peace "Skyrim:Kyne's Peace") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts").

## Related Quests

- **[Ragnvald](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragnvald_(quest) "Skyrim:Ragnvald (quest)")**: Discover the secrets of Ragnvald.
- **[Alteration Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Alteration Ritual Spell")**: Acquire [Kahvozein's Fang](/wiki/Skyrim:Kahvozein%27s_Fang "Skyrim:Kahvozein's Fang") and use it to get [heartscales](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Heartscales "Skyrim:Dragon Heartscales") from a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") for [Tolfdir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

Two leveled draugr roam the steps before the entrance: one archer and one melee fighter. Other than a few scattered [ingredient](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients")-bearing plants, the only thing of note here is the body of a dead [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") hidden in a golden shrub to the left of and behind the entrance. A small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and two loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") lie on the ground next to him. There are also at least three more hidden loose coins scattered around this area, so check the ground thoroughly.

### Ragnvald Temple

The first chamber contains a stone table with a dead [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Draugr "Skyrim:Containers") and a random [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons") on top, and a [burial urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn") on the ground beside the table. The ceiling has large holes in it and the sky is visible, but it is not possible to fast-travel from here. The only exit corridor leads downward before doubling back, passing a dead end with a dead draugr, another random poison, and an empty random [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") on the ground, then ending at a T-junction. To the right, the corridor quickly ends at an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). To the left, the path enters a narrow passage. This again doubles back as it descends.

As you follow it, you will hear a [swinging blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Blades "Skyrim:Swinging Blades") trap somewhere ahead. After a couple turns, the corridor leads to a doorway and a bridge into a large, complex open chamber. This is where you will find the first substantial opposition: two boss-level draugr, one on a platform on the far side of the bridge, and the other below the bridge, with wooden stairs leading up on your right to the platform. There is an [oil slick](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Slick "Skyrim:Oil Slick") with an [oil lantern](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Lanterns "Skyrim:Oil Lanterns") hanging over it on the central platform, which you can use to your advantage. From the platform on the far side of the bridge, it is easy to see that there are several separate lower levels. There are several patches of [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") fungus in the chamber on both the upper platform and the lower level, and several [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") growing throughout the ruins. On your right, by the top of the stairs, are two large [urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn"), with another at the bottom. Descending the stairs brings you to a stone table with a [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health") and an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet") on top. To either side of this table are a total of three sets of shelves holding several [ruined books](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruined_Book "Skyrim:Ruined Book"), a bowl each of [ectoplasm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ectoplasm "Skyrim:Ectoplasm"), [fire salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts"), and [void salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Void_Salts "Skyrim:Void Salts"), and a burial urn. To the south are two small alcoves; the left of these contains an unlocked chest and a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"). Opposite this is a doorway to a passage with the swinging blades trap you could hear previously, a dead draugr that appears to have been killed by the trap, and at the far end, a small room containing another unlocked chest, a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a lever that stops the blades, and just out of sight, an upright sarcophagus containing a slumbering draugr that will awaken as soon as you enter the room.

From the platform, to the south is another flight of wooden stairs leading down, but this small area is completely empty. Just past these stairs is a stone bridge that crosses to the south to another raised section, with another urn on the central platform opposite this bridge. There is another oil slick on the far side of the bridge and two doors: a wooden one which is barred from the other side, and an iron one that takes you to *[Ragnvald Crypts](#Ragnvald_Crypts)*. Heading across a pair of stone bridges to the north will take you to a wooden door, which is also barred from the other side. However, beneath this door and guarded by a third boss-level draugr is an iron door that leads into *[Ragnvald Canal](#Ragnvald_Canal)*.

_03.jpg)

Otar the Mad rises

At the western end of the central platform are stairs that descend to the main lower level that includes the access door to the Canal. In front of the base of the stairs is a sarcophagus with two large locks clamping it closed; this sarcophagus contains the remains of the dragon priest Otar the Mad, with the locks preventing his escape. Behind his sarcophagus are stairs leading up to raised spears blocking access beyond. As you approach the spears, you will be able to hear the music for the word wall and see a boss chest. There are numerous large urns and burial urns in this area, while to the north, on a broken sideboard, is an unlocked chest and a leveled potion of healing, and farther back to the northeast are three empty sets of shelves with a sideboard between two of them holding a random [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") and an empty random soul gem.

To gain access to the chamber beyond the barred archway, you must insert [Saerek's skull key](/wiki/Skyrim:Saerek%27s_Skull_Key "Skyrim:Saerek's Skull Key"), found in *Ragnvald Crypts*, and [Torsten's skull key](/wiki/Skyrim:Torsten%27s_Skull_Key "Skyrim:Torsten's Skull Key"), found in *Ragnvald Canal*, into the slots in the sarcophagus, retracting the spears and releasing Otar the Mad. Resistance to lightning magic is a definite boon when battling him. After defeating him, be sure to loot his ash pile for [his mask](/wiki/Skyrim:Otar "Skyrim:Otar") and [lightning staff](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_the_Storm_Wall "Skyrim:Staff of the Storm Wall"). The chamber behind Otar's sarcophagus contains a word wall for the Kyne's Peace shout, as well as a boss chest; to the right among the cave-in is an apprentice-locked chest in the northwest corner, while a dead draugr that can be looted is farther to the east. Before you leave, don't forget to remove the two skull keys from Otar's sarcophagus, as they are worth a fair bit of gold. After finishing your exploration, exit back the way you entered, as there is no shortcut.

### Ragnvald Crypts

*Ragnvald Crypts* begins with a small room containing a black sarcophagus that appears inert, guarded by a single draugr. There are several more urns, burial urns, and sets of shelves holding a few food sacks around the room. Opposite the inert sarcophagus is a stone table holding two minor potions of healing. Two parallel passages lead out of this room. Notice that above the sarcophagus on the wall ledge, there is a burial urn that may appear to glow purple. You can reach that ledge with a single word of [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint"), but the urn appears to be empty. Of the two passages, the one to the left has four [poison dart traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap") triggered by four successive [pressure plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate"), but since the traps aim not at the plates but in front of them, pausing directly on each plate until the darts are exhausted allows safe passage. The passage on the right has no traps. Both end in a standard burial chamber lined with wall slots for remains. Following the crypt down, the first turn to the left will see three lower-level draugr and a boss-level draugr revive and attack you. The passage curves right and then left, leading past a large urn on the right and a draugr in an alcove on the left who will revive. After more turns, the corridor ends on the lower level of a medium-sized room with an upper level, with another boss-level draugr near the entrance. There is a chest in an alcove at the opposite end of this room; be sure to disengage the apprentice-level [trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Tension_Cable "Skyrim:Tension Cable") on the right-hand side of the chest before opening, or avoid the [spear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_Trap "Skyrim:Spear Trap") that shoots from the floor. Also watch out for a lower-level draugr wandering around the upper level of the room. A copy of the [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Mystery of Talara, v 2](/wiki/Skyrim:Mystery_of_Talara,_v_2 "Skyrim:Mystery of Talara, v 2")* sits on the ledge behind the trapped chest.

A staircase ascending to the upper level of the room is found on the right. From here, it is possible to go either left into another large room, or right across a bridge you passed under earlier and into a passageway that leads back to *Ragnvald Temple*. The large room on the left has the skull key on a [trapped](/wiki/Skyrim:Weight_Sensitive_Plate "Skyrim:Weight Sensitive Plate") pedestal in the middle, which will raise the draugr slumbering in all three sarcophagi: a large black sarcophagus at the far end of the room contains [Guardian Saerek](/wiki/Skyrim:Guardian_Saerek "Skyrim:Guardian Saerek"), and two other sarcophagi are on balconies to either side. It is possible to avoid this obvious trap by casting fire rune spells at each of the sarcophagi and fighting each of the occupants individually, with the rear door still open for a retreat if necessary. Once complete, the skull key can be removed in safety. Be sure to take Saerek's leveled two-handed weapon. There is an unlocked chest to the right of Saerek's sarcophagus, and various burial urns and urns around the room and on the balconies. Also on the left-hand balcony by the sarcophagus is a leveled potion of magicka.

### Ragnvald Canal

This is another complex space, with the floor covered in water and several draugr with a bit more fight in them than any encountered before: one will attempt to summon a [frost atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Atronach "Skyrim:Frost Atronach"). To the left of where you enter, where the first draugr is standing, is a stone table holding a random healing potion and random empty soul gem, with a set of shelves beside it holding a random potion. Once the draugr are defeated, proceed to the left and ahead, keeping an eye on the bridges higher up in the room to shoot any draugr passing over them. Past the wooden bridge over the water, there is an unlocked chest with a dead draugr lying next to it in a dead-end room to the right. To the left and forward, progress appears to be blocked by a raised bridge. To your right is a sideboard with a large urn and a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") on top. The lever to lower the bridge is found on the floor a bit farther to the left, or simply circumvented. The black iron door behind the lever is trapped by an expert-level [tension cable](/wiki/Skyrim:Tension_Cable "Skyrim:Tension Cable") on the bottom left of the door, which triggers a [flamethrower statue](/wiki/Skyrim:Flamethrower_Statues "Skyrim:Flamethrower Statues") trap; disarm the trap, or just wait for it to burn out. The dead-end room behind the door features an unlocked chest with a moderate amount of loot and a couple of sets of shelves, one of which has a bowl of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal") next to some food sacks. Once across the lowered bridge, you pass some urns and a set of shelves holding another salt pile before exiting to the south.

Continuing to follow the passages leads you to a chamber with the second skull key, this one on a platform with a bridge running to it and another leading off to the left, with stairs leading to the lower level on the opposite side. At the far end of the chamber is a large black sarcophagus, the resting place of [Guardian Torsten](/wiki/Skyrim:Guardian_Torsten "Skyrim:Guardian Torsten"), flanked by two others on raised balconies. This trap can be dismantled in the same way the previous one was. There is an unlocked chest to the right of Guardian Torsten's sarcophagus, and several urns and burial urns are around the room. Take the second skull key and return to the main chamber via the bridge leading east. The path leads through the main chamber on a higher walkway; continue straight across to a dead end with a novice-locked chest and a random [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina") beside it. Be careful not to set off the swinging blades trap by stepping on the pressure plate at the start of the passage, immediately after exiting the main chamber a second time. Along the way back to *Ragnvald Temple*, there is an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters") with a random potion of healing and a random filled soul gem on top, and opposite, another set of shelves holding a novice-locked chest and another empty random soul gem.

## Notes

- Ragnvald also appears in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online") as [Ragnvald Ritual Site](/wiki/Online:Ragnvald_Ritual_Site "Online:Ragnvald Ritual Site").

## Bugs

- Using [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") or placing a rune near or on the sarcophagus will make Otar the Mad jump out even if the locks are still in place. **?**
- If you use a single key in the sarcophagus, enter a different zone, and return, Otar will clip through the sarcophagus in an A-pose. Attacking him will cause him to properly emerge from the coffin and begin attacking you.
- If you return to Ragnvald after completing the dungeon and killing Otar, it is possible to find his intact corpse behind the boss chest on the pile of rubble. **?**
- It is possible for followers to be killed instantly by the swinging blades trap in the upper passage from *Ragnvald Canal* back to *Ragnvald Temple*. **?**
- The Draugr outside of the dungeon respawn despite it being classed as a "no reset zone".
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Raldbthar

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
