Raldbthar

**Raldbthar** is a medium-sized [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") west-southwest of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). It contains two zones: *[Raldbthar](#Raldbthar)* and *[Raldbthar Deep Market](#Raldbthar_Deep_Market)*.

Raldbthar is one of only three sites that provide initial access to [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach").

## Related Quests

- **[Lost to the Ages](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_to_the_Ages "Skyrim:Lost to the Ages")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Search for the Dwemer's [Aetherium Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Aetherium_Forge "Skyrim:The Aetherium Forge").
- **[Mourning Never Comes](/wiki/Skyrim:Mourning_Never_Comes "Skyrim:Mourning Never Comes")**: Help [Muiri](/wiki/Skyrim:Muiri "Skyrim:Muiri") get her revenge.

### Exterior

A small group of leveled [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") has set up camp outside the main entrance to Raldbthar, and will attack on sight. It is possible to jump up to the upper portion of the ruins, where you can find a [silver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Silver Ore Vein") behind a tree, and an alcove containing an expert-locked Dwarven [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), several Dwemer metal items and [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"), and a filled random [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"). Farther up the stairs beyond the alcove is a locked enclosure that, once unlocked from the inside, allows access to [a Dwemer lift](/wiki/Skyrim:Great_Lift_at_Raldbthar "Skyrim:Great Lift at Raldbthar") that will take you straight down to Raldbthar Deep Market, while a [moonstone ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Moonstone_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Moonstone Ore Vein") is just up the hill from the lift. An [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") can be found near the bottom of the stairs leading up to the ruins.

### Raldbthar

The first section of this zone is inhabited by a large group of bandits, who have cleared out the few [Dwarven automatons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Automatons "Skyrim:Dwarven Automatons") that guarded the entrance area. The bandits are led by [Alain Dufont](/wiki/Skyrim:Alain_Dufont "Skyrim:Alain Dufont") (if you do not yet have the quest [Mourning Never Comes](/wiki/Skyrim:Mourning_Never_Comes "Skyrim:Mourning Never Comes") active, see [notes](#Notes) below before killing him). Dufont carries the unique, enchanted [warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Warhammer "Skyrim:Warhammer") [Aegisbane](/wiki/Skyrim:Aegisbane "Skyrim:Aegisbane").

Upon entering, there is a short passage with various items of Dwemer metal scattered across the floor. Ahead on the left are two unowned bedrolls, one of which is occupied by a sleeping bandit, with a food barrel beside them. Opposite the bedrolls is a cart containing more Dwemer metal items. Past the bandit is a toppled gate with two [flame spouts](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Spout_Trap "Skyrim:Flame Spout Trap") firing intermittently across the passage in front of a second open gateway, serving as heat to cook a charred skeever on a rack to the left. There is a passage to the left of the flame spouts leading into a domestic area with stone beds and tables and chairs, with several bandits patrolling or sleeping in this area. There are Dwemer items found on the floor, tables, and shelves. After you pass a cave-in on the left, around the corner to the left is a chest, while across the passage in an alcove ahead are two unusable stone beds. Farther along the passage is a shelf along the right wall with three [Dwarven arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Arrow "Skyrim:Dwarven Arrow") on top. Across the corridor from this shelf is a table holding a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll") and a copy of *[The Aetherium Wars](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Aetherium_Wars "Skyrim:The Aetherium Wars")*([DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard")), with a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") on the floor beside it. A bandit is patrolling ahead.

Farther ahead to the southwest is another bandit near a lit fireplace. To the left of this bandit is a room containing five stone beds, two of which are occupied by sleeping bandits. There is also a table with a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), four bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a [red apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), a sheaf of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat"), and a random set of [armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor") on top. By one of the beds is a pair of [iron boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots"). By the fire is a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a [carrot](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot"), two bottles of Nord mead, and some cheese. There is a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench") next to where the bandit was standing. The passage continues ahead to a junction. A ramp down to the right leads to a room containing two bandits and the bandit leader Alain Dufont by a campfire. Alternatively, continuing straight ahead leads to a level-locked gate.

Beyond the gate is a ramp leading up to an area with an [oil slick](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Slicks "Skyrim:Oil Slicks") and out onto a balcony above the room containing Alain Dufont and the two other bandits. From here, you are able to fire two [Dwemer ballistae](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Ballista "Skyrim:Dwemer Ballista") at the group of bandits around the fire, possibly also igniting another oil slick that has pooled around them; this will make the fight significantly easier, but will also scatter various loot in the area. This room can also be reached by passing through the flame spouts near the ruin entrance and descending to a master-locked gate that opens directly into the room, opposite the campfire. There is wooden scaffolding descending from the balcony to the room below. The room's main level features two unowned bedrolls each with a random pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Boots "Skyrim:Armor") beside them, the remains of a leveled [Dwarven sphere](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Sphere "Skyrim:Dwarven Sphere"), and a barrel near the fire with a common [book](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books") on top. Under the wooden scaffolding, well hidden and partially in the dark, is an unlocked wooden chest.

There is a locked gate underneath the balcony, with another bandit patrolling the room behind; the bandit will open the gate and join any fighting by the fire. Two long shelves with metal grating above separate the two rooms. The shelves hold many Dwemer items, a loose gold coin, a [gold ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ingot "Skyrim:Gold Ingot"), an [iron ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot"), a piece of [iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore"), two bottles of alto wine, and a copy of the [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[2920, Last Seed, v8](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Last_Seed,_v8 "Skyrim:2920, Last Seed, v8")*. Under the two long shelves on the side under the balcony are two chests, one apprentice-locked, the other unlocked. The room under the balcony has suffered severe damage, with cave-ins and fallen masonry lying in piles, and an empty chest in one of the piles. Along the wall to the left of the two shelves separating the rooms is a stone table holding a random [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"), a random [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), a random [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), and more Dwemer metal items, with a sack on the floor nearby. Above the table is a wall shelf with a bottle of alto wine, a random [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet"), a leveled potion of stamina, a leveled [potion of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Strength "Skyrim:Potion of Strength"), and a random [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow") on top. Farther to the left along the same wall at the rear of the room is a master-locked gate up some steps. Behind this is a long stone table holding an unlocked Dwemer chest, two Dwarven metal ingots, three pieces of [gold ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore "Skyrim:Gold Ore"), a random enchanted [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield"), and three large [coin purses](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse").

At the rear of the room to the left of the locked gate is an unlocked door that leads further into the zone to areas that are still guarded by leveled [Dwarven spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spider "Skyrim:Dwarven Spider") and Dwarven spheres, a few of which will pop out of the [Dwarven scuttles](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Scuttle "Skyrim:Dwarven Scuttle") that abound in this section. The next room contains a magicka potion and two loose gold coins just around the corner to the left, an apprentice-locked chest to the right, and a medium coin purse behind a pile of fallen masonry to the left. Watch for several oil slicks that can be used to damage your foes, as well as a double [spinning blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Spinning_Blades "Skyrim:Spinning Blades") trap on an ascending stairway and a [steam piston](/wiki/Skyrim:Steam_Piston "Skyrim:Steam Piston") beyond. There are safe areas to the sides of the spinning blades to ascend the stairs. Beyond these traps is a novice-locked chest hidden in a corner behind some horizontal pipes, just past a flight of stairs leading up. At the top of the stairs are three alcoves. The right alcove contains a workbench and a novice-locked chest, the middle alcove contains a stone table with several Dwemer metal items on top, and the left alcove contains a master-locked chest beside another table holding a random filled soul gem and the remains of a Dwarven spider. More stairs to the left lead up to a passage with scuttles on either side. At the end is a lift that will take you down to *Raldbthar Deep Market*.

### Raldbthar Deep Market

The lift down to the Deep Market drops you off at the top of a short ramp protected by another spinning blade trap. At the bottom on the right is a novice-locked chest. Doors ahead open into a large, multi-level chamber inhabited by [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"), and a pair of their captive [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") in a gated pen on your right. Beside the pen is a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack"), a small table to the left holding three [leather strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips") and a piece of [human flesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Human_Flesh "Skyrim:Human Flesh"), and another table to the right with three pieces of [leather](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather "Skyrim:Leather") and a [Falmer war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_War_Axe "Skyrim:Falmer War Axe"). In front of the tanning rack is the body of a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord"). There are three Falmer tents on the lowest level of this chamber. The tent on the right has a small campfire in front, and contains a [hay pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping "Skyrim:Sleeping") you can rest on. Beside the fire is a [Dwemer pan](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Pan "Skyrim:Dwemer Pan"), two [skeever tails](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever_Tail "Skyrim:Skeever Tail"), and a unique [charred skeever meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Meat "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Meat"). The middle tent is at the rear of the chamber to the left of stairs leading up, and contains two pieces of [chaurus chitin](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Chitin "Skyrim:Chaurus Chitin") and an unlocked Falmer chest. The final tent is empty. There are two clusters of [chaurus egg sacs](/wiki/Skyrim:Egg_Sacs "Skyrim:Egg Sacs") along the southern wall. At the top of the stairs are the remains of a skeever, with blood splattered all around and the head lying a few feet away. Immediately behind the remains is an apprentice-locked chest, with three [charred skeever hides](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide") to the left, and a small area to the right featuring a Falmer tent with a campfire and a [weak poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Poison") inside. More stairs lead up from here to the first ramp that winds its way up to a platform where two leveled Falmer await. There are two empty tents on this platform, with a campfire in front. Walking around the edge of the platform to the other side of the pillar directly behind the campfire, you will find a chest. A metal grating forms a ramp down to another platform, where another Falmer is standing in front of another tent with a campfire inside. Behind this tent is an unlocked Falmer chest and a table with several metal items, a [magicka poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka_Poison "Skyrim:Magicka Poison"), and a button that lowers another ramp from the first platform into place, enabling you to climb to a passage above. At the end of the passage, another ramp descends to a ledge along the tops of the lower structures, with a passage behind a metal grating at the end leading to another set of doors.

Beware the Dwemer ballista trap at the top of a flight of stairs just beyond these doors. It can result in enormous amounts of damage, but alert explorers can spot the [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") trigger and avoid it. Just past these stairs is another trap, this one a [slicer](/wiki/Skyrim:Slicer "Skyrim:Slicer") also triggered by an obvious pressure plate. Watch out for Dwarven spiders and spheres emerging from more Dwarven scuttles in the next corridor. On the east wall by the first set of slanted pipes is an unlocked chest. It is also possible to climb the slanted pipes, turn to the southeast, and then use Whirlwind Sprint or the Vampire Lord Bats power to travel to a section above the trapped passage below. It may also be possible to ride the slicer blades up to this location. There is a hidden chest found by the south wall up here. By the next slanted pipes are several metal items and a random filled soul gem on the ground. The corridor beyond the next doorway contains a closed portcullis, and a platform set with four blue buttons. Pushing the first button on the left will trigger a set of [flamethrower traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Flamethrower_Statues "Skyrim:Flamethrower Statues"), while the third button from the left will lower the portcullis. There are three shelves to the right of the buttons holding various Dwemer metal items, with more on a stone table around to the left.

The next area is a large chamber inhabited by four leveled Falmer standing by the openings to four Falmer tents around the chamber. Near the entrance is a small novice-locked room housing two [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus") or [chaurus hunters](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Hunter "Skyrim:Chaurus Hunter")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"), a stone table holding a [corundum ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ingot "Skyrim:Corundum Ingot"), two [silver ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ingot "Skyrim:Silver Ingot"), a gold ingot, a piece of [gold ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore "Skyrim:Gold Ore"), and a piece of [ebony ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Ore "Skyrim:Ebony Ore"), and three Dwarven treasure chests: one unlocked, one expert-locked, and the third apprentice-locked. There are many chaurus egg sacs in and around the room, and four loose [chaurus eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs") on a shelf at the front. To the left of the small room is a Falmer tent containing a poison and a hay pile. To the right of the main room entrance is a set of three large shelves holding various Dwemer metal items, beside which is a statue of a head with two random soul gems beside it. The first tent on the right contains a potion and has an unlocked chest beside it, while the second tent on the right contains a [Falmer bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Bow "Skyrim:Falmer Bow") and a hay pile. A fourth, empty tent is around the corner to the right of the small room. The nearby fifth and final tent, without a Falmer standing in front, has an expert-locked gate at the entrance, and contains an unlocked chest. Past the fifth tent are more chaurus egg sacs as well as another unlocked chest next to a Dwemer bowl.

The bridge in this large chamber can be lowered by removing bones or metal scraps from four jammed gears. One bone is lodged in the gear on your right as you enter the room. A metal scrap is located in the water under the bridge (although sometimes this scrap is on the ground below instead of in the gear; interact with the scrap as you normally would). The remaining two bones jamming gears are in the far corners of the room. After removing all four obstructions, go onto the platform and press the button to lower the bridge ahead. Once lowered, the bridge releases a leveled [Dwarven centurion](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Centurion "Skyrim:Dwarven Centurion"). There is a large Dwarven chest next to the centurion's gantry that contains [leveled loot](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"), and a door behind it opening into a passage that leads to spears blocking your way. On the left is a lever that will lower the spears, allowing you to access a room guarded by two leveled Dwarven spiders. There is an adept-locked chest on the wall opposite the entrance, and two sets of wall shelves running most of the way around the room holding many ruined books, a random potion, various Dwemer metal items, two Dwarven metal ingots, a gold ingot, a corundum ingot, and a [Dwarven helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Helmet "Skyrim:Dwarven Helmet"). A door to the right opens into a small room containing an [Aetherium Shard](/wiki/Skyrim:Aetherium_Shard "Skyrim:Aetherium Shard") for [Lost to the Ages](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_to_the_Ages "Skyrim:Lost to the Ages")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") and two unlocked chests. Opposite this room is a gate with a lift behind that takes you back to the surface.

If you have an [Attunement Sphere](/wiki/Skyrim:Attunement_Sphere "Skyrim:Attunement Sphere") in your inventory, activating the Dwarven mechanism in the center of the final room will reveal a staircase. Following this staircase down leads to a short corridor ending at a set of double doors that open into [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach"). An expert-locked gate along this corridor protects two Dwemer treasure chests containing leveled loot.

## Notes

- [Alain Dufont](/wiki/Skyrim:Alain_Dufont "Skyrim:Alain Dufont") is present even if [Mourning Never Comes](/wiki/Skyrim:Mourning_Never_Comes "Skyrim:Mourning Never Comes") is not active. This can cause problems for players trying to complete the optional objective for that quest, since it makes it very easy to kill him before the quest is begun, later resulting in the optional objective not being available.
  - You can kill all of the bandits in this area, even the ones sitting next to Alain around the campfire, and he will not turn hostile. However, if you get too close to him, he will tell you *"I don't know how you made it this far, but you'll go no farther."* and attack. If this happens, simply run as far away from him as you can and enter sneak mode. He will quickly lose sight of you and stop being hostile, allowing you to walk past him and continue deeper into Raldbthar. He may also accept a yield if you sheathe your weapon.
  -  Using the console, you can also input `prid 000D2AFF` then `disable`, which will disable Alain, but not kill him. He should automatically be re-enabled eventually. However, if he does remain disabled, you can simply input `prid 000D2AFF` then `enable`.
- The elevator leading to the surface is not reset when the corresponding exterior cell has respawned. The elevator can be reached again from the lower part of the exterior ruin by climbing the rocks and optionally using the [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") shout. So, if you originally used the elevator to exit the ruin, you can use it again to access the final part of Deep Market leading to Blackreach, thus bypassing most of the dungeon.
- If you are having trouble with the Dwarven centurion near the end of the ruin, you can lead it back to the room with the slanted pipes (where you were attacked by spiders and spheres) and the centurion won't enter, allowing you to safely pick it off from a distance with magic or archery.
- You can avoid fighting the leveled chaurus in the large room in Raldbthar Deep Market simply by not opening the door to their enclosure.

## Bugs

- If you return to the Deep Market after completing it once, the bridge may be up again. It's possible no bones will be in the gears, leaving no way to lower the bridge again. Even if the bones are there, you may not be able to interact with them properly (even if you dislodge them with a weapon, the gears won't turn).
  - Use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") command `tcl` to float across the gap and through the raised drawbridge.
  - Go to the end of the platform while the bridge is still up and use the [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") shout to cross the gap to the raised bridge. At this point, you can use the [clipping glitch](/wiki/Skyrim:Glitches#Clipping "Skyrim:Glitches") to pass through the raised bridge. Once through, kill the Dwarven centurion, and you can continue as normal.
  - If you return to Raldbthar during the quest [Lost to the Ages](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_to_the_Ages "Skyrim:Lost to the Ages"), the bones will have been replaced in the gears, and you will be able to interact with them normally, allowing you to progress through the dungeon.
- One of the bandits near Alain carries the [Irkngthand Consortium Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Irkngthand_Consortium_Key "Skyrim:Irkngthand Consortium Key"), which doesn't open anything.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.8, addresses this issue. The bandit will carry the [Raldbthar Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Keys#Raldbthar_Key "Skyrim:Keys") instead.
- During Mourning Never Comes, Alain Dufont's initial dialogue cuts off before you are allowed to give a response and he enters combat before he's supposed to.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.7, addresses this issue. It was incorrectly set as a goodbye response, and the script never should have been added to it.
- One of the Falmer huts in the large room with the stuck gears has a texture glitch near the back of the interior, showing a void rather than the floor. **?**

The Ramshackle Trading Post at dusk

The **Ramshackle Trading Post** is an old [shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn_Places#Shacks "Skyrim:Dragonborn Places") south of [Kagrumez](/wiki/Skyrim:Kagrumez "Skyrim:Kagrumez") and west-northwest of [Ashfallow Citadel](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashfallow_Citadel "Skyrim:Ashfallow Citadel").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Falas Selvayn](/wiki/Skyrim:Falas_Selvayn "Skyrim:Falas Selvayn") \* |

\* Appears only between midnight 12am and 4am.

## Related Quests

- **[Pain in the Necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Pain_in_the_Necklace "Skyrim:Pain in the Necklace")**: Find [East Empire pendants](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Pendant "Skyrim:East Empire Pendant") for [Fethis Alor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fethis_Alor "Skyrim:Fethis Alor").

## Ramshackle Trading Post

As the name suggests, the building is derelict, with the doors, windows, and part of the roof missing, and large holes in the walls. The shack is against a cliff facing a valley down to the sea. In the northeast corner of the interior is a small round table with two overturned chairs and an upright chair, which has clearly been used by someone drinking [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), judging by the three [empty wine bottles](/wiki/Skyrim:Empty_Wine_Bottle "Skyrim:Empty Wine Bottle") on the floor and the full wine bottle on the table. In the northwest corner is a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Note "Skyrim:A Note") pinned to the wall by a leveled [arrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Arrows "Skyrim:Arrows"), which reads *Meet me here at midnight.* Outside the shack, against the west wall is a crate holding an [East Empire Company strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Strongbox "Skyrim:East Empire Company Strongbox"). In front of the shack are two [scathecraw](/wiki/Skyrim:Scathecraw "Skyrim:Scathecraw") plants and an empty barrel.

## Notes

- If you arrive between midnight 12am and 4am, you will find [Falas Selvayn](/wiki/Skyrim:Falas_Selvayn "Skyrim:Falas Selvayn") here, sitting at the table and willing to trade with you. However, arriving before midnight and waiting will not cause him to appear.

# Skyrim:Rannveig's Fast (quest)

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Claim the [force of power](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") from [Rannveig's Fast](/wiki/Skyrim:Rannveig%27s_Fast "Skyrim:Rannveig's Fast").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Location(s): | [Rannveig's Fast](/wiki/Skyrim:Rannveig%27s_Fast "Skyrim:Rannveig's Fast") |
| Reward: | A word for the [Kyne's Peace](/wiki/Skyrim:Kyne%27s_Peace "Skyrim:Kyne's Peace") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"). |
| ID: | dunRannveigQST |
| Suggested Level: | 8 |

The regretful ghosts outside [Rannveig's Fast](/wiki/Skyrim:Rannveig%27s_Fast "Skyrim:Rannveig's Fast")

## Quick Walkthrough

**Note**: This quest does not appear in your journal.

1. Encounter the regretful [ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Subjugated_Ghost "Skyrim:Subjugated Ghost") outside [Rannveig's Fast](/wiki/Skyrim:Rannveig%27s_Fast "Skyrim:Rannveig's Fast").
2. Fall into the [trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Trap_Door "Skyrim:Trap Door") of a [sadistic warlock](/wiki/Skyrim:Sild_the_Warlock "Skyrim:Sild the Warlock") **or** (optional) sneak behind the warlock for an ambush attack.
3. Claim the treasure and learn a word for the [Kyne's Peace](/wiki/Skyrim:Kyne%27s_Peace "Skyrim:Kyne's Peace") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts").

### The Ghosts of Rannveig's Fast

The [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") called [Rannveig's Fast](/wiki/Skyrim:Rannveig%27s_Fast "Skyrim:Rannveig's Fast") is located in the wilderness south and slightly to the west of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"), not far from the shores of [River Hjaal](/wiki/Skyrim:River_Hjaal "Skyrim:River Hjaal"). No road will take you there, so either follow the river or take a shortcut through [Cold Rock Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Cold_Rock_Pass "Skyrim:Cold Rock Pass") to reach the ruin. The exterior is quite large and guarded by some rather unusual [Subjugated Ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Subjugated_Ghost "Skyrim:Subjugated Ghost") and a single [Ghost Adventurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost_Adventurer "Skyrim:Ghost Adventurer"), all of whom will apologize for attacking you. You can either choose to put them out of their misery or simply enter the ruin, as they will not follow you inside.

### The Setup

The door opens to a huge chamber with the sky visible above and the floor overgrown with ferns. Proceed north and you will meet another subjugated ghost, who is unwilling to attack you but forced to by unknown powers. The next huge chamber has another regretful ghost wandering around. There are several paths to choose: the locked southern door leads to a small chamber with a minor loot chest, while the northern door will offer an alternate route to discover the secrets of the ruin. The most tempting option will obviously be the chiming [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") to the east, with a huge glowing chest in front.

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| *"This is actually going to hurt a lot."*  **Falling Down** If you walk directly toward the word wall and the glowing chest, the darkened part of the walkway will turn out to be a cleverly hidden [trap door](/wiki/Skyrim:Trap_Door "Skyrim:Trap Door") and you will fall down to another level through another trap door until you finally land inside a locked cage. Here you find yourself surrounded by the bodies of dead [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") floating in knee-deep water. Outside the cage, Sild the Warlock will be wandering around and will be pleasantly surprised by yet another rat in the trap: *"Ooooh...yes...yes. You've fallen for my trap! Greed makes a great lure. Odd you didn't die from the fall though. Most do."* Due to your unexpected, but most welcome survival, he will start messing around the chamber, looking for something with which he can dispose of you as quickly as possible, so he can subjugate you as part of his army of ghosts. When he finally locates his desired item he will say: *"Ah...Here it is. Now, if you'd be so kind as to stand still this will be much easier for me to do. Oh, and I wasn't entirely truthful before. This is actually going to hurt a lot. You see, you have to be dead in order for the spell to take hold."* Sild will then proceed to cast [Oakflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Oakflesh "Skyrim:Oakflesh") on himself and then shower you with [flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Flames "Skyrim:Flames") or [firebolts](/wiki/Skyrim:Firebolt "Skyrim:Firebolt"). Without resorting to dragon shouts from inside the cage, there are three ways to get out and fight Sild face-to-face. First, you can examine the dead bandits in the water; one of them has ten [lockpicks](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick"). Alternatively, search the [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Satchel "Skyrim:Satchel") found just to the left on the cage door. It contains the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Rannveigs_Fast_Key "Skyrim:Rannveigs Fast Key") to the door. Lastly, when your health is almost down to zero, Sild will open the cage himself to finish you off. | *"This one didn't survive the fall either."*  **Ambush** If you manage to resist the temptation of the word wall and the glowing chest, the northern tunnel leads to a closed gate with a handle visible on the other side. Go south from the gate and up two sets of stairs until you reach a handle. The western path leads to the overhead bridges above the huge chamber and a room with another subjugated ghost and some minor loot, including a locked chest and a [diamond](/wiki/Skyrim:Diamond "Skyrim:Diamond") in the hands of a dead [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). Backtrack to the handle, pull it, and head downstairs to the iron gate, which will now be raised. Fight another ghost and take the only available path into the depths of the ruin. You will see a wooden door, but that will be your escape route so skip that for now and follow the voice coming from the western chamber, preferably using [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") to avoid detection. Before long you will see Sild the Warlock wandering restlessly around in his chamber, waiting for yet another victim to fall for his glowing chest-trap, mumbling to himself: *"Come on! You know you want what's in that chest. Just walk toward it!"*, *"Just walk toward the chest! Gravity will do the rest."* and *"I know you're up there. Go get the treasure. Doesn't it look pretty?"* If you wait long enough, an [Orc bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(dead)#Orc_Male "Skyrim:Bandit (dead)") will take the bait and fall down in the chamber, dying immediately. A frustrated Sild will comment: *"Well...that's disappointing. This one didn't survive the fall either. No matter. Another one will be along any time now."* He will then keep wandering around the cage, hoping for more victims, but nothing else will happen. Note that Sild is hard to sneak up on, so just get as close to him as possible, then fight and kill him. |

### The Truth About Sild

After battling Sild, make sure to claim the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Rannveigs_Fast_Key "Skyrim:Rannveigs Fast Key") if you haven't picked it up already. Notice the dead body of [Sild's assistant](/wiki/Skyrim:Sild%27s_Assistant "Skyrim:Sild's Assistant") near the cage, then examine the chamber for answers. The rows of cages contain more dead bandits, a dead [dog](/wiki/Skyrim:Dog "Skyrim:Dog"), a dead [Wood Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Elf_(dead) "Skyrim:Wood Elf (dead)"), and a dead [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton_(dead) "Skyrim:Breton (dead)"). Most importantly, examine the table next to the [Alchemy Lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") for *[Sild's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Sild%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Sild's Journal")* to learn the truth of Sild's sadistic activities. Lastly, unlock the boss-leveled chest for your reward, and check the table for an [Unusual Gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") and the [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") skill book *[Horror of Castle Xyr](/wiki/Skyrim:Horror_of_Castle_Xyr "Skyrim:Horror of Castle Xyr")*. When all is said and done, head east and, when you reach the wooden door, open it and head south. In the last room, a door leads outside to a small ledge east of the main entrance.

## Notes

- Learning the word of Kyne's Peace can be done after or before confronting Sild. The trap door is before the word wall, but you can either walk on the edge of the floor or jump over the trap door making it possible to run past the door without falling down.

## Bugs

- The quest is never shut down when Sild the Warlock dies.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

- All of the quest stages are empty: 0, 10, 20, 25, 27, 30.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage dunRannveigQST stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest dunRannveigQST`.

# Skyrim:Rannveig's Fast

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Nordic Ruin.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Nordic_Ruin.png) | Nordic Ruin: Rannveig's Fast ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Rannveig%27s+Fast)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | Never (storage is [safe](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Safe_Locations "Skyrim:Containers")) |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 8 |
| Occupants | |
| [Subjugated Ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Subjugated_Ghost "Skyrim:Subjugated Ghost"), [Ghost Adventurer‎](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost_Adventurer "Skyrim:Ghost Adventurer"), [Skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"), [Sild the Warlock](/wiki/Skyrim:Sild_the_Warlock "Skyrim:Sild the Warlock") | |

| *[Horror of Castle Xyr](/wiki/Skyrim:Horror_of_Castle_Xyr "Skyrim:Horror of Castle Xyr")* [Unusual Gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") | |

Rannveig's Fast

**Rannveig's Fast** is a small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") east-northeast of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead") containing [subjugated ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Subjugated_Ghost "Skyrim:Subjugated Ghost") and [Sild the Warlock](/wiki/Skyrim:Sild_the_Warlock "Skyrim:Sild the Warlock"). It contains only one zone, *[Rannveig's Fast](#Rannveig.27s_Fast)*.

Its [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") teaches part of the [Kyne's Peace](/wiki/Skyrim:Kyne%27s_Peace "Skyrim:Kyne's Peace") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts").

## Related Quests

- **[Arniel's Endeavor](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor")**: Uncover an ancient Dwemer secret. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned")**: Find the [24 gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") to restore the Crown of Barenziah.
- **[Rannveig's Fast](/wiki/Skyrim:Rannveig%27s_Fast_(quest) "Skyrim:Rannveig's Fast (quest)")**: Claim the [force of power](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") from Rannveig's Fast.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

There are three subjugated ghosts and a [ghost adventurer‎](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost_Adventurer "Skyrim:Ghost Adventurer") guarding the exterior of the barrow. Traveling from Rorikstead, you will encounter the first subjugated ghost on the path shortly before reaching the first set of stairs leading up to the entrance. On the next level up are two more subjugated ghosts, with the ghost adventurer on the highest level of the exterior. There are several barrels on various levels and an old camp consisting of two tents and an extinguished campfire on the same level as the entrance. Above the entrance a spellcasting [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") who carries a random low-level staff can be found.

### Rannveig's Fast

You enter into a large room with natural lighting from the outside through holes in the ceiling. There are a number of stone pillars supporting the roof and quite a bit of plant material covering the floor including two [red mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower") and a [blue mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"). There is nothing else of interest in this first room. The next corridor is to the north and descends some steps before ending with a wooden slated wall; the path continues around this wall to the right. Just past the wall there is a subjugated ghost standing in front of a stone table holding a troll skull, a [potion of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), a random potion and a leveled healing potion. To the right of the table is an [urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn"). The corridor continues to the north, down some more steps. At the bottom there are three [burial urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn") with a random potion and a [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health") among them.

The corridor continues to the east before opening out onto a balcony with stairs leading down to a large room with a subjugated ghost patrolling and plant material covering a large portion of the floor. There are several opened sarcophagi with [dead draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Draugr "Skyrim:Containers") on the ground. Among the plants is a [thistle](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle "Skyrim:Thistle") and at the far end of the room you can see the word wall and a [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). If you approach the chest and word wall down the middle, you will activate a [trap door](/wiki/Skyrim:Trap_Door "Skyrim:Trap Door") in the darkest part of the floor. The chest is unlocked and empty, just there as bait for the trap which will drop you quite a way into a locked cage with several dead [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). There is an apprentice-locked wooden door on the south wall which opens into a small room with an unlocked chest, a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") and a dead draugr. Opposite this door is a doorway in the north wall that immediately turns to the east and splits with a closed gate to the left and to the right a corridor that twists and turns and climbs several flights of stairs before leading to a small room that contains a lever that operates the closed gate previously seen. There is also a doorway that leads to a walkway above the room with the word wall. The walkway leads across to another small room containing a subjugated ghost, a dead bandit whose hand is reaching for a [diamond](/wiki/Skyrim:Diamond "Skyrim:Diamond") inside a stone bowl. Next to the bowl is a bookcase with an apprentice-locked chest partially on the bottom shelf with two potions of minor healing on the shelf above.

Backtrack to the previously gated path and proceed down the steps to another corridor heading east down some more stairs; there is a subjugated ghost guarding the top of this corridor. At the bottom of the first flight of stairs the corridor turns to the south and continues down several more flights of stairs before opening out into a room with a wooden door opposite you and a lit brazier on your left. Most of the room is off to your right and you will see Sild the Warlock roaming around some cages, including the one that you would have fallen into if you fell through the trap door. There are bookcases on either side of the room between where you enter and where you can see him, the one on the right has a potion of minor healing on a shelf, past this on the right is a stone table with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), a potion of minor healing and a [potion of regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration"). If you approach sneaking and undetected, Sild will say, "I know you're up there. Go get the treasure. Doesn't it look pretty?" At this point a body will drop into the circular cage and he will complain, saying "Well... that's disappointing. This one didn't survive the fall either. No matter. Another one will be along any time now." Just past the table the room is split in half by twin gates, with the left half being closed, but the right gate being open. On the far side of the pillar that separates them is a pull chain that operates these gates.

You'll next pass four cages, with two on either side. The first cage on the left contains a dead bandit. The next on the right has been destroyed by a cave-in and the second on the left is standing empty and open. Next to this is an expert-locked chest and table containing an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"), *[Sild's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Sild%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Sild's Journal")*, a copy of the [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Horror of Castle Xyr](/wiki/Skyrim:Horror_of_Castle_Xyr "Skyrim:Horror of Castle Xyr")*, an enchanted iron dagger, three random poisons and an [unusual gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem"). Next to the table is a bookcase with two potions of minor healing, a poison and a copy of *[The Aetherium Wars](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Aetherium_Wars "Skyrim:The Aetherium Wars")*. In the center of this end of the room is the large circular expert-locked cage with four dead bandits in it. To the right of this cage is the corpse of [Sild's assistant](/wiki/Skyrim:Sild%27s_Assistant "Skyrim:Sild's Assistant"), and between her and the circular cage is a [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Satchel "Skyrim:Satchel") containing a copy of the [Rannveigs Fast key](/wiki/Skyrim:Rannveigs_Fast_Key "Skyrim:Rannveigs Fast Key"), which will open all of the cages in this room. Farther to the right are four more cages, three locked and one standing open. One contains a [dead Wood Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Elf_(dead) "Skyrim:Wood Elf (dead)") and one a dead [dog](/wiki/Skyrim:Dog "Skyrim:Dog"). There is a locked cage containing a dead bandit behind the circular cage. To the left are four final cages, three locked and one standing empty and open. In one of these cages is a [dead Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton_(dead) "Skyrim:Breton (dead)") with a [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health"). Between the first bookcase and the four cages on the left is a second bookcase, but it contains nothing of interest. Sild also carries a copy of the Rannveigs *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]* Fast key.

All the way back to the eastern end of this area where you entered, there is an unlocked wooden door leading to the south and up some steps before turning to the west and continuing up several more flights of stairs. There is a subjugated ghost patrolling here, even if Sild is dead. At the top of the stairs there is a wooden door on your right that leads up to a small room containing a dead draugr. On the left of the previous corridor is an expert-locked iron door that is opened using Rannveig's Fast key and leads into a room containing a stone table with two potions of minor healing and an unlocked chest on it. To the right of this is an empty bookcase. In the southwest corner is an iron door that leads outside. If you turn and face the door as soon as you exit, you will find four samples of [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") growing. Using this exit places you near [Drelas' Cottage](/wiki/Skyrim:Drelas%27_Cottage "Skyrim:Drelas' Cottage").

## Notes

- Even after Sild is slain, the subjugated ghosts continue to function and remain unwillingly hostile.
- If you are skilled in archery, it may be beneficial to fall through the trap door. Keep your bow drawn as you approach the word wall and fall into the trap, and when you land, Sild and his assistant will be right in front of you. The holes in the cage are wide enough to fire through, and they won't be able to get to you inside the cage, possibly allowing you to kill them even before Sild has finished talking. You can then open the cage and loot their bodies for the key and other items. If the cage is not already unlocked, their bodies will fall close enough to it to access from inside the cage.
- If you want to use the numerous adept/expert-level cage locks in the dungeon to train your lockpicking skills, pass the key to your follower (if they fell into the pit with you) or stash the key in a container before attempting to open any of the cages, as you cannot drop keys from your inventory, and this key opens every cage in the room.
- With the [Bone Wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Wolf "Skyrim:Bone Wolf") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, two hostile bone wolves and a skeleton mage may spawn at the graveyard uphill from the entrance, instead of the skeleton warriors and/or archers that normally appear.

## Bugs

- The subjugated ghosts are revealed by the [Detect Life](/wiki/Skyrim:Detect_Life_(spell) "Skyrim:Detect Life (spell)") spell rather than the [Detect Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Detect_Dead "Skyrim:Detect Dead") spell.
- When you approach the word wall, the word may be absorbed as normal but not appear in the shout menu and be permanently unavailable to unlock.
  -  This can be fixed by using the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") command `teachword shoutID`, where `shoutID` is `6029d` (Kaan), `6029e` (Drem), or `6029f` (Ov). The word will appear in your shout menu and you will be able to unlock it.
- When falling through the trap door, you will see the message "Door closed and Sild moved", a debugging note remaining from the dungeon's development.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.6, fixes this bug.
- The ghosts and containers outside of the dungeon may respawn despite it being classed as a "no reset zone".
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.
- The ghosts do not drop proper ghost loot or turn into the right kind of ash piles when killed. **?**
- Sometimes the gates can be opened without lockpicking or a key.

# Skyrim:Rare Gifts

## Overview

| ID: | Favor110 |

Get a [mammoth tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Tusk "Skyrim:Mammoth Tusk") for [Ysolda](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda "Skyrim:Ysolda").

## Radiant Options

This is a radiant quest which you can receive from any of the following people. The books have a fixed location the quest marker points to, but returning any copy will do. You must find the other items on your own. **Note**: Only one radiant quest of this type can be assigned at any given time. You must clear the radiant quest from your miscellaneous quests in order to be eligible to receive another of the same type.

| Region | Location | Quest Giver | Quest Item | Dialogue Trigger | Reward |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"), [House of Clan Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:House of Clan Shatter-Shield") | [Torbjorn Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Torbjorn_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:Torbjorn Shatter-Shield") | [Amulet of Arkay](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_Arkay "Skyrim:Amulet of Arkay") | "Your wife is in mourning?" | Leveled amount of gold |
| [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") | [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"), [Jarl's Longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl%27s_Longhouse_(Falkreath) "Skyrim:Jarl's Longhouse (Falkreath)") | [Siddgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Siddgeir "Skyrim:Siddgeir")[†](#intnote_byoh) | [Black-Briar Mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead") | "You're the Jarl? I'm looking for work." | Two or three leveled potions |
| [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") | [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), [Castle Dour](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour") | [Captain Aldis](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Aldis "Skyrim:Captain Aldis") | *[The Mirror](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mirror "Skyrim:The Mirror")* | "Are you with the Legion?" | Leveled amount of gold |
| [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") | [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"), [Jorgen and Lami's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorgen_and_Lami%27s_House "Skyrim:Jorgen and Lami's House") | [Lami](/wiki/Skyrim:Lami "Skyrim:Lami") | *[Song of the Alchemists](/wiki/Skyrim:Song_of_the_Alchemists "Skyrim:Song of the Alchemists")* | "How long have you studied alchemy?" | One point [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") skill increase |
| [The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") | [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"), [Rustleif's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Rustleif%27s_House "Skyrim:Rustleif's House") | [Rustleif](/wiki/Skyrim:Rustleif "Skyrim:Rustleif") | *[Night Falls on Sentinel](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Falls_on_Sentinel "Skyrim:Night Falls on Sentinel")* | "You in charge of this forge?" | One point [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") skill increase |
| [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") | [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), [Ysolda's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda%27s_House "Skyrim:Ysolda's House") | [Ysolda](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda "Skyrim:Ysolda") | [Mammoth Tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Tusk "Skyrim:Mammoth Tusk") | "You're looking to become a merchant?" | One point [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") skill increase |

[†](#note_byoh) Siddgeir must be Jarl of Falkreath for him to give this quest. Receiving the [*Letter from Jarl Siddgeir of Falkreath*](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Jarl_(Jarl%27s_Name)_of_(Jarl%27s_City) "Skyrim:Letter from Jarl (Jarl's Name) of (Jarl's City)")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") at level 9 also makes it impossible to acquire this quest, even if you don't read it.

## Quick Walkthrough

All of the items can be found in multiple places in the game. For more thorough lists of locations, see the item's page.

### Amulet of Arkay

There is a guaranteed [Amulet of Arkay](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_Arkay "Skyrim:Amulet of Arkay") at [Wayward Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Wayward_Pass "Skyrim:Wayward Pass") at the [Shrine of Arkay](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Arkay "Skyrim:Shrine of Arkay"). You can also obtain one easily by starting [The Taste of Death](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Taste_of_Death "Skyrim:The Taste of Death") in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth").

**Note**: Be careful when bringing the amulet back to [Torbjorn Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Torbjorn_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:Torbjorn Shatter-Shield"). The quest marker may indicate that you should enter his house, the door of which may be unlocked, but if you enter you may be treated as a trespasser with no option to tell Torbjorn or his wife what your errand is. Meet him on the street during the day instead.

### Black-Briar Mead

[Black-Briar Mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead") can be found in large quantities or bought at the [Black-Briar Meadery](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Meadery "Skyrim:Black-Briar Meadery"), and are guaranteed in other locations as well, most closely in [Lod's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Lod%27s_House "Skyrim:Lod's House") (on the table with the [private letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Private_Letter "Skyrim:Private Letter") required by [Dengeir of Stuhn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dengeir_of_Stuhn "Skyrim:Dengeir of Stuhn")'s quest [Some Light Theft](/wiki/Skyrim:Some_Light_Theft "Skyrim:Some Light Theft")). They may also be bought from most innkeeper merchants. There is also one at the end of the cave in [Unbound](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound "Skyrim:Unbound"), right where you are told to sneak past the bear.

### Mammoth Tusk

If you are willing to steal, you can find a [mammoth tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Tusk "Skyrim:Mammoth Tusk") in several places in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"):

- [Dragonsreach Jarl's Quarters](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach") — go upstairs and into the main room then head into the room to your right; the tusk is atop the bookcases to the right of the door
- [Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr") — on the table in the left room
- [The Bannered Mare](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bannered_Mare "Skyrim:The Bannered Mare") — located on top of a bookshelf right behind the counter; jump on the rafters from the room for rent and pluck it off the shelf

If you'd prefer not to steal one and are unable or unwilling to kill a [mammoth](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth "Skyrim:Mammoth"), [Halted Stream Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Halted_Stream_Camp "Skyrim:Halted Stream Camp") just north of Whiterun contains several mammoth tusks. [Belethor](/wiki/Skyrim:Belethor "Skyrim:Belethor"), the general goods merchant, has a chance of stocking one if you're willing to pay for it. With [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire"), a free one can be found in the [Main Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Main_Hall#Main_Hall "Skyrim:Main Hall") of your home, if you build one. With [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"), one can be found in [Severin Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Severin_Manor "Skyrim:Severin Manor"), and is free to take after you take ownership.

### The Mirror

After accepting this quest, a copy of *[The Mirror](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mirror "Skyrim:The Mirror")* can be found in [Windhelm's Palace of Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:Palace_of_the_Kings "Skyrim:Palace of the Kings"). This is where your quest marker will point you, but it will count as stealing unless you are [Thane of Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Eastmarch "Skyrim:Thane of Eastmarch"). [Captain Aldis](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Aldis "Skyrim:Captain Aldis") *will* accept a stolen copy.

Copies may also be found on the bookshelf in the sleeping area of [Broken Tower Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Tower_Redoubt "Skyrim:Broken Tower Redoubt") in [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach"), or in
[Forsaken Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsaken_Cave "Skyrim:Forsaken Cave") in [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale"), over a table in the first tomb's zone.

With [Hendraheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Hendraheim "Skyrim:Hendraheim"), another copy can be found on the table towards right side end of the hall of the [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Hendraheim_(place) "Skyrim:Hendraheim (place)").

### Night Falls on Sentinel

A copy of *[Night Falls on Sentinel](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Falls_on_Sentinel "Skyrim:Night Falls on Sentinel")* will spawn on a crate in [Swindler's Den](/wiki/Skyrim:Swindler%27s_Den "Skyrim:Swindler's Den") after accepting the quest. Copies may also be found in a bandit camp near [The Guardian Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Guardian_Stones "Skyrim:The Guardian Stones"), and in [Volunruud](/wiki/Skyrim:Volunruud "Skyrim:Volunruud") during the quest [Silenced Tongues](/wiki/Skyrim:Silenced_Tongues "Skyrim:Silenced Tongues").

### Song of the Alchemists

Unfortunately, *[Song of the Alchemists](/wiki/Skyrim:Song_of_the_Alchemists "Skyrim:Song of the Alchemists")* cannot be obtained without stealing in the base game. After activating this quest, a copy spawns in the [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College") on the main floor, to the right from the entrance on the counter (a blue book). It is not marked as stolen, but you will still incur the penalties of stealing if you are caught taking it. The book can also be stolen from [Anise's Cabin](/wiki/Skyrim:Anise%27s_Cabin "Skyrim:Anise's Cabin") near [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood").

If you have the [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") expansion, a copy which does not require stealing can be found in [Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha "Skyrim:Apocrypha"), inside the Black Book called *[Waking Dreams](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha_(Waking_Dreams) "Skyrim:Apocrypha (Waking Dreams)")*, in Chapter III.

A copy of the book can also be found in the hidden alchemy laboratory of [Goldenhills Plantation](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenhills_Plantation "Skyrim:Goldenhills Plantation").

## Notes

- [Halted Stream Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Halted_Stream_Camp "Skyrim:Halted Stream Camp") is the location of a [bounty quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Bandit_Boss "Skyrim:Bounty: Bandit Boss"), possible location of a [Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Bandits) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Bandits)") quest from [Amren](/wiki/Skyrim:Amren "Skyrim:Amren"), and possible location of the [Amulet of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Amulet of the Moon") quest, making it easy to complete multiple quests at once if you choose to find your mammoth tusk there. It is also one of only two locations where the [Transmute](/wiki/Skyrim:Transmute "Skyrim:Transmute") spell tome may be found.
- If Hearthfire is installed, then the Jarl of Falkreath will send you a [message via courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Jarl_(Jarl%27s_Name)_of_(Jarl%27s_City) "Skyrim:Letter from Jarl (Jarl's Name) of (Jarl's City)") once you have become level 9, as long as you have not yet started the Falkreath thane quest. If Rare Gifts is in your journal when the courier is given the message, you will fail the quest and it will be removed from your journal. Reading the note the courier gives you will start the quest [Build Your Own Home](/wiki/Skyrim:Build_Your_Own_Home "Skyrim:Build Your Own Home").
- You must have the item in your inventory for the quest giver's quest pointer and dialogue to display.

## Bugs

- If you complete the Stormcloaks quest [Battle for Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Solitude "Skyrim:Battle for Solitude"), Captain Aldis will no longer be part of the city and the indication arrow for you to follow will lead to a blank floor, where Aldis previously stood.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, addresses this issue. This quest will fail as soon as Battle for Solitude is started.
  -  Captain Aldis can be spawned again using the console command `player.placeatme 00041FB8`. Afterwards, you can speak with him about quests like normal.
  -  An alternative is to type `SetObjectiveCompleted Favor110 10 1` in the console to complete the quest and then to remove *The Mirror* from your inventory by typing `player.additem 0001AFDE -1`.
- It seems likely that Siddgeir was intended to give a leveled piece of armor as a reward, however he gives potions instead. It's also possible that this was a last-minute change.

  **Mod Notes**: The FavorRewardArmor property on TIF\_\_00090DEE is set to FavorRewardPotion.

## Quest Stages

| Rare Gifts (Favor110) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Bring one <Alias=QuestItem> to <Alias.ShortName=QuestGiver> |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 20, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage Favor110 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest Favor110`.

Raven Rock Mine

**Raven Rock Mine** is a small [ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony "Skyrim:Ebony") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") in northern [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") initially containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"), and the [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") [Zahkriisos](/wiki/Skyrim:Zahkriisos_(creature) "Skyrim:Zahkriisos (creature)"). It contains only one zone, *[Raven Rock Mine](#Raven_Rock_Mine)*.

Its [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") teaches part of the [Dragon Aspect](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Aspect "Skyrim:Dragon Aspect") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"). There are two entrances to the mine, with the exterior entrance in Raven Rock and another entrance inside [Bloodskal Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodskal_Barrow "Skyrim:Bloodskal Barrow"). Much of the interior of the barrow can initially be accessed from the barrow's own exterior entrance, but the deepest section of the barrow can only initially be accessed from the mine, as reflected in the walkthrough below. A tiny separate room in the barrow with an upright sarcophagus containing a [stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim "Skyrim:Stalhrim") deposit flanked by two large [urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn") can also only be accessed from the mine, as also described in the walkthrough below.
