## Related Quests

- **[An Axe to Find](/wiki/Skyrim:An_Axe_to_Find "Skyrim:An Axe to Find")**: Retrieve an [ancient Nordic pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nordic_Pickaxe "Skyrim:Ancient Nordic Pickaxe") for [Glover Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Glover_Mallory "Skyrim:Glover Mallory").
- **[Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book_(quest) "Skyrim:Black Book (quest)")**: Retrieve a Black Book from a dungeon.
- **[Black Book: The Winds of Change](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Winds_of_Change_(quest) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Winds of Change (quest)")**: Learn the [Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Winds_of_Change_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Winds of Change (book)")'s hidden knowledge.
- **[The Final Descent](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Final_Descent "Skyrim:The Final Descent")**: Find out what happened to the [great-grandfather](/wiki/Skyrim:Gratian_Caerellius "Skyrim:Gratian Caerellius") of [Crescius Caerellius](/wiki/Skyrim:Crescius_Caerellius "Skyrim:Crescius Caerellius").
- **[Lost Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Knowledge "Skyrim:Lost Knowledge")**: Retrieve the [Black Books](/wiki/Lore:Black_Book "Lore:Black Book") for [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth").
- **[Pain in the Necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Pain_in_the_Necklace "Skyrim:Pain in the Necklace")**: Find [East Empire pendants](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Pendant "Skyrim:East Empire Pendant") for [Fethis Alor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fethis_Alor "Skyrim:Fethis Alor").

### Exterior

To the left of the path leading north between [Ienth Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ienth_Farm "Skyrim:Ienth Farm") and [Alor House](/wiki/Skyrim:Alor_House "Skyrim:Alor House") toward the mine is the farm's ash yam field, while to the right of the path is a [trama root](/wiki/Skyrim:Trama_Root "Skyrim:Trama Root"), a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block"), a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") on top of an unusable barrel, and a [smelter](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter"). In front of the entrance are many unusable barrels and crates, including two crates marked with the [East Empire Company](/wiki/Lore:East_Empire_Company "Lore:East Empire Company") emblem, and another trama root. A pair of lit braziers flank the entrance.

### Raven Rock Mine

The entrance leads into a tunnel descending to the north past several unusable barrels and crates, with one crate and a sign on the wall bearing the mark of the East Empire Company. At the bottom, turn west and enter a habitable area serving as a base camp for exploration of the mine.

Typical marriage

The first time you enter the mine, you will overhear an argument between [Aphia Velothi](/wiki/Skyrim:Aphia_Velothi "Skyrim:Aphia Velothi") and her husband [Crescius Caerellius](/wiki/Skyrim:Crescius_Caerellius "Skyrim:Crescius Caerellius"). Crescius wants to search the mine, but his wife is worried that he will get killed. Speaking with Aphia will give you insight into their relationship, as well as the history of the mine, her husband, and his family. Speaking with Crescius will initiate the quest [The Final Descent](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Final_Descent "Skyrim:The Final Descent"). If the quest [An Axe to Find](/wiki/Skyrim:An_Axe_to_Find "Skyrim:An Axe to Find") is active, you may recover an [ancient Nordic pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nordic_Pickaxe "Skyrim:Ancient Nordic Pickaxe") from Crescius while talking to him; this will prove useful when exploring the mine. Crescius will also give you the [Raven Rock Mine key](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock_Mine_Key "Skyrim:Raven Rock Mine Key") during the conversation.

Into the hole

Along the south wall, a copy of *[History of Raven Rock, Vol. I](/wiki/Skyrim:History_of_Raven_Rock,_Vol._I "Skyrim:History of Raven Rock, Vol. I")* is on the floor between two benches, with two sacks beneath one of the benches. Along the north wall, a small shelving unit on a table holds two loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). To the left of the table is a set of shelves holding various items of clothing, two [leather helmets](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Helmet "Skyrim:Leather Helmet"), and copies of *[Lives of the Saints](/wiki/Skyrim:Lives_of_the_Saints "Skyrim:Lives of the Saints")* and *[The Red Year, Vol. I](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Red_Year,_Vol._I "Skyrim:The Red Year, Vol. I")*, with a fish barrel to the left of the set of shelves. A flight of wooden stairs leads up to a loft. Under the stairs are more barrels, crates, and open boxes, one of which contains a sample of [iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore"). One of the crates has a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") on top, and three more pickaxes hang from a row of six weapon racks in the northwest corner. In the loft, mechanisms for lowering and raising buckets into and out of the mine below are on the walls. In the southwest corner is a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), and in the northwest corner is a table holding a copy of *[The Poison Song, Book III](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Poison_Song,_Book_III "Skyrim:The Poison Song, Book III")*. An [East Empire Company strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Strongbox "Skyrim:East Empire Company Strongbox") is beneath the table, and a sack is to the left of the table. Three more pickaxes hang from racks between the grindstone and the table.

Blocked!

The wooden stairs next to the fish barrel lead down to a series of wooden ramps descending into the mine. After passing an illuminated crate holding a mead barrel on a platform, you will reach a fork in the path. To the left heading south are some exhausted ore deposits, a table holding a sample of iron ore, and a skeever. To the right heading north is the continuation of the descending walkway, with three frostbite spiders and some [flammable gas](/wiki/Skyrim:Flammable_Gas "Skyrim:Flammable Gas") along the way. Eventually your path will be blocked by wooden slats ahead. Remove these with magic or a weapon, and continue to a chamber with a key-locked gate. An East Empire Company strongbox is on a crate to the right of the gate. The gate can only be unlocked with the Raven Rock Mine key you received from Crescius. Opening the gate allows you to enter the Nordic ruins mentioned in the letter received from Crescius at the start of the quest. Shallow water covers the floor of the crypt ahead. Follow the wall to the left to find a [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") in an upper burial alcove. A draugr slumbers in an alcove nearby; three other sleeping draugr in the area will be roused by any fighting.

A [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") that activates a [spike wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Spike_Wall "Skyrim:Spike Wall") trap is in the middle of the passage onward. Pass by the spike wall and up a flight of stairs with a [dead draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Draugr "Skyrim:Containers") lying at the top. The path turns to the west at this point and continues to a chamber with four draugr-occupied thrones; two thrones are facing you, and two are just behind facing the other direction. Two of the four draugr on the thrones are dead, and another dead draugr lies in front of the thrones, while a third active draugr roams in the distance. A random potion and a rare [potion of waterwalking](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Waterwalking "Skyrim:Potion of Waterwalking") are in a basin between the thrones. After disposing of the three active draugr, optionally loot three [burial urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn") and two more dead draugr in and near the wall alcoves in the area, then climb the path to the west through a doorway next to a large urn into a circular chamber with a metal grate covering most of the center of the room. Around the perimeter of the room are thrones occupied by draugr. Five of the draugr will rise while you move about the room, while five dead draugr sit in other thrones or lie on the floor. Along the south wall, among some rubble from a cave-in, is a master-locked chest. The room's exit door is to the west.

Stalhrim deposit

In the next room, two upright sarcophagi are ahead to the left, with a filled [common soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Common_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Common Soul Gem") on a plinth between them. The path twists around to the west to a raised area with two dead draugr seated on thrones and two embalming tables between the thrones. One of the dead draugr wears an [ancient Nord helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nord_Helmet "Skyrim:Ancient Nord Helmet") and holds a [honed ancient Nord sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Honed_Ancient_Nord_Sword "Skyrim:Honed Ancient Nord Sword"), and the other dead draugr holds an [ancient Nord bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nord_Bow "Skyrim:Ancient Nord Bow"). On the tables are two more dead draugr, two random potions, a random strength potion, a random soul gem, a sample of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), a [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") flower, a bowl of [vampire dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Dust "Skyrim:Vampire Dust"), a sample of [scaly pholiota](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaly_Pholiota "Skyrim:Scaly Pholiota"), and a random poison, with a large urn to the left of the table on the left. Between the two tables is an upright sarcophagus containing a stalhrim deposit, which you can mine if you have an ancient Nordic pickaxe. Mining this deposit reveals another dead draugr. An [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs") is around the corner along the east wall, with an [ashen grass pod](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashen_Grass_Pod "Skyrim:Ashen Grass Pod") and two bowls of [netch jelly](/wiki/Skyrim:Netch_Jelly "Skyrim:Netch Jelly") on top. The lab is between two sets of shelves. The set of shelves on the left holds a sample of [emperor parasol moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Parasol_Moss "Skyrim:Emperor Parasol Moss"), a [luna moth wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Luna_Moth_Wing "Skyrim:Luna Moth Wing"), a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), a bowl of [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts"), a sample of [scathecraw](/wiki/Skyrim:Scathecraw "Skyrim:Scathecraw"), a sprig of [dragon's tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue"), and a burial urn. The set of shelves on the right holds a bowl of [void salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Void_Salts "Skyrim:Void Salts"), a pot of [spawn ash](/wiki/Skyrim:Spawn_Ash "Skyrim:Spawn Ash"), a potion of waterwalking, a sample of [ash creep cluster](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Creep_Cluster "Skyrim:Ash Creep Cluster"), another luna moth wing, a bowl of [fire salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts"), a [boar tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Boar_Tusk "Skyrim:Boar Tusk"), and a burial urn.

Sparkly

The path continues to the north, climbing to a plateau with two [Sparks](/wiki/Skyrim:Sparks "Skyrim:Sparks") [spellcaster traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Spellcaster_Trap "Skyrim:Spellcaster Trap") flanking the path. Knocking out or removing the filled soul gems will disable the traps. The path then descends into shallow water to a pair of wooden doors. Beyond the doors is a multi-level room with shallow water covering the floor. At the east end of the room is a waterfall, behind which is an apprentice-locked door leading to a single tiny room within Bloodskal Barrow. This room features an upright sarcophagus containing a stalhrim deposit flanked by two large urns; once mined, the deposit reveals a dead draugr. There are no other exits from this room in the barrow. Returning to the mine, a raised area is to the left along the south wall, with a patrolling draugr wandering along it. Engaging the patrolling draugr will cause up to five additional draugr to converge and attack you. Climb up the wooden ramp to a balcony with four upright sarcophagi, two of which have been opened. Along the south wall is a lowered portcullis, and at the east end is a lit fireplace, with a wooden walkway next to the fireplace crossing to the north over the room below. On the far side of the walkway is another balcony. In the northwest corner is an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters") on a sideboard, with an expert-locked chest beneath the enchanter and a potion of waterwalking and a weapon on the floor nearby. Near the edge of the balcony to the south is a plinth with a handle that opens the portcullis on the other side.

Up there

Head back across the walkway and through the open portcullis, which leads to a short corridor ending in a fork. To the left heading east is a room with a plinth surrounded by lit candles holding a *[Spell Tome: Ice Spike](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Ice_Spike "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Ice Spike")*; above the plinth is an upper level with a spellcaster trap visible to the east, which can be disabled safely from here using ranged attacks. To the right heading west is a wooden spiral ramp leading up and onward. Beneath the ramp is an adept-locked chest, a large urn, and a burial urn among the rubble. At the top of the ramp, you will see three pots on a ledge in the northwest corner; if you jump to this ledge, you will find the fourth and final potion of waterwalking behind the pots. On the landing at the top of the ramp is a [long bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Bow "Skyrim:Long Bow") and a quiver of [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow"). In the southwest corner is a bowl on another small ledge you can jump to; a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") is behind the bowl. A wooden wall ahead to the east shields you from the [Lightning Bolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Lightning_Bolt "Skyrim:Lightning Bolt") spellcaster trap seen earlier from below. In a darkened alcove to the right of the wooden wall is a plinth holding a [scroll of fireball](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Fireball "Skyrim:Scroll of Fireball"). Cross over the walkway, bypassing the spellcaster trap, to find a set of shelves in the northeast corner holding a sample of [canis root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root") and a bowl of frost salts, with a large urn to the left of the set of shelves. The east wall directly behind the spellcaster trap has a concealed door, which can be opened using the pull chain among the cobwebs to the left of the door. Beyond the door is a small alcove with a sideboard holding a potion, a chest, and a large coin purse. The path continues through a door to the west into a corridor and across a caged walkway leading north. On the far side of the walkway is a wide corridor with three upright sarcophagi along each side. Three pressure plates on the floor in front of the sarcophagi each activate a [dart trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap"). The stairs ahead to the north ascend to a door, beyond which is an adept-locked chest. The second sarcophagus along the west wall has fallen, revealing a tunnel leading west.

The strange door

Following the tunnel as it twists and turns, you will emerge on a small ledge overlooking a large cavern far below. A large, strange door is visible to the north at the far end of the room between two waterfalls, and a stream cuts through the cavern. Jump down from your perch to the rocky landing below and proceed to the door. In front of the door are the skeletal remains of [Gratian Caerellius](/wiki/Skyrim:Gratian_Caerellius "Skyrim:Gratian Caerellius") lying on a bedroll, with the remains of his assistant [Millius](/wiki/Skyrim:Millius "Skyrim:Millius") at the base of the short set of stairs nearby. Gratian's remains still hold his [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Gratian%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Gratian's Journal") and the [Bloodskal Blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodskal_Blade "Skyrim:Bloodskal Blade"), a unique two-handed greatsword. The journal reveals what Gratian had learned about the blade and how it may be used to open the strange door. Next to Gratian's remains is a [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Satchel "Skyrim:Satchel") and an [elixir of vigor](/wiki/Skyrim:Elixir_of_Vigor "Skyrim:Elixir of Vigor"). Also in the cavern are three dead draugr, as well as a chest to the southeast in the alcove at the end of the stream. Three small cages hanging in front of the door contain a [burnt corpse](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Burnt_Corpse "Skyrim:Containers"), a dead draugr, and a skeleton, all of which can be looted.

The strange door is opened by equipping the Bloodskal Blade, then performing a [power attack](/wiki/Skyrim:Combat#Power_Attacks "Skyrim:Combat") in front of each of the glowing red lines in the door to roughly match the lines' orientation, either vertical (forward attack) or horizontal (strafing attack). Begin with the bottom pair of lines and work upwards. Wait until your stamina gauge is full and aim your cursor at the glowing red line before starting each power attack. Each time you perform a swing correctly, the door will slowly rearrange itself and extinguish the glowing red line that matched your attack.

Once you have completed all seven of the required attacks, the door will open into a long wide corridor lined with seven sets of three [swinging blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Blades "Skyrim:Swinging Blades") in a row. Similar to some traps in Dwemer and other ruins, these blade traps are triggered entirely by proximity, and cannot be disabled by the lever at the far end of the corridor, which only operates the nearby portcullis. The blades will stop after you have reached the lever. If the blades are again approached from the far end, regardless of the state of the portcullis lever, the blades will once again begin swinging, making it very difficult to bring followers past the blades unharmed.

Risen from the dead

The Black Book

Beyond the portcullis is a large water-filled cavern. Ahead to the east is a chest overlooking the water, which contains very little loot. Approaching the chest will cause the [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") [Zahkriisos](/wiki/Skyrim:Zahkriisos_(creature) "Skyrim:Zahkriisos (creature)") to rise from the water in front of you and start attacking you with powerful shock magic. Once you have destroyed him, you can take his [mask](/wiki/Skyrim:Zahkriisos_(item) "Skyrim:Zahkriisos (item)"), which grants its wearer shock resistance of 50% and a boost to shock damage of 25%. At the far end of the cavern to the east is a word wall which teaches part of the Dragon Aspect shout. Under the water are six [Nordic barnacle clusters](/wiki/Skyrim:Passive_Creatures#Nordic_Barnacle_Cluster "Skyrim:Passive Creatures") and two [slaughterfish egg nests](/wiki/Skyrim:Passive_Creatures#Slaughterfish_Egg_Nest "Skyrim:Passive Creatures").

In the west corner of the cavern is a portcullis with a lever; defeating Zahkriisos or using the lever will raise the portcullis. Beyond the portcullis is a room containing a plinth holding the [Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book (book)") *[The Winds of Change](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Winds_of_Change_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Winds of Change (book)")*. Taking the book will transport you to [Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha "Skyrim:Apocrypha") and begin the quest [The Winds of Change](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Winds_of_Change_(quest) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Winds of Change (quest)"). Along the north wall is an arcane enchanter flanked by two stands each holding a soul gem, and a set of shelves holding two random potions, a random helmet, a pair of random boots, and a bowl containing a [petty soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem"), thirteen loose coins, a [garnet](/wiki/Skyrim:Garnet "Skyrim:Garnet"), and an [amethyst](/wiki/Skyrim:Amethyst "Skyrim:Amethyst"). Along the south wall is a sideboard holding two burial urns, with a boss-level chest to the right of the sideboard. In the middle of the room is a waterfall cascading into a grate in the floor, above which is a wooden spiral staircase leading up to an iron door to Bloodskal Barrow.

## Notes

- The four potions of waterwalking here are the only such potions in the entire game. No merchants sell them, and they cannot be crafted.
- The two bowls of netch jelly in the mine are the only guaranteed source of netch jelly in the game that doesn't involve killing netches.
- Another copy of the Bloodskal Blade (`RefID xx027281`) is present behind the word wall, though it is unobtainable through normal means.
- Completing The Final Descent allows the mine to reopen for business. The mine has the second-highest number of ebony ore veins in the game, after [Gloombound Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Gloombound_Mine "Skyrim:Gloombound Mine"). There are nine ebony ore in Raven Rock Mine, three in one alcove and three in another alcove near the top of the mine, the last three are at the very bottom of the mine. Go through the iron door, down the ramp and turn right. There is a new area that was blocked off before completing the quest which contains the last three ore veins. If you are not sure how to locate these areas, just follow the miners. They will go to all three locations to mine ebony.
- Crescius Caerellius partially supports his claim that his grandfather must have died by some means other than a tunnel collapse by stating his belief that the mine's tunnels are too sound for such an event to occur. Though he is correct that his grandfather's disappearance was due to other causes, his confidence in the tunnels may be misplaced: a short distance down the tunnels from the entrance to the mine, you will discover a pair of skeletal arms protruding from beneath a boulder near the tunnel wall, apparently the remains of someone killed by a collapse.

## Bugs

- When returning to the mine from the tiny room in the barrow behind the waterfall, the door displays the destination as "Bloodskal Barrow" instead of "Raven Rock Mine".
- One of the East Empire Company strongboxes can be unlocked with a version of [Brand-Shei's strongbox key](/wiki/Skyrim:Brand-Shei%27s_Strongbox_Key "Skyrim:Brand-Shei's Strongbox Key") that's unavailable in the game.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 1.0.5, fixes this bug.
  - If you have the [Wax Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Wax_Key "Skyrim:Wax Key") [Lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking") perk and unlock this strongbox, you will obtain Brand-Shei's strongbox key.
- The word wall may fail to activate when you approach. The word of power will stop glowing and turn red, but you will not learn the word itself.
  - Saving, exiting, and relaunching the game then loading the save may fix this issue.
  - Learning at least one of the other words of Dragon Aspect before approaching the wall may prevent this bug.
  - Using the [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") shout to speed into the word when its textures are still glowing may allow the word to be learned. This may require a few attempts from different starting points, so be sure to save the game first. Similarly, using the [Silent Roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Silent_Roll "Skyrim:Silent Roll") [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") perk to roll into the word when its textures are still glowing may allow the word to be learned.
  -  PC users can use the "tcl" console command to disable collisions before approaching the wall to allow the word to be learned. However, if you save the game and then use the "tcl" console command while standing within the trigger radius of the wall, then reload that save, the word wall will become bugged even further: the word will not only not be learned, but will also no longer be glowing, despite the "mana flow" effect and sound continuing. In this case, neither "tcl" nor Whirlwind Sprint will allow the word to be learned. Therefore, be sure to save the game while far from the wall.
- If you reenter the mine after everything has respawned, the stalhrim deposit near the alchemy lab may appear to have more stalhrim. However, when you approach, you will not have the option to "mine deposit", but instead will only have the option to "search draugr", as if the deposit were not there.
- If you reenter the mine after everything has respawned, only three of the ebony deposits may have respawned. The other deposits can't be mined, and seem to not actually be present, as you can walk through them, and they don't make a sound when a pickaxe is swung at them manually.
- If you reenter the mine after everything has respawned, the stone door near Gratian's corpse may appear closed again, and you may be unable to reopen it with the Bloodskal Blade. **?**
- The satchel next to Gratian's corpse resets even though it has a quest-related template.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.7, fixes this bug.
- One of the Nordic barnacle clusters and one of the slaughterfish egg nests in the chamber with Zahkriisos can't be harvested.
- The frostbite spiders and skeevers may respawn, which can be deadly to the weak miners.
- The remains of Millius may not spawn. **?**

# Skyrim:Raven Rock

Raven Rock

**Raven Rock** is a [city](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn_Places#Cities "Skyrim:Dragonborn Places") on the southwest coast of [Solstheim](/wiki/Lore:Solstheim "Lore:Solstheim"). It is the first place discovered in the [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") expansion. Once an [East Empire Company](/wiki/Lore:East_Empire_Company "Lore:East Empire Company") mining outpost, it is now a [House Redoran](/wiki/Lore:House_Redoran "Lore:House Redoran") colony. A far cry from the prosperous mining town of the past, Raven Rock has become a mostly forgotten settlement, its ebony mine depleted.

The city consists of a single thoroughfare running from the entrance through [the Bulwark](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bulwark "Skyrim:The Bulwark") in the east to the [Earth Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Earth_Stone "Skyrim:Earth Stone") in the west, following the line of the small adjacent bay. The jail and the Redoran guards' garrison are built into the Bulwark, which is the city's main defense against the ash from the [Red Mountain](/wiki/Lore:Red_Mountain "Lore:Red Mountain").

A curved wooden boardwalk runs along the bay, with a short pier near the center and a longer pier to the east. The [Northern Maiden](/wiki/Skyrim:Northern_Maiden "Skyrim:Northern Maiden"), which plies its trade between Solstheim and the city of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"), is docked at the long pier, and three rowboats are docked elsewhere in the bay. The various shops and services of Raven Rock can be found in the central marketplace around the city's well north of the bay, while the [Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple "Skyrim:Temple") is near the Bulwark to the east. There are many freely available crafting stations outside in the city, including three [wood chopping blocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block"), two [tanning racks](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack"), two [smelters](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter"), a [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge"), a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"), a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), and an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"). These stations are outside [Alor House](/wiki/Skyrim:Alor_House "Skyrim:Alor House"), [Glover Mallory's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Glover_Mallory%27s_House "Skyrim:Glover Mallory's House"), [Ienth Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ienth_Farm "Skyrim:Ienth Farm"), and [Raven Rock Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock_Mine "Skyrim:Raven Rock Mine"), as well as on the long pier.

It is possible to acquire a home here, [Severin Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Severin_Manor "Skyrim:Severin Manor"), after completing the quest [Served Cold](/wiki/Skyrim:Served_Cold "Skyrim:Served Cold").

For historical information on Raven Rock and House Redoran, see the respective lore articles on [Raven Rock](/wiki/Lore:Raven_Rock "Lore:Raven Rock") and [House Redoran](/wiki/Lore:House_Redoran "Lore:House Redoran").

#### Side Quests

- **[A New Debt](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Debt "Skyrim:A New Debt")**: Help [Drovas Relvi](/wiki/Skyrim:Drovas_Relvi "Skyrim:Drovas Relvi") with his debt to [Mogrul](/wiki/Skyrim:Mogrul_(Dragonborn) "Skyrim:Mogrul (Dragonborn)").
- **[Black Book: The Winds of Change](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Winds_of_Change_(quest) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Winds of Change (quest)")**: Learn the [Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Winds_of_Change_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Winds of Change (book)")'s hidden knowledge.
- **[March of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:March_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:March of the Dead")**: Stop the [ash spawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Spawn "Skyrim:Ash Spawn") attacks on Raven Rock.
- **[Served Cold](/wiki/Skyrim:Served_Cold "Skyrim:Served Cold")**: Save [Councilor Morvayn](/wiki/Skyrim:Lleril_Morvayn "Skyrim:Lleril Morvayn") from an assassination plot.
- **[The Final Descent](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Final_Descent "Skyrim:The Final Descent")**: Find out what happened to the [great-grandfather](/wiki/Skyrim:Gratian_Caerellius "Skyrim:Gratian Caerellius") of [Crescius Caerellius](/wiki/Skyrim:Crescius_Caerellius "Skyrim:Crescius Caerellius").

#### Tribunal Temple CC

- **[Ghosts of the Tribunal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal_(quest) "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal"): Decide the fate of a [heretical cult](/wiki/Skyrim:Tribunal_Temple "Skyrim:Tribunal Temple").
- **[Buyer Beware](/wiki/Skyrim:Buyer_Beware "Skyrim:Buyer Beware")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal"): Ambush a meeting to retrieve the [Mask of Vivec](/wiki/Skyrim:Mask_of_Vivec "Skyrim:Mask of Vivec").
- **[Careless Curation](/wiki/Skyrim:Careless_Curation "Skyrim:Careless Curation")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal"): Find the missing Curate to retrieve the [Mask of Sotha Sil](/wiki/Skyrim:Mask_of_Sotha_Sil "Skyrim:Mask of Sotha Sil").
- **[Her Word Against Theirs](/wiki/Skyrim:Her_Word_Against_Theirs "Skyrim:Her Word Against Theirs")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal"): Spread the word of the Goddess [Almalexia](/wiki/Lore:Almalexia "Lore:Almalexia").

#### Dragonborn

- **[Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn_(quest) "Skyrim:Dragonborn (quest)")**: Travel to the island of [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") to find out what's happening there.

#### Side Quests

- **[Reluctant Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Reluctant_Steward "Skyrim:Reluctant Steward")**: Find a new steward for [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") in Raven Rock.

#### Creation Club

- **[My Pet Nix-Hound](/wiki/Skyrim:My_Pet_Nix-Hound "Skyrim:My Pet Nix-Hound")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Nix-Hound "Skyrim:Nix-Hound"): Buy a tame [nix-hound](/wiki/Skyrim:Nix-Hound_(creature) "Skyrim:Nix-Hound (creature)").
- **[Nordic Jewelry](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Jewelry_(quest) "Skyrim:Nordic Jewelry (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Jewelry "Skyrim:Nordic Jewelry"): Learn about Nordic jewelry.
- **[Put A Fork In It](/wiki/Skyrim:Put_A_Fork_In_It "Skyrim:Put A Fork In It")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Sheogorath "Skyrim:Staff of Sheogorath"): Pass [Sheogorath](/wiki/Skyrim:Sheogorath "Skyrim:Sheogorath")'s trial to earn his staff.

## Notes

- The boat ride scene upon arriving here for the first time is absent from [Skyrim VR](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim_VR "Skyrim:Skyrim VR").
- Version 2.1.2 of the [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch") marks the ash yam urns as owned by the village.

## Bugs

- The ominous music heard in [Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha "Skyrim:Apocrypha") was incorrectly assigned to many of the buildings in Raven Rock, despite their unthreatening atmospheres.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 1.0.1, fixes this bug.
- The favor quests here don't improve the dispositions of their respective quest givers.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.1, fixes this bug.

## Achievements

One [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements#Dragonborn "Skyrim:Achievements") is related to Raven Rock:

-  **Raven Rock Owner** (20 points/Bronze) — Own a house in Raven Rock

# Skyrim:Ravenscar Hollow

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Cave.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Cave.png) | Cave: Ravenscar Hollow ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ravenscar+Hollow)) | | |

Entrance to Ravenscar Hollow

**Ravenscar Hollow** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") inhabited by [hagravens](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven") west of the [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy") and due east of the [Steed Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Steed_Stone "Skyrim:The Steed Stone").

It is found by going east along the road that passes [Wolfskull Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolfskull_Cave "Skyrim:Wolfskull Cave") and following the road a ways downhill past a switchback until you see two cairns on the left. A path begins here that winds its way downhill past several more cairns and along the shore to the entrance of the cave.

## Ravenscar Hollow

Ravenscar Hollow interior

Outside the cave, there are several [blue mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower") and a [purple mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") around the piles of rocks marking the start of the path off the main road, with several [spiky grass](/wiki/Skyrim:Spiky_Grass "Skyrim:Spiky Grass") plants, [nightshades](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade"), and a tree stump with [mora tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella") growing on it along the path. There is a leveled [animal](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals") guarding the entrance, and a waterfall just to the right that forms a stream across the path. Outside of the entrance are the typical sharpened stakes, human bones, and goat and skeever heads on stakes found near hagraven dwellings.

Upon entering, there is a darkened tunnel with a pool of water ahead on the left-hand side of the cave. There is nothing of interest in the water. The path follows the shore along the west wall of the cave past a couple [bone chimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Chimes "Skyrim:Bone Chimes") hanging from the ceiling. To the southeast can be seen a raised ledge with stakes along the side. Just past the hanging bone chimes, there is another set of chimes stretched across the path. A short way past this there is an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") against the west wall. The path continues around the water before passing behind a rock pillar and turning to the north; here there are steps up to the raised section, where a [hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven") and a leveled [creature](/wiki/Skyrim:Creatures "Skyrim:Creatures") reside. The hagraven has a copy of the [Ravenscar Hallow cage key](/wiki/Skyrim:Ravenscar_Hallow_Cage_Key "Skyrim:Ravenscar Hallow Cage Key") in her possession. There is a hagraven tent at the rear of the raised section with a dead [skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") in front of it, and a lever in the northeastern corner that opens a hidden door to the left of it.

Beyond the hidden door is another room with a long wooden table immediately on the right with a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), an [enchanter's draught](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanter%27s_Draught "Skyrim:Enchanter's Draught"), a [ruined book](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruined_Book "Skyrim:Ruined Book"), a [ruby](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruby "Skyrim:Ruby"), an [amethyst](/wiki/Skyrim:Amethyst "Skyrim:Amethyst"), and a [garnet](/wiki/Skyrim:Garnet "Skyrim:Garnet") on top. A second potion of minor healing can be found on the ground in front of the table. To the northeast is a [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") trapped in an adept-locked cage, who will spot you as soon as you enter the room and repeatedly ask you to let him out, offering to help you "slaughter the rest of the crows". There is a second (empty) cage beside the first, and against the north wall are two dead bandits and a dead [spriggan](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan"). To the west is a ramp leading up to raised area with another tent on top, while to the northwest is a lower area with two more cages. One of the cages is adept-locked and holds a dead bandit and two potions of minor healing; like the live bandit's cage, this cage may also be opened with the Ravenscar Hallow cage key. There is a hagraven in the lower area, and a second one behind the tent in the upper area. If you released the bandit before clearing the room, he will aid you in killing any enemies before he turns on you, demanding everything you have. A few moments later he automatically begins attacking you. If you released the bandit after defeating the hagravens, he will just go straight to demanding your stuff and then attacking you. This adversary is not a serious threat, as he does not equip the armor he carries, and is armed only with a random "lucky [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger")".

On the lower level near the second set of cages is an unlocked boss [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") next to a long wooden table with a random [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons") and a copy of the [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Art of War Magic](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Art_of_War_Magic "Skyrim:The Art of War Magic")* on top. A [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") is nearby on the ground against the north wall. The tent in the upper area is empty (see [bugs](#Bugs)). Behind the tent is a balcony that overlooks the pool of water in the first room; this can be used as a shortcut back to the exit.

## Notes

- If you are noisy while defeating the first hagraven, it will alert the others in the room behind the secret door. They will likely be attacking the imprisoned bandit.
- Before entering Ravenscar Hollow, there is an iron ore vein located to the left of the cave entrance, on the opposite side of the inlet by the shore.
- There is a [Nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot") growing on a ledge just a few meters above the previously mentioned iron ore vein.

## Bugs

- It is possible to get stuck in the tent on the upper level.
  - You can free yourself with a lot of wiggling. Turning sideways may help.
- Equipping a bow while in the tent may cause the player to become stuck. To fix this, simply unequip the bow. **?**

## Maps

- 

  Ravenscar Hollow

Reach Imperial Camp

**Reach Imperial Camp** is an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Camps "Skyrim:Imperial Camps") in [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach"), located south of [Bthardamz](/wiki/Skyrim:Bthardamz "Skyrim:Bthardamz") and west of [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten").

This camp will only be present if the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") hold [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") and the rest of the Reach, whether through martial might or via the negotiation during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending"). [Imperial Soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Soldier "Skyrim:Imperial Soldier") are camped here under the command of [Legate Emmanuel Admand](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Emmanuel_Admand "Skyrim:Legate Emmanuel Admand"), except during the related quest, when [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") takes command. Like similar Imperial camps that only exist when the hold has changed hands, it has neither a [quartermaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Quartermaster "Skyrim:Imperial Quartermaster") or any [horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Legate Emmanuel Admand](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Emmanuel_Admand "Skyrim:Legate Emmanuel Admand") (commander)  [Imperial Soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Soldier "Skyrim:Imperial Soldier")  [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") (commander)[†](#intnote_Q) |

[†](#note_Q)This person only resides here during the related quest.

## Related Quests

- **[The Battle for Fort Sungard](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Sungard_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Sungard (Imperial)")**: Retake [Fort Sungard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Sungard "Skyrim:Fort Sungard") for the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Reach Imperial Camp

Unlike most camps, this camp is laid out on two levels. The lower level has a campfire with a [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Spit "Skyrim:Cooking Spit") hanging over it, and an [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil") beside the fire. To the north are three small tents containing unowned bed rolls, while to the east is a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"), a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), and a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block"). To the west, on a higher level, is the Legate's tent, containing an owned single bed, with an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") at the foot of the bed and an end table beside it. Farther west is the command tent, containing an end table and a large table covered with a map of Skyrim showing the progress of the civil war and the various forts and cities held by each side. This is where the Legate spends most of their time. To the southeast is the hospital tent, containing two bed rolls, both of which are occupied by wounded soldiers, and an unlocked chest containing various items to treat the sick, including potions of [cure poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Cure_Poison "Skyrim:Cure Poison"), potions of [cure disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Cure_Disease "Skyrim:Cure Disease"), and [leather strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"). Outside the hospital tent is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"). Between the hospital tent and the lower part of the camp is a tree stump with [mora tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella") growing on it, a bird nest containing a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"), and a [juniper](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries") tree. There is a wild leveled [animal](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals") nearby that will often attack the soldiers while they are patrolling around the camp.

Any time [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") is controlled by the Imperials, this camp will not be present. As long as you haven't completed [Joining the Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Joining the Stormcloaks"), you are free to sleep in the small tents.

## Notes

- Two ore veins are near the camp: a [silver ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore "Skyrim:Silver Ore") vein north-northeast of the camp, and an [iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore") vein northeast of the camp.
- This wiki's current Skyrim satellite map only displays the camp's location; the previous one displayed the camp as well.

Reach Stormcloak Camp

**Reach Stormcloak Camp** is a [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Camps "Skyrim:Stormcloak Camps") in [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach"), located west of [Liar's Retreat](/wiki/Skyrim:Liar%27s_Retreat "Skyrim:Liar's Retreat") and northeast of [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten").

The camp is normally commanded by [Kottir Red-Shoal](/wiki/Skyrim:Kottir_Red-Shoal "Skyrim:Kottir Red-Shoal"), except during the related quests, at which point [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist") will assume command.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Kottir Red-Shoal](/wiki/Skyrim:Kottir_Red-Shoal "Skyrim:Kottir Red-Shoal") (commander)  [Stormcloak Quartermaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Quartermaster "Skyrim:Stormcloak Quartermaster")  [Stormcloak Soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Soldier "Skyrim:Stormcloak Soldier")  [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist") (commander) [†](#intnote_Q) |

[†](#note_Q)This person only resides here during the related quests.

## Related Quests

- **[Compelling Tribute](/wiki/Skyrim:Compelling_Tribute_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Compelling Tribute (Stormcloaks)")**: Blackmail a [Talos worshipper](/wiki/Skyrim:Raerek "Skyrim:Raerek") into helping the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The Battle for Fort Sungard](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Sungard_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Sungard (Stormcloaks)")**: Take [this fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Sungard "Skyrim:Fort Sungard") in the name of the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Reach Stormcloak Camp

It is a typical Stormcloak camp, consisting of a central campfire with a [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Spit "Skyrim:Cooking Spit") hanging over it, around which the rest of the camp is arranged. To the north and east of the campfire are three small tents containing unowned hay piles. Between the small tents is the command tent, containing a lit brazier, a round table, and a large table covered with a map of Skyrim showing the progress of the civil war and the various forts and cities held by each side. This is where the commander spends most of their time. Southwest of the fire is the hospital tent, which contains three hay piles occupied by wounded soldiers and an unlocked chest containing various items to treat the sick, including potions of [cure poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Cure_Poison "Skyrim:Cure Poison"), potions of [cure disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Cure_Disease "Skyrim:Cure Disease"), and [leather strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"). Beside the tent is a table with a built-in [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") and a low table holding a random [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health") and a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"). Down the hill behind the hospital tent is a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block"). Beside the block are two picketed [horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses "Skyrim:Horses"). Unlike other camps, taking them is not considered stealing; however, if the camp no longer exists, the horses will still be present, and taking them will then be considered stealing. West of the campfire is the commander's tent, containing an owned bedroll, an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), and an end table. To the right of the commander's tent are some barrels. Farther west is the workstation for the [Stormcloak quartermaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Quartermaster "Skyrim:Stormcloak Quartermaster"), consisting of an [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil"), a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), and a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"). A long wooden table and a crate hold various [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Weapons "Skyrim:Iron Weapons") and [steel weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Weapons "Skyrim:Steel Weapons") and [armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor").

Any time [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") is controlled by the Stormcloaks, this camp will not be present. As long as you haven't completed [Joining the Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Legion "Skyrim:Joining the Legion"), you are free to sleep in the small tents and trade with the quartermaster.

## Bugs

- The horse spawn point is partially imbedded in the ground which can cause the horses to float above the ground and fall to their deaths.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.

| ReachcliffCaveExterior, ReachcliffCave01, ReachcliffCaveExit | |
| Region | |
| [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") | |
| Location | |
| East-southeast of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") Northeast of [Dushnikh Yal](/wiki/Skyrim:Dushnikh_Yal "Skyrim:Dushnikh Yal") | |
| [Ore Veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") | |
| # of [Iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore") | 1 |

Reachcliff Cave

**Reachcliff Cave** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") east-southeast of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"). It contains only one zone, *[Reachcliff Cave](#Reachcliff_Cave)*.

The cave also features the [shrine](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Shrines "Skyrim:Daedric Shrines") to the [Daedric Prince](/wiki/Lore:Daedric_Princes "Lore:Daedric Princes") [Namira](/wiki/Lore:Namira "Lore:Namira"). When not on the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Taste_of_Death "Skyrim:The Taste of Death"), the cave can only be partly explored. The dungeon includes two map markers, "Reachcliff Cave" [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Reachcliff+Cave&zoom=14&legacy=true) and "Reachcliff Secret Entrance" [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Reachcliff+Secret+Entrance&zoom=14&legacy=true), counting as two separate locations for the "Locations Discovered" statistic.

## Related Quests

- **[The Taste of Death](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Taste_of_Death "Skyrim:The Taste of Death")**: Prepare a [feast](/wiki/Skyrim:Brother_Verulus "Skyrim:Brother Verulus") for the [Lady of Decay](/wiki/Lore:Namira "Lore:Namira").

### Exterior

A path to the entrance branches to the south from the main road heading west to Markarth. The winding path starts opposite the bridge to [Karthspire Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthspire_Camp "Skyrim:Karthspire Camp"), and branches to the west near one of several cairns along the path. The western path passes under two large intact stone arches, with three upright stones and three [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool") fungus near the cave entrance. The cave has another entrance north of [Dushnikh Yal](/wiki/Skyrim:Dushnikh_Yal "Skyrim:Dushnikh Yal"), with a map marker called **Reachcliff Secret Entrance**; however, this entrance doesn't exist until you use it as an exit from within the cave. Near this secret entrance are two leveled [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals").

### Reachcliff Cave

The entrance passage descends to the south in what appears to be a mined area, with wooden posts shoring up the sides and roof. The passage leads out onto a ledge overlooking a chamber, with an open sarcophagus on the right containing a leveled [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), and another draugr out of sight at the top of some stairs at the rear of the chamber. The draugr will both attack as soon as they are alerted to your presence. There is nothing else of interest in this room. At the top of the stairs at the rear of the room is another passage, which descends to the east before turning south and exiting into another chamber, with a rock pillar ahead, and stairs down to the left. This chamber contains two more leveled draugr, one of which is a magic-user. There are several steps down to the bottom of the chamber, and a passage heading west into some catacombs.

At the first crossroads is a draugr slumbering upright in an alcove opposite, and a [burial urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn") in an alcove on your right. Next to the burial urn to your right is a broken sideboard holding a random [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield") and a random [potion of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"). Passages continue to the south and west. To the south, the passage enters a walkway over a chamber containing two draugr, one of them a magic-user. The walkway leads out to a pillar, with a second pillar to the left with a [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") beside it. The chest has a novice-level [trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Tension_Cable "Skyrim:Tension Cable") that triggers a [poison dart trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap") from the pillar behind. From here, you can either drop down into the chamber, or return to the junction and follow the passage west. Heading west are stairs that lead down to a small area containing an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein"), with the path continuing south through another passage that eventually enters the same chamber through the doorway to the west. The chamber holds nothing else of interest. A second doorway to the south leads directly into a room with an upright sarcophagus on the wall opposite, which bursts open as soon as you enter the room. An unlocked chest and two large [urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn") are to your left. To your right are two burial urns to the right of a sarcophagus, with a set of shelves farther to the right holding two random [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), a random [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet"), six common [books](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books"), an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), and a copy of the [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Doors of Oblivion](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Doors_of_Oblivion "Skyrim:The Doors of Oblivion")*. To the right of the shelves is another burial urn.

This is as far as you can go without starting the quest The Taste of Death. Everything that follows is described as when the quest is active, as this is the first time you will be able to access the below areas.

The sarcophagus to the right by the two burial urns has a loose back, which falls to reveal a tunnel. The tunnel descends to an open concealed door with a handle to the left, and enters a short passage with an iron door at the far end. On either side of the short passage are two large statues, on the left are three burial urns and a leveled potion of healing, magicka, or stamina, and on the right is another concealed door. Through the iron door is a room containing two roaming leveled draugr and a third leveled boss draugr (up to [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest")) sitting on a throne at the far end of a long stone table. The table is on a raised section running the length of the room, with four stone benches on either side. There are many burial urns and large urns around the room, including seven large urns flanking the raised shrine to [Namira](/wiki/Lore:Namira "Lore:Namira") at the rear of the room behind the throne, two large urns and two burial urns next to and on top of a stone table by the west wall, and three burial urns near the east wall. A set of shelves is on each side of the table; the set to the west holds a pair of [iron boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots"), while the set to the east holds two [goblets](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet") and two common books. To the right of the throne is a boss-level chest.

Once the boss draugr is defeated, the concealed door in the short passage lowers, giving access to the secret entrance to the cave, while the open concealed door you entered the passage through will have closed, with a chain to open it to the right. Eola will eventually join you inside if she wasn't previously accompanying you, and will instruct you to bring someone to a special feast as part of the related quest. The tunnel behind the second concealed door leads to another small room containing two large urns, a sideboard holding three common books, and an iron door that leads to the secret entrance outside.

When you return with [Brother Verulus](/wiki/Skyrim:Brother_Verulus "Skyrim:Brother Verulus"), you will find the long table has been laid, and a number of other guests are already sitting waiting for you. In addition to Eola, they are [Banning](/wiki/Skyrim:Banning "Skyrim:Banning"), [Lisbet](/wiki/Skyrim:Lisbet "Skyrim:Lisbet"), and [Hogni Red-Arm](/wiki/Skyrim:Hogni_Red-Arm "Skyrim:Hogni Red-Arm") from Markarth, as well as [Sanyon](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanyon "Skyrim:Sanyon") and [Nimphaneth](/wiki/Skyrim:Nimphaneth "Skyrim:Nimphaneth"). On the table are three bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), five bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), two bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), three [sweet rolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), two [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), two loaves and two pieces of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), two [goat cheese wheels](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), four [goat cheese wedges](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), two pieces of [human flesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Human_Flesh "Skyrim:Human Flesh"), and many gory human bones. The western set of shelves now holds two more bottles of alto wine, a bottle of wine, a goat cheese wheel, and three goat cheese wedges.

## Bugs

- During [The Taste of Death](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Taste_of_Death "Skyrim:The Taste of Death"), the persuade option to have [Brother Verulus](/wiki/Skyrim:Brother_Verulus "Skyrim:Brother Verulus") follow you here always fails without the [Amulet of Articulation](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_Articulation "Skyrim:Amulet of Articulation") because the speech check is done on him, rather than yourself.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 2.0.9, fixes this bug.
- The secret entry/exit from Reachcliff Cave has no proper navmeshing at the exit so NPCs would go around to the main cave entrance instead even after it was made available.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.8, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Reachwater Rock

## Overview

Reachwater Rock

**Reachwater Rock** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") east-southeast of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"). It contains only one zone, *[Reachwater Rock](#Reachwater_Rock)*.

The cave is home to the crypt of [Archmage Gauldur](/wiki/Skyrim:Gauldur "Skyrim:Gauldur"), and can only be fully explored near the end of the quest [Forbidden Legend](/wiki/Skyrim:Forbidden_Legend "Skyrim:Forbidden Legend").

## Related Quests

- **[Forbidden Legend](/wiki/Skyrim:Forbidden_Legend "Skyrim:Forbidden Legend")**: Investigate the forgotten [Gauldur Legend](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Legends "Skyrim:Lost Legends").

### Exterior

The path to Reachwater Rock is on your right along the road toward [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") heading southeast, just before crossing the last bridge before the turning for [Karthspire camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthspire "Skyrim:Karthspire"). One [silver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Silver Ore Vein") is to the right of the path before reaching the stream. The path ends at a stream falling from the mountains above; the cave entrance is through the waterfall. One [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") is on the opposite side of the stream where the path ends.

### Reachwater Rock

The *Ancient Edict*

This place was sealed at great price...

Upon entering this natural cavern, you will find a waterfall on your right, with the stream heading north-south into the cavern. With the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, some [Fishing Supplies](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Supplies "Skyrim:Fishing Supplies") can be found here; fish from [Underground](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_(activity)#Biomes "Skyrim:Fishing (activity)") waters can be caught here. There are many mushroom [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") growing in this first room and throughout the ruin; see the table below for the totals. The stream drops into a pool of water, with an adept-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") and a lootable skeleton with a random [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield") and a random [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword") at the bottom. The path winds around the pool to the left; on your left is a lit brazier with an [orichalcum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Orichalcum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Orichalcum Ore Vein") next to it. The path continues over a rock bridge to an island in the middle, with a dead [adventurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Adventurer#Adventurer7 "Skyrim:Adventurer") next to a tree. To the left is a plinth holding the [emerald dragon claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Emerald_Dragon_Claw "Skyrim:Emerald Dragon Claw"), which is needed for the door in this chamber across the next bridge. Underneath the claw is an *[Ancient Edict](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Edict "Skyrim:Ancient Edict")*, which continues the lore for the related quest Forbidden Legend and warns you to not to continue. Looking east from the puzzle door, you will see above the ore vein on the far side of the cavern a ledge containing an unlocked chest. This can be reached by using the [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"). With only one word, you will need to stand on top of the claw-like piece of broken statue near the tree and move forward or jump after shouting until you scramble onto the ledge. With two or three words, the ledge is more readily accessible.

Climb the second rock bridge up to a [puzzle door](/wiki/Skyrim:Puzzle_Door "Skyrim:Puzzle Door"). Examine the underside of the emerald dragon claw in your inventory menu for the correct combination, **Bear—Whale—Snake**. Upon opening the door, you will see that it in fact opens a series of four similar doors in a row. Follow the corridor through the now open four doors to a second puzzle door. This door is opened using the [ivory dragon claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivory_Dragon_Claw "Skyrim:Ivory Dragon Claw") found in [Folgunthur](/wiki/Skyrim:Folgunthur "Skyrim:Folgunthur") during the related quest; the correct combination is **Eagle—Eagle—Dragon**. This door is protected by a [dart trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap"), which shoots from either side after incorrect combinations.

The door opens to the top of a flight of stairs, with a bench on your left and a [burial urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn") on your right. At the bottom of the stairs are four lit braziers; behind the back right-hand brazier is a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), and behind the back left-hand brazier is a burial urn. To the south is a large [urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn"). The path continues down to the north, opening into a large room with a total of eight upright sarcophagi around the room on different levels. At the northern end of the room is a stone table where you place the three parts of [the Gauldur Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gauldur_Amulet "Skyrim:The Gauldur Amulet") during the related quest. Behind this is a ninth sarcophagus which contain the remains of Archmage Gauldur; once you have completed the quest, search his remains for a large number of [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). All of the inhabitants of the upright sarcophagi can be dealt with using a [rune](/wiki/Skyrim:Rune_(effect) "Skyrim:Rune (effect)") spell prior to placing the amulet parts.

Behind the seal

On your way back out of this room after the end of the related quest, you will see that next to the large urn to the south, a doorway has opened in the wall. Past the doorway is a boss chest, a random [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet"), [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword"), shield, and [battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Battleaxe "Skyrim:Battleaxe"), a filled [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), and a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse").

|  |
| --- |
| Ingredients found growing throughout the cave and ruins:  - 7 [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown") - 4 [blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort") - 12 [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") - 6 [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool") - 2 [juniper berries](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries") - 1 [mora tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella") - 7 [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot") - 6 [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") |

## Notes

- The dead adventurer in the first chamber has a copy of *[Lost Legends](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Legends "Skyrim:Lost Legends")* in their inventory.
- In the river to the northwest, just below and west of [Sky Haven Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Sky_Haven_Temple "Skyrim:Sky Haven Temple"), there is a capsized rowboat containing a [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox") and various [gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Gems "Skyrim:Gems") (including a [flawless ruby](/wiki/Skyrim:Flawless_Ruby "Skyrim:Flawless Ruby") and a [flawless diamond](/wiki/Skyrim:Flawless_Diamond "Skyrim:Flawless Diamond")). There is also a chest in the riverbed nearby.
- According to the *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")*, Reachwater Rock is named after the eponymous stone pedestal within.[[1]](#cite_note-PRIMA-1):343 The guide names the cavern where the tomb is located "Reachwater Cavern".[[1]](#cite_note-PRIMA-1):519

## Bugs

- Guard rumors in Markarth are unable to add the map marker for Reachwater Rock because the dialogue has the wrong property set.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
- In the pool of water in the main chamber, there are several "holes" in the water where you can breathe and walk normally. The most noticeable one is at the deepest part of the pool.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, fixes this bug.
- The emerald dragon claw may not spawn. **?**
  - Load an old save to fix this, or simply walk out of the cave and re-enter.
- The emerald dragon claw may not show up in your inventory after picking it up, but can still be used on doors. **?**
  - Use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") command `player.additem ed417 1` to add it to your inventory.
- If the puzzle door does not work, check [here](/wiki/Skyrim:Puzzle_Totems#Bugs "Skyrim:Puzzle Totems") for possible fixes.
- Sigdis Gauldurson may use [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") and knock you past the barrier separating you from the ghosts, glitching you to the point where you must reload a save.
  - It may be possible to use ranged shouts or magic to kill the ghosts and lift the barrier, or you can conjure a creature on the other side of the barrier (if combat stops after conjuring, use hostile magic to start it again).
  -  You can use the console command `tcl` to pass through the barrier.
  - It may be necessary to load a previous save to fix this.
- The ghost may not come down for you to fight him, and instead may just stand and stare at the wall.
- If [Dawnbreaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnbreaker "Skyrim:Dawnbreaker") is used to destroy one of the ghosts and its ability activates, the ghost may not return to the shelf, and the next one will not come down to fight.

Reachwind Eyrie

**Reachwind Eyrie** is a small [Dwarven](/wiki/Lore:Dwemer "Lore:Dwemer") tower east-southeast of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). It contains only one zone, *[Reachwind Eyrie](#Reachwind_Eyrie)*.

The tower is perched atop a large cliff overlooking the [Karth River](/wiki/Skyrim:Karth_River "Skyrim:Karth River"), surrounded by some of Skyrim's greener lands. The building is remarkably well-preserved, considering the thousands of years it has stood unlocked.

## Related Quests

- **[Mightier than the Sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Mightier_than_the_Sword "Skyrim:Mightier than the Sword")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Orcish_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Orcish Plate"): Track down some Dwarven loot and beat the competition.

### Reachwind Eyrie

Upon entering, there is a stone bench on either side of the door. Continuing up the winding stairway, you will come to a small room strewn with various [Dwemer scrap](/wiki/Skyrim:Ores_and_Ingots#Dwemer_Metal_.28Smeltable.29 "Skyrim:Ores and Ingots") and [Dwemer dishes](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Items#Dwemer_Dishes "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Items"). There is also a Dwemer dresser that has a 25% chance of containing 1-9 gold, as well as up to three random Dwemer scrap (75% chance each). If you accumulate all the scrap metals found in the room, you can smelt a total of 23 [Dwarven metal ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Metal_Ingot "Skyrim:Dwarven Metal Ingot") (more if the random items found in the dresser are smeltable).

Apart from Dwemer clutter, there are a few items of interest resting on the desk with the Dwemer banner hanging above it. These include a copy of the [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Chimarvamidium](/wiki/Skyrim:Chimarvamidium "Skyrim:Chimarvamidium")*, a random [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), a random [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"), and a random [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet"), which can be either light or heavy. Also, there is an apprentice-locked chest containing random [loot](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"). There are also two [wine bottles](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") lying around the room.

### Exterior: Reachwind Eyrie Overlook

Reachwind Eyrie Overlook is an outdoor balcony that is accessible through a door to the left of the desk. Looking out of the balcony, you will see a spectacular view of western Skyrim. You will be able to see [Pavo's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Pavo%27s_House "Skyrim:Pavo's House") toward the northwest, and [Kolskeggr Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolskeggr_Mine "Skyrim:Kolskeggr Mine") and [Sky Haven Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Sky_Haven_Temple "Skyrim:Sky Haven Temple") toward the north. Looking out to the northeast, you can see the ruined [Sundered Towers](/wiki/Skyrim:Sundered_Towers "Skyrim:Sundered Towers") and the tower at [Bleakwind Bluff](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleakwind_Bluff "Skyrim:Bleakwind Bluff") slightly east of it. Finally, if you look toward the east, you should be able to see [Old Hroldan Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Hroldan_Inn "Skyrim:Old Hroldan Inn").

To the left of the balcony door lies a birds' nest containing a [pine thrush egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg"). There is a random [one-handed sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword") resting on the parapet of the balcony. To the right of the balcony rests an expert-locked chest containing random loot.

## Notes

- This may be the tower of [Gauldur](/wiki/Lore:Gauldur "Lore:Gauldur"), as *[Daynas Valen's Notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Daynas_Valen%27s_Notes "Skyrim:Daynas Valen's Notes")* reveals that he was buried near it, and [Reachwater Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Reachwater_Rock "Skyrim:Reachwater Rock") isn't too far away.
- The guards at [Dushnikh Yal](/wiki/Skyrim:Dushnikh_Yal "Skyrim:Dushnikh Yal") may add this location to your map if you talk to them.
- [Dwarven Spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spider "Skyrim:Dwarven Spider") may spawn here at higher levels.

# Skyrim:Reaper's Lair

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Building: Reaper's Lair | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Occupants | |
| [Bonemen](/wiki/Skyrim:Boneman "Skyrim:Boneman"), [Reaper](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaper "Skyrim:Reaper") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DLC1SoulCairnReaperCell | |
| Location | |
| [Soul Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Cairn "Skyrim:Soul Cairn") | |

Reaper's Lair

The **Reaper's Lair** is an enclosed ruin in the [Soul Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Cairn "Skyrim:Soul Cairn").

After emerging from [Valerica](/wiki/Skyrim:Valerica "Skyrim:Valerica")'s portal and following the path through the large stone wall that bisects the Soul Cairn, the building is found along the southeastern edge of the area. It is a large black ruin, similar to other structures in the realm, but can be distinguished by the presence of a door.

## Walkthrough

The interior is very dark and barren. Lightning will occasionally strike the center of the room, illuminating the jagged walls. In the middle of the room stands a pedestal where a set of three [Reaper Gem Fragments](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaper_Gem_Fragment "Skyrim:Reaper Gem Fragment") can be placed. Doing so will summon the [Reaper](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaper "Skyrim:Reaper") and three [bonemen](/wiki/Skyrim:Boneman "Skyrim:Boneman"). After defeating the summoned enemies, there is little to do other than loot their remains and exit the ruin.

In the center of the circle is a square grate over what appears to be a teleport well; however, there is no way of accessing the well below, which in any event does nothing.

## Bugs

- The Reaper and his minions may not spawn. You can work around this by scattering a few [Fire Runes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Rune "Skyrim:Fire Rune") on the ground around the chamber. This will summon his minions from below and draw him out for the fight. Likewise, you can move to the back of the room and cast a rune on the large pile of bones, slightly above where the bone wall meets the bone floor. If you don't have Fire Rune, the Reaper can also be summoned by climbing the bone pile to where it joins the wall and shield bashing toward the small glowing light. Using the [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") there will also work.
- If the Reaper dies over the grated well in the middle of the floor, his corpse may fall through the grate and be unlootable.
- The bonemen's corpses may be unlootable.

## Gallery

- 

  Reaper's Lair map
- 

  Reaper's Lair interior
- 

  The Reaper and his minions attack
