# Skyrim:Rebel's Cairn (quest)

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by multiple users, *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Chris3145](/wiki/User:Chris3145 "User:Chris3145"), *not checked* |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Find [Red Eagle's](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle "Skyrim:Red Eagle") [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle%27s_Bane "Skyrim:Red Eagle's Bane").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Reading *[The Legend of Red Eagle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Legend_of_Red_Eagle "Skyrim:The Legend of Red Eagle")* |
| Location(s): | [Red Eagle Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle_Redoubt "Skyrim:Red Eagle Redoubt"), [Sundered Towers](/wiki/Skyrim:Sundered_Towers "Skyrim:Sundered Towers"), [Rebel's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebel%27s_Cairn "Skyrim:Rebel's Cairn") |
| Reward: | [Red Eagle's Bane](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle%27s_Bane "Skyrim:Red Eagle's Bane") |
| ID: | dunRebelsCairnQST |
| Suggested Level: | 14 |

Red Eagle's Fury in place at Rebel's Cairn

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Clear [Red Eagle Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle_Redoubt "Skyrim:Red Eagle Redoubt").
2. Climb to the top of [Sundered Towers](/wiki/Skyrim:Sundered_Towers "Skyrim:Sundered Towers").
3. Kill the Forsworn Leader and retrieve the sword [Red Eagle's Fury](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle%27s_Fury "Skyrim:Red Eagle's Fury").
4. Go to [Rebel's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebel%27s_Cairn "Skyrim:Rebel's Cairn").
5. Place Red Eagle's Fury into the holder to open the door.
6. Kill [Red Eagle](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle "Skyrim:Red Eagle").
7. Retrieve sword that is now called [Red Eagle's Bane](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle%27s_Bane "Skyrim:Red Eagle's Bane") with different stats.

## Detailed Walkthrough

This quest starts when reading the book *[The Legend of Red Eagle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Legend_of_Red_Eagle "Skyrim:The Legend of Red Eagle")*, and is found in the Miscellaneous section of your journal. The first waypoint leads to [Red Eagle Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle_Redoubt "Skyrim:Red Eagle Redoubt"), an outdoor encampment with a couple Forsworn and some minor loot. Next head into the cave [Red Eagle Ascent](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle_Ascent "Skyrim:Red Eagle Ascent"). There's not much to speak of in here, just a handful of Forsworn, a few easily-avoided traps, and some alchemy ingredients in various places. At the end of the cave you'll exit back out into Skyrim through an exit marked [Red Eagle Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle_Redoubt "Skyrim:Red Eagle Redoubt") (not the same door through which you entered). Head up the stairs to your right and kill all of the Forsworn along the way. Note that once the stairs end there is a sizable camp to the left with a [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge"), an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"), an adept-locked chest, and the [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") [Reality & Other Falsehoods](/wiki/Skyrim:Reality_%26_Other_Falsehoods "Skyrim:Reality & Other Falsehoods"). To the east of the camp (to the right as you reach the top of the stairs) is the large stone structure [Sundered Towers](/wiki/Skyrim:Sundered_Towers "Skyrim:Sundered Towers"). The structure is actually the personal encampment for the [Forsworn Briarheart](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Briarheart "Skyrim:Forsworn Briarheart"), who you find seated at a throne as you approach. Kill him in order to retrieve [Red Eagle's Fury](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle%27s_Fury "Skyrim:Red Eagle's Fury"). The quest will auto-update and ask you to unlock the secret of Red Eagle's Tomb. There's a [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle%27s_Rite "Skyrim:Red Eagle's Rite") on the altar near the Forsworn Briarheart with details on what you have to do, as well as a nearby chest. Don't forget to grab the key off of the [Forsworn Briarheart](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Briarheart "Skyrim:Forsworn Briarheart")'s body.

Head back across the throne and up the wooden stairs to a master-locked door, which unlocks with the key you just found. Follow the path up the tower (there are no enemies nearby) and use the pullchain to lower a drawbridge you need to cross to reach your next destination. Once you cross the bridge, you can loot some items here, and go downstairs to a door. You exit the tower facing east. You can see ruins to the north, which are empty but do provide a nice view. The next destination is [Rebel's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebel%27s_Cairn "Skyrim:Rebel's Cairn"), to the southeast. Rebel's Cairn is not the tower you can see in the distance to the southeast; that tower is [Bleakwind Bluff](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleakwind_Bluff "Skyrim:Bleakwind Bluff"), which you may want to discover if you haven't already. Rebel's Cairn is located before you reach that tower.

### Inside Rebel's Cairn

Red Eagle's Tomb

Upon entering Rebel's Cairn you will find a good amount of fungus-type alchemy ingredients (some of which you may need to use [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") to access), a dead adventurer, an iron ore vein, and an altar with a weapon slot. Activate the weapon slot to insert [Red Eagle's Fury](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle%27s_Fury "Skyrim:Red Eagle's Fury"), which will open the way ahead into [Red Eagle](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle "Skyrim:Red Eagle")'s tomb and the next phase of the quest. The top of the first flight of stairs here triggers a trio of skeletons and Red Eagle himself to rise. If you are sneaking, it seems that the skeletons sometimes turn on Red Eagle himself, so it may pay to initially stay out of sight and take some pot shots at Red Eagle while he dismisses the skeletons. Take them out how you see fit, although do note that Red Eagle can raise the skeletons, so you might want to take him out first (the skeletons are actually summons; after a while they may collapse on their own). You can also head around to the far right or left behind some spiked sticks to give you some cover from Red Eagle (while still leaving you room to attack him).

Once defeated, Red Eagle will drop a [honed ancient Nord greatsword of burning](/wiki/Skyrim:Honed_Ancient_Nord_Greatsword_of_Burning "Skyrim:Honed Ancient Nord Greatsword of Burning"). A chest behind Red Eagle's coffin contains some loot. Head back out to the first chamber and grab Red Eagle's Fury, which is now [Red Eagle's Bane](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle%27s_Bane "Skyrim:Red Eagle's Bane").

## Notes

- If Red Eagle's Fury is removed from the pedestal after Red Eagle is awakened but before he is killed, it will not become Red Eagle's Bane.
- If Red Eagle's Bane is removed from the pedestal, the door closes so be sure to remove all the loot from the tomb if you intend to sell the sword.
- The final quest area does not provide an easy exit back to the beginning. Thus, if you typically travel with a horse, you'll need to walk all the way back to [Red Eagle Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle_Redoubt "Skyrim:Red Eagle Redoubt") to retrieve your horse if you are over-encumbered.
- When you activate the pedestal, the model for an [ancient Nord greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nord_Greatsword "Skyrim:Ancient Nord Greatsword") is placed inside instead.

## Bugs

- After completing this quest, reading another copy of the book will assign the quest again. However, Red Eagle will not be there, and Red Eagle's Fury will not become Red Eagle's Bane. Keeping Red Eagle's Fury in your personal inventory does not stop the quest from being reassigned.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
- Picking up another Red Eagle's Fury sword will make it a quest item and it cannot be removed from your inventory by dropping it. You must travel to Rebel's Cairn and activate the weapon slot in the first room to have it removed from your inventory. After activating the weapon slot, you should be able to take the Red Eagle's Fury into your inventory as a non-quest item. [*verification needed — Which versions/patches is this true for? (see [talk page](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Rebel%27s_Cairn_(quest)#restarted_quest_in_more_recent_versions_of_game))*] Alternately, if you own a house, the weapon plaques can be used to remove quest marked weapons from your inventory.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, addresses this issue. The quest will no longer restart itself after completion, which is what led to this bug.
- The book *[Red Eagle's Rite](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle%27s_Rite "Skyrim:Red Eagle's Rite")* on the altar at Sundered Towers might clip beneath the surface making it unreachable without the console.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.
  - You can knock the book into view by using a shout or spell.
- This quest can fail to start if the boss at Rebel's Cairn has been reserved by another radiant quest, or if you already took the note there.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
- Sometimes the Forsworn Briarheart carrying the Red Eagle's Fury sword will carry duplicates of the sword in their inventory. At this point, it is unknown whether this happens because of the quest reassignment or a normal bug. The swords are able to be dropped, sold, or stored after you use one to open the secret passage to complete the quest. **?**

## Quest Stages

| Rebel's Cairn (dunRebelsCairnQST) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Find Red Eagle's sword |
| 22 |  | *Objective 22:* Unlock the secret of Red Eagle's Tomb |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 20, 21, 30.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage dunRebelsCairnQST stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest dunRebelsCairnQST`.

# Skyrim:Rebel's Cairn

## Overview

| --- | --- | --- | --- |

| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |

| [Ore Veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") | |
| # of [Iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore") | 1 |

Rebel's Cairn

**Rebel's Cairn** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") northwest of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead"). It contains only one zone, *[Rebel's Cairn](#Rebel.27s_Cairn)*.

Picking up [Red Eagle's Fury](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle%27s_Fury "Skyrim:Red Eagle's Fury") in [Sundered Towers](/wiki/Skyrim:Sundered_Towers "Skyrim:Sundered Towers") adds this location to your map. In the first room lies a dead [adventurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Adventurer#Adventurer11 "Skyrim:Adventurer") clinging to a copy of *[The Legend of Red Eagle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Legend_of_Red_Eagle "Skyrim:The Legend of Red Eagle")*. Reading the book starts the related quest, [Rebel's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebel%27s_Cairn_(quest) "Skyrim:Rebel's Cairn (quest)").

## Related Quests

- **[Rebel's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebel%27s_Cairn_(quest) "Skyrim:Rebel's Cairn (quest)")**: Find [Red Eagle's](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle "Skyrim:Red Eagle") [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle%27s_Bane "Skyrim:Red Eagle's Bane").
- **[Salty Sea-Dogs](/wiki/Skyrim:Salty_Sea-Dogs "Skyrim:Salty Sea-Dogs")**: Find some [void salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine-Cut_Void_Salts "Skyrim:Fine-Cut Void Salts") for an inexperienced [sea captain](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Wayfinder "Skyrim:Captain Wayfinder"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Rebel's Cairn

Rebel's Cairn interior

A [steel sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Steel Sword") is stuck in a pile of rocks to the left of the entrance, and an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") is on the right side of the room with the pedestal. The cave is a good location to gather alchemical ingredients, as it contains 7 [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown"), 5 [blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort"), 12 [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"), 13 [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool"), 2 [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), 7 [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot"), 2 [Nordic barnacles](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Barnacle "Skyrim:Nordic Barnacle"), 1 [slaughterfish egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Egg "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Egg") nest, and 23 [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap").

## Notes

- [Red Eagle's Bane](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle%27s_Bane "Skyrim:Red Eagle's Bane") can be removed from the weapon stand at any time, but doing so will cause the secret door to close.
- If you interact with the weapon stand when you do not have Red Eagle's Fury in your inventory, nothing will happen, and a temporary message will be displayed in the top left-hand corner of the screen stating "None of your weapons fit in this slot."
- If you are sent to the cave by a radiant quest, you must first start the quest Rebel's Cairn to enter the cave. After completing that quest, you may want to keep Red Eagle's Bane to allow you to easily explore the cave on subsequent visits.

# Skyrim:Rebuilding the Blades

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. | --- | --- |
| **Recruit new members for the [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Delphine](/wiki/Skyrim:Delphine "Skyrim:Delphine") |
| Location(s): | [Sky Haven Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Sky_Haven_Temple "Skyrim:Sky Haven Temple") |
| Reward: | Use the Blades to go [Dragon Hunting](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Hunting "Skyrim:Dragon Hunting") |
| ID: | FreeformSkyhavenTempleA |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Alduin's Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Wall "Skyrim:Alduin's Wall") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Alduin's Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Wall "Skyrim:Alduin's Wall") | | |

[Faendal](/wiki/Skyrim:Faendal "Skyrim:Faendal") and [Uthgerd the Unbroken](/wiki/Skyrim:Uthgerd_the_Unbroken "Skyrim:Uthgerd the Unbroken") as newly-recruited Blades

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Locate and bring three suitable [followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") to Delphine.
2. Induct these followers into the [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades").
3. Ask [Esbern](/wiki/Skyrim:Esbern "Skyrim:Esbern") about [dragon lairs](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs") to start the repeatable quest [Dragon Hunting](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Hunting "Skyrim:Dragon Hunting").

### Help Wanted

Delphine inducting [Lydia](/wiki/Skyrim:Lydia "Skyrim:Lydia") into the Blades

After completing [Alduin's Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Wall "Skyrim:Alduin's Wall"), you may notice that the [Blades'](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades") mission of ridding Skyrim of [dragons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") may be rather daunting for just two people. Ask [Delphine](/wiki/Skyrim:Delphine "Skyrim:Delphine") about her apparent staffing shortage and she will reply, *"The [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor") hunted us down, remember? It wasn't exactly great for recruitment. But we have a headquarters of a sort now. We'll rebuild the Blades. Someday."* As you are the [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dovahkiin "Skyrim:Dovahkiin"), and the Blades are sworn to protect you, you might be inclined to help Delphine find new recruits. When you offer, she will say, *"If you find anyone you think would make a good recruit, I can certainly take a look at them. Remember, though, being a Blade is a lifelong commitment. Their loyalty has to be with us once they're in."*

### Recruiting

To recruit a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") into the Blades, simply bring your new recruit to Delphine in [Sky Haven Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Sky_Haven_Temple "Skyrim:Sky Haven Temple") for introductions. Since being a Blade is binding, Delphine will ask you for confirmation: *"Are you sure? I'll need to ask them to take an oath to leave their old life behind and stay here from now on."* Confirm your selection and Delphine will agree. She will then give the oath to your first recruit:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Delphine**: | *"You there. The Dragonborn wishes to give you the chance to join the lost guardians of Tamriel. The dragon slayers. The Blades. Do you wish to become a Blade?"* |
| **Follower**: | *"I do."* |
| **Delphine**: | *"Are you willing to trade away all claims and titles of your former life? To live here and devote yourself to protecting Tamriel from danger?"* |
| **Follower**: | *"I do."* |
| **Delphine**: | *"Then by my right as acting grandmaster, I name you a Blade, with all the privileges, rights, and burdens that brings. Godspeed."* |

### Happy Hunting

You can bring two more recruits to Delphine for the oath taking. After the third, she will say *"That's enough recruits for now. Ask Esbern about the dragon lairs he's been studying. We'll have the recruits do some hunting with you."* Speak to Esbern to complete the quest and begin the [Dragon Hunting](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Hunting "Skyrim:Dragon Hunting") repeatable quest.

## Notes

- You can still ask recruited Blades to follow you, but they will be situated at Sky Haven Temple rather than their place of usual residence.
  - If you induct your spouse into the Blades, then you can still move your spouse to a house you own. If you choose to live at your spouse's home, you will be directed to Sky Haven Temple.
- All [permanent followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers#Permanent_Followers "Skyrim:Followers") are eligible to join the Blades except [Serana](/wiki/Skyrim:Serana "Skyrim:Serana") and those from the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood").
- When a new recruit joins the Blades, they automatically leave your service, so a new follower can be recruited. Bugs affecting your ability to obtain new followers may be solved in this manner, though only three followers may be recruited.
- Hirelings that join the Blades can be hired for free after they move to the temple.
- If one of the new recruits dies for whatever reason, they cannot be replaced by inducting another follower. It is therefore best to choose [essential characters](/wiki/Skyrim:Essential_NPCs "Skyrim:Essential NPCs").
- If the optional quest [Paarthurnax](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(quest) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (quest)") has started, you can still recruit followers for Delphine. When it comes time to talk to Esbern however, he will not finish this quest or start the Dragon Hunting quest until Paarthurnax is slain.
- Blades armor is Heavy Armor, so recruits who do not favor that skill will be at a disadvantage. Similarly, Skyrim's Blades only have one-handed swords, so followers unskilled in One-handed may be at a disadvantage. Both of these however do not apply for essential characters.
  - If playing without the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), followers who are skilled with this equipment are: [Cosnach](/wiki/Skyrim:Cosnach "Skyrim:Cosnach"), [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo"), [Uthgerd the Unbroken](/wiki/Skyrim:Uthgerd_the_Unbroken "Skyrim:Uthgerd the Unbroken"), [Golldir](/wiki/Skyrim:Golldir "Skyrim:Golldir"), [Vorstag](/wiki/Skyrim:Vorstag "Skyrim:Vorstag"), [Athis](/wiki/Skyrim:Athis "Skyrim:Athis"), [Ria](/wiki/Skyrim:Ria "Skyrim:Ria"), [Torvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Torvar "Skyrim:Torvar"), [Borgakh the Steel Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Borgakh_the_Steel_Heart "Skyrim:Borgakh the Steel Heart"), [Ogol](/wiki/Skyrim:Ogol "Skyrim:Ogol"), and [Celann](/wiki/Skyrim:Celann "Skyrim:Celann").
  - If using the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") 2.0.9. or higher, followers who are skilled with this equipment are: [Erik the Slayer](/wiki/Skyrim:Erik_the_Slayer "Skyrim:Erik the Slayer"), [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo"), [Adelaisa Vendicci](/wiki/Skyrim:Adelaisa_Vendicci "Skyrim:Adelaisa Vendicci"), [Golldir](/wiki/Skyrim:Golldir "Skyrim:Golldir"), [Ria](/wiki/Skyrim:Ria "Skyrim:Ria"), [Torvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Torvar "Skyrim:Torvar"), [Borgakh the Steel Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Borgakh_the_Steel_Heart "Skyrim:Borgakh the Steel Heart"), [Ghorbash the Iron Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghorbash_the_Iron_Hand "Skyrim:Ghorbash the Iron Hand"), and [Celann](/wiki/Skyrim:Celann "Skyrim:Celann").
  - With or without the Unofficial Skyrim patch, most of the player's Housecarls also make excellent Blades since they mostly specialise in Heavy Armor, sword and shield fighting, and can level up to 50 which is higher than most other followers. Exceptions are Valdimar, who favors Light Armor, and Rayya, who favors dual-wielding rather than sword and shield. They are also all "protected" and thus should not be killable by anybody but the player.

## Bugs

- Any armor given to Blades inductees prior to their induction may be removed from their inventory.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.
  - Due to this bug, it appears that dragon priest masks are also lost. This renders the quest in [Bromjunaar Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Bromjunaar_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Bromjunaar Sanctuary") impossible to complete.
- When dismissing Blade followers who were formerly [housecarls](/wiki/Skyrim:Housecarl "Skyrim:Housecarl"), they will say *"I will be back at your house if you need me, Thane"*, though they will actually return to Sky Haven Temple.
- Sometimes, followers recruited into the blades will travel back to where you recruited them, even though Delphine accepted them. A possible fix could be to load before recruiting the previous Blade (only possible if this wasn't the first follower you introduced to the Blades), recruit that previous Blade again and try again with your second one.
- Esbern may be unavailable when you try to talk to him. There is no dialogue option and he just says 'Did you say something?'.
- Followers may attack one another killing one of your blades members.

## Quest Stages

| Rebuilding the Blades (FreeformSkyhavenTempleA) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Bring a follower to Delphine |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Bring a follower to Delphine |
| 30 |  | *Objective 30:* Bring a follower to Delphine |
| 40 |  | *Objective 40:* Ask Esbern about dragon lairs |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 50.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformSkyhavenTempleA stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformSkyhavenTempleA`.

# Skyrim:Recipe for Disaster

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Dark Brotherhood.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Dark_Brotherhood.png) | **Assume the identity of the famous [Gourmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Balagog_gro-Nolob "Skyrim:Balagog gro-Nolob") in an effort to assassinate the Emperor.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Astrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Astrid "Skyrim:Astrid") |
| Location(s): | [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"), [Nightgate Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightgate_Inn "Skyrim:Nightgate Inn") |
| Reward: | Leveled Gold, and potentially [Nightweaver's Band](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightweaver%27s_Band "Skyrim:Nightweaver's Band") |
| ID: | DB08 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [The Cure for Madness](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cure_for_Madness "Skyrim:The Cure for Madness") | **Next →** [To Kill an Empire](/wiki/Skyrim:To_Kill_an_Empire "Skyrim:To Kill an Empire") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [The Cure for Madness](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cure_for_Madness "Skyrim:The Cure for Madness") | | → Next | [To Kill an Empire](/wiki/Skyrim:To_Kill_an_Empire "Skyrim:To Kill an Empire") | | |

[Anton Virane](/wiki/Skyrim:Anton_Virane "Skyrim:Anton Virane"), the first assassination target for this quest

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Festus Krex](/wiki/Skyrim:Festus_Krex "Skyrim:Festus Krex").
2. Find [Anton Virane](/wiki/Skyrim:Anton_Virane "Skyrim:Anton Virane") and make him talk.
3. Kill Anton Virane.
4. Find [Balagog gro-Nolob](/wiki/Skyrim:Balagog_gro-Nolob "Skyrim:Balagog gro-Nolob") and kill him.
5. Take the [invitation](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourmet%27s_Writ_of_Passage "Skyrim:Gourmet's Writ of Passage") off of Balagog's corpse.
6. *(Optional)* Hide Balagog's corpse.
7. Return to Festus Krex.

### A Pinch of Assault

After [dealing with Cicero](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cure_for_Madness "Skyrim:The Cure for Madness"), [Astrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Astrid "Skyrim:Astrid") is anxious to get back on task. She mentions something about a famous, elusive chef and a crazy scheme to impersonate him while cooking for the Emperor. She then points you to [Festus Krex](/wiki/Skyrim:Festus_Krex "Skyrim:Festus Krex"), who will be directing this phase of the Emperor's assassination. Festus explains that your new objective is to kill [the Gourmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Balagog_gro-Nolob "Skyrim:Balagog gro-Nolob") and while assuming his identity, poison the meal being prepared for the Emperor. What complicates this matter is that the Gourmet's identity is known by only a select few. Luckily, Festus has obtained an autographed copy of the Gourmet's book [Uncommon Taste](/wiki/Skyrim:Uncommon_Taste_-_Signed "Skyrim:Uncommon Taste - Signed") owned by [Anton Virane](/wiki/Skyrim:Anton_Virane "Skyrim:Anton Virane"). This suggests that Virane may know the true identity of the Gourmet.

### Carving the Cook

Your first task is to track down Anton Virane, obtain the Gourmet's name, and kill Virane to prevent his interference in the operation. He works at [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") in the [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep") kitchen. He is at first not willing to give you any information, but after some special persuasion, he will quickly reveal the name of the Gourmet: an [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") named [Balagog gro-Nolob](/wiki/Skyrim:Balagog_gro-Nolob "Skyrim:Balagog gro-Nolob"). After he reveals the name it is advisable to tell Virane that he will not be harmed or to remain silent, else he will start running around in a panic. Wait for an opportunity to present itself and kill him, preferably without any pesky witnesses present who could cause you to incur a bounty. Conversely, instead of having him remain in the crowded kitchen it may be better to scare him and have him run out to a more private place where you can kill him with no witnesses. When this is finished, it's on to the main course...

You'll have a few options with Anton once he asks you if he's free to go:

| Topic | Dialogue | Response |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Of course, Anton. Thank you. (Lie)** | *"Okay. All right. Wonderful. You're welcome! I'll just be on my way, then..."* | Anton walks away |
| **I'm afraid not. Loose ends, and all that.** | *"No. Oh, please no..."* | Anton runs away |
| **(Remain Silent)** | *"So... we're done?"* | Anton walks away |

### Just a Dash of Blood

Balagog gro-Nolob, the second assassination target for this quest

The Gourmet, Balagog gro-Nolob, can be found at the [Nightgate Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightgate_Inn "Skyrim:Nightgate Inn"), either inside or outside, depending on the time of day: during the afternoon, he stands at the dock right outside the inn and gazes out over the pond, making it very easy to sneak attack him for a quick kill. After he is dead take the [writ of passage](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourmet%27s_Writ_of_Passage "Skyrim:Gourmet's Writ of Passage") from him, and simply drag his body into the pond (see Notes below) to fulfill the bonus objective. Another way to dispose of the body is to use the [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") shout to send it into the water.
At night, Balagog gro-Nolob can be found in the [Nightgate Inn Cellar](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightgate_Inn_Cellar "Skyrim:Nightgate Inn Cellar"), which can be entered either from inside the inn or via a small hatch near the north exterior wall. Balagog will be asleep much of the time, but as there are no witnesses, the kill will be easy whether he is awake or not. When presented with an opportunity, kill him and take the Writ of Passage from his corpse. Make sure not to kill him in the chair that he sits in because his body may get trapped in the chair, rendering him unable to be dragged to a hiding spot. To successfully hide the body in the cellar, drag him behind the haystack or drop him into the large barrel at the end of the cellar next to the ladder. If you kill him while he cowers behind the wine barrels, this will automatically count as hiding the body. If you successfully hide the body, you will be awarded with the [Nightweaver's Band](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightweaver%27s_Band "Skyrim:Nightweaver's Band").
You may also have a small conversation with him:

| Topic | Dialogue | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- |
| *"You've served your last meal... Gourmet."* | *"Gourmet? Why I... Um... Oh dear. You're going to kill me now, aren't you?"* | Cowers behind the barrels of wine. |
| *"Soon, the Emperor will die. Murdered, by the Gourmet."* | *"What? The Emperor? But I... Oh. Oh, by the gods, no. No, you can't do this. You can't!"* | Cowers behind the barrels of wine. |
| *(Remain Silent)* | *"Yes, well. Perhaps the proprietor of this establishment can assist you. Please, you're starting to... frighten me."* | Ends conversation. |

### No More Soup for You

With the Writ of Passage in hand, return to the sanctuary for your reward. Astrid greets you with special news: All of the pieces are in place, and the [time is at hand](/wiki/Skyrim:To_Kill_an_Empire "Skyrim:To Kill an Empire"). She instructs you to head to [Castle Dour](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") to fulfill your duties as Listener.

## Notes

- If Balagog drops his dagger when he is killed, it will still count as part of his body, allowing you to drag just the dagger to one of the hiding locations specified above to satisfy the bonus requirements of this quest. This is useful if you are having difficulty dragging his body. Alternatively, open his inventory and take the dagger to make his body easier to drag.
- If you decapitate Balagog, you'll need to hide his head along with the rest of his corpse.
- If you kill Balagog outside and drag him into the pond, the water will turn red, as if tainted with blood.
- Be careful if you have the [Disintegrate](/wiki/Skyrim:Disintegrate "Skyrim:Disintegrate") perk for lightning-based magic active, or if the [Dragonborn Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn_Force "Skyrim:Dragonborn Force")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") enhancement for your Unrelenting Force shout is active, as they can turn Balagog's corpse into an ash pile, making it impossible to hide.
- If you have the writ of passage in your inventory when you encounter [Balbus](/wiki/Skyrim:Balbus "Skyrim:Balbus"), you can convince him that you are the Gourmet, and the star-struck Balbus will give you a collection of ingredients he has acquired to impress the Gourmet.
- If you fail to hide the Gourmet's body, don't retrieve his papers, or if you spare Anton Virane, [Festus Krex](/wiki/Skyrim:Festus_Krex "Skyrim:Festus Krex") will criticize you, depending on the circumstances:
  - If you don't hide the Gourmet's body, Festus will be angry with you, saying *"Good, good. And you've got the Writ of Passage, too, I see. So there's that. I've also received word from Markarth. It would seem Anton Virane has suffered an untimely fate, as well. Good. But unfortunately, that inn is abuzz with the news of somebody killing one of their guests! What, hiding the body was too much for you to handle? Bah! Useless. Here's your gold. Now go see Astrid. The time to move against the Emperor has finally come. Sithis help us all."*
  - If you tell Festus that the Gourmet is dead but you don't have his papers with you, Festus will be upset, and say *"Good. And his Writ of Passage? Oh wait, let me guess - you don't have them. Fool! Amateur! Without those papers you'll never be able to present yourself as the Gourmet! Off with you! Back to the body to retrieve them!"*
  - If the Gourmet is dead and you have the papers, but you spared Anton Virane, Festus will go on a similar rant, and say *"Good, good. And you've got the Writ of Passage too, I see, so that's done. But why? Why, pray tell, have I received word that Anton Virane is still walking around Markarth, hale and healthy as the day he was born? Back to Markarth with you! Virane must be silenced! He's a potential witness, you witless dagger jabber!"*

## Bugs

- Balagog's corpse may be positioned in or around furniture after dying, making it impossible to drag it to a hiding place and complete the bonus objective.

:   - Casting Firebolt or similar area-of-effect spells on his body may free his body from the furniture.

- When talking to Anton Virane, you can exit dialogue before telling him you are going to kill him, then restart dialogue with him and repeat the intimidation check to get additional Speech experience. This can be repeated as often as you like to level your [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") skill.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.
- After your conversation with Anton Virane is finished, the script may not update the quest to remove his essential status and allow you to kill him.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.6, fixes this bug.
- Occasionally, when attempting to take the Gourmet's Writ of Passage, it will not show up in his inventory. **?**
  -  You can give the Gourmet the Writ by going into the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console"), clicking on the Gourmet, and then entering `additem 0003beb6 1`.
  -  Alternatively, you can enter `setstage db08 200` to complete the quest, `player.additem 3beb6 1` to give yourself the Writ, then `setstage db09 5` to start the next quest.
- [Hadring](/wiki/Skyrim:Hadring "Skyrim:Hadring")'s and [Fultheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Fultheim "Skyrim:Fultheim")'s dialogue topics about Balagog no longer make sense after you kill him.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, addresses this issue. A condition check has been added so that the topic is unavailable once Balagog is dead.
- If you choose to "Eat" Balagog with the [Ring of Namira](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring_of_Namira "Skyrim:Ring of Namira") equipped, it may trigger a "complete" for the bonus objective, but you may not get the bonus reward. **?**
- Balagog may appear dead and naked in his room in the Nightgate Inn Cellar without the Writ of Passage, making the quest impossible to finish. **?**

## Quest Stages

| Recipe for Disaster (DB08) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 2 |  | I must speak with Festus Krex about my next target, the renowned chef known only as the "Gourmet." *Objective 2:* Report to Festus Krex |
| 4 |  | I have been tasked with killing the Gourmet, but only one person knows the famous chef's true identity and location - a man named Anton Virane. I must get this information from Anton Virane, and then kill him. *Objective 4:* Question Anton Virane |
| 6 |  | *Objective 6:* Kill Anton Virane |
| 10 |  | I must kill the Gourmet, who is actually an Orc named Balagog gro-Nolob. Once he's dead, I must steal his Writ of Passage. And, if I can manage to hide the body, I'll receive a bonus. *Objective 10:* Kill Balagog gro-Nolob |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Take the Writ of Passage |
| 30 |  | *Objective 30:* Report back to Festus Krex |
| 200 | ☑ | The Gourmet is dead, and I'm now in possession of his Writ of Passage. Soon, I will take his place as chef for the Emperor... |
| *Unknown* |  | *Objective 15:* (Optional) Drag Balagog's body to a hiding place |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 255.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DB08 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DB08`.

| **Locate a hidden stash of [Emberbrand Wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Emberbrand_Wine "Skyrim:Emberbrand Wine") for [Captain Veleth](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Veleth "Skyrim:Captain Veleth") in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").** | |

|  |  |

| Quest Giver: | [Captain Veleth](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Veleth "Skyrim:Captain Veleth") |

| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [March of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:March_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:March of the Dead") | | |

A well hidden barrel

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Captain Veleth](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Veleth "Skyrim:Captain Veleth").
2. Find the hidden stash of [Emberbrand Wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Emberbrand_Wine "Skyrim:Emberbrand Wine") in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").
3. Return to Captain Veleth.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Speak to [Captain Veleth](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Veleth "Skyrim:Captain Veleth") in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock"). He tells you that he's concerned about some [Emberbrand Wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Emberbrand_Wine "Skyrim:Emberbrand Wine") being stashed by his men. He'd like you to locate the stash and report back to him. He suggests you search near any abandoned buildings in the area:

:   **Is it difficult commanding the Redoran Guard?**
:   *"It can be. Even the most experienced warriors can fall prey to petty distractions. They usually didn't amount to much, but they make my job that much harder."*
:   **Petty distractions?**
:   *"Some of my own men have become quite accustomed to a spirit they called '[Emberbrand Wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Emberbrand_Wine "Skyrim:Emberbrand Wine").' Despise the stuff myself. It's powerful and tremendously addicting... I've seen men fail to finish even a single flask. If I knew where they were stashing the bottles, I'd put an end to it myself."*
:   **I could track the stash down for you.**
:   *"You would? That would be helpful. I just don't have time to do it myself right now."*
:   **Any idea where I can begin?**
:   *"They're too smart to have left it in the Bulwark. I'd search one of the abandoned houses on the outskirts of town."*

Locate the [abandoned building](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_Building "Skyrim:Abandoned Building") in town, which is just past the [blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Glover_Mallory%27s_House "Skyrim:Glover Mallory's House"). Stay outside, and head along the road southwest of the abandoned building to find eight jars of the wine in a barrel between the foundations of two destroyed houses nearby. Return to Captain Veleth for your reward:

:   **I found the Emberbrand Wine stash.**
:   *"Good, this will help me keep things running without having to worry about a bunch of soldiers falling asleep on duty. Here, take this for your trouble."*

### Reward

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1-29 | 250 |
| 30-39 | 500 |
| 40-49 | 1000 |
| 50-59 | 1500 |
| 60+ | 2000 |

## Notes

- The barrel containing the wine does not exist until you start the quest.
- It is not necessary to take the wine to complete the quest - merely finding the barrel and seeing its contents is enough. If you do take it, you can keep it for your own use.
- You won't be able to speak to Captain Veleth to turn in this quest if you've only just started the quest [Served Cold](/wiki/Skyrim:Served_Cold "Skyrim:Served Cold"), as he will only say, *"I'm sorry. I've already said too much. Talk to Second Councilor Arano if you're willing to help us."* Speaking to Arano to advance Served Cold will allow you to converse with Veleth and turn in this quest.

| 200 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 10.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2RRFavor01 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2RRFavor01`.

# Skyrim:Red Eagle Redoubt

## Overview

Red Eagle Redoubt

**Red Eagle Redoubt** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") and two exterior camps east of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") containing [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"). It contains only one zone, *[Red Eagle Ascent](#Red_Eagle_Ascent)*.

Looking down over the altar area in Red Eagle Ascent

The map marker is near the highest point of the small mountain range southwest of [Sundered Towers](/wiki/Skyrim:Sundered_Towers "Skyrim:Sundered Towers"). The surrounding area is populated by a large number of Forsworn of increasing skill as you approach the peak, which itself is home to several [elk](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer#Elk "Skyrim:Deer").

#### Miscellaneous Quests

- **[Rebel's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebel%27s_Cairn_(quest) "Skyrim:Rebel's Cairn (quest)")**: Find [Red Eagle's](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle "Skyrim:Red Eagle") [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle%27s_Bane "Skyrim:Red Eagle's Bane").

#### Radiant Quests

- **[Bounty: Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Forsworn "Skyrim:Bounty: Forsworn")**: Kill a [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") leader for a bounty reward.
- **[The Ghost of Old Hroldan](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ghost_of_Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:The Ghost of Old Hroldan")**: Put an [ancient ghost](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost_of_Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:Ghost of Old Hroldan") to rest.
- **[The House of Horrors](/wiki/Skyrim:The_House_of_Horrors "Skyrim:The House of Horrors")**: Help [Molag Bal](/wiki/Lore:Molag_Bal "Lore:Molag Bal") take revenge upon a servant of [Boethiah](/wiki/Lore:Boethiah "Lore:Boethiah").
- **[Kill the Forsworn Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Forsworn_Leader_(Jarl) "Skyrim:Kill the Forsworn Leader (Jarl)")**: Do a favor for [Jarl Igmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Igmund "Skyrim:Igmund") by killing a [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") leader.
- **[Lisbet's Missing Shipment](/wiki/Skyrim:Lisbet%27s_Missing_Shipment "Skyrim:Lisbet's Missing Shipment")**: Retrieve a missing Dibella Statue for a struggling store.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior: Lower Camp

Two leveled Forsworn guard the approach from the northwest. One of them is next to a campfire, with an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") and a rack for drying hides nearby. The second Forsworn is on top of a rock with a small wooden table and chair and wooden steps up to it. The entrance to Red Eagle Ascent is to the left of this raised area.

### Red Eagle Ascent

This cave is a typical Forsworn encampment with the normal sharpened stakes and goat head decorations as well as vegetation throughout. Upon entering, there is a tunnel that twists and turns, until you pass a tree stump with a patch of [mora tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella") growing from it, after which the tunnel opens up. There is an elk head off to the left with a lit lantern in front of it, with a [deer hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer_Hide "Skyrim:Deer Hide") nearby. Just after this, on your right is an iron ore vein behind some of the sharpened stakes, next to a tree with a couple taproot ornaments. Across the path by this is a [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") that drops an [oil lantern](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Lanterns "Skyrim:Oil Lanterns") on an [oil slick trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Slicks "Skyrim:Oil Slicks"). Setting this off will alert the two Forsworn that are guarding this part of the cave and can be used to your advantage in dealing with them. Behind the previously mentioned tree is a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") on the ground. Near where the two Forsworn are standing is a lit brazier with a random healing potion next to it, while an adept-locked chest is behind some roots on the opposite side of a tunnel entrance heading east.

Through the tunnel there are [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") and several [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") fungi before a flight of stone steps up to the next cavern. There is a [bear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap") just after entering this cavern, hidden among some of the vegetation. Three more Forsworn make this room their home; the first is at the top of another flight of stone stairs, and the other two are at the rear of the room. Before reaching the stairs, you pass another white cap patch on your right, and just before the stairs, a [burial urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn") is on your left.

At the top of the flight of stone stairs is a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") that activates a [dart trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap") fired from your right across the path in front of you, and on your left is a handle that can be used by the Forsworn to activate a [falling boulders](/wiki/Skyrim:Falling_Boulders "Skyrim:Falling Boulders") trap below. Off on your left behind a tall pillar is a lit brazier with a random [battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Battleaxe "Skyrim:Battleaxe") and [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet") lying beside it. Following the path up over a few wide steps, you reach an area with a blood-covered altar holding a leveled [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow"), a random potion of magicka, and a decapitated skeever. Also on this plateau are a chair and a flight of wooden stairs with an unlocked chest and random stamina potion underneath.

The stairs lead up to a corridor that branches off to your right to the exit, and ahead to a blocked corridor with a fly amanita, two [bleeding crowns](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown"), a [blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort"), and a medium coin purse. Taking the branch to the right and up a few more steps, you reach an unlocked iron door that leads outside to the upper camp of the redoubt.

### Exterior: Upper Camp

Upon exiting, you are at the bottom of several flights of stairs up. There is a campfire with a pile of firewood behind. Each flight of stairs has Forsworn guarding them, each increasing in skill as you go higher. Before climbing, if you travel around to the left of the first flight of stairs, underneath a fallen stone tower you will find a large coin purse.

At the top of the first flight of stairs there is a Forsworn either wandering or sitting on a wooden bench. Taking this one out can alert the Forsworn at the top of the next flight. Before climbing again, at the top of the first flight, turn right and double back to find a novice-locked chest. Climb the third flight and start the next flight; now there are three Forsworn, two at the top of the fourth flight, and one above you to your right on higher ground. It is possible to take out the first two without the third finding you if your Sneak skill is high enough. The one above you is always an archer.

Ahead are more steps passing under three arches. Growing from the second of these is a [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") plant. As you pass under the third, there is a small Forsworn camp on your left with two open tents and two long wooden tables and benches between them. There is a Forsworn sitting at the tables and a second sitting in a chair in the farthest tent. Too much noise taking these out can alert a Forsworn wizard from a tent farther behind on the next plateau up. The first tent contains a single hay pile and a barrel, while the second tent contains the chair the Forsworn was sitting on.

Back on the path, you pass a stone pillar and a lit brazier on a stand on your left. Here the camp splits, with a single tent with the wizard on your left and the main part of the camp to your right. Inside the tent with the wizard are an unowned single bed, an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"), and a food barrel with a leveled [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") and a copy of the [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Reality & Other Falsehoods](/wiki/Skyrim:Reality_%26_Other_Falsehoods "Skyrim:Reality & Other Falsehoods")* on top and random boots beside it.

The main camp consists of four tents around a campfire with a [blacksmith forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge") beside the nearest tent. Between the nearest tent and the forge is an adept-locked chest. Three Forsworn are guarding this area: one sleeping in the nearest tent, one wandering or sitting on a wooden bench, and the third behind on a raised area. On top of the forge anvil is a random [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"). Each of the tents contains a hay pile, with the first also containing a wooden bench, the next two also containing chairs, and the last also containing a dresser. There are also a wooden table with a mead barrel and sack on top and several other sacks and wooden benches around the camp. To the right of the last tent is a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block"). If you are here seeking the priest of Boethiah for the quest [The House of Horrors](/wiki/Skyrim:The_House_of_Horrors "Skyrim:The House of Horrors"), he will be found kneeling in the tent next to the table with the mead barrel.

The path continues heading east toward Sundered Towers and the boss of this redoubt along with one other Forsworn and another raised area reached via stone stairs. Before that, traveling south down the side of one of the tents, you'll reach a melee practice area including two dummies and a wooden table holding a random [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword"). On your left before reaching the stairs up to the boss is an archery practice area including two archery targets and a wooden table holding a random bow.

Climbing the stone stairs, you'll encounter the last Forsworn before the boss, and pass a wooden flight of stairs up to Sundered Towers, with a tree stump with a mora tapinella growth on the left of these stairs. Ahead, the Forsworn boss will be sitting on a throne, or if alerted, searching for you near an altar. The boss will have [Red Eagle's Fury](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle%27s_Fury "Skyrim:Red Eagle's Fury"). Past the throne and altar are a few steps down to another tent containing an unowned single bed, a boss leveled chest, a chair and wooden table holding a mead barrel, a copy of *[The Legend of Red Eagle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Legend_of_Red_Eagle "Skyrim:The Legend of Red Eagle")*, a leveled stamina potion, a random [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield"), and a lit lantern. This chest will hold any item you have been sent to Red Eagle Redoubt to find.

## Notes

- One [silver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Silver Ore Vein") is 120 feet east of the entrance, slightly uphill.

## Bugs

- Looking at the world map when inside Red Eagle Ascent places your marker north-northwest of Markarth.
- If you have previously killed the leader of Red Eagle Redoubt and get the task to kill him again, you must reanimate the body and kill him a second time. You may get this task while trying to purchase a house in Markarth from the Jarl.
- The book *[Red Eagle's Rite](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle%27s_Rite "Skyrim:Red Eagle's Rite")* on the altar might clip beneath the surface, making it unreachable without the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.
  - It is sometimes possible to move the book out of the altar by using an explosive spell such as [Fireball](/wiki/Skyrim:Fireball "Skyrim:Fireball").
